Etterlay 1

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandyay._


Stay. Etersburghpay, Ecday. 11th, 17—.


Youyay illway ejoiceray otay earhay atthay onay isasterday ashay accompaniedyay ethay
ommencementcay ofyay anyay enterpriseyay ichwhay youyay avehay egardedray ithway uchsay evilyay
orebodingsfay. Iyay arrivedyay erehay yesterdayyay, andyay ymay irstfay asktay isyay otay assureyay
ymay earday istersay ofyay ymay elfareway andyay increasingyay onfidencecay inyay ethay uccesssay
ofyay ymay undertakingyay.

Iyay amyay alreadyyay arfay orthnay ofyay Ondonlay, andyay asyay Iyay alkway inyay ethay eetsstray ofyay
Etersburghpay, Iyay eelfay ayay oldcay orthernnay eezebray ayplay uponyay ymay eekschay, ichwhay
acesbray ymay ervesnay andyay illsfay emay ithway elightday. Oday youyay understandyay isthay
eelingfay? Isthay eezebray, ichwhay ashay avelledtray omfray ethay egionsray owardstay
ichwhay Iyay amyay advancingyay, ivesgay emay ayay oretastefay ofyay osethay icyyay imesclay.
Inspiritedyay ybay isthay indway ofyay omisepray, ymay aydreamsday ecomebay oremay erventfay
andyay ividvay. Iyay ytray inyay ainvay otay ebay ersuadedpay atthay ethay olepay isyay ethay eatsay ofyay
ostfray andyay esolationday; ityay everyay esentspray itselfyay otay ymay imaginationyay asyay ethay
egionray ofyay eautybay andyay elightday. Erethay, Argaretmay, ethay unsay isyay orfay everyay
isiblevay, itsyay oadbray iskday ustjay irtingskay ethay orizonhay andyay iffusingday ayay
erpetualpay endoursplay. Ere—forthay ithway youryay eavelay, ymay istersay, Iyay illway utpay
omesay usttray inyay ecedingpray avigators—therenay owsnay andyay ostfray areyay anishedbay;
andyay, ailingsay overyay ayay almcay easay, eway aymay ebay aftedway otay ayay andlay urpassingsay inyay
ondersway andyay inyay eautybay everyyay egionray ithertohay iscoveredday onyay ethay abitablehay
obeglay. Itsyay oductionspray andyay eaturesfay aymay ebay ithoutway exampleyay, asyay ethay
enomenaphay ofyay ethay eavenlyhay odiesbay undoubtedlyyay areyay inyay osethay undiscoveredyay
olitudessay. Atwhay aymay otnay ebay expectedyay inyay ayay ountrycay ofyay eternalyay ightlay? Iyay
aymay erethay iscoverday ethay ondrousway owerpay ichwhay attractsyay ethay eedlenay andyay aymay
egulateray ayay ousandthay elestialcay observationsyay atthay equireray onlyyay isthay
oyagevay otay enderray eirthay eemingsay eccentricitiesyay onsistentcay orfay everyay. Iyay
allshay atiatesay ymay ardentyay uriositycay ithway ethay ightsay ofyay ayay artpay ofyay ethay orldway
evernay eforebay isitedvay, andyay aymay eadtray ayay andlay evernay eforebay imprintedyay ybay
ethay ootfay ofyay anmay. Esethay areyay ymay enticementsyay, andyay eythay areyay ufficientsay otay
onquercay allyay earfay ofyay angerday oryay eathday andyay otay induceyay emay otay ommencecay isthay
aboriouslay oyagevay ithway ethay oyjay ayay ildchay eelsfay enwhay ehay embarksyay inyay ayay ittlelay
oatbay, ithway ishay olidayhay atesmay, onyay anyay expeditionyay ofyay iscoveryday upyay ishay
ativenay iverray. Utbay upposingsay allyay esethay onjecturescay otay ebay alsefay, youyay
annotcay ontestcay ethay inestimableyay enefitbay ichwhay Iyay allshay onfercay onyay allyay
ankindmay, otay ethay astlay enerationgay, ybay iscoveringday ayay assagepay earnay ethay olepay
otay osethay ountriescay, otay eachray ichwhay atyay esentpray osay anymay onthsmay areyay
equisiteray; oryay ybay ascertainingyay ethay ecretsay ofyay ethay agnetmay, ichwhay, ifyay atyay
allyay ossiblepay, ancay onlyyay ebay effectedyay ybay anyay undertakingyay uchsay asyay inemay.

Esethay eflectionsray avehay ispelledday ethay agitationyay ithway ichwhay Iyay eganbay ymay
etterlay, andyay Iyay eelfay ymay earthay owglay ithway anyay enthusiasmyay ichwhay elevatesyay emay
otay eavenhay, orfay othingnay ontributescay osay uchmay otay anquillisetray ethay indmay asyay
ayay eadystay urpose—apay ointpay onyay ichwhay ethay oulsay aymay ixfay itsyay intellectualyay
eyeyay. Isthay expeditionyay ashay eenbay ethay avouritefay eamdray ofyay ymay earlyyay yearsyay. Iyay
avehay eadray ithway ardouryay ethay accountsyay ofyay ethay ariousvay oyagesvay ichwhay avehay
eenbay ademay inyay ethay ospectpray ofyay arrivingyay atyay ethay Orthnay Acificpay Oceanyay
oughthray ethay eassay ichwhay urroundsay ethay olepay. Youyay aymay ememberray atthay ayay
istoryhay ofyay allyay ethay oyagesvay ademay orfay urposespay ofyay iscoveryday omposedcay ethay
olewhay ofyay ouryay oodgay Uncleyay Omasthay’ ibrarylay. Ymay educationyay asway eglectednay,
yetyay Iyay asway assionatelypay ondfay ofyay eadingray. Esethay olumesvay ereway ymay udystay
ayday andyay ightnay, andyay ymay amiliarityfay ithway emthay increasedyay atthay egretray ichwhay
Iyay adhay eltfay, asyay ayay ildchay, onyay earninglay atthay ymay ather’sfay yingday injunctionyay
adhay orbiddenfay ymay uncleyay otay allowyay emay otay embarkyay inyay ayay eafaringsay ifelay.

Esethay isionsvay adedfay enwhay Iyay erusedpay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, osethay oetspay
osewhay effusionsyay entrancedyay ymay oulsay andyay iftedlay ityay otay eavenhay. Iyay alsoyay
ecamebay ayay oetpay andyay orfay oneyay yearyay ivedlay inyay ayay aradisepay ofyay ymay ownyay eationcray;
Iyay imaginedyay atthay Iyay alsoyay ightmay obtainyay ayay ichenay inyay ethay empletay erewhay ethay
amesnay ofyay Omerhay andyay Akespeareshay areyay onsecratedcay. Youyay areyay ellway
acquaintedyay ithway ymay ailurefay andyay owhay eavilyhay Iyay orebay ethay isappointmentday.
Utbay ustjay atyay atthay imetay Iyay inheritedyay ethay ortunefay ofyay ymay ousincay, andyay ymay
oughtsthay ereway urnedtay intoyay ethay annelchay ofyay eirthay earlieryay entbay.

Ixsay yearsyay avehay assedpay incesay Iyay esolvedray onyay ymay esentpray undertakingyay. Iyay
ancay, evenyay ownay, ememberray ethay ourhay omfray ichwhay Iyay edicatedday yselfmay otay isthay
eatgray enterpriseyay. Iyay ommencedcay ybay inuringyay ymay odybay otay ardshiphay. Iyay
accompaniedyay ethay ale-fisherswhay onyay everalsay expeditionsyay otay ethay Orthnay Easay;
Iyay oluntarilyvay enduredyay oldcay, aminefay, irstthay, andyay antway ofyay eepslay; Iyay oftenyay
orkedway arderhay anthay ethay ommoncay ailorssay uringday ethay ayday andyay evotedday ymay
ightsnay otay ethay udystay ofyay athematicsmay, ethay eorythay ofyay edicinemay, andyay osethay
anchesbray ofyay ysicalphay iencescay omfray ichwhay ayay avalnay adventureryay ightmay eriveday
ethay eatestgray acticalpray advantageyay. Icetway Iyay actuallyyay iredhay yselfmay asyay anyay
under-mateyay inyay ayay Eenlandgray alerwhay, andyay acquittedyay yselfmay otay admirationyay. Iyay
ustmay ownyay Iyay eltfay ayay ittlelay oudpray enwhay ymay aptaincay offeredyay emay ethay econdsay
ignityday inyay ethay esselvay andyay entreatedyay emay otay emainray ithway ethay eatestgray
earnestnessyay, osay aluablevay idday ehay onsidercay ymay ervicessay.

Andyay ownay, earday Argaretmay, oday Iyay otnay eserveday otay accomplishyay omesay eatgray urposepay?
Ymay ifelay ightmay avehay eenbay assedpay inyay easeyay andyay uxurylay, utbay Iyay eferredpray oryglay otay
everyyay enticementyay atthay ealthway acedplay inyay ymay athpay. Ohyay, atthay omesay encouragingyay
oicevay ouldway answeryay inyay ethay affirmativeyay! Ymay ouragecay andyay ymay esolutionray isyay
irmfay; utbay ymay opeshay uctuateflay, andyay ymay iritsspay areyay oftenyay epressedday. Iyay amyay
aboutyay otay oceedpray onyay ayay onglay andyay ifficultday oyagevay, ethay emergenciesyay ofyay ichwhay
illway emandday allyay ymay ortitudefay: Iyay amyay equiredray otnay onlyyay otay aiseray ethay iritsspay
ofyay othersyay, utbay ometimessay otay ustainsay ymay ownyay, enwhay eirsthay areyay ailingfay.

Isthay isyay ethay ostmay avourablefay eriodpay orfay avellingtray inyay Ussiaray. Eythay yflay
uicklyqay overyay ethay owsnay inyay eirthay edgesslay; ethay otionmay isyay easantplay, andyay, inyay
ymay opinionyay, arfay oremay agreeableyay anthay atthay ofyay anyay Englishyay agecoachstay. Ethay
oldcay isyay otnay excessiveyay, ifyay youyay areyay appedwray inyay urs—afay essdray ichwhay Iyay avehay
alreadyyay adoptedyay, orfay erethay isyay ayay eatgray ifferenceday etweenbay alkingway ethay
eckday andyay emainingray eatedsay otionlessmay orfay ourshay, enwhay onay exerciseyay
eventspray ethay oodblay omfray actuallyyay eezingfray inyay youryay einsvay. Iyay avehay onay
ambitionyay otay oselay ymay ifelay onyay ethay ost-roadpay etweenbay Stay. Etersburghpay andyay
Archangelyay.

Iyay allshay epartday orfay ethay atterlay owntay inyay ayay ortnightfay oryay eethray eeksway; andyay ymay
intentionyay isyay otay irehay ayay ipshay erethay, ichwhay ancay easilyyay ebay oneday ybay ayingpay ethay
insuranceyay orfay ethay owneryay, andyay otay engageyay asyay anymay ailorssay asyay Iyay inkthay ecessarynay
amongyay osethay owhay areyay accustomedyay otay ethay ale-fishingwhay. Iyay oday otnay intendyay otay
ailsay untilyay ethay onthmay ofyay Unejay; andyay enwhay allshay Iyay eturnray? Ahyay, earday istersay, owhay
ancay Iyay answeryay isthay uestionqay? Ifyay Iyay ucceedsay, anymay, anymay onthsmay, erhapspay yearsyay,
illway asspay eforebay youyay andyay Iyay aymay eetmay. Ifyay Iyay ailfay, youyay illway eesay emay againyay oonsay,
oryay evernay.

Arewellfay, ymay earday, excellentyay Argaretmay. Eavenhay owershay ownday essingsblay onyay youyay,
andyay avesay emay, atthay Iyay aymay againyay andyay againyay estifytay ymay atitudegray orfay allyay youryay
ovelay andyay indnesskay.

Youryay affectionateyay otherbray,

Ray. Altonway




Etterlay 2

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandyay._

Archangelyay, 28th Archmay, 17—.


Owhay owlyslay ethay imetay assespay erehay, encompassedyay asyay Iyay amyay ybay ostfray andyay owsnay!
Yetyay ayay econdsay epstay isyay akentay owardstay ymay enterpriseyay. Iyay avehay iredhay ayay
esselvay andyay amyay occupiedyay inyay ollectingcay ymay ailorssay; osethay omwhay Iyay avehay
alreadyyay engagedyay appearyay otay ebay enmay onyay omwhay Iyay ancay ependday andyay areyay ertainlycay
ossessedpay ofyay auntlessday ouragecay.

Utbay Iyay avehay oneyay antway ichwhay Iyay avehay evernay yetyay eenbay ableyay otay atisfysay, andyay ethay
absenceyay ofyay ethay objectyay ofyay ichwhay Iyay ownay eelfay asyay ayay ostmay everesay evilyay, Iyay avehay onay
iendfray, Argaretmay: enwhay Iyay amyay owingglay ithway ethay enthusiasmyay ofyay uccesssay, erethay
illway ebay onenay otay articipatepay ymay oyjay; ifyay Iyay amyay assailedyay ybay isappointmentday, onay
oneyay illway endeavouryay otay ustainsay emay inyay ejectionday. Iyay allshay ommitcay ymay oughtsthay
otay aperpay, ityay isyay uetray; utbay atthay isyay ayay oorpay ediummay orfay ethay ommunicationcay ofyay
eelingfay. Iyay esireday ethay ompanycay ofyay ayay anmay owhay ouldcay ympathisesay ithway emay, osewhay
eyesyay ouldway eplyray otay inemay. Youyay aymay eemday emay omanticray, ymay earday istersay, utbay Iyay
itterlybay eelfay ethay antway ofyay ayay iendfray. Iyay avehay onay oneyay earnay emay, entlegay yetyay
ourageouscay, ossessedpay ofyay ayay ultivatedcay asyay ellway asyay ofyay ayay apaciouscay indmay, osewhay
astestay areyay ikelay ymay ownyay, otay approveyay oryay amendyay ymay ansplay. Owhay ouldway uchsay ayay
iendfray epairray ethay aultsfay ofyay youryay oorpay otherbray! Iyay amyay ootay ardentyay inyay executionyay
andyay ootay impatientyay ofyay ifficultiesday. Utbay ityay isyay ayay illstay eatergray evilyay otay emay
atthay Iyay amyay elf-educatedsay: orfay ethay irstfay ourteenfay yearsyay ofyay ymay ifelay Iyay anray ildway
onyay ayay ommoncay andyay eadray othingnay utbay ouryay Uncleyay Omasthay’ ooksbay ofyay oyagesvay.
Atyay atthay ageyay Iyay ecamebay acquaintedyay ithway ethay elebratedcay oetspay ofyay ouryay ownyay
ountrycay; utbay ityay asway onlyyay enwhay ityay adhay easedcay otay ebay inyay ymay owerpay otay eriveday itsyay
ostmay importantyay enefitsbay omfray uchsay ayay onvictioncay atthay Iyay erceivedpay ethay
ecessitynay ofyay ecomingbay acquaintedyay ithway oremay anguageslay anthay atthay ofyay ymay ativenay
ountrycay. Ownay Iyay amyay enty-eighttway andyay amyay inyay ealityray oremay illiterateyay anthay anymay
oolboysschay ofyay ifteenfay. Ityay isyay uetray atthay Iyay avehay oughtthay oremay andyay atthay ymay
aydreamsday areyay oremay extendedyay andyay agnificentmay, utbay eythay antway as(ay ethay ainterspay
allcay ityay) eeping_kay;_ andyay Iyay eatlygray eednay ayay iendfray owhay ouldway avehay ensesay
enoughyay otnay otay espiseday emay asyay omanticray, andyay affectionyay enoughyay orfay emay otay
endeavouryay otay egulateray ymay indmay.

Ellway, esethay areyay uselessyay omplaintscay; Iyay allshay ertainlycay indfay onay iendfray onyay ethay
ideway oceanyay, ornay evenyay erehay inyay Archangelyay, amongyay erchantsmay andyay eamensay. Yetyay
omesay eelingsfay, unalliedyay otay ethay ossdray ofyay umanhay aturenay, eatbay evenyay inyay esethay
uggedray osomsbay. Ymay ieutenantlay, orfay instanceyay, isyay ayay anmay ofyay onderfulway ouragecay
andyay enterpriseyay; ehay isyay adlymay esirousday ofyay oryglay, oryay atherray, otay ordway ymay asephray
oremay aracteristicallychay, ofyay advancementyay inyay ishay ofessionpray. Ehay isyay anyay
Englishmanyay, andyay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay ationalnay andyay ofessionalpray ejudicespray,
unsoftenedyay ybay ultivationcay, etainsray omesay ofyay ethay oblestnay endowmentsyay ofyay
umanityhay. Iyay irstfay ecamebay acquaintedyay ithway imhay onyay oardbay ayay alewhay esselvay;
indingfay atthay ehay asway unemployedyay inyay isthay itycay, Iyay easilyyay engagedyay imhay otay assistyay
inyay ymay enterpriseyay.

Ethay astermay isyay ayay ersonpay ofyay anyay excellentyay ispositionday andyay isyay emarkableray inyay ethay
ipshay orfay ishay entlenessgay andyay ethay ildnessmay ofyay ishay isciplineday. Isthay
ircumstancecay, addedyay otay ishay ell-knownway integrityyay andyay auntlessday ouragecay, ademay
emay eryvay esirousday otay engageyay imhay. Ayay youthyay assedpay inyay olitudesay, ymay estbay yearsyay
entspay underyay youryay entlegay andyay emininefay osteragefay, ashay osay efinedray ethay
oundworkgray ofyay ymay aracterchay atthay Iyay annotcay overcomeyay anyay intenseyay istasteday otay
ethay usualyay utalitybray exercisedyay onyay oardbay ipshay: Iyay avehay evernay elievedbay ityay otay ebay
ecessarynay, andyay enwhay Iyay eardhay ofyay ayay arinermay equallyyay otednay orfay ishay indlinesskay
ofyay earthay andyay ethay espectray andyay obedienceyay aidpay otay imhay ybay ishay ewcray, Iyay eltfay
yselfmay eculiarlypay ortunatefay inyay eingbay ableyay otay ecuresay ishay ervicessay. Iyay eardhay
ofyay imhay irstfay inyay atherray ayay omanticray annermay, omfray ayay adylay owhay owesyay otay imhay ethay
appinesshay ofyay erhay ifelay. Isthay, ieflybray, isyay ishay orystay. Omesay yearsyay agoyay ehay ovedlay
ayay youngyay Ussianray adylay ofyay oderatemay ortunefay, andyay avinghay amassedyay ayay onsiderablecay
umsay inyay ize-moneypray, ethay atherfay ofyay ethay irlgay onsentedcay otay ethay atchmay. Ehay awsay
ishay istressmay onceyay eforebay ethay estinedday eremonycay; utbay eshay asway athedbay inyay
earstay, andyay owingthray erselfhay atyay ishay eetfay, entreatedyay imhay otay arespay erhay,
onfessingcay atyay ethay amesay imetay atthay eshay ovedlay anotheryay, utbay atthay ehay asway oorpay,
andyay atthay erhay atherfay ouldway evernay onsentcay otay ethay unionyay. Ymay enerousgay iendfray
eassuredray ethay uppliantsay, andyay onyay eingbay informedyay ofyay ethay amenay ofyay erhay overlay,
instantlyyay abandonedyay ishay ursuitpay. Ehay adhay alreadyyay oughtbay ayay armfay ithway ishay
oneymay, onyay ichwhay ehay adhay esignedday otay asspay ethay emainderray ofyay ishay ifelay; utbay ehay
estowedbay ethay olewhay onyay ishay ivalray, ogethertay ithway ethay emainsray ofyay ishay
ize-moneypray otay urchasepay ockstay, andyay enthay imselfhay olicitedsay ethay youngyay
oman’sway atherfay otay onsentcay otay erhay arriagemay ithway erhay overlay. Utbay ethay oldyay
anmay ecidedlyday efusedray, inkingthay imselfhay oundbay inyay onourhay otay ymay iendfray, owhay,
enwhay ehay oundfay ethay atherfay inexorableyay, uittedqay ishay ountrycay, ornay eturnedray
untilyay ehay eardhay atthay ishay ormerfay istressmay asway arriedmay accordingyay otay erhay
inclinationsyay. at“whay ayay oblenay ellowfay!” youyay illway exclaimyay. Ehay isyay
osay; utbay enthay ehay isyay ollywhay uneducatedyay: ehay isyay asyay ilentsay asyay ayay Urktay, andyay ayay indkay
ofyay ignorantyay arelessnesscay attendsyay imhay, ichwhay, ilewhay ityay endersray ishay onductcay
ethay oremay astonishingyay, etractsday omfray ethay interestyay andyay ympathysay ichwhay
otherwiseyay ehay ouldway ommandcay.

Yetyay oday otnay upposesay, ecausebay Iyay omplaincay ayay ittlelay oryay ecausebay Iyay ancay
onceivecay ayay onsolationcay orfay ymay oilstay ichwhay Iyay aymay evernay owknay, atthay Iyay amyay
averingway inyay ymay esolutionsray. Osethay areyay asyay ixedfay asyay atefay, andyay ymay oyagevay
isyay onlyyay ownay elayedday untilyay ethay eatherway allshay ermitpay ymay embarkationyay. Ethay
interway ashay eenbay eadfullydray everesay, utbay ethay ingspray omisespray ellway, andyay ityay
isyay onsideredcay asyay ayay emarkablyray earlyyay easonsay, osay atthay erhapspay Iyay aymay ailsay
oonersay anthay Iyay expectedyay. Iyay allshay oday othingnay ashlyray: youyay owknay emay
ufficientlysay otay onfidecay inyay ymay udencepray andyay onsideratenesscay eneverwhay ethay
afetysay ofyay othersyay isyay ommittedcay otay ymay arecay.

Iyay annotcay escribeday otay youyay ymay ensationssay onyay ethay earnay ospectpray ofyay ymay
undertakingyay. Ityay isyay impossibleyay otay ommunicatecay otay youyay ayay onceptioncay ofyay
ethay emblingtray ensationsay, alfhay easurableplay andyay alfhay earfulfay, ithway ichwhay
Iyay amyay eparingpray otay epartday. Iyay amyay oinggay otay unexploredyay egionsray, otay e“thay
andlay ofyay istmay andyay owsnay,” utbay Iyay allshay illkay onay albatrossyay; ereforethay oday otnay
ebay alarmedyay orfay ymay afetysay oryay ifyay Iyay ouldshay omecay ackbay otay youyay asyay ornway andyay
oefulway asyay ethay ancient“ay Arinermay.” Youyay illway ilesmay atyay ymay allusionyay, utbay Iyay
illway iscloseday ayay ecretsay. Iyay avehay oftenyay attributedyay ymay attachmentyay otay, ymay
assionatepay enthusiasmyay orfay, ethay angerousday ysteriesmay ofyay oceanyay otay atthay
oductionpray ofyay ethay ostmay imaginativeyay ofyay odernmay oetspay. Erethay isyay omethingsay
atyay orkway inyay ymay oulsay ichwhay Iyay oday otnay understandyay. Iyay amyay acticallypray
industrious—painstakingyay, ayay orkmanway otay executeyay ithway erseverancepay andyay
abour—butlay esidesbay isthay erethay isyay ayay ovelay orfay ethay arvellousmay, ayay eliefbay
inyay ethay arvellousmay, intertwinedyay inyay allyay ymay ojectspray, ichwhay urrieshay emay outyay
ofyay ethay ommoncay athwayspay ofyay enmay, evenyay otay ethay ildway easay andyay unvisitedyay
egionsray Iyay amyay aboutyay otay exploreyay.

Utbay otay eturnray otay earerday onsiderationscay. Allshay Iyay eetmay youyay againyay, afteryay
avinghay aversedtray immenseyay eassay, andyay eturnedray ybay ethay ostmay outhernsay apecay ofyay
Africayay oryay Americayay? Iyay areday otnay expectyay uchsay uccesssay, yetyay Iyay annotcay earbay otay
ooklay onyay ethay everseray ofyay ethay icturepay. Ontinuecay orfay ethay esentpray otay itewray otay
emay ybay everyyay opportunityyay: Iyay aymay eceiveray youryay etterslay onyay omesay occasionsyay enwhay
Iyay eednay emthay ostmay otay upportsay ymay iritsspay. Iyay ovelay youyay eryvay enderlytay. 
Ememberray emay ithway affectionyay, ouldshay youyay evernay earhay omfray emay againyay.

Youryay affectionateyay otherbray,
 Obertray Altonway




Etterlay 3

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandyay._

Ulyjay 7th, 17—.


Ymay earday Istersay,

Iyay itewray ayay ewfay ineslay inyay astehay otay aysay atthay Iyay amyay afe—andsay ellway advancedyay
onyay ymay oyagevay. Isthay etterlay illway eachray Englandyay ybay ayay erchantmanmay ownay onyay
itsyay omewardhay oyagevay omfray Archangelyay; oremay ortunatefay anthay Iyay, owhay aymay otnay
eesay ymay ativenay andlay, erhapspay, orfay anymay yearsyay. Iyay amyay, oweverhay, inyay oodgay
iritsspay: ymay enmay areyay oldbay andyay apparentlyyay irmfay ofyay urposepay, ornay oday ethay
oatingflay eetsshay ofyay iceyay atthay ontinuallycay asspay usyay, indicatingyay ethay angersday
ofyay ethay egionray owardstay ichwhay eway areyay advancingyay, appearyay otay ismayday emthay. Eway
avehay alreadyyay eachedray ayay eryvay ighhay atitudelay; utbay ityay isyay ethay eighthay ofyay
ummersay, andyay althoughyay otnay osay armway asyay inyay Englandyay, ethay outhernsay alesgay,
ichwhay owblay usyay eedilyspay owardstay osethay oresshay ichwhay Iyay osay ardentlyyay esireday
otay attainyay, eathebray ayay egreeday ofyay enovatingray armthway ichwhay Iyay adhay otnay
expectedyay.

Onay incidentsyay avehay ithertohay efallenbay usyay atthay ouldway akemay ayay igurefay inyay ayay
etterlay. Oneyay oryay otway iffstay alesgay andyay ethay ingingspray ofyay ayay eaklay areyay
accidentsyay ichwhay experiencedyay avigatorsnay arcelyscay ememberray otay ecordray, andyay
Iyay allshay ebay ellway ontentcay ifyay othingnay orseway appenhay otay usyay uringday ouryay oyagevay.

Adieuyay, ymay earday Argaretmay. Ebay assuredyay atthay orfay ymay ownyay akesay, asyay ellway asyay
yoursyay, Iyay illway otnay ashlyray encounteryay angerday. Iyay illway ebay oolcay,
erseveringpay, andyay udentpray.

Utbay uccesssay all_shay_ owncray ymay endeavoursyay. Ereforewhay otnay? Usthay arfay Iyay
avehay onegay, acingtray ayay ecuresay ayway overyay ethay athlesspay eassay, ethay eryvay arsstay
emselvesthay eingbay itnessesway andyay estimoniestay ofyay ymay iumphtray. Ywhay otnay
illstay oceedpray overyay ethay untamedyay yetyay obedientyay elementyay? Atwhay ancay opstay ethay
eterminedday earthay andyay esolvedray illway ofyay anmay?

Ymay ellingsway earthay involuntarilyyay ourspay itselfyay outyay usthay. Utbay Iyay ustmay
inishfay. Eavenhay essblay ymay elovedbay istersay!

R.way.




Etterlay 4


o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englandyay._

Augustyay 5th, 17—.

Osay angestray anyay accidentyay ashay appenedhay otay usyay atthay Iyay annotcay orbearfay
ecordingray ityay, althoughyay ityay isyay eryvay obablepray atthay youyay illway eesay emay eforebay
esethay aperspay ancay omecay intoyay youryay ossessionpay.

Astlay Ondaymay uly(jay 31st) eway ereway earlynay urroundedsay ybay iceyay, ichwhay osedclay
inyay ethay ipshay onyay allyay idessay, arcelyscay eavinglay erhay ethay ea-roomsay inyay ichwhay
eshay oatedflay. Ouryay ituationsay asway omewhatsay angerousday, especiallyyay asyay eway
ereway ompassedcay oundray ybay ayay eryvay ickthay ogfay. Eway accordinglyyay aylay otay,
opinghay atthay omesay angechay ouldway aketay aceplay inyay ethay atmosphereyay andyay eatherway.

Aboutyay otway o’clockyay ethay istmay earedclay awayyay, andyay eway eheldbay, etchedstray outyay
inyay everyyay irectionday, astvay andyay irregularyay ainsplay ofyay iceyay, ichwhay eemedsay otay
avehay onay endyay. Omesay ofyay ymay omradescay oanedgray, andyay ymay ownyay indmay eganbay otay
owgray atchfulway ithway anxiousyay oughtsthay, enwhay ayay angestray ightsay uddenlysay
attractedyay ouryay attentionyay andyay ivertedday ouryay olicitudesay omfray ouryay ownyay
ituationsay. Eway erceivedpay ayay owlay arriagecay, ixedfay onyay ayay edgeslay andyay awndray ybay
ogsday, asspay onyay owardstay ethay orthnay, atyay ethay istanceday ofyay alfhay ayay ilemay; ayay
eingbay ichwhay adhay ethay apeshay ofyay ayay anmay, utbay apparentlyyay ofyay iganticgay aturestay,
atsay inyay ethay edgeslay andyay uidedgay ethay ogsday. Eway atchedway ethay apidray ogresspray
ofyay ethay avellertray ithway ouryay elescopestay untilyay ehay asway ostlay amongyay ethay
istantday inequalitiesyay ofyay ethay iceyay.

Isthay appearanceyay excitedyay ouryay unqualifiedyay onderway. Eway ereway, asyay eway elievedbay,
anymay undredhay ilesmay omfray anyyay andlay; utbay isthay apparitionyay eemedsay otay enoteday atthay
ityay asway otnay, inyay ealityray, osay istantday asyay eway adhay upposedsay. Utshay inyay, oweverhay, ybay
iceyay, ityay asway impossibleyay otay ollowfay ishay acktray, ichwhay eway adhay observedyay ithway ethay
eatestgray attentionyay.

Aboutyay otway ourshay afteryay isthay occurrenceyay eway eardhay ethay oundgray easay, andyay eforebay
ightnay ethay iceyay okebray andyay eedfray ouryay ipshay. Eway, oweverhay, aylay otay untilyay ethay
orningmay, earingfay otay encounteryay inyay ethay arkday osethay argelay ooselay assesmay ichwhay
oatflay aboutyay afteryay ethay eakingbray upyay ofyay ethay iceyay. Iyay ofitedpray ofyay isthay imetay otay
estray orfay ayay ewfay ourshay.

Inyay ethay orningmay, oweverhay, asyay oonsay asyay ityay asway ightlay, Iyay entway uponyay eckday andyay
oundfay allyay ethay ailorssay usybay onyay oneyay idesay ofyay ethay esselvay, apparentlyyay
alkingtay otay omeonesay inyay ethay easay. Ityay asway, inyay actfay, ayay edgeslay, ikelay atthay eway
adhay eensay eforebay, ichwhay adhay ifteddray owardstay usyay inyay ethay ightnay onyay ayay argelay
agmentfray ofyay iceyay. Onlyyay oneyay ogday emainedray aliveyay; utbay erethay asway ayay umanhay
eingbay ithinway ityay omwhay ethay ailorssay ereway ersuadingpay otay enteryay ethay esselvay.
Ehay asway otnay, asyay ethay otheryay avellertray eemedsay otay ebay, ayay avagesay inhabitantyay ofyay
omesay undiscoveredyay islandyay, utbay ayay Europeanyay. Enwhay Iyay appearedyay onyay eckday ethay
astermay aidsay, ere“hay isyay ouryay aptaincay, andyay ehay illway otnay allowyay youyay otay erishpay
onyay ethay openyay easay.”

Onyay erceivingpay emay, ethay angerstray addressedyay emay inyay Englishyay, althoughyay ithway ayay
oreignfay accentyay. efore“bay Iyay omecay onyay oardbay youryay esselvay,” aidsay ehay,
ill“way youyay avehay ethay indnesskay otay informyay emay itherwhay youyay areyay oundbay?”

Youyay aymay onceivecay ymay astonishmentyay onyay earinghay uchsay ayay uestionqay addressedyay
otay emay omfray ayay anmay onyay ethay inkbray ofyay estructionday andyay otay omwhay Iyay ouldshay avehay
upposedsay atthay ymay esselvay ouldway avehay eenbay ayay esourceray ichwhay ehay ouldway otnay
avehay exchangedyay orfay ethay ostmay eciouspray ealthway ethay earthyay ancay affordyay. Iyay
epliedray, oweverhay, atthay eway ereway onyay ayay oyagevay ofyay iscoveryday owardstay ethay
orthernnay olepay.

Uponyay earinghay isthay ehay appearedyay atisfiedsay andyay onsentedcay otay omecay onyay oardbay.
Oodgay Odgay! Argaretmay, ifyay youyay adhay eensay ethay anmay owhay usthay apitulatedcay orfay
ishay afetysay, youryay urprisesay ouldway avehay eenbay oundlessbay. Ishay imbslay ereway
earlynay ozenfray, andyay ishay odybay eadfullydray emaciatedyay ybay atiguefay andyay
ufferingsay. Iyay evernay awsay ayay anmay inyay osay etchedwray ayay onditioncay. Eway attemptedyay
otay arrycay imhay intoyay ethay abincay, utbay asyay oonsay asyay ehay adhay uittedqay ethay eshfray
airyay ehay aintedfay. Eway accordinglyyay oughtbray imhay ackbay otay ethay eckday andyay
estoredray imhay otay animationyay ybay ubbingray imhay ithway andybray andyay orcingfay imhay otay
allowsway ayay allsmay uantityqay. Asyay oonsay asyay ehay owedshay ignssay ofyay ifelay eway
appedwray imhay upyay inyay anketsblay andyay acedplay imhay earnay ethay imneychay ofyay ethay
itchenkay ovestay. Ybay owslay egreesday ehay ecoveredray andyay ateyay ayay ittlelay oupsay,
ichwhay estoredray imhay onderfullyway.

Otway aysday assedpay inyay isthay annermay eforebay ehay asway ableyay otay eakspay, andyay Iyay oftenyay
earedfay atthay ishay ufferingssay adhay eprivedday imhay ofyay understandingyay. Enwhay ehay
adhay inyay omesay easuremay ecoveredray, Iyay emovedray imhay otay ymay ownyay abincay andyay
attendedyay onyay imhay asyay uchmay asyay ymay utyday ouldway ermitpay. Iyay evernay awsay ayay oremay
interestingyay eaturecray: ishay eyesyay avehay enerallygay anyay expressionyay ofyay
ildnessway, andyay evenyay adnessmay, utbay erethay areyay omentsmay enwhay, ifyay anyoneyay
erformspay anyay actyay ofyay indnesskay owardstay imhay oryay oesday imhay anyyay ethay ostmay
iflingtray ervicesay, ishay olewhay ountenancecay isyay ightedlay upyay, asyay ityay ereway, ithway
ayay eambay ofyay enevolencebay andyay eetnesssway atthay Iyay evernay awsay equalledyay. Utbay ehay
isyay enerallygay elancholymay andyay espairingday, andyay ometimessay ehay ashesgnay ishay
eethtay, asyay ifyay impatientyay ofyay ethay eightway ofyay oesway atthay oppressesyay imhay.

Enwhay ymay uestgay asway ayay ittlelay ecoveredray Iyay adhay eatgray oubletray otay eepkay offyay
ethay enmay, owhay ishedway otay askyay imhay ayay ousandthay uestionsqay; utbay Iyay ouldway otnay
allowyay imhay otay ebay ormentedtay ybay eirthay idleyay uriositycay, inyay ayay atestay ofyay odybay
andyay indmay osewhay estorationray evidentlyyay ependedday uponyay entireyay eposeray.
Onceyay, oweverhay, ethay ieutenantlay askedyay ywhay ehay adhay omecay osay arfay uponyay ethay iceyay
inyay osay angestray ayay ehiclevay.

Ishay ountenancecay instantlyyay assumedyay anyay aspectyay ofyay ethay eepestday oomglay, andyay
ehay epliedray, o“tay eeksay oneyay owhay edflay omfray emay.”

and“ay idday ethay anmay omwhay youyay ursuedpay aveltray inyay ethay amesay ashionfay?”

yes“ay.”

en“thay Iyay ancyfay eway avehay eensay imhay, orfay ethay ayday eforebay eway ickedpay youyay upyay eway
awsay omesay ogsday awingdray ayay edgeslay, ithway ayay anmay inyay ityay, acrossyay ethay iceyay.”

Isthay arousedyay ethay anger’sstray attentionyay, andyay ehay askedyay ayay ultitudemay ofyay
uestionsqay oncerningcay ethay outeray ichwhay ethay ondæmay, asyay ehay alledcay imhay, adhay
ursuedpay. Oonsay afteryay, enwhay ehay asway aloneyay ithway emay, ehay aidsay, i“ay avehay,
oubtlessday, excitedyay youryay uriositycay, asyay ellway asyay atthay ofyay esethay oodgay
eoplepay; utbay youyay areyay ootay onsideratecay otay akemay inquiriesyay.”

ertainly“cay; ityay ouldway indeedyay ebay eryvay impertinentyay andyay inhumanyay inyay emay otay
oubletray youyay ithway anyyay inquisitivenessyay ofyay inemay.”

and“ay yetyay youyay escuedray emay omfray ayay angestray andyay erilouspay ituationsay; youyay avehay
enevolentlybay estoredray emay otay ifelay.”

Oonsay afteryay isthay ehay inquiredyay ifyay Iyay oughtthay atthay ethay eakingbray upyay ofyay ethay
iceyay adhay estroyedday ethay otheryay edgeslay. Iyay epliedray atthay Iyay ouldcay otnay answeryay
ithway anyyay egreeday ofyay ertaintycay, orfay ethay iceyay adhay otnay okenbray untilyay earnay
idnightmay, andyay ethay avellertray ightmay avehay arrivedyay atyay ayay aceplay ofyay afetysay
eforebay atthay imetay; utbay ofyay isthay Iyay ouldcay otnay udgejay.

Omfray isthay imetay ayay ewnay iritspay ofyay ifelay animatedyay ethay ecayingday amefray ofyay ethay
angerstray. Ehay anifestedmay ethay eatestgray eagernessyay otay ebay uponyay eckday otay atchway orfay
ethay edgeslay ichwhay adhay eforebay appearedyay; utbay Iyay avehay ersuadedpay imhay otay emainray inyay
ethay abincay, orfay ehay isyay arfay ootay eakway otay ustainsay ethay awnessray ofyay ethay atmosphereyay.
Iyay avehay omisedpray atthay omeonesay ouldshay atchway orfay imhay andyay ivegay imhay instantyay
oticenay ifyay anyyay ewnay objectyay ouldshay appearyay inyay ightsay.

Uchsay isyay ymay ournaljay ofyay atwhay elatesray otay isthay angestray occurrenceyay upyay otay ethay
esentpray ayday. Ethay angerstray ashay aduallygray improvedyay inyay ealthhay utbay isyay eryvay
ilentsay andyay appearsyay uneasyyay enwhay anyoneyay exceptyay yselfmay entersyay ishay abincay.
Yetyay ishay annersmay areyay osay onciliatingcay andyay entlegay atthay ethay ailorssay areyay allyay
interestedyay inyay imhay, althoughyay eythay avehay adhay eryvay ittlelay ommunicationcay
ithway imhay. Orfay ymay ownyay artpay, Iyay eginbay otay ovelay imhay asyay ayay otherbray, andyay ishay
onstantcay andyay eepday iefgray illsfay emay ithway ympathysay andyay ompassioncay. Ehay ustmay
avehay eenbay ayay oblenay eaturecray inyay ishay etterbay aysday, eingbay evenyay ownay inyay eckwray
osay attractiveyay andyay amiableyay.

Iyay aidsay inyay oneyay ofyay ymay etterslay, ymay earday Argaretmay, atthay Iyay ouldshay indfay onay iendfray
onyay ethay ideway oceanyay; yetyay Iyay avehay oundfay ayay anmay owhay, eforebay ishay iritspay adhay eenbay
okenbray ybay iserymay, Iyay ouldshay avehay eenbay appyhay otay avehay ossessedpay asyay ethay otherbray
ofyay ymay earthay.

Iyay allshay ontinuecay ymay ournaljay oncerningcay ethay angerstray atyay intervalsyay,
ouldshay Iyay avehay anyyay eshfray incidentsyay otay ecordray.




Augustyay 13th, 17—.


Ymay affectionyay orfay ymay uestgay increasesyay everyyay ayday. Ehay excitesyay atyay onceyay ymay
admirationyay andyay ymay itypay otay anyay astonishingyay egreeday. Owhay ancay Iyay eesay osay
oblenay ayay eaturecray estroyedday ybay iserymay ithoutway eelingfay ethay ostmay oignantpay
iefgray? Ehay isyay osay entlegay, yetyay osay iseway; ishay indmay isyay osay ultivatedcay, andyay
enwhay ehay eaksspay, althoughyay ishay ordsway areyay ulledcay ithway ethay oicestchay artyay,
yetyay eythay owflay ithway apidityray andyay unparalleledyay eloquenceyay.

Ehay isyay ownay uchmay ecoveredray omfray ishay illnessyay andyay isyay ontinuallycay onyay ethay eckday,
apparentlyyay atchingway orfay ethay edgeslay atthay ecededpray ishay ownyay. Yetyay, althoughyay
unhappyyay, ehay isyay otnay osay utterlyyay occupiedyay ybay ishay ownyay iserymay utbay atthay ehay
interestsyay imselfhay eeplyday inyay ethay ojectspray ofyay othersyay. Ehay ashay equentlyfray
onversedcay ithway emay onyay inemay, ichwhay Iyay avehay ommunicatedcay otay imhay ithoutway
isguiseday. Ehay enteredyay attentivelyyay intoyay allyay ymay argumentsyay inyay avourfay ofyay ymay
eventualyay uccesssay andyay intoyay everyyay inutemay etailday ofyay ethay easuresmay Iyay adhay akentay
otay ecuresay ityay. Iyay asway easilyyay edlay ybay ethay ympathysay ichwhay ehay evincedyay otay useyay ethay
anguagelay ofyay ymay earthay, otay ivegay utteranceyay otay ethay urningbay ardouryay ofyay ymay oulsay
andyay otay aysay, ithway allyay ethay ervourfay atthay armedway emay, owhay adlyglay Iyay ouldway
acrificesay ymay ortunefay, ymay existenceyay, ymay everyyay opehay, otay ethay urtherancefay ofyay ymay
enterpriseyay. Oneyay an’smay ifelay oryay eathday ereway utbay ayay allsmay icepray otay aypay orfay
ethay acquirementyay ofyay ethay owledgeknay ichwhay Iyay oughtsay, orfay ethay ominionday Iyay ouldshay
acquireyay andyay ansmittray overyay ethay elementalyay oesfay ofyay ouryay aceray. Asyay Iyay okespay, ayay
arkday oomglay eadspray overyay ymay istener’slay ountenancecay. Atyay irstfay Iyay
erceivedpay atthay ehay iedtray otay uppresssay ishay emotionyay; ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay
ishay eyesyay, andyay ymay oicevay uiveredqay andyay ailedfay emay asyay Iyay eheldbay earstay ickletray
astfay omfray etweenbay ishay ingersfay; ayay oangray urstbay omfray ishay eavinghay eastbray. Iyay
ausedpay; atyay engthlay ehay okespay, inyay okenbray accentsyay: unhappy“ay anmay! Oday youyay
areshay ymay adnessmay? Avehay youyay unkdray alsoyay ofyay ethay intoxicatingyay aughtdray? Earhay emay;
etlay emay evealray ymay aletay, andyay youyay illway ashday ethay upcay omfray youryay ipslay!”

Uchsay ordsway, youyay aymay imagineyay, onglystray excitedyay ymay uriositycay; utbay ethay
aroxysmpay ofyay iefgray atthay adhay eizedsay ethay angerstray overcameyay ishay eakenedway
owerspay, andyay anymay ourshay ofyay eposeray andyay anquiltray onversationcay ereway
ecessarynay otay estoreray ishay omposurecay.

Avinghay onqueredcay ethay iolencevay ofyay ishay eelingsfay, ehay appearedyay otay espiseday
imselfhay orfay eingbay ethay aveslay ofyay assionpay; andyay uellingqay ethay arkday yrannytay ofyay
espairday, ehay edlay emay againyay otay onversecay oncerningcay yselfmay ersonallypay. Ehay askedyay
emay ethay istoryhay ofyay ymay earlieryay yearsyay. Ethay aletay asway uicklyqay oldtay, utbay ityay
awakenedyay ariousvay ainstray ofyay eflectionray. Iyay okespay ofyay ymay esireday ofyay indingfay ayay
iendfray, ofyay ymay irstthay orfay ayay oremay intimateyay ympathysay ithway ayay ellowfay indmay anthay
adhay everyay allenfay otay ymay otlay, andyay expressedyay ymay onvictioncay atthay ayay anmay ouldcay
oastbay ofyay ittlelay appinesshay owhay idday otnay enjoyyay isthay essingblay.

i“ay agreeyay ithway youyay,” epliedray ethay angerstray; e“way areyay
unfashionedyay eaturescray, utbay alfhay ademay upyay, ifyay oneyay iserway, etterbay, earerday anthay
ourselves—suchyay ayay iendfray oughtyay otay e—dobay otnay endlay ishay aidyay otay
erfectionatepay ouryay eakway andyay aultyfay aturesnay. Iyay onceyay adhay ayay iendfray, ethay ostmay
oblenay ofyay umanhay eaturescray, andyay amyay entitledyay, ereforethay, otay udgejay espectingray
iendshipfray. Youyay avehay opehay, andyay ethay orldway eforebay youyay, andyay avehay onay ausecay orfay
espairday. Utbay I—iyay avehay ostlay everythingyay andyay annotcay eginbay ifelay
anewyay.”

Asyay ehay aidsay isthay ishay ountenancecay ecamebay expressiveyay ofyay ayay almcay, ettledsay
iefgray atthay ouchedtay emay otay ethay earthay. Utbay ehay asway ilentsay andyay esentlypray
etiredray otay ishay abincay.

Evenyay okenbray inyay iritspay asyay ehay isyay, onay oneyay ancay eelfay oremay eeplyday anthay ehay
oesday ethay eautiesbay ofyay aturenay. Ethay arrystay yskay, ethay easay, andyay everyyay ightsay
affordedyay ybay esethay onderfulway egionsray eemsay illstay otay avehay ethay owerpay ofyay
elevatingyay ishay oulsay omfray earthyay. Uchsay ayay anmay ashay ayay oubleday existenceyay: ehay
aymay uffersay iserymay andyay ebay overwhelmedyay ybay isappointmentsday, yetyay enwhay ehay
ashay etiredray intoyay imselfhay, ehay illway ebay ikelay ayay elestialcay iritspay atthay ashay ayay
alohay aroundyay imhay, ithinway osewhay irclecay onay iefgray oryay ollyfay enturesvay.

Illway youyay ilesmay atyay ethay enthusiasmyay Iyay expressyay oncerningcay isthay ivineday
andererway? Youyay ouldway otnay ifyay youyay awsay imhay. Youyay avehay eenbay utoredtay andyay
efinedray ybay ooksbay andyay etirementray omfray ethay orldway, andyay youyay areyay ereforethay
omewhatsay astidiousfay; utbay isthay onlyyay endersray youyay ethay oremay itfay otay
appreciateyay ethay extraordinaryyay eritsmay ofyay isthay onderfulway anmay. Ometimessay Iyay
avehay endeavouredyay otay iscoverday atwhay ualityqay ityay isyay ichwhay ehay ossessespay atthay
elevatesyay imhay osay immeasurablyyay aboveyay anyyay otheryay ersonpay Iyay everyay ewknay. Iyay
elievebay ityay otay ebay anyay intuitiveyay iscernmentday, ayay uickqay utbay ever-failingnay
owerpay ofyay udgmentjay, ayay enetrationpay intoyay ethay ausescay ofyay ingsthay, unequalledyay
orfay earnessclay andyay ecisionpray; addyay otay isthay ayay acilityfay ofyay expressionyay andyay ayay
oicevay osewhay ariedvay intonationsyay areyay oul-subduingsay usicmay.




Augustyay 19th, 17—.


Yesterdayyay ethay angerstray aidsay otay emay, you“ay aymay easilyyay erceivepay, Aptaincay
Altonway, atthay Iyay avehay ufferedsay eatgray andyay unparalleledyay isfortunesmay. Iyay adhay
eterminedday atyay oneyay imetay atthay ethay emorymay ofyay esethay evilsyay ouldshay ieday ithway
emay, utbay youyay avehay onway emay otay alteryay ymay eterminationday. Youyay eeksay orfay
owledgeknay andyay isdomway, asyay Iyay onceyay idday; andyay Iyay ardentlyyay opehay atthay ethay
atificationgray ofyay youryay ishesway aymay otnay ebay ayay erpentsay otay ingstay youyay, asyay inemay
ashay eenbay. Iyay oday otnay owknay atthay ethay elationray ofyay ymay isastersday illway ebay
usefulyay otay youyay; yetyay, enwhay Iyay eflectray atthay youyay areyay ursuingpay ethay amesay
oursecay, exposingyay yourselfyay otay ethay amesay angersday ichwhay avehay enderedray emay
atwhay Iyay amyay, Iyay imagineyay atthay youyay aymay educeday anyay aptyay oralmay omfray ymay aletay, oneyay
atthay aymay irectday youyay ifyay youyay ucceedsay inyay youryay undertakingyay andyay onsolecay youyay
inyay asecay ofyay ailurefay. Eparepray otay earhay ofyay occurrencesyay ichwhay areyay usuallyyay
eemedday arvellousmay. Ereway eway amongyay ethay amertay enesscay ofyay aturenay Iyay ightmay
earfay otay encounteryay youryay unbeliefyay, erhapspay youryay idiculeray; utbay anymay ingsthay
illway appearyay ossiblepay inyay esethay ildway andyay ysteriousmay egionsray ichwhay ouldway
ovokepray ethay aughterlay ofyay osethay unacquaintedyay ithway ethay ever-variedyay owerspay
ofyay aturenay; ornay ancay Iyay oubtday utbay atthay ymay aletay onveyscay inyay itsyay eriessay
internalyay evidenceyay ofyay ethay uthtray ofyay ethay eventsyay ofyay ichwhay ityay isyay omposedcay.”

Youyay aymay easilyyay imagineyay atthay Iyay asway uchmay atifiedgray ybay ethay offeredyay
ommunicationcay, yetyay Iyay ouldcay otnay endureyay atthay ehay ouldshay enewray ishay iefgray ybay
ayay ecitalray ofyay ishay isfortunesmay. Iyay eltfay ethay eatestgray eagernessyay otay earhay
ethay omisedpray arrativenay, artlypay omfray uriositycay andyay artlypay omfray ayay ongstray
esireday otay ameliorateyay ishay atefay ifyay ityay ereway inyay ymay owerpay. Iyay expressedyay
esethay eelingsfay inyay ymay answeryay.

i“ay ankthay youyay,” ehay epliedray, or“fay youryay ympathysay, utbay ityay isyay
uselessyay; ymay atefay isyay earlynay ulfilledfay. Iyay aitway utbay orfay oneyay eventyay, andyay enthay Iyay
allshay eposeray inyay eacepay. Iyay understandyay youryay eelingfay,” ontinuedcay ehay,
erceivingpay atthay Iyay ishedway otay interruptyay imhay; ut“bay youyay areyay istakenmay, ymay
iendfray, ifyay usthay youyay illway allowyay emay otay amenay youyay; othingnay ancay alteryay ymay
estinyday; istenlay otay ymay istoryhay, andyay youyay illway erceivepay owhay irrevocablyyay ityay isyay
eterminedday.”

Ehay enthay oldtay emay atthay ehay ouldway ommencecay ishay arrativenay ethay extnay ayday enwhay Iyay
ouldshay ebay atyay eisurelay. Isthay omisepray ewdray omfray emay ethay armestway anksthay. Iyay avehay
esolvedray everyyay ightnay, enwhay Iyay amyay otnay imperativelyyay occupiedyay ybay ymay utiesday, otay
ecordray, asyay earlynay asyay ossiblepay inyay ishay ownyay ordsway, atwhay ehay ashay elatedray uringday
ethay ayday. Ifyay Iyay ouldshay ebay engagedyay, Iyay illway atyay eastlay akemay otesnay. Isthay
anuscriptmay illway oubtlessday affordyay youyay ethay eatestgray easureplay; utbay otay emay, owhay
owknay imhay, andyay owhay earhay ityay omfray ishay ownyay ips—withlay atwhay interestyay andyay
ympathysay allshay Iyay eadray ityay inyay omesay uturefay ayday! Evenyay ownay, asyay Iyay ommencecay ymay
asktay, ishay ull-tonedfay oicevay ellssway inyay ymay earsyay; ishay ustrouslay eyesyay elldway onyay emay
ithway allyay eirthay elancholymay eetnesssway; Iyay eesay ishay inthay andhay aisedray inyay
animationyay, ilewhay ethay ineamentslay ofyay ishay acefay areyay irradiatedyay ybay ethay oulsay
ithinway. Angestray andyay arrowinghay ustmay ebay ishay orystay, ightfulfray ethay ormstay ichwhay
embracedyay ethay allantgay esselvay onyay itsyay oursecay andyay eckedwray it—thusyay!




Apterchay 1


Iyay amyay ybay irthbay ayay Enevesegay, andyay ymay amilyfay isyay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay
istinguishedday ofyay atthay epublicray. Ymay ancestorsyay adhay eenbay orfay anymay yearsyay
ounsellorscay andyay yndicssay, andyay ymay atherfay adhay illedfay everalsay ublicpay
ituationssay ithway onourhay andyay eputationray. Ehay asway espectedray ybay allyay owhay
ewknay imhay orfay ishay integrityyay andyay indefatigableyay attentionyay otay ublicpay
usinessbay. Ehay assedpay ishay youngeryay aysday erpetuallypay occupiedyay ybay ethay
affairsyay ofyay ishay ountrycay; ayay arietyvay ofyay ircumstancescay adhay eventedpray ishay
arryingmay earlyyay, ornay asway ityay untilyay ethay eclineday ofyay ifelay atthay ehay ecamebay ayay
usbandhay andyay ethay atherfay ofyay ayay amilyfay.

Asyay ethay ircumstancescay ofyay ishay arriagemay illustrateyay ishay aracterchay, Iyay annotcay
efrainray omfray elatingray emthay. Oneyay ofyay ishay ostmay intimateyay iendsfray asway ayay
erchantmay owhay, omfray ayay ourishingflay atestay, ellfay, oughthray umerousnay
ischancesmay, intoyay overtypay. Isthay anmay, osewhay amenay asway Eaufortbay, asway ofyay ayay
oudpray andyay unbendingyay ispositionday andyay ouldcay otnay earbay otay ivelay inyay overtypay
andyay oblivionyay inyay ethay amesay ountrycay erewhay ehay adhay ormerlyfay eenbay
istinguishedday orfay ishay ankray andyay agnificencemay. Avinghay aidpay ishay ebtsday,
ereforethay, inyay ethay ostmay onourablehay annermay, ehay etreatedray ithway ishay
aughterday otay ethay owntay ofyay Ucernelay, erewhay ehay ivedlay unknownyay andyay inyay
etchednesswray. Ymay atherfay ovedlay Eaufortbay ithway ethay uesttray iendshipfray andyay
asway eeplyday ievedgray ybay ishay etreatray inyay esethay unfortunateyay ircumstancescay.
Ehay itterlybay eploredday ethay alsefay idepray ichwhay edlay ishay iendfray otay ayay onductcay
osay ittlelay orthyway ofyay ethay affectionyay atthay unitedyay emthay. Ehay ostlay onay imetay inyay
endeavouringyay otay eeksay imhay outyay, ithway ethay opehay ofyay ersuadingpay imhay otay eginbay
ethay orldway againyay oughthray ishay editcray andyay assistanceyay.

Eaufortbay adhay akentay effectualyay easuresmay otay oncealcay imselfhay, andyay ityay asway entay
onthsmay eforebay ymay atherfay iscoveredday ishay abodeyay. Overjoyedyay atyay isthay iscoveryday,
ehay astenedhay otay ethay ousehay, ichwhay asway ituatedsay inyay ayay eanmay eetstray earnay ethay
Eussray. Utbay enwhay ehay enteredyay, iserymay andyay espairday aloneyay elcomedway imhay. Eaufortbay
adhay avedsay utbay ayay eryvay allsmay umsay ofyay oneymay omfray ethay eckwray ofyay ishay ortunesfay, utbay
ityay asway ufficientsay otay ovidepray imhay ithway ustenancesay orfay omesay onthsmay, andyay inyay
ethay eantimemay ehay opedhay otay ocurepray omesay espectableray employmentyay inyay ayay
erchant’smay ousehay. Ethay intervalyay asway, onsequentlycay, entspay inyay inactionyay;
ishay iefgray onlyyay ecamebay oremay eepday andyay anklingray enwhay ehay adhay eisurelay orfay
eflectionray, andyay atyay engthlay ityay ooktay osay astfay oldhay ofyay ishay indmay atthay atyay ethay endyay
ofyay eethray onthsmay ehay aylay onyay ayay edbay ofyay icknesssay, incapableyay ofyay anyyay exertionyay.

Ishay aughterday attendedyay imhay ithway ethay eatestgray endernesstay, utbay eshay awsay
ithway espairday atthay eirthay ittlelay undfay asway apidlyray ecreasingday andyay atthay
erethay asway onay otheryay ospectpray ofyay upportsay. Utbay Arolinecay Eaufortbay
ossessedpay ayay indmay ofyay anyay uncommonyay ouldmay, andyay erhay ouragecay oseray otay upportsay
erhay inyay erhay adversityyay. Eshay ocuredpray ainplay orkway; eshay aitedplay awstray andyay
ybay ariousvay eansmay ontrivedcay otay earnyay ayay ittancepay arcelyscay ufficientsay otay
upportsay ifelay.

Everalsay onthsmay assedpay inyay isthay annermay. Erhay atherfay ewgray orseway; erhay imetay
asway oremay entirelyyay occupiedyay inyay attendingyay imhay; erhay eansmay ofyay ubsistencesay
ecreasedday; andyay inyay ethay enthtay onthmay erhay atherfay iedday inyay erhay armsyay, eavinglay
erhay anyay orphanyay andyay ayay eggarbay. Isthay astlay owblay overcameyay erhay, andyay eshay eltknay
ybay Eaufort’sbay offincay eepingway itterlybay, enwhay ymay atherfay enteredyay ethay
amberchay. Ehay amecay ikelay ayay otectingpray iritspay otay ethay oorpay irlgay, owhay
ommittedcay erselfhay otay ishay arecay; andyay afteryay ethay intermentyay ofyay ishay iendfray ehay
onductedcay erhay otay Enevagay andyay acedplay erhay underyay ethay otectionpray ofyay ayay
elationray. Otway yearsyay afteryay isthay eventyay Arolinecay ecamebay ishay ifeway.

Erethay asway ayay onsiderablecay ifferenceday etweenbay ethay agesyay ofyay ymay arentspay, utbay
isthay ircumstancecay eemedsay otay uniteyay emthay onlyyay oserclay inyay ondsbay ofyay evotedday
affectionyay. Erethay asway ayay ensesay ofyay usticejay inyay ymay ather’sfay uprightyay indmay
ichwhay enderedray ityay ecessarynay atthay ehay ouldshay approveyay ighlyhay otay ovelay
onglystray. Erhapspay uringday ormerfay yearsyay ehay adhay ufferedsay omfray ethay
ate-discoveredlay unworthinessyay ofyay oneyay elovedbay andyay osay asway isposedday otay etsay
ayay eatergray aluevay onyay iedtray orthway. Erethay asway ayay owshay ofyay atitudegray andyay
orshipway inyay ishay attachmentyay otay ymay othermay, ifferingday ollywhay omfray ethay
otingday ondnessfay ofyay ageyay, orfay ityay asway inspiredyay ybay everenceray orfay erhay
irtuesvay andyay ayay esireday otay ebay ethay eansmay ofyay, inyay omesay egreeday, ecompensingray
erhay orfay ethay orrowssay eshay adhay enduredyay, utbay ichwhay avegay inexpressibleyay acegray
otay ishay ehaviourbay otay erhay. Everythingyay asway ademay otay yieldyay otay erhay ishesway
andyay erhay onveniencecay. Ehay ovestray otay eltershay erhay, asyay ayay airfay exoticyay isyay
elteredshay ybay ethay ardenergay, omfray everyyay ougherray indway andyay otay urroundsay erhay
ithway allyay atthay ouldcay endtay otay exciteyay easurableplay emotionyay inyay erhay oftsay andyay
enevolentbay indmay. Erhay ealthhay, andyay evenyay ethay anquillitytray ofyay erhay ithertohay
onstantcay iritspay, adhay eenbay akenshay ybay atwhay eshay adhay onegay oughthray. Uringday
ethay otway yearsyay atthay adhay elapsedyay eviouspray otay eirthay arriagemay ymay atherfay adhay
aduallygray elinquishedray allyay ishay ublicpay unctionsfay; andyay immediatelyyay afteryay
eirthay unionyay eythay oughtsay ethay easantplay imateclay ofyay Italyyay, andyay ethay angechay
ofyay enescay andyay interestyay attendantyay onyay ayay ourtay oughthray atthay andlay ofyay ondersway,
asyay ayay estorativeray orfay erhay eakenedway amefray.

Omfray Italyyay eythay isitedvay Ermanygay andyay Ancefray. Iyay, eirthay eldestyay ildchay, asway ornbay
atyay Aplesnay, andyay asyay anyay infantyay accompaniedyay emthay inyay eirthay amblesray. Iyay emainedray
orfay everalsay yearsyay eirthay onlyyay ildchay. Uchmay asyay eythay ereway attachedyay otay eachyay
otheryay, eythay eemedsay otay awdray inexhaustibleyay oresstay ofyay affectionyay omfray ayay eryvay
inemay ofyay ovelay otay estowbay emthay uponyay emay. Ymay other’smay endertay aressescay andyay
ymay ather’sfay ilesmay ofyay enevolentbay easureplay ilewhay egardingray emay areyay ymay
irstfay ecollectionsray. Iyay asway eirthay aythingplay andyay eirthay idolyay, andyay omethingsay
etter—theirbay ildchay, ethay innocentyay andyay elplesshay eaturecray estowedbay onyay
emthay ybay Eavenhay, omwhay otay ingbray upyay otay oodgay, andyay osewhay uturefay otlay ityay asway inyay
eirthay andshay otay irectday otay appinesshay oryay iserymay, accordingyay asyay eythay ulfilledfay
eirthay utiesday owardstay emay. Ithway isthay eepday onsciousnesscay ofyay atwhay eythay owedyay
owardstay ethay eingbay otay ichwhay eythay adhay ivengay ifelay, addedyay otay ethay activeyay iritspay
ofyay endernesstay atthay animatedyay othbay, ityay aymay ebay imaginedyay atthay ilewhay uringday
everyyay ourhay ofyay ymay infantyay ifelay Iyay eceivedray ayay essonlay ofyay atiencepay, ofyay aritychay,
andyay ofyay elf-controlsay, Iyay asway osay uidedgay ybay ayay ilkensay ordcay atthay allyay eemedsay utbay
oneyay aintray ofyay enjoymentyay otay emay.

Orfay ayay onglay imetay Iyay asway eirthay onlyyay arecay. Ymay othermay adhay uchmay esiredday otay avehay ayay
aughterday, utbay Iyay ontinuedcay eirthay inglesay offspringyay. Enwhay Iyay asway aboutyay ivefay
yearsyay oldyay, ilewhay akingmay anyay excursionyay eyondbay ethay ontiersfray ofyay Italyyay, eythay
assedpay ayay eekway onyay ethay oresshay ofyay ethay Akelay ofyay Omocay. Eirthay enevolentbay
ispositionday oftenyay ademay emthay enteryay ethay ottagescay ofyay ethay oorpay. Isthay, otay ymay
othermay, asway oremay anthay ayay utyday; ityay asway ayay ecessitynay, ayay
assion—rememberingpay atwhay eshay adhay ufferedsay, andyay owhay eshay adhay eenbay
elieved—forray erhay otay actyay inyay erhay urntay ethay uardiangay angelyay otay ethay
afflictedyay. Uringday oneyay ofyay eirthay alksway ayay oorpay otcay inyay ethay oldingsfay ofyay ayay alevay
attractedyay eirthay oticenay asyay eingbay ingularlysay isconsolateday, ilewhay ethay umbernay
ofyay alf-clothedhay ildrenchay atheredgay aboutyay ityay okespay ofyay enurypay inyay itsyay orstway
apeshay. Oneyay ayday, enwhay ymay atherfay adhay onegay ybay imselfhay otay Ilanmay, ymay othermay,
accompaniedyay ybay emay, isitedvay isthay abodeyay. Eshay oundfay ayay easantpay andyay ishay ifeway,
ardhay orkingway, entbay ownday ybay arecay andyay abourlay, istributingday ayay antyscay ealmay otay
ivefay ungryhay abesbay. Amongyay esethay erethay asway oneyay ichwhay attractedyay ymay othermay arfay
aboveyay allyay ethay estray. Eshay appearedyay ofyay ayay ifferentday ockstay. Ethay ourfay othersyay ereway
ark-eyedday, ardyhay ittlelay agrantsvay; isthay ildchay asway inthay andyay eryvay airfay. Erhay
airhay asway ethay ightestbray ivinglay oldgay, andyay espiteday ethay overtypay ofyay erhay
othingclay, eemedsay otay etsay ayay owncray ofyay istinctionday onyay erhay eadhay. Erhay owbray asway
earclay andyay ampleyay, erhay ueblay eyesyay oudlessclay, andyay erhay ipslay andyay ethay ouldingmay ofyay
erhay acefay osay expressiveyay ofyay ensibilitysay andyay eetnesssway atthay onenay ouldcay eholdbay
erhay ithoutway ookinglay onyay erhay asyay ofyay ayay istinctday eciesspay, ayay eingbay eaven-senthay,
andyay earingbay ayay elestialcay ampstay inyay allyay erhay eaturesfay.

Ethay easantpay omanway, erceivingpay atthay ymay othermay ixedfay eyesyay ofyay onderway andyay
admirationyay onyay isthay ovelylay irlgay, eagerlyyay ommunicatedcay erhay istoryhay. Eshay asway
otnay erhay ildchay, utbay ethay aughterday ofyay ayay Ilanesemay oblemannay. Erhay othermay asway ayay
Ermangay andyay adhay iedday onyay ivinggay erhay irthbay. Ethay infantyay adhay eenbay acedplay ithway
esethay oodgay eoplepay otay ursenay: eythay ereway etterbay offyay enthay. Eythay adhay otnay eenbay
onglay arriedmay, andyay eirthay eldestyay ildchay asway utbay ustjay ornbay. Ethay atherfay ofyay eirthay
argechay asway oneyay ofyay osethay Italiansyay ursednay inyay ethay emorymay ofyay ethay antiqueyay oryglay
ofyay Italy—oneyay amongyay ethay iavi_schay ognoryay ementifray,_ owhay exertedyay
imselfhay otay obtainyay ethay ibertylay ofyay ishay ountrycay. Ehay ecamebay ethay ictimvay ofyay itsyay
eaknessway. Etherwhay ehay adhay iedday oryay illstay ingeredlay inyay ethay ungeonsday ofyay Austriayay
asway otnay ownknay. Ishay opertypray asway onfiscatedcay; ishay ildchay ecamebay anyay orphanyay andyay
ayay eggarbay. Eshay ontinuedcay ithway erhay osterfay arentspay andyay oomedblay inyay eirthay uderay
abodeyay, airerfay anthay ayay ardengay oseray amongyay ark-leavedday amblesbray.

Enwhay ymay atherfay eturnedray omfray Ilanmay, ehay oundfay ayingplay ithway emay inyay ethay allhay ofyay
ouryay illavay ayay ildchay airerfay anthay icturedpay erub—achay eaturecray owhay eemedsay
otay edshay adianceray omfray erhay ookslay andyay osewhay ormfay andyay otionsmay ereway ighterlay
anthay ethay amoischay ofyay ethay illshay. Ethay apparitionyay asway oonsay explainedyay. Ithway ishay
ermissionpay ymay othermay evailedpray onyay erhay usticray uardiansgay otay yieldyay eirthay
argechay otay erhay. Eythay ereway ondfay ofyay ethay eetsway orphanyay. Erhay esencepray adhay eemedsay
ayay essingblay otay emthay, utbay ityay ouldway ebay unfairyay otay erhay otay eepkay erhay inyay overtypay
andyay antway enwhay Ovidencepray affordedyay erhay uchsay owerfulpay otectionpray. Eythay
onsultedcay eirthay illagevay iestpray, andyay ethay esultray asway atthay Elizabethyay Avenzalay
ecamebay ethay inmateyay ofyay ymay arentspay’ ouse—myhay oremay anthay
ister—thesay eautifulbay andyay adoredyay ompanioncay ofyay allyay ymay occupationsyay andyay
ymay easuresplay.

Everyoneyay ovedlay Elizabethyay. Ethay assionatepay andyay almostyay everentialray
attachmentyay ithway ichwhay allyay egardedray erhay ecamebay, ilewhay Iyay aredshay ityay, ymay
idepray andyay ymay elightday. Onyay ethay eveningyay eviouspray otay erhay eingbay oughtbray otay
ymay omehay, ymay othermay adhay aidsay ayfullyplay, i“ay avehay ayay ettypray esentpray orfay ymay
Ictor—tomorrowvay ehay allshay avehay ityay.” Andyay enwhay, onyay ethay orrowmay, eshay
esentedpray Elizabethyay otay emay asyay erhay omisedpray iftgay, Iyay, ithway ildishchay
eriousnesssay, interpretedyay erhay ordsway iterallylay andyay ookedlay uponyay Elizabethyay
asyay ine—minemay otay otectpray, ovelay, andyay erishchay. Allyay aisespray estowedbay onyay
erhay Iyay eceivedray asyay ademay otay ayay ossessionpay ofyay ymay ownyay. Eway alledcay eachyay otheryay
amiliarlyfay ybay ethay amenay ofyay ousincay. Onay ordway, onay expressionyay ouldcay odybay
orthfay ethay indkay ofyay elationray inyay ichwhay eshay oodstay otay e—mymay oremay anthay
istersay, incesay illtay eathday eshay asway otay ebay inemay onlyyay.




Apterchay 2


Eway ereway oughtbray upyay ogethertay; erethay asway otnay uiteqay ayay yearyay ifferenceday inyay
ouryay agesyay. Iyay eednay otnay aysay atthay eway ereway angersstray otay anyyay eciesspay ofyay
isunionday oryay isputeday. Armonyhay asway ethay oulsay ofyay ouryay ompanionshipcay, andyay
ethay iversityday andyay ontrastcay atthay ubsistedsay inyay ouryay aracterschay ewdray usyay
earernay ogethertay. Elizabethyay asway ofyay ayay almercay andyay oremay oncentratedcay
ispositionday; utbay, ithway allyay ymay ardouryay, Iyay asway apablecay ofyay ayay oremay intenseyay
applicationyay andyay asway oremay eeplyday ittensmay ithway ethay irstthay orfay owledgeknay.
Eshay usiedbay erselfhay ithway ollowingfay ethay aerialyay eationscray ofyay ethay oetspay;
andyay inyay ethay ajesticmay andyay ondrousway enesscay ichwhay urroundedsay ouryay Isssway
omehay e—thay ublimesay apesshay ofyay ethay ountainsmay, ethay angeschay ofyay ethay easonssay,
empesttay andyay almcay, ethay ilencesay ofyay interway, andyay ethay ifelay andyay urbulencetay ofyay
ouryay Alpineyay ummers—shesay oundfay ampleyay opescay orfay admirationyay andyay elightday.
Ilewhay ymay ompanioncay ontemplatedcay ithway ayay erioussay andyay atisfiedsay iritspay ethay
agnificentmay appearancesyay ofyay ingsthay, Iyay elightedday inyay investigatingyay eirthay
ausescay. Ethay orldway asway otay emay ayay ecretsay ichwhay Iyay esiredday otay ivineday.
Uriositycay, earnestyay esearchray otay earnlay ethay iddenhay awslay ofyay aturenay,
adnessglay akinyay otay aptureray, asyay eythay ereway unfoldedyay otay emay, areyay amongyay ethay
earliestyay ensationssay Iyay ancay ememberray.

Onyay ethay irthbay ofyay ayay econdsay onsay, ymay uniorjay ybay evensay yearsyay, ymay arentspay avegay
upyay entirelyyay eirthay anderingway ifelay andyay ixedfay emselvesthay inyay eirthay ativenay
ountrycay. Eway ossessedpay ayay ousehay inyay Enevagay, andyay ayay ampagne_cay_ onyay Elrivebay,
ethay easternyay oreshay ofyay ethay akelay, atyay ethay istanceday ofyay atherray oremay anthay ayay
eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Eway esidedray incipallypray inyay ethay atterlay, andyay ethay
iveslay ofyay ymay arentspay ereway assedpay inyay onsiderablecay eclusionsay. Ityay asway ymay
empertay otay avoidyay ayay owdcray andyay otay attachyay yselfmay erventlyfay otay ayay ewfay. Iyay asway
indifferentyay, ereforethay, otay ymay ool-fellowsschay inyay eneralgay; utbay Iyay unitedyay
yselfmay inyay ethay ondsbay ofyay ethay osestclay iendshipfray otay oneyay amongyay emthay. Enryhay
Ervalclay asway ethay onsay ofyay ayay erchantmay ofyay Enevagay. Ehay asway ayay oybay ofyay ingularsay
alenttay andyay ancyfay. Ehay ovedlay enterpriseyay, ardshiphay, andyay evenyay angerday orfay
itsyay ownyay akesay. Ehay asway eeplyday eadray inyay ooksbay ofyay ivalrychay andyay omanceray. Ehay
omposedcay eroichay ongssay andyay eganbay otay itewray anymay ayay aletay ofyay enchantmentyay andyay
ightlyknay adventureyay. Ehay iedtray otay akemay usyay actyay aysplay andyay otay enteryay intoyay
asqueradesmay, inyay ichwhay ethay aracterschay ereway awndray omfray ethay eroeshay ofyay
Oncesvallesray, ofyay ethay Oundray Abletay ofyay Ingkay Arthuryay, andyay ethay ivalrouschay
aintray owhay edshay eirthay oodblay otay edeemray ethay olyhay epulchresay omfray ethay andshay
ofyay ethay infidelsyay.

Onay umanhay eingbay ouldcay avehay assedpay ayay appierhay ildhoodchay anthay yselfmay. Ymay
arentspay ereway ossessedpay ybay ethay eryvay iritspay ofyay indnesskay andyay indulgenceyay.
Eway eltfay atthay eythay ereway otnay ethay yrantstay otay uleray ouryay otlay accordingyay otay
eirthay apricecay, utbay ethay agentsyay andyay eatorscray ofyay allyay ethay anymay elightsday
ichwhay eway enjoyedyay. Enwhay Iyay ingledmay ithway otheryay amiliesfay Iyay istinctlyday
iscernedday owhay eculiarlypay ortunatefay ymay otlay asway, andyay atitudegray assistedyay
ethay evelopmentday ofyay ilialfay ovelay.

Ymay empertay asway ometimessay iolentvay, andyay ymay assionspay ehementvay; utbay ybay omesay
awlay inyay ymay emperaturetay eythay ereway urnedtay otnay owardstay ildishchay ursuitspay
utbay otay anyay eageryay esireday otay earnlay, andyay otnay otay earnlay allyay ingsthay
indiscriminatelyyay. Iyay onfesscay atthay eithernay ethay ucturestray ofyay anguageslay,
ornay ethay odecay ofyay overnmentsgay, ornay ethay oliticspay ofyay ariousvay atesstay
ossessedpay attractionsyay orfay emay. Ityay asway ethay ecretssay ofyay eavenhay andyay earthyay
atthay Iyay esiredday otay earnlay; andyay etherwhay ityay asway ethay outwardyay ubstancesay ofyay
ingsthay oryay ethay inneryay iritspay ofyay aturenay andyay ethay ysteriousmay oulsay ofyay anmay
atthay occupiedyay emay, illstay ymay inquiriesyay ereway irectedday otay ethay etaphysicalmay,
oryay inyay itsyay ighesthay ensesay, ethay ysicalphay ecretssay ofyay ethay orldway.

Eanwhilemay Ervalclay occupiedyay imselfhay, osay otay eakspay, ithway ethay oralmay
elationsray ofyay ingsthay. Ethay usybay agestay ofyay ifelay, ethay irtuesvay ofyay eroeshay,
andyay ethay actionsyay ofyay enmay ereway ishay emethay; andyay ishay opehay andyay ishay eamdray asway
otay ecomebay oneyay amongyay osethay osewhay amesnay areyay ecordedray inyay orystay asyay ethay
allantgay andyay adventurousyay enefactorsbay ofyay ouryay eciesspay. Ethay aintlysay oulsay
ofyay Elizabethyay oneshay ikelay ayay ine-dedicatedshray amplay inyay ouryay eacefulpay omehay.
Erhay ympathysay asway oursyay; erhay ilesmay, erhay oftsay oicevay, ethay eetsway anceglay ofyay
erhay elestialcay eyesyay, ereway everyay erethay otay essblay andyay animateyay usyay. Eshay asway
ethay ivinglay iritspay ofyay ovelay otay oftensay andyay attractyay; Iyay ightmay avehay ecomebay
ullensay inyay ymay udystay, oughray oughthray ethay ardouryay ofyay ymay aturenay, utbay atthay
eshay asway erethay otay ubduesay emay otay ayay emblancesay ofyay erhay ownyay entlenessgay. Andyay
Erval—couldclay aughtyay illyay entrenchyay onyay ethay oblenay iritspay ofyay Ervalclay? Yetyay
ehay ightmay otnay avehay eenbay osay erfectlypay umanehay, osay oughtfulthay inyay ishay
enerositygay, osay ullfay ofyay indnesskay andyay endernesstay amidstyay ishay assionpay orfay
adventurousyay exploityay, adhay eshay otnay unfoldedyay otay imhay ethay ealray ovelinesslay ofyay
eneficencebay andyay ademay ethay oingday oodgay ethay endyay andyay aimyay ofyay ishay oaringsay
ambitionyay.

Iyay eelfay exquisiteyay easureplay inyay ellingdway onyay ethay ecollectionsray ofyay ildhoodchay,
eforebay isfortunemay adhay aintedtay ymay indmay andyay angedchay itsyay ightbray isionsvay ofyay
extensiveyay usefulnessyay intoyay oomyglay andyay arrownay eflectionsray uponyay elfsay. Esidesbay,
inyay awingdray ethay icturepay ofyay ymay earlyyay aysday, Iyay alsoyay ecordray osethay eventsyay ichwhay
edlay, ybay insensibleyay epsstay, otay ymay afteryay aletay ofyay iserymay, orfay enwhay Iyay ouldway
accountyay otay yselfmay orfay ethay irthbay ofyay atthay assionpay ichwhay afterwardsyay uledray ymay
estinyday Iyay indfay ityay ariseyay, ikelay ayay ountainmay iverray, omfray ignobleyay andyay almostyay
orgottenfay ourcessay; utbay, ellingsway asyay ityay oceededpray, ityay ecamebay ethay orrenttay
ichwhay, inyay itsyay oursecay, ashay eptsway awayyay allyay ymay opeshay andyay oysjay.

Aturalnay ilosophyphay isyay ethay eniusgay atthay ashay egulatedray ymay atefay; Iyay esireday,
ereforethay, inyay isthay arrationnay, otay atestay osethay actsfay ichwhay edlay otay ymay
edilectionpray orfay atthay iencescay. Enwhay Iyay asway irteenthay yearsyay ofyay ageyay eway allyay entway
onyay ayay artypay ofyay easureplay otay ethay athsbay earnay Ononthay; ethay inclemencyyay ofyay ethay
eatherway obligedyay usyay otay emainray ayay ayday onfinedcay otay ethay innyay. Inyay isthay ousehay Iyay
ancedchay otay indfay ayay olumevay ofyay ethay orksway ofyay Orneliuscay Agrippayay. Iyay openedyay ityay
ithway apathyyay; ethay eorythay ichwhay ehay attemptsyay otay emonstrateday andyay ethay onderfulway
actsfay ichwhay ehay elatesray oonsay angedchay isthay eelingfay intoyay enthusiasmyay. Ayay ewnay
ightlay eemedsay otay awnday uponyay ymay indmay, andyay oundingbay ithway oyjay, Iyay ommunicatedcay ymay
iscoveryday otay ymay atherfay. Ymay atherfay ookedlay arelesslycay atyay ethay itletay agepay ofyay ymay
ookbay andyay aidsay, ah“ay! Orneliuscay Agrippayay! Ymay earday Ictorvay, oday otnay asteway
youryay imetay uponyay isthay; ityay isyay adsay ashtray.”

Ifyay, insteadyay ofyay isthay emarkray, ymay atherfay adhay akentay ethay ainspay otay explainyay otay emay
atthay ethay inciplespray ofyay Agrippayay adhay eenbay entirelyyay explodedyay andyay atthay ayay odernmay
ystemsay ofyay iencescay adhay eenbay introducedyay ichwhay ossessedpay uchmay eatergray owerspay
anthay ethay ancientyay, ecausebay ethay owerspay ofyay ethay atterlay ereway imericalchay, ilewhay
osethay ofyay ethay ormerfay ereway ealray andyay acticalpray, underyay uchsay ircumstancescay Iyay
ouldshay ertainlycay avehay ownthray Agrippayay asideyay andyay avehay ontentedcay ymay
imaginationyay, armedway asyay ityay asway, ybay eturningray ithway eatergray ardouryay otay ymay
ormerfay udiesstay. Ityay isyay evenyay ossiblepay atthay ethay aintray ofyay ymay ideasyay ouldway evernay
avehay eceivedray ethay atalfay impulseyay atthay edlay otay ymay uinray. Utbay ethay ursorycay anceglay
ymay atherfay adhay akentay ofyay ymay olumevay ybay onay eansmay assuredyay emay atthay ehay asway
acquaintedyay ithway itsyay ontentscay, andyay Iyay ontinuedcay otay eadray ithway ethay eatestgray
avidityyay.

Enwhay Iyay eturnedray omehay ymay irstfay arecay asway otay ocurepray ethay olewhay orksway ofyay isthay
authoryay, andyay afterwardsyay ofyay Aracelsuspay andyay Albertusyay Agnusmay. Iyay eadray andyay
udiedstay ethay ildway anciesfay ofyay esethay iterswray ithway elightday; eythay appearedyay otay emay
easurestray ownknay otay ewfay esidesbay yselfmay. Iyay avehay escribedday yselfmay asyay alwaysyay
avinghay eenbay imbuedyay ithway ayay erventfay onginglay otay enetratepay ethay ecretssay ofyay
aturenay. Inyay itespay ofyay ethay intenseyay abourlay andyay onderfulway iscoveriesday ofyay odernmay
ilosophersphay, Iyay alwaysyay amecay omfray ymay udiesstay iscontentedday andyay unsatisfiedyay.
Irsay Isaacyay Ewtonnay isyay aidsay otay avehay avowedyay atthay ehay eltfay ikelay ayay ildchay ickingpay
upyay ellsshay esidebay ethay eatgray andyay unexploredyay oceanyay ofyay uthtray. Osethay ofyay ishay
uccessorssay inyay eachyay anchbray ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay ithway omwhay Iyay asway acquaintedyay
appearedyay evenyay otay ymay oy’sbay apprehensionsyay asyay yrostay engagedyay inyay ethay amesay
ursuitpay.

Ethay untaughtyay easantpay eheldbay ethay elementsyay aroundyay imhay andyay asway acquaintedyay
ithway eirthay acticalpray usesyay. Ethay ostmay earnedlay ilosopherphay ewknay ittlelay
oremay. Ehay adhay artiallypay unveiledyay ethay acefay ofyay Aturenay, utbay erhay immortalyay
ineamentslay ereway illstay ayay onderway andyay ayay ysterymay. Ehay ightmay issectday,
anatomiseyay, andyay ivegay amesnay; utbay, otnay otay eakspay ofyay ayay inalfay ausecay, ausescay
inyay eirthay econdarysay andyay ertiarytay adesgray ereway utterlyyay unknownyay otay imhay. Iyay
adhay azedgay uponyay ethay ortificationsfay andyay impedimentsyay atthay eemedsay otay eepkay
umanhay eingsbay omfray enteringyay ethay itadelcay ofyay aturenay, andyay ashlyray andyay
ignorantlyyay Iyay adhay epinedray.

Utbay erehay ereway ooksbay, andyay erehay ereway enmay owhay adhay enetratedpay eeperday andyay ewknay
oremay. Iyay ooktay eirthay ordway orfay allyay atthay eythay averredyay, andyay Iyay ecamebay eirthay
iscipleday. Ityay aymay appearyay angestray atthay uchsay ouldshay ariseyay inyay ethay eighteenthyay
enturycay; utbay ilewhay Iyay ollowedfay ethay outineray ofyay educationyay inyay ethay oolsschay ofyay
Enevagay, Iyay asway, otay ayay eatgray egreeday, elf-taughtsay ithway egardray otay ymay avouritefay
udiesstay. Ymay atherfay asway otnay ientificscay, andyay Iyay asway eftlay otay ugglestray ithway ayay
ild’schay indnessblay, addedyay otay ayay udent’sstay irstthay orfay owledgeknay.
Underyay ethay uidancegay ofyay ymay ewnay eceptorspray Iyay enteredyay ithway ethay eatestgray
iligenceday intoyay ethay earchsay ofyay ethay ilosopher’sphay onestay andyay ethay elixiryay
ofyay ifelay; utbay ethay atterlay oonsay obtainedyay ymay undividedyay attentionyay. Ealthway asway anyay
inferioryay objectyay, utbay atwhay oryglay ouldway attendyay ethay iscoveryday ifyay Iyay ouldcay
anishbay iseaseday omfray ethay umanhay amefray andyay enderray anmay invulnerableyay otay anyyay utbay
ayay iolentvay eathday!

Ornay ereway esethay ymay onlyyay isionsvay. Ethay aisingray ofyay ostsghay oryay evilsday asway ayay
omisepray iberallylay accordedyay ybay ymay avouritefay authorsyay, ethay ulfilmentfay ofyay ichwhay
Iyay ostmay eagerlyyay oughtsay; andyay ifyay ymay incantationsyay ereway alwaysyay unsuccessfulyay, Iyay
attributedyay ethay ailurefay atherray otay ymay ownyay inexperienceyay andyay istakemay anthay otay ayay
antway ofyay illskay oryay idelityfay inyay ymay instructorsyay. Andyay usthay orfay ayay imetay Iyay asway
occupiedyay ybay explodedyay ystemssay, inglingmay, ikelay anyay unadeptyay, ayay ousandthay
ontradictorycay eoriesthay andyay ounderingflay esperatelyday inyay ayay eryvay oughslay ofyay
ultifariousmay owledgeknay, uidedgay ybay anyay ardentyay imaginationyay andyay ildishchay
easoningray, illtay anyay accidentyay againyay angedchay ethay urrentcay ofyay ymay ideasyay.

Enwhay Iyay asway aboutyay ifteenfay yearsyay oldyay eway adhay etiredray otay ouryay ousehay earnay
Elrivebay, enwhay eway itnessedway ayay ostmay iolentvay andyay erribletay understormthay. Ityay
advancedyay omfray ehindbay ethay ountainsmay ofyay Urajay, andyay ethay underthay urstbay atyay onceyay
ithway ightfulfray oudnesslay omfray ariousvay uartersqay ofyay ethay eavenshay. Iyay emainedray,
ilewhay ethay ormstay astedlay, atchingway itsyay ogresspray ithway uriositycay andyay elightday.
Asyay Iyay oodstay atyay ethay oorday, onyay ayay uddensay Iyay eheldbay ayay eamstray ofyay irefay issueyay omfray anyay
oldyay andyay eautifulbay oakyay ichwhay oodstay aboutyay entytway yardsyay omfray ouryay ousehay; andyay osay
oonsay asyay ethay azzlingday ightlay anishedvay, ethay oakyay adhay isappearedday, andyay othingnay
emainedray utbay ayay astedblay umpstay. Enwhay eway isitedvay ityay ethay extnay orningmay, eway oundfay
ethay eetray atteredshay inyay ayay ingularsay annermay. Ityay asway otnay interedsplay ybay ethay
ockshay, utbay entirelyyay educedray otay inthay ibbonsray ofyay oodway. Iyay evernay eheldbay
anythingyay osay utterlyyay estroyedday.

Eforebay isthay Iyay asway otnay unacquaintedyay ithway ethay oremay obviousyay awslay ofyay
electricityyay. Onyay isthay occasionyay ayay anmay ofyay eatgray esearchray inyay aturalnay
ilosophyphay asway ithway usyay, andyay excitedyay ybay isthay atastrophecay, ehay enteredyay onyay
ethay explanationyay ofyay ayay eorythay ichwhay ehay adhay ormedfay onyay ethay ubjectsay ofyay
electricityyay andyay alvanismgay, ichwhay asway atyay onceyay ewnay andyay astonishingyay otay emay.
Allyay atthay ehay aidsay ewthray eatlygray intoyay ethay adeshay Orneliuscay Agrippayay,
Albertusyay Agnusmay, andyay Aracelsuspay, ethay ordslay ofyay ymay imaginationyay; utbay ybay
omesay atalityfay ethay overthrowyay ofyay esethay enmay isinclinedday emay otay ursuepay ymay
accustomedyay udiesstay. Ityay eemedsay otay emay asyay ifyay othingnay ouldway oryay ouldcay everyay
ebay ownknay. Allyay atthay adhay osay onglay engagedyay ymay attentionyay uddenlysay ewgray
espicableday. Ybay oneyay ofyay osethay apricescay ofyay ethay indmay ichwhay eway areyay erhapspay
ostmay ubjectsay otay inyay earlyyay youthyay, Iyay atyay onceyay avegay upyay ymay ormerfay
occupationsyay, etsay ownday aturalnay istoryhay andyay allyay itsyay ogenypray asyay ayay eformedday
andyay abortiveyay eationcray, andyay entertainedyay ethay eatestgray isdainday orfay ayay
ould-beway iencescay ichwhay ouldcay evernay evenyay epstay ithinway ethay esholdthray ofyay
ealray owledgeknay. Inyay isthay oodmay ofyay indmay Iyay etookbay yselfmay otay ethay
athematicsmay andyay ethay anchesbray ofyay udystay appertainingyay otay atthay iencescay asyay
eingbay uiltbay uponyay ecuresay oundationsfay, andyay osay orthyway ofyay ymay onsiderationcay.

Usthay angelystray areyay ouryay oulssay onstructedcay, andyay ybay uchsay ightslay igamentslay
areyay eway oundbay otay osperitypray oryay uinray. Enwhay Iyay ooklay ackbay, ityay eemssay otay emay
asyay ifyay isthay almostyay iraculousmay angechay ofyay inclinationyay andyay illway asway ethay
immediateyay uggestionsay ofyay ethay uardiangay angelyay ofyay ymay ife—thelay astlay effortyay
ademay ybay ethay iritspay ofyay eservationpray otay avertyay ethay ormstay atthay asway evenyay
enthay anginghay inyay ethay arsstay andyay eadyray otay envelopyay emay. Erhay ictoryvay asway
announcedyay ybay anyay unusualyay anquillitytray andyay adnessglay ofyay oulsay ichwhay
ollowedfay ethay elinquishingray ofyay ymay ancientyay andyay atterlylay ormentingtay
udiesstay. Ityay asway usthay atthay Iyay asway otay ebay aughttay otay associateyay evilyay ithway
eirthay osecutionpray, appinesshay ithway eirthay isregardday.

Ityay asway ayay ongstray effortyay ofyay ethay iritspay ofyay oodgay, utbay ityay asway ineffectualyay.
Estinyday asway ootay otentpay, andyay erhay immutableyay awslay adhay ecreedday ymay utteryay andyay
erribletay estructionday.




Apterchay 3


Enwhay Iyay adhay attainedyay ethay ageyay ofyay eventeensay ymay arentspay esolvedray atthay Iyay
ouldshay ecomebay ayay udentstay atyay ethay universityyay ofyay Ingolstadtyay. Iyay adhay
ithertohay attendedyay ethay oolsschay ofyay Enevagay, utbay ymay atherfay oughtthay ityay
ecessarynay orfay ethay ompletioncay ofyay ymay educationyay atthay Iyay ouldshay ebay ademay
acquaintedyay ithway otheryay ustomscay anthay osethay ofyay ymay ativenay ountrycay. Ymay
epartureday asway ereforethay ixedfay atyay anyay earlyyay ateday, utbay eforebay ethay ayday
esolvedray uponyay ouldcay arriveyay, ethay irstfay isfortunemay ofyay ymay ifelay
occurred—anyay omenyay, asyay ityay ereway, ofyay ymay uturefay iserymay.

Elizabethyay adhay aughtcay ethay arletscay everfay; erhay illnessyay asway everesay, andyay eshay asway
inyay ethay eatestgray angerday. Uringday erhay illnessyay anymay argumentsyay adhay eenbay urgedyay otay
ersuadepay ymay othermay otay efrainray omfray attendingyay uponyay erhay. Eshay adhay atyay irstfay
yieldedyay otay ouryay entreatiesyay, utbay enwhay eshay eardhay atthay ethay ifelay ofyay erhay
avouritefay asway enacedmay, eshay ouldcay onay ongerlay ontrolcay erhay anxietyyay. Eshay
attendedyay erhay ickbedsay; erhay atchfulway attentionsyay iumphedtray overyay ethay alignitymay
ofyay ethay istemper—elizabethday asway avedsay, utbay ethay onsequencescay ofyay isthay
imprudenceyay ereway atalfay otay erhay eserverpray. Onyay ethay irdthay ayday ymay othermay
ickenedsay; erhay everfay asway accompaniedyay ybay ethay ostmay alarmingyay ymptomssay, andyay ethay
ookslay ofyay erhay edicalmay attendantsyay ognosticatedpray ethay orstway eventyay. Onyay erhay
eathbedday ethay ortitudefay andyay enignitybay ofyay isthay estbay ofyay omenway idday otnay esertday
erhay. Eshay oinedjay ethay andshay ofyay Elizabethyay andyay yselfmay. y“may
ildrenchay,” eshay aidsay, y“may irmestfay opeshay ofyay uturefay appinesshay ereway
acedplay onyay ethay ospectpray ofyay youryay unionyay. Isthay expectationyay illway ownay ebay ethay
onsolationcay ofyay youryay atherfay. Elizabethyay, ymay ovelay, youyay ustmay upplysay ymay aceplay otay
ymay youngeryay ildrenchay. Alasyay! Iyay egretray atthay Iyay amyay akentay omfray youyay; andyay, appyhay
andyay elovedbay asyay Iyay avehay eenbay, isyay ityay otnay ardhay otay uitqay youyay allyay? Utbay esethay areyay
otnay oughtsthay efittingbay emay; Iyay illway endeavouryay otay esignray yselfmay eerfullychay otay
eathday andyay illway indulgeyay ayay opehay ofyay eetingmay youyay inyay anotheryay orldway.”

Eshay iedday almlycay, andyay erhay ountenancecay expressedyay affectionyay evenyay inyay eathday.
Iyay eednay otnay escribeday ethay eelingsfay ofyay osethay osewhay earestday iestay areyay entray
ybay atthay ostmay irreparableyay evilyay, ethay oidvay atthay esentspray itselfyay otay ethay
oulsay, andyay ethay espairday atthay isyay exhibitedyay onyay ethay ountenancecay. Ityay isyay osay
onglay eforebay ethay indmay ancay ersuadepay itselfyay atthay eshay omwhay eway awsay everyyay ayday
andyay osewhay eryvay existenceyay appearedyay ayay artpay ofyay ouryay ownyay ancay avehay epartedday
orfay ever—thatyay ethay ightnessbray ofyay ayay elovedbay eyeyay ancay avehay eenbay
extinguishedyay andyay ethay oundsay ofyay ayay oicevay osay amiliarfay andyay earday otay ethay earyay
ancay ebay ushedhay, evernay oremay otay ebay eardhay. Esethay areyay ethay eflectionsray ofyay
ethay irstfay aysday; utbay enwhay ethay apselay ofyay imetay ovespray ethay ealityray ofyay ethay
evilyay, enthay ethay actualyay itternessbay ofyay iefgray ommencescay. Yetyay omfray omwhay ashay
otnay atthay uderay andhay entray awayyay omesay earday onnectioncay? Andyay ywhay ouldshay Iyay
escribeday ayay orrowsay ichwhay allyay avehay eltfay, andyay ustmay eelfay? Ethay imetay atyay
engthlay arrivesyay enwhay iefgray isyay atherray anyay indulgenceyay anthay ayay ecessitynay; andyay
