ethay ilesmay atthay aysplay uponyay ethay ipslay, althoughyay ityay aymay ebay eemedday ayay
acrilegesay, isyay otnay anishedbay. Ymay othermay asway eadday, utbay eway adhay illstay
utiesday ichwhay eway oughtyay otay erformpay; eway ustmay ontinuecay ouryay oursecay ithway ethay
estray andyay earnlay otay inkthay ourselvesyay ortunatefay ilstwhay oneyay emainsray omwhay ethay
oilerspay ashay otnay eizedsay.

Ymay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtyay, ichwhay adhay eenbay eferredday ybay esethay eventsyay,
asway ownay againyay eterminedday uponyay. Iyay obtainedyay omfray ymay atherfay ayay espiteray ofyay
omesay eeksway. Ityay appearedyay otay emay acrilegesay osay oonsay otay eavelay ethay eposeray,
akinyay otay eathday, ofyay ethay ousehay ofyay ourningmay andyay otay ushray intoyay ethay ickthay ofyay
ifelay. Iyay asway ewnay otay orrowsay, utbay ityay idday otnay ethay esslay alarmyay emay. Iyay asway
unwillingyay otay uitqay ethay ightsay ofyay osethay atthay emainedray otay emay, andyay aboveyay
allyay, Iyay esiredday otay eesay ymay eetsway Elizabethyay inyay omesay egreeday onsoledcay.

Eshay indeedyay eiledvay erhay iefgray andyay ovestray otay actyay ethay omfortercay otay usyay allyay.
Eshay ookedlay eadilystay onyay ifelay andyay assumedyay itsyay utiesday ithway ouragecay andyay
ealzay. Eshay evotedday erselfhay otay osethay omwhay eshay adhay eenbay aughttay otay allcay
erhay uncleyay andyay ousinscay. Evernay asway eshay osay enchantingyay asyay atyay isthay imetay,
enwhay eshay ecalledray ethay unshinesay ofyay erhay ilessmay andyay entspay emthay uponyay usyay.
Eshay orgotfay evenyay erhay ownyay egretray inyay erhay endeavoursyay otay akemay usyay orgetfay.

Ethay ayday ofyay ymay epartureday atyay engthlay arrivedyay. Ervalclay entspay ethay astlay
eveningyay ithway usyay. Ehay adhay endeavouredyay otay ersuadepay ishay atherfay otay ermitpay
imhay otay accompanyyay emay andyay otay ecomebay ymay ellowfay udentstay, utbay inyay ainvay. Ishay
atherfay asway ayay arrow-mindednay adertray andyay awsay idlenessyay andyay uinray inyay ethay
aspirationsyay andyay ambitionyay ofyay ishay onsay. Enryhay eeplyday eltfay ethay isfortunemay
ofyay eingbay ebarredday omfray ayay iberallay educationyay. Ehay aidsay ittlelay, utbay enwhay
ehay okespay Iyay eadray inyay ishay indlingkay eyeyay andyay inyay ishay animatedyay anceglay ayay
estrainedray utbay irmfay esolveray otnay otay ebay ainedchay otay ethay iserablemay etailsday
ofyay ommercecay.

Eway atsay atelay. Eway ouldcay otnay eartay ourselvesyay awayyay omfray eachyay otheryay ornay
ersuadepay ourselvesyay otay aysay ethay ordway arewell“fay!” Ityay asway aidsay, andyay eway
etiredray underyay ethay etencepray ofyay eekingsay eposeray, eachyay ancyingfay atthay ethay
otheryay asway eceivedday; utbay enwhay atyay orning’smay awnday Iyay escendedday otay ethay
arriagecay ichwhay asway otay onveycay emay awayyay, eythay ereway allyay ere—mythay atherfay
againyay otay essblay emay, Ervalclay otay esspray ymay andhay onceyay oremay, ymay Elizabethyay otay
enewray erhay entreatiesyay atthay Iyay ouldway itewray oftenyay andyay otay estowbay ethay astlay
emininefay attentionsyay onyay erhay aymateplay andyay iendfray.

Iyay ewthray yselfmay intoyay ethay aisechay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayyay andyay indulgedyay inyay
ethay ostmay elancholymay eflectionsray. Iyay, owhay adhay everyay eenbay urroundedsay ybay
amiableyay ompanionscay, ontinuallycay engagedyay inyay endeavouringyay otay estowbay utualmay
easure—iplay asway ownay aloneyay. Inyay ethay universityyay itherwhay Iyay asway oinggay Iyay
ustmay ormfay ymay ownyay iendsfray andyay ebay ymay ownyay otectorpray. Ymay ifelay adhay ithertohay
eenbay emarkablyray ecludedsay andyay omesticday, andyay isthay adhay ivengay emay invincibleyay
epugnanceray otay ewnay ountenancescay. Iyay ovedlay ymay othersbray, Elizabethyay, andyay
Ervalclay; esethay ereway old“ay amiliarfay acesfay,” utbay Iyay elievedbay yselfmay
otallytay unfittedyay orfay ethay ompanycay ofyay angersstray. Uchsay ereway ymay eflectionsray asyay
Iyay ommencedcay ymay ourneyjay; utbay asyay Iyay oceededpray, ymay iritsspay andyay opeshay oseray. Iyay
ardentlyyay esiredday ethay acquisitionyay ofyay owledgeknay. Iyay adhay oftenyay, enwhay atyay omehay,
oughtthay ityay ardhay otay emainray uringday ymay youthyay oopedcay upyay inyay oneyay aceplay andyay adhay
ongedlay otay enteryay ethay orldway andyay aketay ymay ationstay amongyay otheryay umanhay eingsbay. 
Ownay ymay esiresday ereway ompliedcay ithway, andyay ityay ouldway, indeedyay, avehay eenbay ollyfay otay
epentray.

Iyay adhay ufficientsay eisurelay orfay esethay andyay anymay otheryay eflectionsray uringday ymay
ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtyay, ichwhay asway onglay andyay atiguingfay. Atyay engthlay ethay
ighhay itewhay eeplestay ofyay ethay owntay etmay ymay eyesyay. Iyay alightedyay andyay asway
onductedcay otay ymay olitarysay apartmentyay otay endspay ethay eveningyay asyay Iyay easedplay.

Ethay extnay orningmay Iyay eliveredday ymay etterslay ofyay introductionyay andyay aidpay ayay isitvay otay
omesay ofyay ethay incipalpray ofessorspray. Ance—orchay atherray ethay evilyay
influenceyay, ethay Angelyay ofyay Estructionday, ichwhay assertedyay omnipotentyay aysway overyay emay
omfray ethay omentmay Iyay urnedtay ymay eluctantray epsstay omfray ymay ather’sfay
oor—ledday emay irstfay otay May. Empekray, ofessorpray ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Ehay
asway anyay uncouthyay anmay, utbay eeplyday imbuedyay inyay ethay ecretssay ofyay ishay iencescay. Ehay
askedyay emay everalsay uestionsqay oncerningcay ymay ogresspray inyay ethay ifferentday anchesbray
ofyay iencescay appertainingyay otay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Iyay epliedray arelesslycay, andyay
artlypay inyay ontemptcay, entionedmay ethay amesnay ofyay ymay alchemistsyay asyay ethay incipalpray
authorsyay Iyay adhay udiedstay. Ethay ofessorpray aredstay. ave“hay youyay,” ehay
aidsay, eally“ray entspay youryay imetay inyay udyingstay uchsay onsensenay?”

Iyay epliedray inyay ethay affirmativeyay. every“ay inutemay,” ontinuedcay May. Empekray ithway
armthway, every“ay instantyay atthay youyay avehay astedway onyay osethay ooksbay isyay utterlyyay
andyay entirelyyay ostlay. Youyay avehay urdenedbay youryay emorymay ithway explodedyay ystemssay
andyay uselessyay amesnay. Oodgay Odgay! Inyay atwhay esertday andlay avehay youyay ivedlay,
erewhay onay oneyay asway indkay enoughyay otay informyay youyay atthay esethay anciesfay ichwhay youyay
avehay osay eedilygray imbibedyay areyay ayay ousandthay yearsyay oldyay andyay asyay ustymay asyay eythay
areyay ancientyay? Iyay ittlelay expectedyay, inyay isthay enlightenedyay andyay ientificscay
ageyay, otay indfay ayay iscipleday ofyay Albertusyay Agnusmay andyay Aracelsuspay. Ymay earday
irsay, youyay ustmay eginbay youryay udiesstay entirelyyay anewyay.”

Osay ayingsay, ehay eppedstay asideyay andyay otewray ownday ayay istlay ofyay everalsay ooksbay
eatingtray ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay ichwhay ehay esiredday emay otay ocurepray, andyay
ismissedday emay afteryay entioningmay atthay inyay ethay eginningbay ofyay ethay ollowingfay
eekway ehay intendedyay otay ommencecay ayay oursecay ofyay ectureslay uponyay aturalnay
ilosophyphay inyay itsyay eneralgay elationsray, andyay atthay May. Aldmanway, ayay ellowfay
ofessorpray, ouldway ecturelay uponyay emistrychay ethay alternateyay aysday atthay ehay
omittedyay.

Iyay eturnedray omehay otnay isappointedday, orfay Iyay avehay aidsay atthay Iyay adhay onglay
onsideredcay osethay authorsyay uselessyay omwhay ethay ofessorpray eprobatedray; utbay Iyay
eturnedray otnay atyay allyay ethay oremay inclinedyay otay ecurray otay esethay udiesstay inyay anyyay
apeshay. May. Empekray asway ayay ittlelay uatsqay anmay ithway ayay uffgray oicevay andyay ayay
epulsiveray ountenancecay; ethay eachertay, ereforethay, idday otnay epossesspray emay inyay
avourfay ofyay ishay ursuitspay. Inyay atherray ayay ootay ilosophicalphay andyay onnectedcay ayay
ainstray, erhapspay, Iyay avehay ivengay anyay accountyay ofyay ethay onclusionscay Iyay adhay omecay
otay oncerningcay emthay inyay ymay earlyyay yearsyay. Asyay ayay ildchay Iyay adhay otnay eenbay
ontentcay ithway ethay esultsray omisedpray ybay ethay odernmay ofessorspray ofyay aturalnay
iencescay. Ithway ayay onfusioncay ofyay ideasyay onlyyay otay ebay accountedyay orfay ybay ymay
extremeyay youthyay andyay ymay antway ofyay ayay uidegay onyay uchsay attersmay, Iyay adhay etrodray ethay
epsstay ofyay owledgeknay alongyay ethay athspay ofyay imetay andyay exchangedyay ethay
iscoveriesday ofyay ecentray inquirersyay orfay ethay eamsdray ofyay orgottenfay alchemistsyay.
Esidesbay, Iyay adhay ayay ontemptcay orfay ethay usesyay ofyay odernmay aturalnay ilosophyphay.
Ityay asway eryvay ifferentday enwhay ethay astersmay ofyay ethay iencescay oughtsay
immortalityyay andyay owerpay; uchsay iewsvay, althoughyay utilefay, ereway andgray; utbay ownay
ethay enescay asway angedchay. Ethay ambitionyay ofyay ethay inquireryay eemedsay otay imitlay
itselfyay otay ethay annihilationyay ofyay osethay isionsvay onyay ichwhay ymay interestyay inyay
iencescay asway ieflychay oundedfay. Iyay asway equiredray otay exchangeyay imeraschay ofyay
oundlessbay andeurgray orfay ealitiesray ofyay ittlelay orthway.

Uchsay ereway ymay eflectionsray uringday ethay irstfay otway oryay eethray aysday ofyay ymay
esidenceray atyay Ingolstadtyay, ichwhay ereway ieflychay entspay inyay ecomingbay
acquaintedyay ithway ethay ocalitieslay andyay ethay incipalpray esidentsray inyay ymay ewnay
abodeyay. Utbay asyay ethay ensuingyay eekway ommencedcay, Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay informationyay
ichwhay May. Empekray adhay ivengay emay oncerningcay ethay ectureslay. Andyay althoughyay Iyay
ouldcay otnay onsentcay otay ogay andyay earhay atthay ittlelay onceitedcay ellowfay eliverday
entencessay outyay ofyay ayay ulpitpay, Iyay ecollectedray atwhay ehay adhay aidsay ofyay May.
Aldmanway, omwhay Iyay adhay evernay eensay, asyay ehay adhay ithertohay eenbay outyay ofyay owntay.

Artlypay omfray uriositycay andyay artlypay omfray idlenessyay, Iyay entway intoyay ethay ecturinglay
oomray, ichwhay May. Aldmanway enteredyay ortlyshay afteryay. Isthay ofessorpray asway eryvay
unlikeyay ishay olleaguecay. Ehay appearedyay aboutyay iftyfay yearsyay ofyay ageyay, utbay ithway anyay
aspectyay expressiveyay ofyay ethay eatestgray enevolencebay; ayay ewfay eygray airshay overedcay ishay
emplestay, utbay osethay atyay ethay ackbay ofyay ishay eadhay ereway earlynay ackblay. Ishay ersonpay
asway ortshay utbay emarkablyray erectyay andyay ishay oicevay ethay eetestsway Iyay adhay everyay eardhay.
Ehay eganbay ishay ecturelay ybay ayay ecapitulationray ofyay ethay istoryhay ofyay emistrychay andyay
ethay ariousvay improvementsyay ademay ybay ifferentday enmay ofyay earninglay, onouncingpray
ithway ervourfay ethay amesnay ofyay ethay ostmay istinguishedday iscoverersday. Ehay enthay ooktay
ayay ursorycay iewvay ofyay ethay esentpray atestay ofyay ethay iencescay andyay explainedyay anymay ofyay
itsyay elementaryyay ermstay. Afteryay avinghay ademay ayay ewfay eparatorypray experimentsyay, ehay
oncludedcay ithway ayay anegyricpay uponyay odernmay emistrychay, ethay ermstay ofyay ichwhay Iyay
allshay evernay orgetfay:

e“thay ancientyay eacherstay ofyay isthay iencescay,” aidsay ehay,
omised“pray impossibilitiesyay andyay erformedpay othingnay. Ethay odernmay astersmay
omisepray eryvay ittlelay; eythay owknay atthay etalsmay annotcay ebay ansmutedtray andyay atthay
ethay elixiryay ofyay ifelay isyay ayay imerachay utbay esethay ilosophersphay, osewhay andshay eemsay
onlyyay ademay otay abbleday inyay irtday, andyay eirthay eyesyay otay orepay overyay ethay icroscopemay oryay
uciblecray, avehay indeedyay erformedpay iraclesmay. Eythay enetratepay intoyay ethay ecessesray
ofyay aturenay andyay owshay owhay eshay orksway inyay erhay iding-placeshay. Eythay ascendyay intoyay ethay
eavenshay; eythay avehay iscoveredday owhay ethay oodblay irculatescay, andyay ethay aturenay ofyay
ethay airyay eway eathebray. Eythay avehay acquiredyay ewnay andyay almostyay unlimitedyay owerspay;
eythay ancay ommandcay ethay understhay ofyay eavenhay, imicmay ethay earthquakeyay, andyay evenyay
ockmay ethay invisibleyay orldway ithway itsyay ownyay adowsshay.”

Uchsay ereway ethay ofessor’spray ords—ratherway etlay emay aysay uchsay ethay ordsway ofyay
ethay ate—enouncedfay otay estroyday emay. Asyay ehay entway onyay Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay ymay oulsay
ereway applinggray ithway ayay alpablepay enemyyay; oneyay ybay oneyay ethay ariousvay eyskay ereway
ouchedtay ichwhay ormedfay ethay echanismmay ofyay ymay eingbay; ordchay afteryay ordchay asway
oundedsay, andyay oonsay ymay indmay asway illedfay ithway oneyay oughtthay, oneyay onceptioncay,
oneyay urposepay. Osay uchmay ashay eenbay oneday, exclaimedyay ethay oulsay ofyay
Ankenstein—morefray, arfay oremay, illway Iyay achieveyay; eadingtray inyay ethay epsstay
alreadyyay arkedmay, Iyay illway ioneerpay ayay ewnay ayway, exploreyay unknownyay owerspay, andyay
unfoldyay otay ethay orldway ethay eepestday ysteriesmay ofyay eationcray.

Iyay osedclay otnay ymay eyesyay atthay ightnay. Ymay internalyay eingbay asway inyay ayay atestay ofyay
insurrectionyay andyay urmoiltay; Iyay eltfay atthay orderyay ouldway encethay ariseyay, utbay Iyay
adhay onay owerpay otay oducepray ityay. Ybay egreesday, afteryay ethay orning’smay awnday,
eepslay amecay. Iyay awokeyay, andyay ymay yesternight’syay oughtsthay ereway asyay ayay eamdray.
Erethay onlyyay emainedray ayay esolutionray otay eturnray otay ymay ancientyay udiesstay andyay otay
evoteday yselfmay otay ayay iencescay orfay ichwhay Iyay elievedbay yselfmay otay ossesspay ayay
aturalnay alenttay. Onyay ethay amesay ayday Iyay aidpay May. Aldmanway ayay isitvay. Ishay
annersmay inyay ivatepray ereway evenyay oremay ildmay andyay attractiveyay anthay inyay ublicpay,
orfay erethay asway ayay ertaincay ignityday inyay ishay ienmay uringday ishay ecturelay ichwhay inyay
ishay ownyay ousehay asway eplacedray ybay ethay eatestgray affabilityyay andyay indnesskay. Iyay
avegay imhay ettypray earlynay ethay amesay accountyay ofyay ymay ormerfay ursuitspay asyay Iyay adhay
ivengay otay ishay ellowfay ofessorpray. Ehay eardhay ithway attentionyay ethay ittlelay
arrationnay oncerningcay ymay udiesstay andyay iledsmay atyay ethay amesnay ofyay Orneliuscay
Agrippayay andyay Aracelsuspay, utbay ithoutway ethay ontemptcay atthay May. Empekray adhay
exhibitedyay. Ehay aidsay atthay ese“thay ereway enmay otay osewhay indefatigableyay ealzay
odernmay ilosophersphay ereway indebtedyay orfay ostmay ofyay ethay oundationsfay ofyay eirthay
owledgeknay. Eythay adhay eftlay otay usyay, asyay anyay easieryay asktay, otay ivegay ewnay amesnay
andyay arrangeyay inyay onnectedcay assificationsclay ethay actsfay ichwhay eythay inyay ayay
eatgray egreeday adhay eenbay ethay instrumentsyay ofyay ingingbray otay ightlay. Ethay
abourslay ofyay enmay ofyay eniusgay, oweverhay erroneouslyyay irectedday, arcelyscay everyay
ailfay inyay ultimatelyyay urningtay otay ethay olidsay advantageyay ofyay ankindmay.” Iyay
istenedlay otay ishay atementstay, ichwhay asway eliveredday ithoutway anyyay esumptionpray
oryay affectationyay, andyay enthay addedyay atthay ishay ecturelay adhay emovedray ymay
ejudicespray againstyay odernmay emistschay; Iyay expressedyay yselfmay inyay easuredmay
ermstay, ithway ethay odestymay andyay eferenceday ueday omfray ayay youthyay otay ishay
instructoryay, ithoutway ettinglay escapeyay inexperience(ay inyay ifelay ouldway avehay
ademay emay ashamedyay) anyyay ofyay ethay enthusiasmyay ichwhay imulatedstay ymay intendedyay
abourslay. Iyay equestedray ishay adviceyay oncerningcay ethay ooksbay Iyay oughtyay otay
ocurepray.

i“ay amyay appyhay,” aidsay May. Aldmanway, o“tay avehay ainedgay ayay
iscipleday; andyay ifyay youryay applicationyay equalsyay youryay abilityyay, Iyay avehay onay oubtday ofyay
youryay uccesssay. Emistrychay isyay atthay anchbray ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay inyay ichwhay ethay
eatestgray improvementsyay avehay eenbay andyay aymay ebay ademay; ityay isyay onyay atthay accountyay atthay
Iyay avehay ademay ityay ymay eculiarpay udystay; utbay atyay ethay amesay imetay, Iyay avehay otnay
eglectednay ethay otheryay anchesbray ofyay iencescay. Ayay anmay ouldway akemay utbay ayay eryvay orrysay
emistchay ifyay ehay attendedyay otay atthay epartmentday ofyay umanhay owledgeknay aloneyay. Ifyay youryay
ishway isyay otay ecomebay eallyray ayay anmay ofyay iencescay andyay otnay erelymay ayay ettypay
experimentalistyay, Iyay ouldshay adviseyay youyay otay applyyay otay everyyay anchbray ofyay aturalnay
ilosophyphay, includingyay athematicsmay.”

Ehay enthay ooktay emay intoyay ishay aboratorylay andyay explainedyay otay emay ethay usesyay ofyay ishay
ariousvay achinesmay, instructingyay emay asyay otay atwhay Iyay oughtyay otay ocurepray andyay
omisingpray emay ethay useyay ofyay ishay ownyay enwhay Iyay ouldshay avehay advancedyay arfay enoughyay inyay
ethay iencescay otnay otay erangeday eirthay echanismmay. Ehay alsoyay avegay emay ethay istlay ofyay
ooksbay ichwhay Iyay adhay equestedray, andyay Iyay ooktay ymay eavelay.

Usthay endedyay ayay ayday emorablemay otay emay; ityay ecidedday ymay uturefay estinyday.




Apterchay 4


Omfray isthay ayday aturalnay ilosophyphay, andyay articularlypay emistrychay, inyay ethay
ostmay omprehensivecay ensesay ofyay ethay ermtay, ecamebay earlynay ymay olesay occupationyay.
Iyay eadray ithway ardouryay osethay orksway, osay ullfay ofyay eniusgay andyay iscriminationday,
ichwhay odernmay inquirersyay avehay ittenwray onyay esethay ubjectssay. Iyay attendedyay ethay
ectureslay andyay ultivatedcay ethay acquaintanceyay ofyay ethay enmay ofyay iencescay ofyay ethay
universityyay, andyay Iyay oundfay evenyay inyay May. Empekray ayay eatgray ealday ofyay oundsay ensesay
andyay ealray informationyay, ombinedcay, ityay isyay uetray, ithway ayay epulsiveray
ysiognomyphay andyay annersmay, utbay otnay onyay atthay accountyay ethay esslay aluablevay. Inyay
May. Aldmanway Iyay oundfay ayay uetray iendfray. Ishay entlenessgay asway evernay ingedtay ybay
ogmatismday, andyay ishay instructionsyay ereway ivengay ithway anyay airyay ofyay anknessfray andyay
oodgay aturenay atthay anishedbay everyyay ideayay ofyay edantrypay. Inyay ayay ousandthay aysway
ehay oothedsmay orfay emay ethay athpay ofyay owledgeknay andyay ademay ethay ostmay abstruseyay
inquiriesyay earclay andyay acilefay otay ymay apprehensionyay. Ymay applicationyay asway atyay
irstfay uctuatingflay andyay uncertainyay; ityay ainedgay engthstray asyay Iyay oceededpray andyay
oonsay ecamebay osay ardentyay andyay eageryay atthay ethay arsstay oftenyay isappearedday inyay ethay
ightlay ofyay orningmay ilstwhay Iyay asway yetyay engagedyay inyay ymay aboratorylay.

Asyay Iyay appliedyay osay oselyclay, ityay aymay ebay easilyyay onceivedcay atthay ymay ogresspray
asway apidray. Ymay ardouryay asway indeedyay ethay astonishmentyay ofyay ethay udentsstay, andyay
ymay oficiencypray atthay ofyay ethay astersmay. Ofessorpray Empekray oftenyay askedyay emay,
ithway ayay yslay ilesmay, owhay Orneliuscay Agrippayay entway onyay, ilstwhay May. Aldmanway
expressedyay ethay ostmay eartfelthay exultationyay inyay ymay ogresspray. Otway yearsyay
assedpay inyay isthay annermay, uringday ichwhay Iyay aidpay onay isitvay otay Enevagay, utbay asway
engagedyay, earthay andyay oulsay, inyay ethay ursuitpay ofyay omesay iscoveriesday ichwhay Iyay
opedhay otay akemay. Onenay utbay osethay owhay avehay experiencedyay emthay ancay onceivecay
ofyay ethay enticementsyay ofyay iencescay. Inyay otheryay udiesstay youyay ogay asyay arfay asyay
othersyay avehay onegay eforebay youyay, andyay erethay isyay othingnay oremay otay owknay; utbay inyay
ayay ientificscay ursuitpay erethay isyay ontinualcay oodfay orfay iscoveryday andyay onderway.
Ayay indmay ofyay oderatemay apacitycay ichwhay oselyclay ursuespay oneyay udystay ustmay
infalliblyyay arriveyay atyay eatgray oficiencypray inyay atthay udystay; andyay Iyay, owhay
ontinuallycay oughtsay ethay attainmentyay ofyay oneyay objectyay ofyay ursuitpay andyay asway
olelysay appedwray upyay inyay isthay, improvedyay osay apidlyray atthay atyay ethay endyay ofyay otway
yearsyay Iyay ademay omesay iscoveriesday inyay ethay improvementyay ofyay omesay emicalchay
instrumentsyay, ichwhay ocuredpray emay eatgray esteemyay andyay admirationyay atyay ethay
universityyay. Enwhay Iyay adhay arrivedyay atyay isthay ointpay andyay adhay ecomebay asyay ellway
acquaintedyay ithway ethay eorythay andyay acticepray ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay asyay
ependedday onyay ethay essonslay ofyay anyyay ofyay ethay ofessorspray atyay Ingolstadtyay, ymay
esidenceray erethay eingbay onay ongerlay onducivecay otay ymay improvementsyay, Iyay oughtthay
ofyay eturningray otay ymay iendsfray andyay ymay ativenay owntay, enwhay anyay incidentyay
appenedhay atthay otractedpray ymay aystay.

Oneyay ofyay ethay enomenaphay ichwhay adhay eculiarlypay attractedyay ymay attentionyay asway
ethay ucturestray ofyay ethay umanhay amefray, andyay, indeedyay, anyyay animalyay enduedyay ithway
ifelay. Encewhay, Iyay oftenyay askedyay yselfmay, idday ethay inciplepray ofyay ifelay oceedpray?
Ityay asway ayay oldbay uestionqay, andyay oneyay ichwhay ashay everyay eenbay onsideredcay asyay ayay
ysterymay; yetyay ithway owhay anymay ingsthay areyay eway uponyay ethay inkbray ofyay ecomingbay
acquaintedyay, ifyay owardicecay oryay arelessnesscay idday otnay estrainray ouryay
inquiriesyay. Iyay evolvedray esethay ircumstancescay inyay ymay indmay andyay eterminedday
enceforththay otay applyyay yselfmay oremay articularlypay otay osethay anchesbray ofyay
aturalnay ilosophyphay ichwhay elateray otay ysiologyphay. Unlessyay Iyay adhay eenbay
animatedyay ybay anyay almostyay upernaturalsay enthusiasmyay, ymay applicationyay otay isthay
udystay ouldway avehay eenbay irksomeyay andyay almostyay intolerableyay. Otay examineyay ethay
ausescay ofyay ifelay, eway ustmay irstfay avehay ecourseray otay eathday. Iyay ecamebay
acquaintedyay ithway ethay iencescay ofyay anatomyyay, utbay isthay asway otnay ufficientsay; Iyay
ustmay alsoyay observeyay ethay aturalnay ecayday andyay orruptioncay ofyay ethay umanhay odybay.
Inyay ymay educationyay ymay atherfay adhay akentay ethay eatestgray ecautionspray atthay ymay
indmay ouldshay ebay impressedyay ithway onay upernaturalsay orrorshay. Iyay oday otnay everyay
ememberray otay avehay embledtray atyay ayay aletay ofyay uperstitionsay oryay otay avehay earedfay
ethay apparitionyay ofyay ayay iritspay. Arknessday adhay onay effectyay uponyay ymay ancyfay, andyay
ayay urchyardchay asway otay emay erelymay ethay eceptacleray ofyay odiesbay eprivedday ofyay
ifelay, ichwhay, omfray eingbay ethay eatsay ofyay eautybay andyay engthstray, adhay ecomebay
oodfay orfay ethay ormway. Ownay Iyay asway edlay otay examineyay ethay ausecay andyay ogresspray ofyay
isthay ecayday andyay orcedfay otay endspay aysday andyay ightsnay inyay aultsvay andyay
arnel-houseschay. Ymay attentionyay asway ixedfay uponyay everyyay objectyay ethay ostmay
insupportableyay otay ethay elicacyday ofyay ethay umanhay eelingsfay. Iyay awsay owhay ethay
inefay ormfay ofyay anmay asway egradedday andyay astedway; Iyay eheldbay ethay orruptioncay ofyay
eathday ucceedsay otay ethay oomingblay eekchay ofyay ifelay; Iyay awsay owhay ethay ormway
inheritedyay ethay ondersway ofyay ethay eyeyay andyay ainbray. Iyay ausedpay, examiningyay andyay
analysingyay allyay ethay inutiaemay ofyay ausationcay, asyay exemplifiedyay inyay ethay angechay
omfray ifelay otay eathday, andyay eathday otay ifelay, untilyay omfray ethay idstmay ofyay isthay
arknessday ayay uddensay ightlay okebray inyay uponyay e—amay ightlay osay illiantbray andyay
ondrousway, yetyay osay implesay, atthay ilewhay Iyay ecamebay izzyday ithway ethay immensityyay
ofyay ethay ospectpray ichwhay ityay illustratedyay, Iyay asway urprisedsay atthay amongyay osay
anymay enmay ofyay eniusgay owhay adhay irectedday eirthay inquiriesyay owardstay ethay amesay
iencescay, atthay Iyay aloneyay ouldshay ebay eservedray otay iscoverday osay astonishingyay ayay
ecretsay.

Ememberray, Iyay amyay otnay ecordingray ethay isionvay ofyay ayay admanmay. Ethay unsay oesday otnay
oremay ertainlycay ineshay inyay ethay eavenshay anthay atthay ichwhay Iyay ownay affirmyay isyay
uetray. Omesay iraclemay ightmay avehay oducedpray ityay, yetyay ethay agesstay ofyay ethay
iscoveryday ereway istinctday andyay obablepray. Afteryay aysday andyay ightsnay ofyay
incredibleyay abourlay andyay atiguefay, Iyay ucceededsay inyay iscoveringday ethay ausecay ofyay
enerationgay andyay ifelay; aynay, oremay, Iyay ecamebay yselfmay apablecay ofyay estowingbay
animationyay uponyay ifelesslay attermay.

Ethay astonishmentyay ichwhay Iyay adhay atyay irstfay experiencedyay onyay isthay iscoveryday
oonsay avegay aceplay otay elightday andyay aptureray. Afteryay osay uchmay imetay entspay inyay
ainfulpay abourlay, otay arriveyay atyay onceyay atyay ethay ummitsay ofyay ymay esiresday asway ethay
ostmay atifyinggray onsummationcay ofyay ymay oilstay. Utbay isthay iscoveryday asway osay
eatgray andyay overwhelmingyay atthay allyay ethay epsstay ybay ichwhay Iyay adhay eenbay
ogressivelypray edlay otay ityay ereway obliteratedyay, andyay Iyay eheldbay onlyyay ethay esultray.
Atwhay adhay eenbay ethay udystay andyay esireday ofyay ethay isestway enmay incesay ethay eationcray
ofyay ethay orldway asway ownay ithinway ymay aspgray. Otnay atthay, ikelay ayay agicmay enescay, ityay
allyay openedyay uponyay emay atyay onceyay: ethay informationyay Iyay adhay obtainedyay asway ofyay ayay
aturenay atherray otay irectday ymay endeavoursyay osay oonsay asyay Iyay ouldshay ointpay emthay
owardstay ethay objectyay ofyay ymay earchsay anthay otay exhibityay atthay objectyay alreadyyay
accomplishedyay. Iyay asway ikelay ethay Arabianyay owhay adhay eenbay uriedbay ithway ethay eadday
andyay oundfay ayay assagepay otay ifelay, aidedyay onlyyay ybay oneyay immeringglay andyay eeminglysay
ineffectualyay ightlay.

Iyay eesay ybay youryay eagernessyay andyay ethay onderway andyay opehay ichwhay youryay eyesyay
expressyay, ymay iendfray, atthay youyay expectyay otay ebay informedyay ofyay ethay ecretsay ithway
ichwhay Iyay amyay acquaintedyay; atthay annotcay ebay; istenlay atientlypay untilyay ethay endyay
ofyay ymay orystay, andyay youyay illway easilyyay erceivepay ywhay Iyay amyay eservedray uponyay atthay
ubjectsay. Iyay illway otnay eadlay youyay onyay, unguardedyay andyay ardentyay asyay Iyay enthay asway,
otay youryay estructionday andyay infallibleyay iserymay. Earnlay omfray emay, ifyay otnay ybay ymay
eceptspray, atyay eastlay ybay ymay exampleyay, owhay angerousday isyay ethay acquirementyay ofyay
owledgeknay andyay owhay uchmay appierhay atthay anmay isyay owhay elievesbay ishay ativenay owntay
otay ebay ethay orldway, anthay ehay owhay aspiresyay otay ecomebay eatergray anthay ishay aturenay
illway allowyay.

Enwhay Iyay oundfay osay astonishingyay ayay owerpay acedplay ithinway ymay andshay, Iyay esitatedhay
ayay onglay imetay oncerningcay ethay annermay inyay ichwhay Iyay ouldshay employyay ityay.
Althoughyay Iyay ossessedpay ethay apacitycay ofyay estowingbay animationyay, yetyay otay
eparepray ayay amefray orfay ethay eceptionray ofyay ityay, ithway allyay itsyay intricaciesyay ofyay
ibresfay, usclesmay, andyay einsvay, illstay emainedray ayay orkway ofyay inconceivableyay
ifficultyday andyay abourlay. Iyay oubtedday atyay irstfay etherwhay Iyay ouldshay attemptyay ethay
eationcray ofyay ayay eingbay ikelay yselfmay, oryay oneyay ofyay implersay organizationyay; utbay ymay
imaginationyay asway ootay uchmay exaltedyay ybay ymay irstfay uccesssay otay ermitpay emay otay
oubtday ofyay ymay abilityyay otay ivegay ifelay otay anyay animalyay asyay omplexcay andyay onderfulway
asyay anmay. Ethay aterialsmay atyay esentpray ithinway ymay ommandcay ardlyhay appearedyay
adequateyay otay osay arduousyay anyay undertakingyay, utbay Iyay oubtedday otnay atthay Iyay ouldshay
ultimatelyyay ucceedsay. Iyay eparedpray yselfmay orfay ayay ultitudemay ofyay eversesray; ymay
operationsyay ightmay ebay incessantlyyay affledbay, andyay atyay astlay ymay orkway ebay
imperfectyay, yetyay enwhay Iyay onsideredcay ethay improvementyay ichwhay everyyay ayday akestay
aceplay inyay iencescay andyay echanicsmay, Iyay asway encouragedyay otay opehay ymay esentpray
attemptsyay ouldway atyay eastlay aylay ethay oundationsfay ofyay uturefay uccesssay. Ornay
ouldcay Iyay onsidercay ethay agnitudemay andyay omplexitycay ofyay ymay anplay asyay anyyay
argumentyay ofyay itsyay impracticabilityyay. Ityay asway ithway esethay eelingsfay atthay Iyay
eganbay ethay eationcray ofyay ayay umanhay eingbay. Asyay ethay inutenessmay ofyay ethay artspay
ormedfay ayay eatgray indrancehay otay ymay eedspay, Iyay esolvedray, ontrarycay otay ymay irstfay
intentionyay, otay akemay ethay eingbay ofyay ayay iganticgay aturestay, atthay isyay otay aysay,
aboutyay eightyay eetfay inyay eighthay, andyay oportionablypray argelay. Afteryay avinghay
ormedfay isthay eterminationday andyay avinghay entspay omesay onthsmay inyay uccessfullysay
ollectingcay andyay arrangingyay ymay aterialsmay, Iyay eganbay.

Onay oneyay ancay onceivecay ethay arietyvay ofyay eelingsfay ichwhay orebay emay onwardsyay, ikelay
ayay urricanehay, inyay ethay irstfay enthusiasmyay ofyay uccesssay. Ifelay andyay eathday
appearedyay otay emay idealyay oundsbay, ichwhay Iyay ouldshay irstfay eakbray oughthray, andyay
ourpay ayay orrenttay ofyay ightlay intoyay ouryay arkday orldway. Ayay ewnay eciesspay ouldway essblay
emay asyay itsyay eatorcray andyay ourcesay; anymay appyhay andyay excellentyay aturesnay ouldway
oweyay eirthay eingbay otay emay. Onay atherfay ouldcay aimclay ethay atitudegray ofyay ishay
ildchay osay ompletelycay asyay Iyay ouldshay eserveday eirsthay. Ursuingpay esethay
eflectionsray, Iyay oughtthay atthay ifyay Iyay ouldcay estowbay animationyay uponyay ifelesslay
attermay, Iyay ightmay inyay ocesspray ofyay imetay although(ay Iyay ownay oundfay ityay impossibleyay)
enewray ifelay erewhay eathday adhay apparentlyyay evotedday ethay odybay otay orruptioncay.

Esethay oughtsthay upportedsay ymay iritsspay, ilewhay Iyay ursuedpay ymay undertakingyay
ithway unremittingyay ardouryay. Ymay eekchay adhay owngray alepay ithway udystay, andyay ymay
ersonpay adhay ecomebay emaciatedyay ithway onfinementcay. Ometimessay, onyay ethay eryvay
inkbray ofyay ertaintycay, Iyay ailedfay; yetyay illstay Iyay ungclay otay ethay opehay ichwhay ethay
extnay ayday oryay ethay extnay ourhay ightmay ealiseray. Oneyay ecretsay ichwhay Iyay aloneyay
ossessedpay asway ethay opehay otay ichwhay Iyay adhay edicatedday yselfmay; andyay ethay oonmay
azedgay onyay ymay idnightmay abourslay, ilewhay, ithway unrelaxedyay andyay eathlessbray
eagernessyay, Iyay ursuedpay aturenay otay erhay iding-placeshay. Owhay allshay onceivecay
ethay orrorshay ofyay ymay ecretsay oiltay asyay Iyay abbledday amongyay ethay unhallowedyay ampsday
ofyay ethay avegray oryay orturedtay ethay ivinglay animalyay otay animateyay ethay ifelesslay
ayclay? Ymay imbslay ownay embletray, andyay ymay eyesyay imsway ithway ethay emembranceray; utbay
enthay ayay esistlessray andyay almostyay anticfray impulseyay urgedyay emay orwardfay; Iyay eemedsay
otay avehay ostlay allyay oulsay oryay ensationsay utbay orfay isthay oneyay ursuitpay. Ityay asway
indeedyay utbay ayay assingpay ancetray, atthay onlyyay ademay emay eelfay ithway enewedray
acutenessyay osay oonsay asyay, ethay unnaturalyay imulusstay easingcay otay operateyay, Iyay adhay
eturnedray otay ymay oldyay abitshay. Iyay ollectedcay onesbay omfray arnel-houseschay andyay
isturbedday, ithway ofanepray ingersfay, ethay emendoustray ecretssay ofyay ethay umanhay
amefray. Inyay ayay olitarysay amberchay, oryay atherray ellcay, atyay ethay optay ofyay ethay ousehay,
andyay eparatedsay omfray allyay ethay otheryay apartmentsyay ybay ayay allerygay andyay aircasestay,
Iyay eptkay ymay orkshopway ofyay ilthyfay eationcray; ymay eyeballsyay ereway artingstay omfray
eirthay ocketssay inyay attendingyay otay ethay etailsday ofyay ymay employmentyay. Ethay
issectingday oomray andyay ethay aughter-houseslay urnishedfay anymay ofyay ymay aterialsmay;
andyay oftenyay idday ymay umanhay aturenay urntay ithway oathinglay omfray ymay occupationyay,
ilstwhay, illstay urgedyay onyay ybay anyay eagernessyay ichwhay erpetuallypay increasedyay, Iyay
oughtbray ymay orkway earnay otay ayay onclusioncay.

Ethay ummersay onthsmay assedpay ilewhay Iyay asway usthay engagedyay, earthay andyay oulsay, inyay
oneyay ursuitpay. Ityay asway ayay ostmay eautifulbay easonsay; evernay idday ethay ieldsfay
estowbay ayay oremay entifulplay arvesthay oryay ethay inesvay yieldyay ayay oremay uxuriantlay
intagevay, utbay ymay eyesyay ereway insensibleyay otay ethay armschay ofyay aturenay. Andyay ethay
amesay eelingsfay ichwhay ademay emay eglectnay ethay enesscay aroundyay emay ausedcay emay alsoyay
otay orgetfay osethay iendsfray owhay ereway osay anymay ilesmay absentyay, andyay omwhay Iyay adhay
otnay eensay orfay osay onglay ayay imetay. Iyay ewknay ymay ilencesay isquietedday emthay, andyay Iyay
ellway ememberedray ethay ordsway ofyay ymay atherfay: i“ay owknay atthay ilewhay youyay areyay
easedplay ithway yourselfyay youyay illway inkthay ofyay usyay ithway affectionyay, andyay eway allshay
earhay egularlyray omfray youyay. Youyay ustmay ardonpay emay ifyay Iyay egardray anyyay
interruptionyay inyay youryay orrespondencecay asyay ayay oofpray atthay youryay otheryay utiesday
areyay equallyyay eglectednay.”

Iyay ewknay ellway ereforethay atwhay ouldway ebay ymay ather’sfay eelingsfay, utbay Iyay ouldcay
otnay eartay ymay oughtsthay omfray ymay employmentyay, oathsomelay inyay itselfyay, utbay ichwhay
adhay akentay anyay irresistibleyay oldhay ofyay ymay imaginationyay. Iyay ishedway, asyay ityay
ereway, otay ocrastinatepray allyay atthay elatedray otay ymay eelingsfay ofyay affectionyay
untilyay ethay eatgray objectyay, ichwhay allowedsway upyay everyyay abithay ofyay ymay aturenay,
ouldshay ebay ompletedcay.

Iyay enthay oughtthay atthay ymay atherfay ouldway ebay unjustyay ifyay ehay ascribedyay ymay eglectnay
otay icevay oryay aultinessfay onyay ymay artpay, utbay Iyay amyay ownay onvincedcay atthay ehay asway
ustifiedjay inyay onceivingcay atthay Iyay ouldshay otnay ebay altogetheryay eefray omfray
ameblay. Ayay umanhay eingbay inyay erfectionpay oughtyay alwaysyay otay eservepray ayay almcay andyay
eacefulpay indmay andyay evernay otay allowyay assionpay oryay ayay ansitorytray esireday otay
isturbday ishay anquillitytray. Iyay oday otnay inkthay atthay ethay ursuitpay ofyay owledgeknay
isyay anyay exceptionyay otay isthay uleray. Ifyay ethay udystay otay ichwhay youyay applyyay yourselfyay
ashay ayay endencytay otay eakenway youryay affectionsyay andyay otay estroyday youryay astetay orfay
osethay implesay easuresplay inyay ichwhay onay alloyyay ancay ossiblypay ixmay, enthay atthay
udystay isyay ertainlycay unlawfulyay, atthay isyay otay aysay, otnay efittingbay ethay umanhay
indmay. Ifyay isthay uleray ereway alwaysyay observedyay; ifyay onay anmay allowedyay anyyay ursuitpay
atsoeverwhay otay interfereyay ithway ethay anquillitytray ofyay ishay omesticday
affectionsyay, Eecegray adhay otnay eenbay enslavedyay, Arcæsay ouldway avehay aredspay ishay
ountrycay, Americayay ouldway avehay eenbay iscoveredday oremay aduallygray, andyay ethay
empiresyay ofyay Exicomay andyay Erupay adhay otnay eenbay estroyedday.

Utbay Iyay orgetfay atthay Iyay amyay oralizingmay inyay ethay ostmay interestingyay artpay ofyay ymay
aletay, andyay youryay ookslay emindray emay otay oceedpray.

Ymay atherfay ademay onay eproachray inyay ishay etterslay andyay onlyyay ooktay oticenay ofyay ymay
ilencesay ybay inquiringyay intoyay ymay occupationsyay oremay articularlypay anthay eforebay.
Interway, ingspray, andyay ummersay assedpay awayyay uringday ymay abourslay; utbay Iyay idday otnay
atchway ethay ossomblay oryay ethay expandingyay eaves—sightslay ichwhay eforebay alwaysyay
yieldedyay emay upremesay elight—soday eeplyday asway Iyay engrossedyay inyay ymay
occupationyay. Ethay eaveslay ofyay atthay yearyay adhay itheredway eforebay ymay orkway ewdray earnay
otay ayay oseclay, andyay ownay everyyay ayday owedshay emay oremay ainlyplay owhay ellway Iyay adhay
ucceededsay. Utbay ymay enthusiasmyay asway eckedchay ybay ymay anxietyyay, andyay Iyay appearedyay
atherray ikelay oneyay oomedday ybay averyslay otay oiltay inyay ethay inesmay, oryay anyyay otheryay
unwholesomeyay adetray anthay anyay artistyay occupiedyay ybay ishay avouritefay employmentyay.
Everyyay ightnay Iyay asway oppressedyay ybay ayay owslay everfay, andyay Iyay ecamebay ervousnay otay ayay ostmay
ainfulpay egreeday; ethay allfay ofyay ayay eaflay artledstay emay, andyay Iyay unnedshay ymay ellowfay
eaturescray asyay ifyay Iyay adhay eenbay uiltygay ofyay ayay imecray. Ometimessay Iyay ewgray alarmedyay atyay
ethay eckwray Iyay erceivedpay atthay Iyay adhay ecomebay; ethay energyyay ofyay ymay urposepay aloneyay
ustainedsay emay: ymay abourslay ouldway oonsay endyay, andyay Iyay elievedbay atthay exerciseyay andyay
amusementyay ouldway enthay ivedray awayyay incipientyay iseaseday; andyay Iyay omisedpray yselfmay
othbay ofyay esethay enwhay ymay eationcray ouldshay ebay ompletecay.




Apterchay 5


Ityay asway onyay ayay earydray ightnay ofyay Ovembernay atthay Iyay eheldbay ethay accomplishmentyay
ofyay ymay oilstay. Ithway anyay anxietyyay atthay almostyay amountedyay otay agonyyay, Iyay
ollectedcay ethay instrumentsyay ofyay ifelay aroundyay emay, atthay Iyay ightmay infuseyay ayay
arkspay ofyay eingbay intoyay ethay ifelesslay ingthay atthay aylay atyay ymay eetfay. Ityay asway
alreadyyay oneyay inyay ethay orningmay; ethay ainray atteredpay ismallyday againstyay ethay
anespay, andyay ymay andlecay asway earlynay urntbay outyay, enwhay, ybay ethay immerglay ofyay ethay
alf-extinguishedhay ightlay, Iyay awsay ethay ullday yellowyay eyeyay ofyay ethay eaturecray
openyay; ityay eathedbray ardhay, andyay ayay onvulsivecay otionmay agitatedyay itsyay imbslay.

Owhay ancay Iyay escribeday ymay emotionsyay atyay isthay atastrophecay, oryay owhay elineateday
ethay etchwray omwhay ithway uchsay infiniteyay ainspay andyay arecay Iyay adhay endeavouredyay otay
ormfay? Ishay imbslay ereway inyay oportionpray, andyay Iyay adhay electedsay ishay eaturesfay asyay
eautifulbay. Eautifulbay! Eatgray Odgay! Ishay yellowyay inskay arcelyscay overedcay
ethay orkway ofyay usclesmay andyay arteriesyay eneathbay; ishay airhay asway ofyay ayay ustrouslay
ackblay, andyay owingflay; ishay eethtay ofyay ayay earlypay itenesswhay; utbay esethay
uxurianceslay onlyyay ormedfay ayay oremay orridhay ontrastcay ithway ishay ateryway eyesyay,
atthay eemedsay almostyay ofyay ethay amesay olourcay asyay ethay un-whiteday ocketssay inyay ichwhay
eythay ereway etsay, ishay ivelledshray omplexioncay andyay aightstray ackblay ipslay.

Ethay ifferentday accidentsyay ofyay ifelay areyay otnay osay angeablechay asyay ethay eelingsfay
ofyay umanhay aturenay. Iyay adhay orkedway ardhay orfay earlynay otway yearsyay, orfay ethay olesay
urposepay ofyay infusingyay ifelay intoyay anyay inanimateyay odybay. Orfay isthay Iyay adhay
eprivedday yselfmay ofyay estray andyay ealthhay. Iyay adhay esiredday ityay ithway anyay ardouryay
atthay arfay exceededyay oderationmay; utbay ownay atthay Iyay adhay inishedfay, ethay eautybay
ofyay ethay eamdray anishedvay, andyay eathlessbray orrorhay andyay isgustday illedfay ymay
earthay. Unableyay otay endureyay ethay aspectyay ofyay ethay eingbay Iyay adhay eatedcray, Iyay
ushedray outyay ofyay ethay oomray andyay ontinuedcay ayay onglay imetay aversingtray ymay
ed-chamberbay, unableyay otay omposecay ymay indmay otay eepslay. Atyay engthlay assitudelay
ucceededsay otay ethay umulttay Iyay adhay eforebay enduredyay, andyay Iyay ewthray yselfmay onyay ethay
edbay inyay ymay othesclay, endeavouringyay otay eeksay ayay ewfay omentsmay ofyay orgetfulnessfay.
Utbay ityay asway inyay ainvay; Iyay eptslay, indeedyay, utbay Iyay asway isturbedday ybay ethay ildestway
eamsdray. Iyay oughtthay Iyay awsay Elizabethyay, inyay ethay oomblay ofyay ealthhay, alkingway inyay
ethay eetsstray ofyay Ingolstadtyay. Elightedday andyay urprisedsay, Iyay embracedyay erhay,
utbay asyay Iyay imprintedyay ethay irstfay isskay onyay erhay ipslay, eythay ecamebay ividlay ithway
ethay uehay ofyay eathday; erhay eaturesfay appearedyay otay angechay, andyay Iyay oughtthay atthay Iyay
eldhay ethay orpsecay ofyay ymay eadday othermay inyay ymay armsyay; ayay oudshray envelopedyay erhay
ormfay, andyay Iyay awsay ethay ave-wormsgray awlingcray inyay ethay oldsfay ofyay ethay annelflay.
Iyay artedstay omfray ymay eepslay ithway orrorhay; ayay oldcay ewday overedcay ymay oreheadfay, ymay
eethtay atteredchay, andyay everyyay imblay ecamebay onvulsedcay; enwhay, ybay ethay imday andyay
yellowyay ightlay ofyay ethay oonmay, asyay ityay orcedfay itsyay ayway oughthray ethay indowway
uttersshay, Iyay eheldbay ethay etch—thewray iserablemay onstermay omwhay Iyay adhay
eatedcray. Ehay eldhay upyay ethay urtaincay ofyay ethay edbay; andyay ishay eyesyay, ifyay eyesyay eythay
aymay ebay alledcay, ereway ixedfay onyay emay. Ishay awsjay openedyay, andyay ehay utteredmay omesay
inarticulateyay oundssay, ilewhay ayay ingray inkledwray ishay eekschay. Ehay ightmay avehay
okenspay, utbay Iyay idday otnay earhay; oneyay andhay asway etchedstray outyay, eeminglysay otay
etainday emay, utbay Iyay escapedyay andyay ushedray ownstairsday. Iyay ooktay efugeray inyay ethay
ourtyardcay elongingbay otay ethay ousehay ichwhay Iyay inhabitedyay, erewhay Iyay emainedray
uringday ethay estray ofyay ethay ightnay, alkingway upyay andyay ownday inyay ethay eatestgray
agitationyay, isteninglay attentivelyyay, atchingcay andyay earingfay eachyay oundsay asyay ifyay
ityay ereway otay announceyay ethay approachyay ofyay ethay emoniacalday orpsecay otay ichwhay Iyay
adhay osay iserablymay ivengay ifelay.

Ohyay! Onay ortalmay ouldcay upportsay ethay orrorhay ofyay atthay ountenancecay. Ayay ummymay
againyay enduedyay ithway animationyay ouldcay otnay ebay osay ideoushay asyay atthay etchwray. Iyay
adhay azedgay onyay imhay ilewhay unfinishedyay; ehay asway uglyyay enthay, utbay enwhay osethay
usclesmay andyay ointsjay ereway enderedray apablecay ofyay otionmay, ityay ecamebay ayay ingthay
uchsay asyay evenyay Anteday ouldcay otnay avehay onceivedcay.

Iyay assedpay ethay ightnay etchedlywray. Ometimessay ymay ulsepay eatbay osay uicklyqay andyay
ardlyhay atthay Iyay eltfay ethay alpitationpay ofyay everyyay arteryyay; atyay othersyay, Iyay earlynay
anksay otay ethay oundgray oughthray anguorlay andyay extremeyay eaknessway. Ingledmay ithway
isthay orrorhay, Iyay eltfay ethay itternessbay ofyay isappointmentday; eamsdray atthay adhay
eenbay ymay oodfay andyay easantplay estray orfay osay onglay ayay acespay ereway ownay ecomebay ayay
ellhay otay emay; andyay ethay angechay asway osay apidray, ethay overthrowyay osay ompletecay!

Orningmay, ismalday andyay etway, atyay engthlay awnedday andyay iscoveredday otay ymay
eeplessslay andyay achingyay eyesyay ethay urchchay ofyay Ingolstadtyay, itsyay itewhay eeplestay
andyay ockclay, ichwhay indicatedyay ethay ixthsay ourhay. Ethay orterpay openedyay ethay atesgay
ofyay ethay ourtcay, ichwhay adhay atthay ightnay eenbay ymay asylumyay, andyay Iyay issuedyay intoyay
ethay eetsstray, acingpay emthay ithway uickqay epsstay, asyay ifyay Iyay oughtsay otay avoidyay ethay
etchwray omwhay Iyay earedfay everyyay urningtay ofyay ethay eetstray ouldway esentpray otay ymay
iewvay. Iyay idday otnay areday eturnray otay ethay apartmentyay ichwhay Iyay inhabitedyay, utbay
eltfay impelledyay otay urryhay onyay, althoughyay encheddray ybay ethay ainray ichwhay ouredpay
omfray ayay ackblay andyay omfortlesscay yskay.

Iyay ontinuedcay alkingway inyay isthay annermay orfay omesay imetay, endeavouringyay ybay
odilybay exerciseyay otay easeyay ethay oadlay atthay eighedway uponyay ymay indmay. Iyay
aversedtray ethay eetsstray ithoutway anyyay earclay onceptioncay ofyay erewhay Iyay asway oryay
atwhay Iyay asway oingday. Ymay earthay alpitatedpay inyay ethay icknesssay ofyay earfay, andyay Iyay
urriedhay onyay ithway irregularyay epsstay, otnay aringday otay ooklay aboutyay emay:
 
 Ikelay oneyay owhay, onyay ayay onelylay oadray,
 Othday alkway inyay earfay andyay eaddray,
 Andyay, avinghay onceyay urnedtay oundray, alksway onyay,
 Andyay urnstay onay oremay ishay eadhay;
 Ecausebay ehay owsknay ayay ightfulfray iendfay
 Othday oseclay ehindbay imhay eadtray.
 
 oleridge’s[cay ancient“ay Arinermay.”]



Ontinuingcay usthay, Iyay amecay atyay engthlay oppositeyay otay ethay innyay atyay ichwhay ethay ariousvay
iligencesday andyay arriagescay usuallyyay oppedstay. Erehay Iyay ausedpay, Iyay ewknay otnay ywhay;
utbay Iyay emainedray omesay inutesmay ithway ymay eyesyay ixedfay onyay ayay oachcay atthay asway omingcay
owardstay emay omfray ethay otheryay endyay ofyay ethay eetstray. Asyay ityay ewdray earernay Iyay observedyay
atthay ityay asway ethay Isssway iligenceday; ityay oppedstay ustjay erewhay Iyay asway andingstay, andyay
onyay ethay oorday eingbay openedyay, Iyay erceivedpay Enryhay Ervalclay, owhay, onyay eeingsay emay,
instantlyyay ungspray outyay. y“may earday Ankensteinfray,” exclaimedyay ehay,
ow“hay adglay Iyay amyay otay eesay youyay! Owhay ortunatefay atthay youyay ouldshay ebay erehay atyay
ethay eryvay omentmay ofyay ymay alightingyay!”

Othingnay ouldcay equalyay ymay elightday onyay eeingsay Ervalclay; ishay esencepray oughtbray ackbay
otay ymay oughtsthay ymay atherfay, Elizabethyay, andyay allyay osethay enesscay ofyay omehay osay earday
otay ymay ecollectionray. Iyay aspedgray ishay andhay, andyay inyay ayay omentmay orgotfay ymay orrorhay
andyay isfortunemay; Iyay eltfay uddenlysay, andyay orfay ethay irstfay imetay uringday anymay onthsmay,
almcay andyay erenesay oyjay. Iyay elcomedway ymay iendfray, ereforethay, inyay ethay ostmay ordialcay
annermay, andyay eway alkedway owardstay ymay ollegecay. Ervalclay ontinuedcay alkingtay orfay
omesay imetay aboutyay ouryay utualmay iendsfray andyay ishay ownyay oodgay ortunefay inyay eingbay
ermittedpay otay omecay otay Ingolstadtyay. you“ay aymay easilyyay elievebay,” aidsay
ehay, ow“hay eatgray asway ethay ifficultyday otay ersuadepay ymay atherfay atthay allyay
ecessarynay owledgeknay asway otnay omprisedcay inyay ethay oblenay artyay ofyay ook-keepingbay;
andyay, indeedyay, Iyay elievebay Iyay eftlay imhay incredulousyay otay ethay astlay, orfay ishay onstantcay
answeryay otay ymay unweariedyay entreatiesyay asway ethay amesay asyay atthay ofyay ethay Utchday
oolmasterschay inyay Ethay Icarvay ofyay Akefieldway: i‘ay avehay entay ousandthay orinsflay
ayay yearyay ithoutway Eekgray, Iyay eatyay eartilyhay ithoutway Eekgray.’ Utbay ishay
affectionyay orfay emay atyay engthlay overcameyay ishay islikeday ofyay earninglay, andyay ehay ashay
ermittedpay emay otay undertakeyay ayay oyagevay ofyay iscoveryday otay ethay andlay ofyay
owledgeknay.”

it“ay ivesgay emay ethay eatestgray elightday otay eesay youyay; utbay elltay emay owhay youyay eftlay
ymay atherfay, othersbray, andyay Elizabethyay.”

ery“vay ellway, andyay eryvay appyhay, onlyyay ayay ittlelay uneasyyay atthay eythay earhay omfray
youyay osay eldomsay. Ybay ethay ybay, Iyay eanmay otay ecturelay youyay ayay ittlelay uponyay eirthay
accountyay yselfmay. Utbay, ymay earday Ankensteinfray,” ontinuedcay ehay, oppingstay
ortshay andyay azinggay ullfay inyay ymay acefay, i“ay idday otnay eforebay emarkray owhay eryvay illyay
youyay appearyay; osay inthay andyay alepay; youyay ooklay asyay ifyay youyay adhay eenbay atchingway orfay
everalsay ightsnay.”

you“ay avehay uessedgay ightray; Iyay avehay atelylay eenbay osay eeplyday engagedyay inyay oneyay
occupationyay atthay Iyay avehay otnay allowedyay yselfmay ufficientsay estray, asyay youyay eesay;
utbay Iyay opehay, Iyay incerelysay opehay, atthay allyay esethay employmentsyay areyay ownay atyay anyay
endyay andyay atthay Iyay amyay atyay engthlay eefray.”

Iyay embledtray excessivelyyay; Iyay ouldcay otnay endureyay otay inkthay ofyay, andyay arfay esslay otay
alludeyay otay, ethay occurrencesyay ofyay ethay ecedingpray ightnay. Iyay alkedway ithway ayay
uickqay acepay, andyay eway oonsay arrivedyay atyay ymay ollegecay. Iyay enthay eflectedray, andyay
ethay oughtthay ademay emay ivershay, atthay ethay eaturecray omwhay Iyay adhay eftlay inyay ymay
apartmentyay ightmay illstay ebay erethay, aliveyay andyay alkingway aboutyay. Iyay eadeddray otay
eholdbay isthay onstermay, utbay Iyay earedfay illstay oremay atthay Enryhay ouldshay eesay imhay.
Entreatingyay imhay, ereforethay, otay emainray ayay ewfay inutesmay atyay ethay ottombay ofyay ethay
airsstay, Iyay artedday upyay owardstay ymay ownyay oomray. Ymay andhay asway alreadyyay onyay ethay
ocklay ofyay ethay oorday eforebay Iyay ecollectedray yselfmay. Iyay enthay ausedpay, andyay ayay
oldcay iveringshay amecay overyay emay. Iyay ewthray ethay oorday orciblyfay openyay, asyay
ildrenchay areyay accustomedyay otay oday enwhay eythay expectyay ayay ectrespay otay andstay inyay
aitingway orfay emthay onyay ethay otheryay idesay; utbay othingnay appearedyay. Iyay eppedstay
earfullyfay inyay: ethay apartmentyay asway emptyyay, andyay ymay edroombay asway alsoyay eedfray
omfray itsyay ideoushay uestgay. Iyay ouldcay ardlyhay elievebay atthay osay eatgray ayay oodgay
ortunefay ouldcay avehay efallenbay emay, utbay enwhay Iyay ecamebay assuredyay atthay ymay enemyyay
adhay indeedyay edflay, Iyay appedclay ymay andshay orfay oyjay andyay anray ownday otay Ervalclay.

Eway ascendedyay intoyay ymay oomray, andyay ethay ervantsay esentlypray oughtbray eakfastbray;
utbay Iyay asway unableyay otay ontaincay yselfmay. Ityay asway otnay oyjay onlyyay atthay ossessedpay
emay; Iyay eltfay ymay eshflay ingletay ithway excessyay ofyay ensitivenesssay, andyay ymay ulsepay
eatbay apidlyray. Iyay asway unableyay otay emainray orfay ayay inglesay instantyay inyay ethay amesay
aceplay; Iyay umpedjay overyay ethay airschay, appedclay ymay andshay, andyay aughedlay aloudyay.
Ervalclay atyay irstfay attributedyay ymay unusualyay iritsspay otay oyjay onyay ishay arrivalyay,
utbay enwhay ehay observedyay emay oremay attentivelyyay, ehay awsay ayay ildnessway inyay ymay eyesyay
orfay ichwhay ehay ouldcay otnay accountyay, andyay ymay oudlay, unrestrainedyay, eartlesshay
aughterlay ightenedfray andyay astonishedyay imhay.

y“may earday Ictorvay,” iedcray ehay, at“whay, orfay Od’sgay akesay,
isyay ethay attermay? Oday otnay aughlay inyay atthay annermay. Owhay illyay youyay areyay! Atwhay isyay ethay
ausecay ofyay allyay isthay?”

o“day otnay askyay emay,” iedcray Iyay, uttingpay ymay andshay eforebay ymay eyesyay, orfay Iyay
oughtthay Iyay awsay ethay eadeddray ectrespay ideglay intoyay ethay oomray; e“_hay_ ancay
elltay. Ohyay, avesay emay! Avesay emay!” Iyay imaginedyay atthay ethay onstermay eizedsay emay;
Iyay uggledstray uriouslyfay andyay ellfay ownday inyay ayay itfay.

Oorpay Ervalclay! Atwhay ustmay avehay eenbay ishay eelingsfay? Ayay eetingmay, ichwhay ehay
anticipatedyay ithway uchsay oyjay, osay angelystray urnedtay otay itternessbay. Utbay Iyay
asway otnay ethay itnessway ofyay ishay iefgray, orfay Iyay asway ifelesslay andyay idday otnay
ecoverray ymay ensessay orfay ayay onglay, onglay imetay.

Isthay asway ethay ommencementcay ofyay ayay ervousnay everfay ichwhay onfinedcay emay orfay
everalsay onthsmay. Uringday allyay atthay imetay Enryhay asway ymay onlyyay ursenay. Iyay
afterwardsyay earnedlay atthay, owingknay ymay ather’sfay advancedyay ageyay andyay unfitnessyay
orfay osay onglay ayay ourneyjay, andyay owhay etchedwray ymay icknesssay ouldway akemay
Elizabethyay, ehay aredspay emthay isthay iefgray ybay oncealingcay ethay extentyay ofyay ymay
isorderday. Ehay ewknay atthay Iyay ouldcay otnay avehay ayay oremay indkay andyay attentiveyay
ursenay anthay imselfhay; andyay, irmfay inyay ethay opehay ehay eltfay ofyay ymay ecoveryray, ehay
idday otnay oubtday atthay, insteadyay ofyay oingday armhay, ehay erformedpay ethay indestkay
actionyay atthay ehay ouldcay owardstay emthay.

Utbay Iyay asway inyay ealityray eryvay illyay, andyay urelysay othingnay utbay ethay unboundedyay andyay
unremittingyay attentionsyay ofyay ymay iendfray ouldcay avehay estoredray emay otay ifelay.
Ethay ormfay ofyay ethay onstermay onyay omwhay Iyay adhay estowedbay existenceyay asway orfay everyay
eforebay ymay eyesyay, andyay Iyay avedray incessantlyyay oncerningcay imhay. Oubtlessday ymay
ordsway urprisedsay Enryhay; ehay atyay irstfay elievedbay emthay otay ebay ethay anderingsway
ofyay ymay isturbedday imaginationyay, utbay ethay ertinacitypay ithway ichwhay Iyay
ontinuallycay ecurredray otay ethay amesay ubjectsay ersuadedpay imhay atthay ymay isorderday
indeedyay owedyay itsyay originyay otay omesay uncommonyay andyay erribletay eventyay.

Ybay eryvay owslay egreesday, andyay ithway equentfray elapsesray atthay alarmedyay andyay
ievedgray ymay iendfray, Iyay ecoveredray. Iyay ememberray ethay irstfay imetay Iyay ecamebay
apablecay ofyay observingyay outwardyay objectsyay ithway anyyay indkay ofyay easureplay, Iyay
erceivedpay atthay ethay allenfay eaveslay adhay isappearedday andyay atthay ethay youngyay
udsbay ereway ootingshay orthfay omfray ethay eestray atthay adedshay ymay indowway. Ityay asway
ayay ivineday ingspray, andyay ethay easonsay ontributedcay eatlygray otay ymay
onvalescencecay. Iyay eltfay alsoyay entimentssay ofyay oyjay andyay affectionyay eviveray inyay
ymay osombay; ymay oomglay isappearedday, andyay inyay ayay ortshay imetay Iyay ecamebay asyay
eerfulchay asyay eforebay Iyay asway attackedyay ybay ethay atalfay assionpay.

earest“day Ervalclay,” exclaimedyay Iyay, ow“hay indkay, owhay eryvay oodgay
youyay areyay otay emay. Isthay olewhay interway, insteadyay ofyay eingbay entspay inyay udystay, asyay youyay
omisedpray yourselfyay, ashay eenbay onsumedcay inyay ymay icksay oomray. Owhay allshay Iyay everyay
epayray youyay? Iyay eelfay ethay eatestgray emorseray orfay ethay isappointmentday ofyay ichwhay Iyay
avehay eenbay ethay occasionyay, utbay youyay illway orgivefay emay.”

you“ay illway epayray emay entirelyyay ifyay youyay oday otnay iscomposeday yourselfyay, utbay etgay
ellway asyay astfay asyay youyay ancay; andyay incesay youyay appearyay inyay uchsay oodgay iritsspay, Iyay
aymay eakspay otay youyay onyay oneyay ubjectsay, aymay Iyay otnay?”

Iyay embledtray. Oneyay ubjectsay! Atwhay ouldcay ityay ebay? Ouldcay ehay alludeyay otay anyay objectyay onyay
omwhay Iyay aredday otnay evenyay inkthay?

ompose“cay yourselfyay,” aidsay Ervalclay, owhay observedyay ymay angechay ofyay
olourcay, i“ay illway otnay entionmay ityay ifyay ityay agitatesyay youyay; utbay youryay atherfay
andyay ousincay ouldway ebay eryvay appyhay ifyay eythay eceivedray ayay etterlay omfray youyay inyay youryay
ownyay andwritinghay. Eythay ardlyhay owknay owhay illyay youyay avehay eenbay andyay areyay uneasyyay atyay
youryay onglay ilencesay.”

is“ay atthay allyay, ymay earday Enryhay? Owhay ouldcay youyay upposesay atthay ymay irstfay
oughtthay ouldway otnay yflay owardstay osethay earday, earday iendsfray omwhay Iyay ovelay andyay
owhay areyay osay eservingday ofyay ymay ovelay?”

if“ay isthay isyay youryay esentpray empertay, ymay iendfray, youyay illway erhapspay ebay adglay
otay eesay ayay etterlay atthay ashay eenbay yinglay erehay omesay aysday orfay youyay; ityay isyay omfray
youryay ousincay, Iyay elievebay.”




Apterchay 6


Ervalclay enthay utpay ethay ollowingfay etterlay intoyay ymay andshay. Ityay asway omfray ymay
ownyay Elizabethyay:

y“may earestday Ousincay,

you“ay avehay eenbay illyay, eryvay illyay, andyay evenyay ethay onstantcay etterslay ofyay earday
indkay Enryhay areyay otnay ufficientsay otay eassureray emay onyay youryay accountyay. Youyay areyay
orbiddenfay otay ite—towray oldhay ayay enpay; yetyay oneyay ordway omfray youyay, earday Ictorvay,
isyay ecessarynay otay almcay ouryay apprehensionsyay. Orfay ayay onglay imetay Iyay avehay oughtthay
atthay eachyay ostpay ouldway ingbray isthay inelay, andyay ymay ersuasionspay avehay
estrainedray ymay uncleyay omfray undertakingyay ayay ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtyay. Iyay avehay
eventedpray ishay encounteringyay ethay inconveniencesyay andyay erhapspay angersday ofyay osay
onglay ayay ourneyjay, yetyay owhay oftenyay avehay Iyay egrettedray otnay eingbay ableyay otay
erformpay ityay yselfmay! Iyay igurefay otay yselfmay atthay ethay asktay ofyay attendingyay onyay
youryay ickbedsay ashay evolvedday onyay omesay ercenarymay oldyay ursenay, owhay ouldcay evernay
uessgay youryay ishesway ornay inistermay otay emthay ithway ethay arecay andyay affectionyay ofyay
youryay oorpay ousincay. Yetyay atthay isyay overyay ownay: Ervalclay iteswray atthay indeedyay
youyay areyay ettinggay etterbay. Iyay eagerlyyay opehay atthay youyay illway onfirmcay isthay
intelligenceyay oonsay inyay youryay ownyay andwritinghay.

et“gay ell—andway eturnray otay usyay. Youyay illway indfay ayay appyhay, eerfulchay omehay andyay
iendsfray owhay ovelay youyay earlyday. Youryay ather’sfay ealthhay isyay igorousvay, andyay ehay
asksyay utbay otay eesay youyay, utbay otay ebay assuredyay atthay youyay areyay ellway; andyay otnay ayay
arecay illway everyay oudclay ishay enevolentbay ountenancecay. Owhay easedplay youyay ouldway
ebay otay emarkray ethay improvementyay ofyay ouryay Ernestyay! Ehay isyay ownay ixteensay andyay ullfay
ofyay activityyay andyay iritspay. Ehay isyay esirousday otay ebay ayay uetray Isssway andyay otay enteryay
intoyay oreignfay ervicesay, utbay eway annotcay artpay ithway imhay, atyay eastlay untilyay ishay
elderyay otherbray eturnsray otay usyay. Ymay uncleyay isyay otnay easedplay ithway ethay ideayay ofyay
ayay ilitarymay areercay inyay ayay istantday ountrycay, utbay Ernestyay evernay adhay youryay
owerspay ofyay applicationyay. Ehay ookslay uponyay udystay asyay anyay odiousyay etterfay; ishay
imetay isyay entspay inyay ethay openyay airyay, imbingclay ethay illshay oryay owingray onyay ethay
akelay. Iyay earfay atthay ehay illway ecomebay anyay idleryay unlessyay eway yieldyay ethay ointpay
andyay ermitpay imhay otay enteryay onyay ethay ofessionpray ichwhay ehay ashay electedsay.

ittle“lay alterationyay, exceptyay ethay owthgray ofyay ouryay earday ildrenchay, ashay akentay
aceplay incesay youyay eftlay usyay. Ethay ueblay akelay andyay ow-cladsnay ountains—theymay
evernay angechay; andyay Iyay inkthay ouryay acidplay omehay andyay ouryay ontentedcay eartshay areyay
egulatedray ybay ethay amesay immutableyay awslay. Ymay iflingtray occupationsyay aketay upyay
ymay imetay andyay amuseyay emay, andyay Iyay amyay ewardedray orfay anyyay exertionsyay ybay eeingsay
onenay utbay appyhay, indkay acesfay aroundyay emay. Incesay youyay eftlay usyay, utbay oneyay
angechay ashay akentay aceplay inyay ouryay ittlelay ouseholdhay. Oday youyay ememberray onyay
atwhay occasionyay Ustinejay Oritzmay enteredyay ouryay amilyfay? Obablypray youyay oday otnay;
Iyay illway elateray erhay istoryhay, ereforethay inyay ayay ewfay ordsway. Adamemay Oritzmay,
erhay othermay, asway ayay idowway ithway ourfay ildrenchay, ofyay omwhay Ustinejay asway ethay
irdthay. Isthay irlgay adhay alwaysyay eenbay ethay avouritefay ofyay erhay atherfay, utbay
oughthray ayay angestray erversitypay, erhay othermay ouldcay otnay endureyay erhay, andyay
afteryay ethay eathday ofyay May. Oritzmay, eatedtray erhay eryvay illyay. Ymay auntyay observedyay
isthay, andyay enwhay Ustinejay asway elvetway yearsyay ofyay ageyay, evailedpray onyay erhay othermay
otay allowyay erhay otay ivelay atyay ouryay ousehay. Ethay epublicanray institutionsyay ofyay ouryay
ountrycay avehay oducedpray implersay andyay appierhay annersmay anthay osethay ichwhay
evailpray inyay ethay eatgray onarchiesmay atthay urroundsay ityay. Encehay erethay isyay esslay
istinctionday etweenbay ethay everalsay assesclay ofyay itsyay inhabitantsyay; andyay ethay
owerlay ordersyay, eingbay eithernay osay oorpay ornay osay espisedday, eirthay annersmay areyay
oremay efinedray andyay oralmay. Ayay ervantsay inyay Enevagay oesday otnay eanmay ethay amesay
ingthay asyay ayay ervantsay inyay Ancefray andyay Englandyay. Ustinejay, usthay eceivedray inyay
ouryay amilyfay, earnedlay ethay utiesday ofyay ayay ervantsay, ayay onditioncay ichwhay, inyay ouryay
ortunatefay ountrycay, oesday otnay includeyay ethay ideayay ofyay ignoranceyay andyay ayay
acrificesay ofyay ethay ignityday ofyay ayay umanhay eingbay.

ustine“jay, youyay aymay ememberray, asway ayay eatgray avouritefay ofyay yoursyay; andyay Iyay
ecollectray youyay onceyay emarkedray atthay ifyay youyay ereway inyay anyay illyay umourhay, oneyay
anceglay omfray Ustinejay ouldcay issipateday ityay, orfay ethay amesay easonray atthay
Ariostoyay ivesgay oncerningcay ethay eautybay ofyay Angelica—sheyay ookedlay osay
ank-heartedfray andyay appyhay. Ymay auntyay onceivedcay ayay eatgray attachmentyay orfay erhay,
ybay ichwhay eshay asway inducedyay otay ivegay erhay anyay educationyay uperiorsay otay atthay
ichwhay eshay adhay atyay irstfay intendedyay. Isthay enefitbay asway ullyfay epaidray;
Ustinejay asway ethay ostmay atefulgray ittlelay eaturecray inyay ethay orldway: Iyay oday otnay
eanmay atthay eshay ademay anyyay ofessionspray Iyay evernay eardhay oneyay asspay erhay ipslay, utbay
youyay ouldcay eesay ybay erhay eyesyay atthay eshay almostyay adoredyay erhay otectresspray.
Althoughyay erhay ispositionday asway aygay andyay inyay anymay espectsray inconsiderateyay,
yetyay eshay aidpay ethay eatestgray attentionyay otay everyyay esturegay ofyay ymay auntyay. Eshay
oughtthay erhay ethay odelmay ofyay allyay excellenceyay andyay endeavouredyay otay imitateyay erhay
aseologyphray andyay annersmay, osay atthay evenyay ownay eshay oftenyay emindsray emay ofyay erhay.

en“whay ymay earestday auntyay iedday everyyay oneyay asway ootay uchmay occupiedyay inyay eirthay ownyay
iefgray otay oticenay oorpay Ustinejay, owhay adhay attendedyay erhay uringday erhay illnessyay
ithway ethay ostmay anxiousyay affectionyay. Oorpay Ustinejay asway eryvay illyay; utbay otheryay
ialstray ereway eservedray orfay erhay.

one“ay ybay oneyay, erhay othersbray andyay istersay iedday; andyay erhay othermay, ithway ethay
exceptionyay ofyay erhay eglectednay aughterday, asway eftlay ildlesschay. Ethay
onsciencecay ofyay ethay omanway asway oubledtray; eshay eganbay otay inkthay atthay ethay
eathsday ofyay erhay avouritesfay asway ayay udgementjay omfray eavenhay otay astisechay erhay
artialitypay. Eshay asway ayay Omanray Atholiccay; andyay Iyay elievebay erhay onfessorcay
onfirmedcay ethay ideayay ichwhay eshay adhay onceivedcay. Accordinglyyay, ayay ewfay onthsmay
afteryay youryay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtyay, Ustinejay asway alledcay omehay ybay erhay
epentantray othermay. Oorpay irlgay! Eshay eptway enwhay eshay uittedqay ouryay ousehay; eshay
asway uchmay alteredyay incesay ethay eathday ofyay ymay auntyay; iefgray adhay ivengay oftnesssay
andyay ayay inningway ildnessmay otay erhay annersmay, ichwhay adhay eforebay eenbay emarkableray
orfay ivacityvay. Ornay asway erhay esidenceray atyay erhay other’smay ousehay ofyay ayay aturenay
otay estoreray erhay aietygay. Ethay oorpay omanway asway eryvay acillatingvay inyay erhay
epentanceray. Eshay ometimessay eggedbay Ustinejay otay orgivefay erhay unkindnessyay,
utbay uchmay ofteneryay accusedyay erhay ofyay avinghay ausedcay ethay eathsday ofyay erhay
othersbray andyay istersay. Erpetualpay ettingfray atyay engthlay ewthray Adamemay Oritzmay
intoyay ayay eclineday, ichwhay atyay irstfay increasedyay erhay irritabilityyay, utbay eshay isyay
ownay atyay eacepay orfay everyay. Eshay iedday onyay ethay irstfay approachyay ofyay oldcay eatherway,
atyay ethay eginningbay ofyay isthay astlay interway. Ustinejay ashay ustjay eturnedray otay usyay;
andyay Iyay assureyay youyay Iyay ovelay erhay enderlytay. Eshay isyay eryvay everclay andyay entlegay,
andyay extremelyyay ettypray; asyay Iyay entionedmay eforebay, erhay ienmay andyay erhay
expressionyay ontinuallycay emindray emay ofyay ymay earday auntyay.

i“ay ustmay aysay alsoyay ayay ewfay ordsway otay youyay, ymay earday ousincay, ofyay ittlelay arlingday
Illiamway. Iyay ishway youyay ouldcay eesay imhay; ehay isyay eryvay alltay ofyay ishay ageyay, ithway
eetsway aughinglay ueblay eyesyay, arkday eyelashesyay, andyay urlingcay airhay. Enwhay ehay
ilessmay, otway ittlelay implesday appearyay onyay eachyay eekchay, ichwhay areyay osyray ithway
ealthhay. Ehay ashay alreadyyay adhay oneyay oryay otway ittlelay ives_way,_ utbay Ouisalay Ironbay
isyay ishay avouritefay, ayay ettypray ittlelay irlgay ofyay ivefay yearsyay ofyay ageyay.

ow“nay, earday Ictorvay, Iyay areday aysay youyay ishway otay ebay indulgedyay inyay ayay ittlelay
ossipgay oncerningcay ethay oodgay eoplepay ofyay Enevagay. Ethay ettypray Issmay Ansfieldmay
ashay alreadyyay eceivedray ethay ongratulatorycay isitsvay onyay erhay approachingyay
arriagemay ithway ayay youngyay Englishmanyay, Ohnjay Elbournemay, Esqyay. Erhay uglyyay
istersay, Anonmay, arriedmay May. Uvillardday, ethay ichray ankerbay, astlay autumnyay. Youryay
avouritefay oolfellowschay, Ouislay Anoirmay, ashay ufferedsay everalsay isfortunesmay
incesay ethay epartureday ofyay Ervalclay omfray Enevagay. Utbay ehay ashay alreadyyay
ecoveredray ishay iritsspay, andyay isyay eportedray otay ebay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay arryingmay ayay
ivelylay ettypray Enchwomanfray, Adamemay Averniertay. Eshay isyay ayay idowway, andyay uchmay
olderyay anthay Anoirmay; utbay eshay isyay eryvay uchmay admiredyay, andyay ayay avouritefay ithway
everybodyyay.

i“ay avehay ittenwray yselfmay intoyay etterbay iritsspay, earday ousincay; utbay ymay anxietyyay
eturnsray uponyay emay asyay Iyay oncludecay. Itewray, earestday Ictor,—onevay ine—onelay
ordway illway ebay ayay essingblay otay usyay. Entay ousandthay anksthay otay Enryhay orfay ishay
indnesskay, ishay affectionyay, andyay ishay anymay etterslay; eway areyay incerelysay
atefulgray. Adieuyay! ymay ousincay; aketay arecay ofyay yourselfyay; andyay, Iyay entreatyay
youyay, itewray!

elizabeth“ay Avenzalay.


eneva“gay, Archmay 18th, 17—.”



ear“day, earday Elizabethyay!” Iyay exclaimedyay, enwhay Iyay adhay eadray erhay
etterlay: i“ay illway itewray instantlyyay andyay elieveray emthay omfray ethay anxietyyay
eythay ustmay eelfay.” Iyay otewray, andyay isthay exertionyay eatlygray atiguedfay emay; utbay
ymay onvalescencecay adhay ommencedcay, andyay oceededpray egularlyray. Inyay anotheryay
ortnightfay Iyay asway ableyay otay eavelay ymay amberchay.

Oneyay ofyay ymay irstfay utiesday onyay ymay ecoveryray asway otay introduceyay Ervalclay otay ethay
everalsay ofessorspray ofyay ethay universityyay. Inyay oingday isthay, Iyay underwentyay ayay
indkay ofyay oughray usageyay, illyay efittingbay ethay oundsway atthay ymay indmay adhay
ustainedsay. Everyay incesay ethay atalfay ightnay, ethay endyay ofyay ymay abourslay, andyay ethay
eginningbay ofyay ymay isfortunesmay, Iyay adhay onceivedcay ayay iolentvay antipathyyay evenyay
otay ethay amenay ofyay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Enwhay Iyay asway otherwiseyay uiteqay estoredray
otay ealthhay, ethay ightsay ofyay ayay emicalchay instrumentyay ouldway enewray allyay ethay agonyyay
ofyay ymay ervousnay ymptomssay. Enryhay awsay isthay, andyay adhay emovedray allyay ymay
apparatusyay omfray ymay iewvay. Ehay adhay alsoyay angedchay ymay apartmentyay; orfay ehay
erceivedpay atthay Iyay adhay acquiredyay ayay islikeday orfay ethay oomray ichwhay adhay
eviouslypray eenbay ymay aboratorylay. Utbay esethay arescay ofyay Ervalclay ereway ademay ofyay
onay availyay enwhay Iyay isitedvay ethay ofessorspray. May. Aldmanway inflictedyay orturetay
enwhay ehay aisedpray, ithway indnesskay andyay armthway, ethay astonishingyay ogresspray Iyay
adhay ademay inyay ethay iencesscay. Ehay oonsay erceivedpay atthay Iyay islikedday ethay
ubjectsay; utbay otnay uessinggay ethay ealray ausecay, ehay attributedyay ymay eelingsfay otay
odestymay, andyay angedchay ethay ubjectsay omfray ymay improvementyay, otay ethay iencescay
itselfyay, ithway ayay esireday, asyay Iyay evidentlyyay awsay, ofyay awingdray emay outyay. Atwhay
ouldcay Iyay oday? Ehay eantmay otay easeplay, andyay ehay ormentedtay emay. Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay ehay
adhay acedplay arefullycay, oneyay ybay oneyay, inyay ymay iewvay osethay instrumentsyay ichwhay
ereway otay ebay afterwardsyay usedyay inyay uttingpay emay otay ayay owslay andyay uelcray eathday. Iyay
ithedwray underyay ishay ordsway, yetyay aredday otnay exhibityay ethay ainpay Iyay eltfay.
Ervalclay, osewhay eyesyay andyay eelingsfay ereway alwaysyay uickqay inyay iscerningday ethay
ensationssay ofyay othersyay, eclinedday ethay ubjectsay, allegingyay, inyay excuseyay, ishay
otaltay ignoranceyay; andyay ethay onversationcay ooktay ayay oremay eneralgay urntay. Iyay
ankedthay ymay iendfray omfray ymay earthay, utbay Iyay idday otnay eakspay. Iyay awsay ainlyplay
atthay ehay asway urprisedsay, utbay ehay evernay attemptedyay otay awdray ymay ecretsay omfray
emay; andyay althoughyay Iyay ovedlay imhay ithway ayay ixturemay ofyay affectionyay andyay everenceray
atthay ewknay onay oundsbay, yetyay Iyay ouldcay evernay ersuadepay yselfmay otay onfidecay inyay
imhay atthay eventyay ichwhay asway osay oftenyay esentpray otay ymay ecollectionray, utbay ichwhay
Iyay earedfay ethay etailday otay anotheryay ouldway onlyyay impressyay oremay eeplyday.

May. Empekray asway otnay equallyyay ocileday; andyay inyay ymay onditioncay atyay atthay imetay, ofyay
almostyay insupportableyay ensitivenesssay, ishay arshhay untblay encomiumsyay avegay emay evenyay
oremay ainpay anthay ethay enevolentbay approbationyay ofyay May. Aldmanway. “d—nay
ethay ellowfay!” iedcray ehay; y“whay, May. Ervalclay, Iyay assureyay youyay ehay ashay
outstriptyay usyay allyay. Ayyay, arestay ifyay youyay easeplay; utbay ityay isyay everthelessnay uetray. Ayay
youngsteryay owhay, utbay ayay ewfay yearsyay agoyay, elievedbay inyay Orneliuscay Agrippayay asyay irmlyfay
asyay inyay ethay ospelgay, ashay ownay etsay imselfhay atyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay universityyay; andyay ifyay
ehay isyay otnay oonsay ulledpay ownday, eway allshay allyay ebay outyay ofyay ountenance.—aycay,
ayyay,” ontinuedcay ehay, observingyay ymay acefay expressiveyay ofyay ufferingsay,
“may. Ankensteinfray isyay odestmay; anyay excellentyay ualityqay inyay ayay youngyay anmay.
Youngyay enmay ouldshay ebay iffidentday ofyay emselvesthay, youyay owknay, May. Ervalclay: Iyay asway
yselfmay enwhay youngyay; utbay atthay earsway outyay inyay ayay eryvay ortshay imetay.”

May. Empekray adhay ownay ommencedcay anyay eulogyyay onyay imselfhay, ichwhay appilyhay urnedtay
ethay onversationcay omfray ayay ubjectsay atthay asway osay annoyingyay otay emay.

Ervalclay adhay evernay ympathisedsay inyay ymay astestay orfay aturalnay iencescay; andyay ishay
iterarylay ursuitspay ifferedday ollywhay omfray osethay ichwhay adhay occupiedyay emay. Ehay
amecay otay ethay universityyay ithway ethay esignday ofyay akingmay imselfhay ompletecay
astermay ofyay ethay orientalyay anguageslay, andyay usthay ehay ouldshay openyay ayay ieldfay orfay
ethay anplay ofyay ifelay ehay adhay arkedmay outyay orfay imselfhay. Esolvedray otay ursuepay onay
ingloriousyay areercay, ehay urnedtay ishay eyesyay owardtay ethay Eastyay, asyay affordingyay
opescay orfay ishay iritspay ofyay enterpriseyay. Ethay Ersianpay, Arabicyay, andyay Anskritsay
anguageslay engagedyay ishay attentionyay, andyay Iyay asway easilyyay inducedyay otay enteryay onyay
ethay amesay udiesstay. Idlenessyay adhay everyay eenbay irksomeyay otay emay, andyay ownay atthay Iyay
ishedway otay yflay omfray eflectionray, andyay atedhay ymay ormerfay udiesstay, Iyay eltfay
eatgray eliefray inyay eingbay ethay ellow-pupilfay ithway ymay iendfray, andyay oundfay otnay
onlyyay instructionyay utbay onsolationcay inyay ethay orksway ofyay ethay orientalistsyay. Iyay
idday otnay, ikelay imhay, attemptyay ayay iticalcray owledgeknay ofyay eirthay ialectsday, orfay
Iyay idday otnay ontemplatecay akingmay anyyay otheryay useyay ofyay emthay anthay emporarytay
amusementyay. Iyay eadray erelymay otay understandyay eirthay eaningmay, andyay eythay ellway
epaidray ymay abourslay. Eirthay elancholymay isyay oothingsay, andyay eirthay oyjay
elevatingyay, otay ayay egreeday Iyay evernay experiencedyay inyay udyingstay ethay authorsyay ofyay
anyyay otheryay ountrycay. Enwhay youyay eadray eirthay itingswray, ifelay appearsyay otay
onsistcay inyay ayay armway unsay andyay ayay ardengay ofyay oses,—inray ethay ilessmay andyay ownsfray
ofyay ayay airfay enemyyay, andyay ethay irefay atthay onsumescay youryay ownyay earthay. Owhay
ifferentday omfray ethay anlymay andyay eroicalhay oetrypay ofyay Eecegray andyay Omeray!

Ummersay assedpay awayyay inyay esethay occupationsyay, andyay ymay eturnray otay Enevagay asway
ixedfay orfay ethay atterlay endyay ofyay autumnyay; utbay eingbay elayedday ybay everalsay
accidentsyay, interway andyay owsnay arrivedyay, ethay oadsray ereway eemedday impassableyay,
andyay ymay ourneyjay asway etardedray untilyay ethay ensuingyay ingspray. Iyay eltfay isthay
elayday eryvay itterlybay; orfay Iyay ongedlay otay eesay ymay ativenay owntay andyay ymay elovedbay
iendsfray. Ymay eturnray adhay onlyyay eenbay elayedday osay onglay, omfray anyay
unwillingnessyay otay eavelay Ervalclay inyay ayay angestray aceplay, eforebay ehay adhay ecomebay
acquaintedyay ithway anyyay ofyay itsyay inhabitantsyay. Ethay interway, oweverhay, asway entspay
eerfullychay; andyay althoughyay ethay ingspray asway uncommonlyyay atelay, enwhay ityay amecay
itsyay eautybay ompensatedcay orfay itsyay ilatorinessday.

Ethay onthmay ofyay Aymay adhay alreadyyay ommencedcay, andyay Iyay expectedyay ethay etterlay ailyday
ichwhay asway otay ixfay ethay ateday ofyay ymay epartureday, enwhay Enryhay oposedpray ayay
edestrianpay ourtay inyay ethay environsyay ofyay Ingolstadtyay, atthay Iyay ightmay idbay ayay
ersonalpay arewellfay otay ethay ountrycay Iyay adhay osay onglay inhabitedyay. Iyay accededyay
ithway easureplay otay isthay opositionpray: Iyay asway ondfay ofyay exerciseyay, andyay Ervalclay
adhay alwaysyay eenbay ymay avouritefay ompanioncay inyay ethay ambleray ofyay isthay aturenay
atthay Iyay adhay akentay amongyay ethay enesscay ofyay ymay ativenay ountrycay.

Eway assedpay ayay ortnightfay inyay esethay erambulationspay: ymay ealthhay andyay iritsspay
adhay onglay eenbay estoredray, andyay eythay ainedgay additionalyay engthstray omfray ethay
alubrioussay airyay Iyay eathedbray, ethay aturalnay incidentsyay ofyay ouryay ogresspray, andyay
ethay onversationcay ofyay ymay iendfray. Udystay adhay eforebay ecludedsay emay omfray ethay
intercourseyay ofyay ymay ellow-creaturesfay, andyay enderedray emay unsocialyay; utbay
Ervalclay alledcay orthfay ethay etterbay eelingsfay ofyay ymay earthay; ehay againyay aughttay
emay otay ovelay ethay aspectyay ofyay aturenay, andyay ethay eerfulchay acesfay ofyay ildrenchay.
Excellentyay iendfray! owhay incerelysay youyay idday ovelay emay, andyay endeavouryay otay
elevateyay ymay indmay untilyay ityay asway onyay ayay evellay ithway youryay ownyay. Ayay elfishsay
ursuitpay adhay ampedcray andyay arrowednay emay, untilyay youryay entlenessgay andyay
affectionyay armedway andyay openedyay ymay ensessay; Iyay ecamebay ethay amesay appyhay eaturecray
owhay, ayay ewfay yearsyay agoyay, ovedlay andyay elovedbay ybay allyay, adhay onay orrowsay oryay arecay.
Enwhay appyhay, inanimateyay aturenay adhay ethay owerpay ofyay estowingbay onyay emay ethay ostmay
elightfulday ensationssay. Ayay erenesay yskay andyay erdantvay ieldsfay illedfay emay ithway
ecstasyyay. Ethay esentpray easonsay asway indeedyay ivineday; ethay owersflay ofyay ingspray
oomedblay inyay ethay edgeshay, ilewhay osethay ofyay ummersay ereway alreadyyay inyay udbay. Iyay
asway undisturbedyay ybay oughtsthay ichwhay uringday ethay ecedingpray yearyay adhay essedpray
uponyay emay, otwithstandingnay ymay endeavoursyay otay owthray emthay offyay, ithway anyay
invincibleyay urdenbay.

Enryhay ejoicedray inyay ymay aietygay, andyay incerelysay ympathisedsay inyay ymay eelingsfay: ehay
exertedyay imselfhay otay amuseyay emay, ilewhay ehay expressedyay ethay ensationssay atthay illedfay
ishay oulsay. Ethay esourcesray ofyay ishay indmay onyay isthay occasionyay ereway ulytray
astonishingyay: ishay onversationcay asway ullfay ofyay imaginationyay; andyay eryvay oftenyay, inyay
imitationyay ofyay ethay Ersianpay andyay Arabicyay iterswray, ehay inventedyay alestay ofyay onderfulway
ancyfay andyay assionpay. Atyay otheryay imestay ehay epeatedray ymay avouritefay oemspay, oryay ewdray
emay outyay intoyay argumentsyay, ichwhay ehay upportedsay ithway eatgray ingenuityyay.

Eway eturnedray otay ouryay ollegecay onyay ayay Undaysay afternoonyay: ethay easantspay ereway
ancingday, andyay everyyay oneyay eway etmay appearedyay aygay andyay appyhay. Ymay ownyay iritsspay ereway
ighhay, andyay Iyay oundedbay alongyay ithway eelingsfay ofyay unbridledyay oyjay andyay ilarityhay.




Apterchay 7


Onyay ymay eturnray, Iyay oundfay ethay ollowingfay etterlay omfray ymay atherfay:—

y“may earday Ictorvay,

you“ay avehay obablypray aitedway impatientlyyay orfay ayay etterlay otay ixfay ethay ateday ofyay
youryay eturnray otay usyay; andyay Iyay asway atyay irstfay emptedtay otay itewray onlyyay ayay ewfay
ineslay, erelymay entioningmay ethay ayday onyay ichwhay Iyay ouldshay expectyay youyay. Utbay
atthay ouldway ebay ayay uelcray indnesskay, andyay Iyay areday otnay oday ityay. Atwhay ouldway ebay
youryay urprisesay, ymay onsay, enwhay youyay expectedyay ayay appyhay andyay adglay elcomeway, otay
eholdbay, onyay ethay ontrarycay, earstay andyay etchednesswray? Andyay owhay, Ictorvay, ancay
Iyay elateray ouryay isfortunemay? Absenceyay annotcay avehay enderedray youyay allouscay otay
ouryay oysjay andyay iefsgray; andyay owhay allshay Iyay inflictyay ainpay onyay ymay onglay absentyay
onsay? Iyay ishway otay eparepray youyay orfay ethay oefulway ewsnay, utbay Iyay owknay ityay isyay
impossibleyay; evenyay ownay youryay eyeyay imsskay overyay ethay agepay otay eeksay ethay ordsway
ichwhay areyay otay onveycay otay youyay ethay orriblehay idingstay.

illiam“way isyay ead!—thatday eetsway ildchay, osewhay ilessmay elightedday andyay armedway
ymay earthay, owhay asway osay entlegay, yetyay osay aygay! Ictorvay, ehay isyay urderedmay!

i“ay illway otnay attemptyay otay onsolecay youyay; utbay illway implysay elateray ethay
ircumstancescay ofyay ethay ansactiontray.

ast“lay Ursdaythay ay(may 7th), Iyay, ymay iecenay, andyay youryay otway othersbray, entway otay
alkway inyay Ainpalaisplay. Ethay eveningyay asway armway andyay erenesay, andyay eway olongedpray
ouryay alkway artherfay anthay usualyay. Ityay asway alreadyyay uskday eforebay eway oughtthay ofyay
eturningray; andyay enthay eway iscoveredday atthay Illiamway andyay Ernestyay, owhay adhay onegay
