onyay eforebay, ereway otnay otay ebay oundfay. Eway accordinglyyay estedray onyay ayay eatsay untilyay
eythay ouldshay eturnray. Esentlypray Ernestyay amecay, andyay enquiredyay ifyay eway adhay eensay
ishay otherbray; ehay aidsay, atthay ehay adhay eenbay ayingplay ithway imhay, atthay Illiamway
adhay unray awayyay otay idehay imselfhay, andyay atthay ehay ainlyvay oughtsay orfay imhay, andyay
afterwardsyay aitedway orfay ayay onglay imetay, utbay atthay ehay idday otnay eturnray.

is“thay accountyay atherray alarmedyay usyay, andyay eway ontinuedcay otay earchsay orfay imhay
untilyay ightnay ellfay, enwhay Elizabethyay onjecturedcay atthay ehay ightmay avehay
eturnedray otay ethay ousehay. Ehay asway otnay erethay. Eway eturnedray againyay, ithway
orchestay; orfay Iyay ouldcay otnay estray, enwhay Iyay oughtthay atthay ymay eetsway oybay adhay
ostlay imselfhay, andyay asway exposedyay otay allyay ethay ampsday andyay ewsday ofyay ightnay;
Elizabethyay alsoyay ufferedsay extremeyay anguishyay. Aboutyay ivefay inyay ethay orningmay Iyay
iscoveredday ymay ovelylay oybay, omwhay ethay ightnay eforebay Iyay adhay eensay oomingblay andyay
activeyay inyay ealthhay, etchedstray onyay ethay assgray ividlay andyay otionlessmay; ethay
intpray ofyay ethay urder’smay ingerfay asway onyay ishay ecknay.

e“hay asway onveyedcay omehay, andyay ethay anguishyay atthay asway isiblevay inyay ymay
ountenancecay etrayedbay ethay ecretsay otay Elizabethyay. Eshay asway eryvay earnestyay otay
eesay ethay orpsecay. Atyay irstfay Iyay attemptedyay otay eventpray erhay utbay eshay ersistedpay,
andyay enteringyay ethay oomray erewhay ityay aylay, astilyhay examinedyay ethay ecknay ofyay ethay
ictimvay, andyay aspingclay erhay andshay exclaimedyay, o‘ay Odgay! Iyay avehay urderedmay ymay
arlingday ildchay!’

e“shay aintedfay, andyay asway estoredray ithway extremeyay ifficultyday. Enwhay eshay againyay
ivedlay, ityay asway onlyyay otay eepway andyay ighsay. Eshay oldtay emay, atthay atthay amesay
eveningyay Illiamway adhay easedtay erhay otay etlay imhay earway ayay eryvay aluablevay
iniaturemay atthay eshay ossessedpay ofyay youryay othermay. Isthay icturepay isyay onegay, andyay
asway oubtlessday ethay emptationtay ichwhay urgedyay ethay urderermay otay ethay eedday. Eway
avehay onay acetray ofyay imhay atyay esentpray, althoughyay ouryay exertionsyay otay iscoverday imhay
areyay unremittedyay; utbay eythay illway otnay estoreray ymay elovedbay Illiamway!

ome“cay, earestday Ictorvay; youyay aloneyay ancay onsolecay Elizabethyay. Eshay eepsway
ontinuallycay, andyay accusesyay erselfhay unjustlyyay asyay ethay ausecay ofyay ishay eathday;
erhay ordsway iercepay ymay earthay. Eway areyay allyay unhappyyay; utbay illway otnay atthay ebay anyay
additionalyay otivemay orfay youyay, ymay onsay, otay eturnray andyay ebay ouryay omfortercay?
Youryay earday othermay! Alasyay, Ictorvay! Iyay ownay aysay, Ankthay Odgay eshay idday otnay ivelay
otay itnessway ethay uelcray, iserablemay eathday ofyay erhay youngestyay arlingday!

ome“cay, Ictorvay; otnay oodingbray oughtsthay ofyay engeancevay againstyay ethay assassinyay,
utbay ithway eelingsfay ofyay eacepay andyay entlenessgay, atthay illway ealhay, insteadyay ofyay
esteringfay, ethay oundsway ofyay ouryay indsmay. Enteryay ethay ousehay ofyay ourningmay, ymay
iendfray, utbay ithway indnesskay andyay affectionyay orfay osethay owhay ovelay youyay, andyay otnay
ithway atredhay orfay youryay enemiesyay.

your“ay affectionateyay andyay afflictedyay atherfay,

alphonse“ay Ankensteinfray.



eneva“gay, Aymay 12th, 17—.”



Ervalclay, owhay adhay atchedway ymay ountenancecay asyay Iyay eadray isthay etterlay, asway
urprisedsay otay observeyay ethay espairday atthay ucceededsay ethay oyjay Iyay atyay irstfay
expressedyay onyay eceivingray ewsnay omfray ymay iendsfray. Iyay ewthray ethay etterlay onyay ethay
abletay, andyay overedcay ymay acefay ithway ymay andshay.

y“may earday Ankensteinfray,” exclaimedyay Enryhay, enwhay ehay erceivedpay emay
eepway ithway itternessbay, are“ay youyay alwaysyay otay ebay unhappyyay? Ymay earday iendfray,
atwhay ashay appenedhay?”

Iyay otionedmay imhay otay aketay upyay ethay etterlay, ilewhay Iyay alkedway upyay andyay ownday ethay
oomray inyay ethay extremestyay agitationyay. Earstay alsoyay ushedgay omfray ethay eyesyay ofyay
Ervalclay, asyay ehay eadray ethay accountyay ofyay ymay isfortunemay.

i“ay ancay offeryay youyay onay onsolationcay, ymay iendfray,” aidsay ehay;
your“ay isasterday isyay irreparableyay. Atwhay oday youyay intendyay otay oday?”

o“tay ogay instantlyyay otay Enevagay: omecay ithway emay, Enryhay, otay orderyay ethay orseshay.”

Uringday ouryay alkway, Ervalclay endeavouredyay otay aysay ayay ewfay ordsway ofyay onsolationcay;
ehay ouldcay onlyyay expressyay ishay eartfelthay ympathysay. oor“pay Illiamway!” aidsay ehay,
ear“day ovelylay ildchay, ehay ownay eepsslay ithway ishay angelyay othermay! Owhay atthay adhay
eensay imhay ightbray andyay oyousjay inyay ishay youngyay eautybay, utbay ustmay eepway overyay ishay
untimelyyay osslay! Otay ieday osay iserablymay; otay eelfay ethay urderer’smay aspgray! Owhay
uchmay oremay ayay urderedmay atthay ouldcay estroyday adiantray innocenceyay! Oorpay ittlelay
ellowfay! oneyay onlyyay onsolationcay avehay eway; ishay iendsfray ournmay andyay eepway, utbay
ehay isyay atyay estray. Ethay angpay isyay overyay, ishay ufferingssay areyay atyay anyay endyay orfay everyay.
Ayay odsay overscay ishay entlegay ormfay, andyay ehay owsknay onay ainpay. Ehay ancay onay ongerlay
ebay ayay ubjectsay orfay itypay; eway ustmay eserveray atthay orfay ishay iserablemay
urvivorssay.”

Ervalclay okespay usthay asyay eway urriedhay oughthray ethay eetsstray; ethay ordsway
impressedyay emselvesthay onyay ymay indmay andyay Iyay ememberedray emthay afterwardsyay inyay
olitudesay. Utbay ownay, asyay oonsay asyay ethay orseshay arrivedyay, Iyay urriedhay intoyay ayay
abrioletcay, andyay adebay arewellfay otay ymay iendfray.

Ymay ourneyjay asway eryvay elancholymay. Atyay irstfay Iyay ishedway otay urryhay onyay, orfay Iyay ongedlay
otay onsolecay andyay ympathisesay ithway ymay ovedlay andyay orrowingsay iendsfray; utbay enwhay Iyay
ewdray earnay ymay ativenay owntay, Iyay ackenedslay ymay ogresspray. Iyay ouldcay ardlyhay ustainsay
ethay ultitudemay ofyay eelingsfay atthay owdedcray intoyay ymay indmay. Iyay assedpay oughthray
enesscay amiliarfay otay ymay youthyay, utbay ichwhay Iyay adhay otnay eensay orfay earlynay ixsay yearsyay.
Owhay alteredyay everyyay ingthay ightmay ebay uringday atthay imetay! Oneyay uddensay andyay
esolatingday angechay adhay akentay aceplay; utbay ayay ousandthay ittlelay ircumstancescay
ightmay avehay ybay egreesday orkedway otheryay alterationsyay, ichwhay, althoughyay eythay ereway
oneday oremay anquillytray, ightmay otnay ebay ethay esslay ecisiveday. Earfay overcameyay emay; Iyay
aredday onay advanceyay, eadingdray ayay ousandthay amelessnay evilsyay atthay ademay emay embletray,
althoughyay Iyay asway unableyay otay efineday emthay.

Iyay emainedray otway aysday atyay Ausannelay, inyay isthay ainfulpay atestay ofyay indmay. Iyay
ontemplatedcay ethay akelay: ethay atersway ereway acidplay; allyay aroundyay asway almcay; andyay ethay
owysnay ountainsmay, e“thay alacespay ofyay aturenay,” ereway otnay angedchay. Ybay
egreesday ethay almcay andyay eavenlyhay enescay estoredray emay, andyay Iyay ontinuedcay ymay ourneyjay
owardstay Enevagay.

Ethay oadray anray ybay ethay idesay ofyay ethay akelay, ichwhay ecamebay arrowernay asyay Iyay
approachedyay ymay ativenay owntay. Iyay iscoveredday oremay istinctlyday ethay ackblay
idessay ofyay Urajay, andyay ethay ightbray ummitsay ofyay Ontmay Ancblay. Iyay eptway ikelay ayay
ildchay. ear“day ountainsmay! ymay ownyay eautifulbay akelay! owhay oday youyay elcomeway youryay
andererway? Youryay ummitssay areyay earclay; ethay yskay andyay akelay areyay ueblay andyay
acidplay. Isyay isthay otay ognosticatepray eacepay, oryay otay ockmay atyay ymay unhappinessyay?”

Iyay earfay, ymay iendfray, atthay Iyay allshay enderray yselfmay edioustay ybay ellingdway onyay
esethay eliminarypray ircumstancescay; utbay eythay ereway aysday ofyay omparativecay
appinesshay, andyay Iyay inkthay ofyay emthay ithway easureplay. Ymay ountrycay, ymay elovedbay
ountrycay! owhay utbay ayay ativenay ancay elltay ethay elightday Iyay ooktay inyay againyay
eholdingbay ythay eamsstray, ythay ountainsmay, andyay, oremay anthay allyay, ythay ovelylay
akelay!

Yetyay, asyay Iyay ewdray earernay omehay, iefgray andyay earfay againyay overcameyay emay. Ightnay alsoyay
osedclay aroundyay; andyay enwhay Iyay ouldcay ardlyhay eesay ethay arkday ountainsmay, Iyay eltfay illstay
oremay oomilyglay. Ethay icturepay appearedyay ayay astvay andyay imday enescay ofyay evilyay, andyay Iyay
oresawfay obscurelyyay atthay Iyay asway estinedday otay ecomebay ethay ostmay etchedwray ofyay umanhay
eingsbay. Alasyay! Iyay ophesiedpray ulytray, andyay ailedfay onlyyay inyay oneyay inglesay
ircumstancecay, atthay inyay allyay ethay iserymay Iyay imaginedyay andyay eadeddray, Iyay idday otnay
onceivecay ethay undredthhay artpay ofyay ethay anguishyay Iyay asway estinedday otay endureyay.

Ityay asway ompletelycay arkday enwhay Iyay arrivedyay inyay ethay environsyay ofyay Enevagay; ethay atesgay
ofyay ethay owntay ereway alreadyyay utshay; andyay Iyay asway obligedyay otay asspay ethay ightnay atyay
Echeronsay, ayay illagevay atyay ethay istanceday ofyay alfhay ayay eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Ethay yskay
asway erenesay; andyay, asyay Iyay asway unableyay otay estray, Iyay esolvedray otay isitvay ethay otspay
erewhay ymay oorpay Illiamway adhay eenbay urderedmay. Asyay Iyay ouldcay otnay asspay oughthray ethay
owntay, Iyay asway obligedyay otay osscray ethay akelay inyay ayay oatbay otay arriveyay atyay Ainpalaisplay.
Uringday isthay ortshay oyagevay Iyay awsay ethay ightninglay ayingplay onyay ethay ummitsay ofyay Ontmay
Ancblay inyay ethay ostmay eautifulbay iguresfay. Ethay ormstay appearedyay otay approachyay
apidlyray, andyay, onyay andinglay, Iyay ascendedyay ayay owlay illhay, atthay Iyay ightmay observeyay itsyay
ogresspray. Ityay advancedyay; ethay eavenshay ereway oudedclay, andyay Iyay oonsay eltfay ethay ainray
omingcay owlyslay inyay argelay opsdray, utbay itsyay iolencevay uicklyqay increasedyay.

Iyay uittedqay ymay eatsay, andyay alkedway onyay, althoughyay ethay arknessday andyay ormstay
increasedyay everyyay inutemay, andyay ethay underthay urstbay ithway ayay errifictay ashcray
overyay ymay eadhay. Ityay asway echoedyay omfray Alêvesay, ethay Urasjay, andyay ethay Alpsyay ofyay
Avoysay; ividvay ashesflay ofyay ightninglay azzledday ymay eyesyay, illuminatingyay ethay
akelay, akingmay ityay appearyay ikelay ayay astvay eetshay ofyay irefay; enthay orfay anyay instantyay
everyyay ingthay eemedsay ofyay ayay itchypay arknessday, untilyay ethay eyeyay ecoveredray itselfyay
omfray ethay ecedingpray ashflay. Ethay ormstay, asyay isyay oftenyay ethay asecay inyay
Itzerlandsway, appearedyay atyay onceyay inyay ariousvay artspay ofyay ethay eavenshay. Ethay
ostmay iolentvay ormstay unghay exactlyyay orthnay ofyay ethay owntay, overyay ethay artpay ofyay ethay
akelay ichwhay ieslay etweenbay ethay omontorypray ofyay Elrivebay andyay ethay illagevay ofyay
Opêtcay. Anotheryay ormstay enlightenedyay Urajay ithway aintfay ashesflay; andyay anotheryay
arkenedday andyay ometimessay isclosedday ethay Emôlay, ayay eakedpay ountainmay otay ethay
eastyay ofyay ethay akelay.

Ilewhay Iyay atchedway ethay empesttay, osay eautifulbay yetyay errifictay, Iyay anderedway onyay ithway
ayay astyhay epstay. Isthay oblenay arway inyay ethay yskay elevatedyay ymay iritsspay; Iyay aspedclay ymay
andshay, andyay exclaimedyay aloudyay, illiam“way, earday angelyay! isthay isyay ythay
uneralfay, isthay ythay irgeday!” Asyay Iyay aidsay esethay ordsway, Iyay erceivedpay inyay ethay
oomglay ayay igurefay ichwhay olestay omfray ehindbay ayay umpclay ofyay eestray earnay emay; Iyay oodstay
ixedfay, azinggay intentlyyay: Iyay ouldcay otnay ebay istakenmay. Ayay ashflay ofyay ightninglay
illuminatedyay ethay objectyay, andyay iscoveredday itsyay apeshay ainlyplay otay emay; itsyay
iganticgay aturestay, andyay ethay eformityday ofyay itsyay aspectyay oremay ideoushay anthay elongsbay
otay umanityhay, instantlyyay informedyay emay atthay ityay asway ethay etchwray, ethay ilthyfay
ondæmay, otay omwhay Iyay adhay ivengay ifelay. Atwhay idday ehay erethay? Ouldcay ehay ebay i(ay
udderedshay atyay ethay onceptioncay) ethay urderermay ofyay ymay otherbray? Onay oonersay idday atthay
ideayay osscray ymay imaginationyay, anthay Iyay ecamebay onvincedcay ofyay itsyay uthtray; ymay eethtay
atteredchay, andyay Iyay asway orcedfay otay eanlay againstyay ayay eetray orfay upportsay. Ethay igurefay
assedpay emay uicklyqay, andyay Iyay ostlay ityay inyay ethay oomglay. Othingnay inyay umanhay apeshay ouldcay
avehay estroyedday ethay airfay ildchay. e_hay_ asway ethay urderermay! Iyay ouldcay otnay
oubtday ityay. Ethay eremay esencepray ofyay ethay ideayay asway anyay irresistibleyay oofpray ofyay ethay
actfay. Iyay oughtthay ofyay ursuingpay ethay evilday; utbay ityay ouldway avehay eenbay inyay ainvay, orfay
anotheryay ashflay iscoveredday imhay otay emay anginghay amongyay ethay ocksray ofyay ethay earlynay
erpendicularpay ascentyay ofyay Ontmay Alêvesay, ayay illhay atthay oundsbay Ainpalaisplay onyay ethay
outhsay. Ehay oonsay eachedray ethay ummitsay, andyay isappearedday.

Iyay emainedray otionlessmay. Ethay underthay easedcay; utbay ethay ainray illstay
ontinuedcay, andyay ethay enescay asway envelopedyay inyay anyay impenetrableyay arknessday. Iyay
evolvedray inyay ymay indmay ethay eventsyay ichwhay Iyay adhay untilyay ownay oughtsay otay orgetfay:
ethay olewhay aintray ofyay ymay ogresspray owardtay ethay eationcray; ethay appearanceyay ofyay
ethay orksway ofyay ymay ownyay andshay atyay ymay edsidebay; itsyay epartureday. Otway yearsyay adhay
ownay earlynay elapsedyay incesay ethay ightnay onyay ichwhay ehay irstfay eceivedray ifelay; andyay
asway isthay ishay irstfay imecray? Alasyay! Iyay adhay urnedtay ooselay intoyay ethay orldway ayay
epravedday etchwray, osewhay elightday asway inyay arnagecay andyay iserymay; adhay ehay otnay
urderedmay ymay otherbray?

Onay oneyay ancay onceivecay ethay anguishyay Iyay ufferedsay uringday ethay emainderray ofyay ethay
ightnay, ichwhay Iyay entspay, oldcay andyay etway, inyay ethay openyay airyay. Utbay Iyay idday otnay
eelfay ethay inconvenienceyay ofyay ethay eatherway; ymay imaginationyay asway usybay inyay
enesscay ofyay evilyay andyay espairday. Iyay onsideredcay ethay eingbay omwhay Iyay adhay astcay
amongyay ankindmay, andyay endowedyay ithway ethay illway andyay owerpay otay effectyay urposespay
ofyay orrorhay, uchsay asyay ethay eedday ichwhay ehay adhay ownay oneday, earlynay inyay ethay ightlay
ofyay ymay ownyay ampirevay, ymay ownyay iritspay etlay ooselay omfray ethay avegray, andyay orcedfay
otay estroyday allyay atthay asway earday otay emay.

Ayday awnedday; andyay Iyay irectedday ymay epsstay owardstay ethay owntay. Ethay atesgay ereway
openyay, andyay Iyay astenedhay otay ymay ather’sfay ousehay. Ymay irstfay oughtthay asway otay
iscoverday atwhay Iyay ewknay ofyay ethay urderermay, andyay ausecay instantyay ursuitpay otay ebay
ademay. Utbay Iyay ausedpay enwhay Iyay eflectedray onyay ethay orystay atthay Iyay adhay otay elltay. Ayay
eingbay omwhay Iyay yselfmay adhay ormedfay, andyay enduedyay ithway ifelay, adhay etmay emay atyay
idnightmay amongyay ethay ecipicespray ofyay anyay inaccessibleyay ountainmay. Iyay
ememberedray alsoyay ethay ervousnay everfay ithway ichwhay Iyay adhay eenbay eizedsay ustjay atyay
ethay imetay atthay Iyay atedday ymay eationcray, andyay ichwhay ouldway ivegay anyay airyay ofyay
eliriumday otay ayay aletay otherwiseyay osay utterlyyay improbableyay. Iyay ellway ewknay atthay
ifyay anyyay otheryay adhay ommunicatedcay uchsay ayay elationray otay emay, Iyay ouldshay avehay
ookedlay uponyay ityay asyay ethay avingsray ofyay insanityyay. Esidesbay, ethay angestray aturenay
ofyay ethay animalyay ouldway eludeyay allyay ursuitpay, evenyay ifyay Iyay ereway osay arfay editedcray
asyay otay ersuadepay ymay elativesray otay ommencecay ityay. Andyay enthay ofyay atwhay useyay ouldway
ebay ursuitpay? Owhay ouldcay arrestyay ayay eaturecray apablecay ofyay alingscay ethay
overhangingyay idessay ofyay Ontmay Alêvesay? Esethay eflectionsray eterminedday emay, andyay
Iyay esolvedray otay emainray ilentsay.

Ityay asway aboutyay ivefay inyay ethay orningmay enwhay Iyay enteredyay ymay ather’sfay ousehay. Iyay
oldtay ethay ervantssay otnay otay isturbday ethay amilyfay, andyay entway intoyay ethay ibrarylay
otay attendyay eirthay usualyay ourhay ofyay isingray.

Ixsay yearsyay adhay elapsedyay, assedpay inyay ayay eamdray utbay orfay oneyay indelibleyay acetray, andyay Iyay
oodstay inyay ethay amesay aceplay erewhay Iyay adhay astlay embracedyay ymay atherfay eforebay ymay
epartureday orfay Ingolstadtyay. Elovedbay andyay enerablevay arentpay! Ehay illstay emainedray
otay emay. Iyay azedgay onyay ethay icturepay ofyay ymay othermay, ichwhay oodstay overyay ethay
antel-piecemay. Ityay asway anyay istoricalhay ubjectsay, aintedpay atyay ymay ather’sfay
esireday, andyay epresentedray Arolinecay Eaufortbay inyay anyay agonyyay ofyay espairday, eelingknay
ybay ethay offincay ofyay erhay eadday atherfay. Erhay arbgay asway usticray, andyay erhay eekchay alepay;
utbay erethay asway anyay airyay ofyay ignityday andyay eautybay, atthay ardlyhay ermittedpay ethay
entimentsay ofyay itypay. Elowbay isthay icturepay asway ayay iniaturemay ofyay Illiamway; andyay ymay
earstay owedflay enwhay Iyay ookedlay uponyay ityay. Ilewhay Iyay asway usthay engagedyay, Ernestyay
enteredyay: ehay adhay eardhay emay arriveyay, andyay astenedhay otay elcomeway emay:
elcome“way, ymay earestday Ictorvay,” aidsay ehay. ah“ay! Iyay ishway youyay
adhay omecay eethray onthsmay agoyay, andyay enthay youyay ouldway avehay oundfay usyay allyay oyousjay andyay
elightedday. Youyay omecay otay usyay ownay otay areshay ayay iserymay ichwhay othingnay ancay
alleviateyay; yetyay youryay esencepray illway, Iyay opehay, eviveray ouryay atherfay, owhay eemssay
inkingsay underyay ishay isfortunemay; andyay youryay ersuasionspay illway induceyay oorpay
Elizabethyay otay easecay erhay ainvay andyay ormentingtay elf-accusations.—poorsay
Illiamway! ehay asway ouryay arlingday andyay ouryay idepray!”

Earstay, unrestrainedyay, ellfay omfray ymay other’sbray eyesyay; ayay ensesay ofyay ortalmay
agonyyay eptcray overyay ymay amefray. Eforebay, Iyay adhay onlyyay imaginedyay ethay
etchednesswray ofyay ymay esolatedday omehay; ethay ealityray amecay onyay emay asyay ayay ewnay, andyay
ayay otnay esslay erribletay, isasterday. Iyay iedtray otay almcay Ernestyay; Iyay enquiredyay oremay
inutelymay oncerningcay ymay atherfay, andyay erehay Iyay amednay ymay ousincay.

e“shay ostmay ofyay allyay,” aidsay Ernestyay, equires“ray onsolationcay; eshay accusedyay
erselfhay ofyay avinghay ausedcay ethay eathday ofyay ymay otherbray, andyay atthay ademay erhay
eryvay etchedwray. Utbay incesay ethay urderermay ashay eenbay iscoveredday—”

e“thay urderermay iscoveredday! Oodgay Odgay! owhay ancay atthay ebay? owhay ouldcay attemptyay
otay ursuepay imhay? Ityay isyay impossibleyay; oneyay ightmay asyay ellway ytray otay overtakeyay ethay
indsway, oryay onfinecay ayay ountain-streammay ithway ayay awstray. Iyay awsay imhay ootay; ehay
asway eefray astlay ightnay!”

i“ay oday otnay owknay atwhay youyay eanmay,” epliedray ymay otherbray, inyay accentsyay ofyay
onderway, ut“bay otay usyay ethay iscoveryday eway avehay ademay ompletescay ouryay iserymay. Onay
oneyay ouldway elievebay ityay atyay irstfay; andyay evenyay ownay Elizabethyay illway otnay ebay
onvincedcay, otwithstandingnay allyay ethay evidenceyay. Indeedyay, owhay ouldway editcray
atthay Ustinejay Oritzmay, owhay asway osay amiableyay, andyay ondfay ofyay allyay ethay amilyfay,
ouldcay uddenlysay ecomebay osay apablecay ofyay osay ightfulfray, osay appallingyay ayay imecray?”

ustine“jay Oritzmay! Oorpay, oorpay irlgay, isyay eshay ethay accusedyay? Utbay ityay isyay
ongfullywray; everyyay oneyay owsknay atthay; onay oneyay elievesbay ityay, urelysay, Ernestyay?”

o“nay oneyay idday atyay irstfay; utbay everalsay ircumstancescay amecay outyay, atthay avehay
almostyay orcedfay onvictioncay uponyay usyay; andyay erhay ownyay ehaviourbay ashay eenbay osay
onfusedcay, asyay otay addyay otay ethay evidenceyay ofyay actsfay ayay eightway atthay, Iyay earfay,
eaveslay onay opehay orfay oubtday. Utbay eshay illway ebay iedtray odaytay, andyay youyay illway
enthay earhay allyay.”

Ehay enthay elatedray atthay, ethay orningmay onyay ichwhay ethay urdermay ofyay oorpay Illiamway
adhay eenbay iscoveredday, Ustinejay adhay eenbay akentay illyay, andyay onfinedcay otay erhay
edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Uringday isthay intervalyay, oneyay ofyay ethay ervantssay,
appeninghay otay examineyay ethay apparelyay eshay adhay ornway onyay ethay ightnay ofyay ethay
urdermay, adhay iscoveredday inyay erhay ocketpay ethay icturepay ofyay ymay othermay, ichwhay
adhay eenbay udgedjay otay ebay ethay emptationtay ofyay ethay urderermay. Ethay ervantsay
instantlyyay owedshay ityay otay oneyay ofyay ethay othersyay, owhay, ithoutway ayingsay ayay ordway otay
anyyay ofyay ethay amilyfay, entway otay ayay agistratemay; andyay, uponyay eirthay epositionday,
Ustinejay asway apprehendedyay. Onyay eingbay argedchay ithway ethay actfay, ethay oorpay irlgay
onfirmedcay ethay uspicionsay inyay ayay eatgray easuremay ybay erhay extremeyay onfusioncay ofyay
annermay.

Isthay asway ayay angestray aletay, utbay ityay idday otnay akeshay ymay aithfay; andyay Iyay epliedray
earnestlyyay, you“ay areyay allyay istakenmay; Iyay owknay ethay urderermay. Ustinejay, oorpay,
oodgay Ustinejay, isyay innocentyay.”

Atyay atthay instantyay ymay atherfay enteredyay. Iyay awsay unhappinessyay eeplyday impressedyay
onyay ishay ountenancecay, utbay ehay endeavouredyay otay elcomeway emay eerfullychay; andyay,
afteryay eway adhay exchangedyay ouryay ournfulmay eetinggray, ouldway avehay introducedyay
omesay otheryay opictay anthay atthay ofyay ouryay isasterday, adhay otnay Ernestyay exclaimedyay,
ood“gay Odgay, apapay! Ictorvay ayssay atthay ehay owsknay owhay asway ethay urderermay ofyay
oorpay Illiamway.”

e“way oday alsoyay, unfortunatelyyay,” epliedray ymay atherfay, or“fay indeedyay Iyay adhay
atherray avehay eenbay orfay everyay ignorantyay anthay avehay iscoveredday osay uchmay
epravityday andyay ungratitudeyay inyay oneyay Iyay aluedvay osay ighlyhay.”

y“may earday atherfay, youyay areyay istakenmay; Ustinejay isyay innocentyay.”

if“ay eshay isyay, Odgay orbidfay atthay eshay ouldshay uffersay asyay uiltygay. Eshay isyay otay ebay
iedtray odaytay, andyay Iyay opehay, Iyay incerelysay opehay, atthay eshay illway ebay acquittedyay.”

Isthay eechspay almedcay emay. Iyay asway irmlyfay onvincedcay inyay ymay ownyay indmay atthay
Ustinejay, andyay indeedyay everyyay umanhay eingbay, asway uiltlessgay ofyay isthay urdermay. Iyay
adhay onay earfay, ereforethay, atthay anyyay ircumstantialcay evidenceyay ouldcay ebay
oughtbray orwardfay ongstray enoughyay otay onvictcay erhay. Ymay aletay asway otnay oneyay otay
announceyay ubliclypay; itsyay astoundingyay orrorhay ouldway ebay ookedlay uponyay asyay
adnessmay ybay ethay ulgarvay. Idday anyyay oneyay indeedyay existyay, exceptyay Iyay, ethay
eatorcray, owhay ouldway elievebay, unlessyay ishay ensessay onvincedcay imhay, inyay ethay
existenceyay ofyay ethay ivinglay onumentmay ofyay esumptionpray andyay ashray ignoranceyay
ichwhay Iyay adhay etlay ooselay uponyay ethay orldway?

Eway ereway oonsay oinedjay ybay Elizabethyay. Imetay adhay alteredyay erhay incesay Iyay astlay
eheldbay erhay; ityay adhay endowedyay erhay ithway ovelinesslay urpassingsay ethay eautybay ofyay
erhay ildishchay yearsyay. Erethay asway ethay amesay andourcay, ethay amesay ivacityvay, utbay
ityay asway alliedyay otay anyay expressionyay oremay ullfay ofyay ensibilitysay andyay intellectyay.
Eshay elcomedway emay ithway ethay eatestgray affectionyay. your“ay arrivalyay, ymay earday
ousincay,” aidsay eshay, ills“fay emay ithway opehay. Youyay erhapspay illway indfay omesay
eansmay otay ustifyjay ymay oorpay uiltlessgay Ustinejay. Alasyay! owhay isyay afesay, ifyay eshay
ebay onvictedcay ofyay imecray? Iyay elyray onyay erhay innocenceyay asyay ertainlycay asyay Iyay oday
uponyay ymay ownyay. Ouryay isfortunemay isyay oublyday ardhay otay usyay; eway avehay otnay onlyyay
ostlay atthay ovelylay arlingday oybay, utbay isthay oorpay irlgay, omwhay Iyay incerelysay
ovelay, isyay otay ebay orntay awayyay ybay evenyay ayay orseway atefay. Ifyay eshay isyay ondemnedcay, Iyay
evernay allshay owknay oyjay oremay. Utbay eshay illway otnay, Iyay amyay uresay eshay illway otnay;
andyay enthay Iyay allshay ebay appyhay againyay, evenyay afteryay ethay adsay eathday ofyay ymay ittlelay
Illiamway.”

e“shay isyay innocentyay, ymay Elizabethyay,” aidsay Iyay, and“ay atthay allshay
ebay ovedpray; earfay othingnay, utbay etlay youryay iritsspay ebay eeredchay ybay ethay assuranceyay
ofyay erhay acquittalyay.”

ow“hay indkay andyay enerousgay youyay areyay! everyyay oneyay elseyay elievesbay inyay erhay uiltgay,
andyay atthay ademay emay etchedwray, orfay Iyay ewknay atthay ityay asway impossibleyay: andyay otay
eesay everyyay oneyay elseyay ejudicedpray inyay osay eadlyday ayay annermay enderedray emay
opelesshay andyay espairingday.” Eshay eptway.

earest“day iecenay,” aidsay ymay atherfay, y“dray youryay earstay. Ifyay eshay
isyay, asyay youyay elievebay, innocentyay, elyray onyay ethay usticejay ofyay ouryay awslay, andyay ethay
activityyay ithway ichwhay Iyay allshay eventpray ethay ightestslay adowshay ofyay
artialitypay.”




Apterchay 8


Eway assedpay ayay ewfay adsay ourshay untilyay elevenyay o’clockyay, enwhay ethay ialtray asway otay
ommencecay. Ymay atherfay andyay ethay estray ofyay ethay amilyfay eingbay obligedyay otay attendyay
asyay itnessesway, Iyay accompaniedyay emthay otay ethay ourtcay. Uringday ethay olewhay ofyay
isthay etchedwray ockerymay ofyay usticejay Iyay ufferedsay ivinglay orturetay. Ityay asway otay
ebay ecidedday etherwhay ethay esultray ofyay ymay uriositycay andyay awlesslay evicesday ouldway
ausecay ethay eathday ofyay otway ofyay ymay ellowfay eingsbay: oneyay ayay ilingsmay abebay ullfay ofyay
innocenceyay andyay oyjay, ethay otheryay arfay oremay eadfullydray urderedmay, ithway everyyay
aggravationyay ofyay infamyyay atthay ouldcay akemay ethay urdermay emorablemay inyay orrorhay.
Ustinejay alsoyay asway ayay irlgay ofyay eritmay andyay ossessedpay ualitiesqay ichwhay omisedpray
otay enderray erhay ifelay appyhay; ownay allyay asway otay ebay obliteratedyay inyay anyay
ignominiousyay avegray, andyay Iyay ethay ausecay! Ayay ousandthay imestay atherray ouldway Iyay
avehay onfessedcay yselfmay uiltygay ofyay ethay imecray ascribedyay otay Ustinejay, utbay Iyay
asway absentyay enwhay ityay asway ommittedcay, andyay uchsay ayay eclarationday ouldway avehay
eenbay onsideredcay asyay ethay avingsray ofyay ayay admanmay andyay ouldway otnay avehay
exculpatedyay erhay owhay ufferedsay oughthray emay.

Ethay appearanceyay ofyay Ustinejay asway almcay. Eshay asway esseddray inyay ourningmay, andyay
erhay ountenancecay, alwaysyay engagingyay, asway enderedray, ybay ethay olemnitysay ofyay erhay
eelingsfay, exquisitelyyay eautifulbay. Yetyay eshay appearedyay onfidentcay inyay
innocenceyay andyay idday otnay embletray, althoughyay azedgay onyay andyay execratedyay ybay
ousandsthay, orfay allyay ethay indnesskay ichwhay erhay eautybay ightmay otherwiseyay avehay
excitedyay asway obliteratedyay inyay ethay indsmay ofyay ethay ectatorsspay ybay ethay
imaginationyay ofyay ethay enormityyay eshay asway upposedsay otay avehay ommittedcay. Eshay
asway anquiltray, yetyay erhay anquillitytray asway evidentlyyay onstrainedcay; andyay asyay
erhay onfusioncay adhay eforebay eenbay adducedyay asyay ayay oofpray ofyay erhay uiltgay, eshay
orkedway upyay erhay indmay otay anyay appearanceyay ofyay ouragecay. Enwhay eshay enteredyay ethay
ourtcay eshay ewthray erhay eyesyay oundray ityay andyay uicklyqay iscoveredday erewhay eway ereway
eatedsay. Ayay eartay eemedsay otay imday erhay eyeyay enwhay eshay awsay usyay, utbay eshay uicklyqay
ecoveredray erselfhay, andyay ayay ooklay ofyay orrowfulsay affectionyay eemedsay otay attestyay
erhay utteryay uiltlessnessgay.

Ethay ialtray eganbay, andyay afteryay ethay advocateyay againstyay erhay adhay atedstay ethay
argechay, everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay. Everalsay angestray actsfay ombinedcay
againstyay erhay, ichwhay ightmay avehay aggeredstay anyoneyay owhay adhay otnay uchsay oofpray
ofyay erhay innocenceyay asyay Iyay adhay. Eshay adhay eenbay outyay ethay olewhay ofyay ethay ightnay onyay
ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay andyay owardstay orningmay adhay eenbay
erceivedpay ybay ayay arket-womanmay otnay arfay omfray ethay otspay erewhay ethay odybay ofyay ethay
urderedmay ildchay adhay eenbay afterwardsyay oundfay. Ethay omanway askedyay erhay atwhay eshay
idday erethay, utbay eshay ookedlay eryvay angelystray andyay onlyyay eturnedray ayay onfusedcay
andyay unintelligibleyay answeryay. Eshay eturnedray otay ethay ousehay aboutyay eightyay
o’clockyay, andyay enwhay oneyay inquiredyay erewhay eshay adhay assedpay ethay ightnay, eshay
epliedray atthay eshay adhay eenbay ookinglay orfay ethay ildchay andyay emandedday earnestlyyay
ifyay anythingyay adhay eenbay eardhay oncerningcay imhay. Enwhay ownshay ethay odybay, eshay
ellfay intoyay iolentvay ystericshay andyay eptkay erhay edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Ethay
icturepay asway enthay oducedpray ichwhay ethay ervantsay adhay oundfay inyay erhay ocketpay;
andyay enwhay Elizabethyay, inyay ayay alteringfay oicevay, ovedpray atthay ityay asway ethay amesay
ichwhay, anyay ourhay eforebay ethay ildchay adhay eenbay issedmay, eshay adhay acedplay oundray
ishay ecknay, ayay urmurmay ofyay orrorhay andyay indignationyay illedfay ethay ourtcay.

Ustinejay asway alledcay onyay orfay erhay efenceday. Asyay ethay ialtray adhay oceededpray, erhay
ountenancecay adhay alteredyay. Urprisesay, orrorhay, andyay iserymay ereway onglystray
expressedyay. Ometimessay eshay uggledstray ithway erhay earstay, utbay enwhay eshay asway
esiredday otay eadplay, eshay ollectedcay erhay owerspay andyay okespay inyay anyay audibleyay
althoughyay ariablevay oicevay.

od“gay owsknay,” eshay aidsay, ow“hay entirelyyay Iyay amyay innocentyay. Utbay Iyay
oday otnay etendpray atthay ymay otestationspray ouldshay acquityay emay; Iyay estray ymay innocenceyay
onyay ayay ainplay andyay implesay explanationyay ofyay ethay actsfay ichwhay avehay eenbay adducedyay
againstyay emay, andyay Iyay opehay ethay aracterchay Iyay avehay alwaysyay ornebay illway inclineyay ymay
udgesjay otay ayay avourablefay interpretationyay erewhay anyyay ircumstancecay appearsyay
oubtfulday oryay uspicioussay.”

Eshay enthay elatedray atthay, ybay ethay ermissionpay ofyay Elizabethyay, eshay adhay assedpay
ethay eveningyay ofyay ethay ightnay onyay ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay atyay ethay
ousehay ofyay anyay auntyay atyay Echênay, ayay illagevay ituatedsay atyay aboutyay ayay eaguelay omfray
Enevagay. Onyay erhay eturnray, atyay aboutyay inenay o’clockyay, eshay etmay ayay anmay owhay askedyay
erhay ifyay eshay adhay eensay anythingyay ofyay ethay ildchay owhay asway ostlay. Eshay asway
alarmedyay ybay isthay accountyay andyay assedpay everalsay ourshay inyay ookinglay orfay imhay,
enwhay ethay atesgay ofyay Enevagay ereway utshay, andyay eshay asway orcedfay otay emainray
everalsay ourshay ofyay ethay ightnay inyay ayay arnbay elongingbay otay ayay ottagecay, eingbay
unwillingyay otay allcay upyay ethay inhabitantsyay, otay omwhay eshay asway ellway ownknay. Ostmay
ofyay ethay ightnay eshay entspay erehay atchingway; owardstay orningmay eshay elievedbay atthay
eshay eptslay orfay ayay ewfay inutesmay; omesay epsstay isturbedday erhay, andyay eshay awokeyay.
Ityay asway awnday, andyay eshay uittedqay erhay asylumyay, atthay eshay ightmay againyay endeavouryay
otay indfay ymay otherbray. Ifyay eshay adhay onegay earnay ethay otspay erewhay ishay odybay aylay,
ityay asway ithoutway erhay owledgeknay. Atthay eshay adhay eenbay ewilderedbay enwhay
uestionedqay ybay ethay arket-womanmay asway otnay urprisingsay, incesay eshay adhay assedpay
ayay eeplessslay ightnay andyay ethay atefay ofyay oorpay Illiamway asway yetyay uncertainyay.
Oncerningcay ethay icturepay eshay ouldcay ivegay onay accountyay.

i“ay owknay,” ontinuedcay ethay unhappyyay ictimvay, ow“hay eavilyhay andyay
atallyfay isthay oneyay ircumstancecay eighsway againstyay emay, utbay Iyay avehay onay owerpay ofyay
explainingyay ityay; andyay enwhay Iyay avehay expressedyay ymay utteryay ignoranceyay, Iyay amyay onlyyay eftlay
otay onjecturecay oncerningcay ethay obabilitiespray ybay ichwhay ityay ightmay avehay eenbay
acedplay inyay ymay ocketpay. Utbay erehay alsoyay Iyay amyay eckedchay. Iyay elievebay atthay Iyay avehay onay
enemyyay onyay earthyay, andyay onenay urelysay ouldway avehay eenbay osay ickedway asyay otay estroyday emay
antonlyway. Idday ethay urderermay aceplay ityay erethay? Iyay owknay ofyay onay opportunityyay
affordedyay imhay orfay osay oingday; oryay, ifyay Iyay adhay, ywhay ouldshay ehay avehay olenstay ethay
eweljay, otay artpay ithway ityay againyay osay oonsay?

i“ay ommitcay ymay ausecay otay ethay usticejay ofyay ymay udgesjay, yetyay Iyay eesay onay oomray orfay
opehay. Iyay egbay ermissionpay otay avehay ayay ewfay itnessesway examinedyay oncerningcay ymay
aracterchay, andyay ifyay eirthay estimonytay allshay otnay overweighyay ymay upposedsay
uiltgay, Iyay ustmay ebay ondemnedcay, althoughyay Iyay ouldway edgeplay ymay alvationsay onyay ymay
innocenceyay.”

Everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay owhay adhay ownknay erhay orfay anymay yearsyay, andyay
eythay okespay ellway ofyay erhay; utbay earfay andyay atredhay ofyay ethay imecray ofyay ichwhay eythay
upposedsay erhay uiltygay enderedray emthay imoroustay andyay unwillingyay otay omecay
orwardfay. Elizabethyay awsay evenyay isthay astlay esourceray, erhay excellentyay
ispositionsday andyay irreproachableyay onductcay, aboutyay otay ailfay ethay accusedyay,
enwhay, althoughyay iolentlyvay agitatedyay, eshay esiredday ermissionpay otay addressyay
ethay ourtcay.

i“ay amyay,” aidsay eshay, e“thay ousincay ofyay ethay unhappyyay ildchay owhay
asway urderedmay, oryay atherray ishay istersay, orfay Iyay asway educatedyay ybay andyay avehay ivedlay
ithway ishay arentspay everyay incesay andyay evenyay onglay eforebay ishay irthbay. Ityay aymay
ereforethay ebay udgedjay indecentyay inyay emay otay omecay orwardfay onyay isthay occasionyay, utbay
enwhay Iyay eesay ayay ellowfay eaturecray aboutyay otay erishpay oughthray ethay owardicecay ofyay erhay
etendedpray iendsfray, Iyay ishway otay ebay allowedyay otay eakspay, atthay Iyay aymay aysay atwhay Iyay
owknay ofyay erhay aracterchay. Iyay amyay ellway acquaintedyay ithway ethay accusedyay. Iyay avehay ivedlay
inyay ethay amesay ousehay ithway erhay, atyay oneyay imetay orfay ivefay andyay atyay anotheryay orfay earlynay
otway yearsyay. Uringday allyay atthay eriodpay eshay appearedyay otay emay ethay ostmay amiableyay andyay
enevolentbay ofyay umanhay eaturescray. Eshay ursednay Adamemay Ankensteinfray, ymay auntyay, inyay
erhay astlay illnessyay, ithway ethay eatestgray affectionyay andyay arecay andyay afterwardsyay
attendedyay erhay ownyay othermay uringday ayay edioustay illnessyay, inyay ayay annermay atthay excitedyay
ethay admirationyay ofyay allyay owhay ewknay erhay, afteryay ichwhay eshay againyay ivedlay inyay ymay
uncle’syay ousehay, erewhay eshay asway elovedbay ybay allyay ethay amilyfay. Eshay asway
armlyway attachedyay otay ethay ildchay owhay isyay ownay eadday andyay actedyay owardstay imhay ikelay ayay
ostmay affectionateyay othermay. Orfay ymay ownyay artpay, Iyay oday otnay esitatehay otay aysay atthay,
otwithstandingnay allyay ethay evidenceyay oducedpray againstyay erhay, Iyay elievebay andyay elyray
onyay erhay erfectpay innocenceyay. Eshay adhay onay emptationtay orfay uchsay anyay actionyay; asyay otay
ethay aublebay onyay ichwhay ethay iefchay oofpray estsray, ifyay eshay adhay earnestlyyay esiredday ityay,
Iyay ouldshay avehay illinglyway ivengay ityay otay erhay, osay uchmay oday Iyay esteemyay andyay aluevay
erhay.”

Ayay urmurmay ofyay approbationyay ollowedfay Elizabeth’syay implesay andyay owerfulpay
appealyay, utbay ityay asway excitedyay ybay erhay enerousgay interferenceyay, andyay otnay inyay
avourfay ofyay oorpay Ustinejay, onyay omwhay ethay ublicpay indignationyay asway urnedtay ithway
enewedray iolencevay, argingchay erhay ithway ethay ackestblay ingratitudeyay. Eshay
erselfhay eptway asyay Elizabethyay okespay, utbay eshay idday otnay answeryay. Ymay ownyay
agitationyay andyay anguishyay asway extremeyay uringday ethay olewhay ialtray. Iyay elievedbay
inyay erhay innocenceyay; Iyay ewknay ityay. Ouldcay ethay ondæmay owhay adhay i(ay idday otnay orfay ayay
inutemay oubtday) urderedmay ymay otherbray alsoyay inyay ishay ellishhay ortspay avehay
etrayedbay ethay innocentyay otay eathday andyay ignominyyay? Iyay ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay
orrorhay ofyay ymay ituationsay, andyay enwhay Iyay erceivedpay atthay ethay opularpay oicevay andyay
ethay ountenancescay ofyay ethay udgesjay adhay alreadyyay ondemnedcay ymay unhappyyay ictimvay,
Iyay ushedray outyay ofyay ethay ourtcay inyay agonyyay. Ethay orturestay ofyay ethay accusedyay idday
otnay equalyay inemay; eshay asway ustainedsay ybay innocenceyay, utbay ethay angsfay ofyay
emorseray oretay ymay osombay andyay ouldway otnay orgofay eirthay oldhay.

Iyay assedpay ayay ightnay ofyay unmingledyay etchednesswray. Inyay ethay orningmay Iyay entway otay
ethay ourtcay; ymay ipslay andyay oatthray ereway archedpay. Iyay aredday otnay askyay ethay atalfay
uestionqay, utbay Iyay asway ownknay, andyay ethay officeryay uessedgay ethay ausecay ofyay ymay
isitvay. Ethay allotsbay adhay eenbay ownthray; eythay ereway allyay ackblay, andyay Ustinejay
asway ondemnedcay.

Iyay annotcay etendpray otay escribeday atwhay Iyay enthay eltfay. Iyay adhay eforebay
experiencedyay ensationssay ofyay orrorhay, andyay Iyay avehay endeavouredyay otay estowbay uponyay
emthay adequateyay expressionsyay, utbay ordsway annotcay onveycay anyay ideayay ofyay ethay
eart-sickeninghay espairday atthay Iyay enthay enduredyay. Ethay ersonpay otay omwhay Iyay
addressedyay yselfmay addedyay atthay Ustinejay adhay alreadyyay onfessedcay erhay uiltgay.
at“thay evidenceyay,” ehay observedyay, as“way ardlyhay equiredray inyay osay aringglay ayay
asecay, utbay Iyay amyay adglay ofyay ityay, andyay, indeedyay, onenay ofyay ouryay udgesjay ikelay otay
ondemncay ayay iminalcray uponyay ircumstantialcay evidenceyay, ebay ityay everyay osay
ecisiveday.”

Isthay asway angestray andyay unexpectedyay intelligenceyay; atwhay ouldcay ityay eanmay? Adhay
ymay eyesyay eceivedday emay? Andyay asway Iyay eallyray asyay admay asyay ethay olewhay orldway ouldway
elievebay emay otay ebay ifyay Iyay isclosedday ethay objectyay ofyay ymay uspicionssay? Iyay
astenedhay otay eturnray omehay, andyay Elizabethyay eagerlyyay emandedday ethay esultray.

y“may ousincay,” epliedray Iyay, it“ay isyay ecidedday asyay youyay aymay avehay expectedyay; allyay
udgesjay adhay atherray atthay entay innocentyay ouldshay uffersay anthay atthay oneyay uiltygay
ouldshay escapeyay. Utbay eshay ashay onfessedcay.”

Isthay asway ayay ireday owblay otay oorpay Elizabethyay, owhay adhay eliedray ithway irmnessfay uponyay
Ustine’sjay innocenceyay. alas“ay!” aidsay eshay. ow“hay allshay Iyay
everyay againyay elievebay inyay umanhay oodnessgay? Ustinejay, omwhay Iyay ovedlay andyay esteemedyay asyay
ymay istersay, owhay ouldcay eshay utpay onyay osethay ilessmay ofyay innocenceyay onlyyay otay etraybay?
Erhay ildmay eyesyay eemedsay incapableyay ofyay anyyay everitysay oryay uilegay, andyay yetyay eshay ashay
ommittedcay ayay urdermay.”

Oonsay afteryay eway eardhay atthay ethay oorpay ictimvay adhay expressedyay ayay esireday otay eesay ymay
ousincay. Ymay atherfay ishedway erhay otnay otay ogay utbay aidsay atthay ehay eftlay ityay otay erhay ownyay
udgmentjay andyay eelingsfay otay ecideday. yes“ay,” aidsay Elizabethyay,
i“ay illway ogay, althoughyay eshay isyay uiltygay; andyay youyay, Ictorvay, allshay accompanyyay
emay; Iyay annotcay ogay aloneyay.” Ethay ideayay ofyay isthay isitvay asway orturetay otay emay, yetyay
Iyay ouldcay otnay efuseray.

Eway enteredyay ethay oomyglay isonpray amberchay andyay eheldbay Ustinejay ittingsay onyay omesay
awstray atyay ethay artherfay endyay; erhay andshay ereway anacledmay, andyay erhay eadhay estedray onyay
erhay eesknay. Eshay oseray onyay eeingsay usyay enteryay, andyay enwhay eway ereway eftlay aloneyay ithway
erhay, eshay ewthray erselfhay atyay ethay eetfay ofyay Elizabethyay, eepingway itterlybay. Ymay
ousincay eptway alsoyay.

oh“ay, Ustinejay!” aidsay eshay. y“whay idday youyay obray emay ofyay ymay astlay onsolationcay?
Iyay eliedray onyay youryay innocenceyay, andyay althoughyay Iyay asway enthay eryvay etchedwray, Iyay
asway otnay osay iserablemay asyay Iyay amyay ownay.”

and“ay oday youyay alsoyay elievebay atthay Iyay amyay osay eryvay, eryvay ickedway? Oday youyay alsoyay
oinjay ithway ymay enemiesyay otay ushcray emay, otay ondemncay emay asyay ayay urderermay?” Erhay
oicevay asway uffocatedsay ithway obssay.

ise“ray, ymay oorpay irlgay,” aidsay Elizabethyay; y“whay oday youyay eelknay,
ifyay youyay areyay innocentyay? Iyay amyay otnay oneyay ofyay youryay enemiesyay, Iyay elievedbay youyay
uiltlessgay, otwithstandingnay everyyay evidenceyay, untilyay Iyay eardhay atthay youyay adhay
yourselfyay eclaredday youryay uiltgay. Atthay eportray, youyay aysay, isyay alsefay; andyay ebay
assuredyay, earday Ustinejay, atthay othingnay ancay akeshay ymay onfidencecay inyay youyay orfay ayay
omentmay, utbay youryay ownyay onfessioncay.”

i“ay idday onfesscay, utbay Iyay onfessedcay ayay ielay. Iyay onfessedcay, atthay Iyay ightmay
obtainyay absolutionyay; utbay ownay atthay alsehoodfay ieslay eavierhay atyay ymay earthay anthay
allyay ymay otheryay inssay. Ethay Odgay ofyay eavenhay orgivefay emay! Everyay incesay Iyay asway
ondemnedcay, ymay onfessorcay ashay esiegedbay emay; ehay eatenedthray andyay enacedmay,
untilyay Iyay almostyay eganbay otay inkthay atthay Iyay asway ethay onstermay atthay ehay aidsay Iyay
asway. Ehay eatenedthray excommunicationyay andyay ellhay irefay inyay ymay astlay omentsmay ifyay
Iyay ontinuedcay obdurateyay. Earday adylay, Iyay adhay onenay otay upportsay emay; allyay ookedlay
onyay emay asyay ayay etchwray oomedday otay ignominyyay andyay erditionpay. Atwhay ouldcay Iyay oday?
Inyay anyay evilyay ourhay Iyay ubscribedsay otay ayay ielay; andyay ownay onlyyay amyay Iyay ulytray
iserablemay.”

Eshay ausedpay, eepingway, andyay enthay ontinuedcay, i“ay oughtthay ithway orrorhay, ymay
eetsway adylay, atthay youyay ouldshay elievebay youryay Ustinejay, omwhay youryay essedblay
auntyay adhay osay ighlyhay onouredhay, andyay omwhay youyay ovedlay, asway ayay eaturecray apablecay
ofyay ayay imecray ichwhay onenay utbay ethay evilday imselfhay ouldcay avehay erpetratedpay.
Earday Illiamway! earestday essedblay ildchay! Iyay oonsay allshay eesay youyay againyay inyay
eavenhay, erewhay eway allshay allyay ebay appyhay; andyay atthay onsolescay emay, oinggay asyay Iyay
amyay otay uffersay ignominyyay andyay eathday.”

oh“ay, Ustinejay! Orgivefay emay orfay avinghay orfay oneyay omentmay istrustedday youyay.
Ywhay idday youyay onfesscay? Utbay oday otnay ournmay, earday irlgay. Oday otnay earfay. Iyay
illway oclaimpray, Iyay illway ovepray youryay innocenceyay. Iyay illway eltmay ethay onystay
eartshay ofyay youryay enemiesyay ybay ymay earstay andyay ayerspray. Youyay allshay otnay ieday!
Youyay, ymay ayfellowplay, ymay ompanioncay, ymay istersay, erishpay onyay ethay affoldscay!
Onay! Onay! Iyay evernay ouldcay urvivesay osay orriblehay ayay isfortunemay.”

Ustinejay ookshay erhay eadhay ournfullymay. i“ay oday otnay earfay otay ieday,” eshay aidsay;
at“thay angpay isyay astpay. Odgay aisesray ymay eaknessway andyay ivesgay emay ouragecay otay
endureyay ethay orstway. Iyay eavelay ayay adsay andyay itterbay orldway; andyay ifyay youyay ememberray
emay andyay inkthay ofyay emay asyay ofyay oneyay unjustlyyay ondemnedcay, Iyay amyay esignedray otay ethay
atefay awaitingyay emay. Earnlay omfray emay, earday adylay, otay ubmitsay inyay atiencepay otay
ethay illway ofyay eavenhay!”

Uringday isthay onversationcay Iyay adhay etiredray otay ayay ornercay ofyay ethay isonpray oomray,
erewhay Iyay ouldcay oncealcay ethay orridhay anguishyay atthay ossessedpay emay. Espairday!
Owhay aredday alktay ofyay atthay? Ethay oorpay ictimvay, owhay onyay ethay orrowmay asway otay asspay
ethay awfulyay oundarybay etweenbay ifelay andyay eathday, eltfay otnay, asyay Iyay idday, uchsay
eepday andyay itterbay agonyyay. Iyay ashedgnay ymay eethtay andyay oundgray emthay ogethertay,
utteringyay ayay oangray atthay amecay omfray ymay inmostyay oulsay. Ustinejay artedstay. Enwhay
eshay awsay owhay ityay asway, eshay approachedyay emay andyay aidsay, ear“day irsay, youyay areyay eryvay
indkay otay isitvay emay; youyay, Iyay opehay, oday otnay elievebay atthay Iyay amyay uiltygay?”

Iyay ouldcay otnay answeryay. o“nay, Ustinejay,” aidsay Elizabethyay; e“hay isyay oremay
onvincedcay ofyay youryay innocenceyay anthay Iyay asway, orfay evenyay enwhay ehay eardhay atthay youyay
adhay onfessedcay, ehay idday otnay editcray ityay.”

i“ay ulytray ankthay imhay. Inyay esethay astlay omentsmay Iyay eelfay ethay incerestsay
atitudegray owardstay osethay owhay inkthay ofyay emay ithway indnesskay. Owhay eetsway isyay
ethay affectionyay ofyay othersyay otay uchsay ayay etchwray asyay Iyay amyay! Ityay emovesray oremay anthay
alfhay ymay isfortunemay, andyay Iyay eelfay asyay ifyay Iyay ouldcay ieday inyay eacepay ownay atthay ymay
innocenceyay isyay acknowledgedyay ybay youyay, earday adylay, andyay youryay ousincay.”

Usthay ethay oorpay ufferersay iedtray otay omfortcay othersyay andyay erselfhay. Eshay indeedyay
ainedgay ethay esignationray eshay esiredday. Utbay Iyay, ethay uetray urderermay, eltfay ethay
ever-dyingnay ormway aliveyay inyay ymay osombay, ichwhay allowedyay ofyay onay opehay oryay
onsolationcay. Elizabethyay alsoyay eptway andyay asway unhappyyay, utbay ershay alsoyay asway
ethay iserymay ofyay innocenceyay, ichwhay, ikelay ayay oudclay atthay assespay overyay ethay airfay
oonmay, orfay ayay ilewhay ideshay utbay annotcay arnishtay itsyay ightnessbray. Anguishyay andyay
espairday adhay enetratedpay intoyay ethay orecay ofyay ymay earthay; Iyay orebay ayay ellhay ithinway
emay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay extinguishyay. Eway ayedstay everalsay ourshay ithway
Ustinejay, andyay ityay asway ithway eatgray ifficultyday atthay Elizabethyay ouldcay eartay
erselfhay awayyay. i“ay ishway,” iedcray eshay, at“thay Iyay ereway otay ieday ithway youyay; Iyay
annotcay ivelay inyay isthay orldway ofyay iserymay.”

Ustinejay assumedyay anyay airyay ofyay eerfulnesschay, ilewhay eshay ithway ifficultyday
epressedray erhay itterbay earstay. Eshay embracedyay Elizabethyay andyay aidsay inyay ayay oicevay
ofyay alf-suppressedhay emotionyay, arewell“fay, eetsway adylay, earestday Elizabethyay,
ymay elovedbay andyay onlyyay iendfray; aymay eavenhay, inyay itsyay ountybay, essblay andyay
eservepray youyay; aymay isthay ebay ethay astlay isfortunemay atthay youyay illway everyay
uffersay! Ivelay, andyay ebay appyhay, andyay akemay othersyay osay.”

Andyay onyay ethay orrowmay Ustinejay iedday. Elizabeth’syay eart-rendinghay eloquenceyay
ailedfay otay ovemay ethay udgesjay omfray eirthay ettledsay onvictioncay inyay ethay
iminalitycray ofyay ethay aintlysay ufferersay. Ymay assionatepay andyay indignantyay
appealsyay ereway ostlay uponyay emthay. Andyay enwhay Iyay eceivedray eirthay oldcay answersyay
andyay eardhay ethay arshhay, unfeelingyay easoningray ofyay esethay enmay, ymay urposedpay
avowalyay iedday awayyay onyay ymay ipslay. Usthay Iyay ightmay oclaimpray yselfmay ayay admanmay,
utbay otnay evokeray ethay entencesay assedpay uponyay ymay etchedwray ictimvay. Eshay
erishedpay onyay ethay affoldscay asyay ayay urderessmay!

Omfray ethay orturestay ofyay ymay ownyay earthay, Iyay urnedtay otay ontemplatecay ethay eepday andyay
oicelessvay iefgray ofyay ymay Elizabethyay. Isthay alsoyay asway ymay oingday! Andyay ymay
ather’sfay oeway, andyay ethay esolationday ofyay atthay atelay osay ilingsmay omehay allyay asway
ethay orkway ofyay ymay ice-accursedthray andshay! Yeyay eepway, unhappyyay onesyay, utbay esethay
areyay otnay youryay astlay earstay! Againyay allshay youyay aiseray ethay uneralfay ailway, andyay
ethay oundsay ofyay youryay amentationslay allshay againyay andyay againyay ebay eardhay!
Ankensteinfray, youryay onsay, youryay insmankay, youryay earlyyay, uch-lovedmay iendfray; ehay
owhay ouldway endspay eachyay italvay opdray ofyay oodblay orfay youryay akessay, owhay ashay onay
oughtthay ornay ensesay ofyay oyjay exceptyay asyay ityay isyay irroredmay alsoyay inyay youryay earday
ountenancescay, owhay ouldway illfay ethay airyay ithway essingsblay andyay endspay ishay ifelay
inyay ervingsay you—heyay idsbay youyay eepway, otay edshay ountlesscay earstay; appyhay eyondbay
ishay opeshay, ifyay usthay inexorableyay atefay ebay atisfiedsay, andyay ifyay ethay estructionday
ausepay eforebay ethay eacepay ofyay ethay avegray avehay ucceededsay otay youryay adsay ormentstay!

Usthay okespay ymay opheticpray oulsay, asyay, orntay ybay emorseray, orrorhay, andyay espairday,
Iyay eheldbay osethay Iyay ovedlay endspay ainvay orrowsay uponyay ethay avesgray ofyay Illiamway andyay
Ustinejay, ethay irstfay aplesshay ictimsvay otay ymay unhallowedyay artsyay.




Apterchay 9


Othingnay isyay oremay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay anthay, afteryay ethay eelingsfay avehay
eenbay orkedway upyay ybay ayay uickqay uccessionsay ofyay eventsyay, ethay eadday almnesscay ofyay
inactionyay andyay ertaintycay ichwhay ollowsfay andyay eprivesday ethay oulsay othbay ofyay opehay
andyay earfay. Ustinejay iedday, eshay estedray, andyay Iyay asway aliveyay. Ethay oodblay owedflay
eelyfray inyay ymay einsvay, utbay ayay eightway ofyay espairday andyay emorseray essedpray onyay ymay
earthay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay emoveray. Eepslay edflay omfray ymay eyesyay; Iyay anderedway
ikelay anyay evilyay iritspay, orfay Iyay adhay ommittedcay eedsday ofyay ischiefmay eyondbay
escriptionday orriblehay, andyay oremay, uchmay oremay i(ay ersuadedpay yselfmay) asway yetyay
ehindbay. Yetyay ymay earthay overflowedyay ithway indnesskay andyay ethay ovelay ofyay irtuevay.
Iyay adhay egunbay ifelay ithway enevolentbay intentionsyay andyay irstedthay orfay ethay omentmay
enwhay Iyay ouldshay utpay emthay inyay acticepray andyay akemay yselfmay usefulyay otay ymay ellowfay
eingsbay. Ownay allyay asway astedblay; insteadyay ofyay atthay erenitysay ofyay onsciencecay
ichwhay allowedyay emay otay ooklay ackbay uponyay ethay astpay ithway elf-satisfactionsay, andyay
omfray encethay otay athergay omisepray ofyay ewnay opeshay, Iyay asway eizedsay ybay emorseray andyay
ethay ensesay ofyay uiltgay, ichwhay urriedhay emay awayyay otay ayay ellhay ofyay intenseyay orturestay
uchsay asyay onay anguagelay ancay escribeday.

Isthay atestay ofyay indmay eyedpray uponyay ymay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay erhapspay evernay
entirelyyay ecoveredray omfray ethay irstfay ockshay ityay adhay ustainedsay. Iyay unnedshay
ethay acefay ofyay anmay; allyay oundsay ofyay oyjay oryay omplacencycay asway orturetay otay emay;
olitudesay asway ymay onlyyay onsolation—deepcay, arkday, eathlikeday olitudesay.

Ymay atherfay observedyay ithway ainpay ethay alterationyay erceptiblepay inyay ymay ispositionday
andyay abitshay andyay endeavouredyay ybay argumentsyay educedday omfray ethay eelingsfay ofyay ishay
erenesay onsciencecay andyay uiltlessgay ifelay otay inspireyay emay ithway ortitudefay andyay
awakenyay inyay emay ethay ouragecay otay ispelday ethay arkday oudclay ichwhay oodedbray overyay emay.
o“day youyay inkthay, Ictorvay,” aidsay ehay, at“thay Iyay oday otnay uffersay
alsoyay? Onay oneyay ouldcay ovelay ayay ildchay oremay anthay Iyay ovedlay youryay
other”—tearsbray amecay intoyay ishay eyesyay asyay ehay oke—“butspay
isyay ityay otnay ayay utyday otay ethay urvivorssay atthay eway ouldshay efrainray omfray augmentingyay
eirthay unhappinessyay ybay anyay appearanceyay ofyay immoderateyay iefgray? Ityay isyay alsoyay ayay utyday
owedyay otay yourselfyay, orfay excessiveyay orrowsay eventspray improvementyay oryay enjoymentyay,
oryay evenyay ethay ischargeday ofyay ailyday usefulnessyay, ithoutway ichwhay onay anmay isyay itfay orfay
ocietysay.”

Isthay adviceyay, althoughyay oodgay, asway otallytay inapplicableyay otay ymay asecay; Iyay
ouldshay avehay eenbay ethay irstfay otay idehay ymay iefgray andyay onsolecay ymay iendsfray ifyay
emorseray adhay otnay ingledmay itsyay itternessbay, andyay errortay itsyay alarmyay, ithway ymay
otheryay ensationssay. Ownay Iyay ouldcay onlyyay answeryay ymay atherfay ithway ayay ooklay ofyay
espairday andyay endeavouryay otay idehay yselfmay omfray ishay iewvay.

Aboutyay isthay imetay eway etiredray otay ouryay ousehay atyay Elrivebay. Isthay angechay asway
articularlypay agreeableyay otay emay. Ethay uttingshay ofyay ethay atesgay egularlyray atyay
entay o’clockyay andyay ethay impossibilityyay ofyay emainingray onyay ethay akelay afteryay atthay
ourhay adhay enderedray ouryay esidenceray ithinway ethay allsway ofyay Enevagay eryvay irksomeyay
otay emay. Iyay asway ownay eefray. Oftenyay, afteryay ethay estray ofyay ethay amilyfay adhay
etiredray orfay ethay ightnay, Iyay ooktay ethay oatbay andyay assedpay anymay ourshay uponyay ethay
aterway. Ometimessay, ithway ymay ailssay etsay, Iyay asway arriedcay ybay ethay indway; andyay
ometimessay, afteryay owingray intoyay ethay iddlemay ofyay ethay akelay, Iyay eftlay ethay oatbay otay
ursuepay itsyay ownyay oursecay andyay avegay ayway otay ymay ownyay iserablemay eflectionsray. Iyay
asway oftenyay emptedtay, enwhay allyay asway atyay eacepay aroundyay emay, andyay Iyay ethay onlyyay
unquietyay ingthay atthay anderedway estlessray inyay ayay enescay osay eautifulbay andyay
eavenly—ifhay Iyay exceptyay omesay atbay, oryay ethay ogsfray, osewhay arshhay andyay
interruptedyay oakingcray asway eardhay onlyyay enwhay Iyay approachedyay ethay ore—oftenshay,
Iyay aysay, Iyay asway emptedtay otay ungeplay intoyay ethay ilentsay akelay, atthay ethay atersway
ightmay oseclay overyay emay andyay ymay alamitiescay orfay everyay. Utbay Iyay asway estrainedray,
enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay eroichay andyay ufferingsay Elizabethyay, omwhay Iyay enderlytay
ovedlay, andyay osewhay existenceyay asway oundbay upyay inyay inemay. Iyay oughtthay alsoyay ofyay ymay
atherfay andyay urvivingsay otherbray; ouldshay Iyay ybay ymay asebay esertionday eavelay emthay
exposedyay andyay unprotectedyay otay ethay alicemay ofyay ethay iendfay omwhay Iyay adhay etlay ooselay
amongyay emthay?

Atyay esethay omentsmay Iyay eptway itterlybay andyay ishedway atthay eacepay ouldway evisitray ymay
indmay onlyyay atthay Iyay ightmay affordyay emthay onsolationcay andyay appinesshay. Utbay atthay
ouldcay otnay ebay. Emorseray extinguishedyay everyyay opehay. Iyay adhay eenbay ethay authoryay ofyay
unalterableyay evilsyay, andyay Iyay ivedlay inyay ailyday earfay estlay ethay onstermay omwhay Iyay adhay
eatedcray ouldshay erpetratepay omesay ewnay ickednessway. Iyay adhay anyay obscureyay eelingfay
atthay allyay asway otnay overyay andyay atthay ehay ouldway illstay ommitcay omesay ignalsay imecray,
ichwhay ybay itsyay enormityyay ouldshay almostyay effaceyay ethay ecollectionray ofyay ethay astpay.
Erethay asway alwaysyay opescay orfay earfay osay onglay asyay anythingyay Iyay ovedlay emainedray
ehindbay. Ymay abhorrenceyay ofyay isthay iendfay annotcay ebay onceivedcay. Enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay
imhay Iyay ashedgnay ymay eethtay, ymay eyesyay ecamebay inflamedyay, andyay Iyay ardentlyyay ishedway otay
extinguishyay atthay ifelay ichwhay Iyay adhay osay oughtlesslythay estowedbay. Enwhay Iyay
eflectedray onyay ishay imescray andyay alicemay, ymay atredhay andyay evengeray urstbay allyay oundsbay
ofyay oderationmay. Iyay ouldway avehay ademay ayay ilgrimagepay otay ethay ighesthay eakpay ofyay ethay
Andesyay, ouldcay Iyay, enwhay erethay, avehay ecipitatedpray imhay otay eirthay asebay. Iyay ishedway
otay eesay imhay againyay, atthay Iyay ightmay eakwray ethay utmostyay extentyay ofyay abhorrenceyay onyay ishay
eadhay andyay avengeyay ethay eathsday ofyay Illiamway andyay Ustinejay.

Ouryay ousehay asway ethay ousehay ofyay ourningmay. Ymay ather’sfay ealthhay asway eeplyday
akenshay ybay ethay orrorhay ofyay ethay ecentray eventsyay. Elizabethyay asway adsay andyay
espondingday; eshay onay ongerlay ooktay elightday inyay erhay ordinaryyay occupationsyay; allyay
easureplay eemedsay otay erhay acrilegesay owardtay ethay eadday; eternalyay oeway andyay earstay eshay
enthay oughtthay asway ethay ustjay ibutetray eshay ouldshay aypay otay innocenceyay osay astedblay
andyay estroyedday. Eshay asway onay ongerlay atthay appyhay eaturecray owhay inyay earlieryay youthyay
anderedway ithway emay onyay ethay anksbay ofyay ethay akelay andyay alkedtay ithway ecstasyyay ofyay ouryay
uturefay ospectspray. Ethay irstfay ofyay osethay orrowssay ichwhay areyay entsay otay eanway usyay omfray
ethay earthyay adhay isitedvay erhay, andyay itsyay immingday influenceyay uenchedqay erhay earestday
ilessmay.

en“whay Iyay eflectray, ymay earday ousincay,” aidsay eshay, on“ay ethay iserablemay eathday ofyay
Ustinejay Oritzmay, Iyay onay ongerlay eesay ethay orldway andyay itsyay orksway asyay eythay eforebay
appearedyay otay emay. Eforebay, Iyay ookedlay uponyay ethay accountsyay ofyay icevay andyay
injusticeyay atthay Iyay eadray inyay ooksbay oryay eardhay omfray othersyay asyay alestay ofyay ancientyay
aysday oryay imaginaryyay evilsyay; atyay eastlay eythay ereway emoteray andyay oremay amiliarfay otay
easonray anthay otay ethay imaginationyay; utbay ownay iserymay ashay omecay omehay, andyay enmay
appearyay otay emay asyay onstersmay irstingthay orfay eachyay other’syay oodblay. Yetyay Iyay amyay
ertainlycay unjustyay. Everybodyyay elievedbay atthay oorpay irlgay otay ebay uiltygay; andyay
ifyay eshay ouldcay avehay ommittedcay ethay imecray orfay ichwhay eshay ufferedsay, assuredlyyay
eshay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay ostmay epravedday ofyay umanhay eaturescray. Orfay ethay akesay
ofyay ayay ewfay ewelsjay, otay avehay urderedmay ethay onsay ofyay erhay enefactorbay andyay iendfray,
ayay ildchay omwhay eshay adhay ursednay omfray itsyay irthbay, andyay appearedyay otay ovelay asyay ifyay
ityay adhay eenbay erhay ownyay! Iyay ouldcay otnay onsentcay otay ethay eathday ofyay anyyay umanhay
eingbay, utbay ertainlycay Iyay ouldshay avehay oughtthay uchsay ayay eaturecray unfityay otay
emainray inyay ethay ocietysay ofyay enmay. Utbay eshay asway innocentyay. Iyay owknay, Iyay eelfay
eshay asway innocentyay; youyay areyay ofyay ethay amesay opinionyay, andyay atthay onfirmscay emay.
Alasyay! Ictorvay, enwhay alsehoodfay ancay ooklay osay ikelay ethay uthtray, owhay ancay
assureyay emselvesthay ofyay ertaincay appinesshay? Iyay eelfay asyay ifyay Iyay ereway alkingway onyay
ethay edgeyay ofyay ayay ecipicepray, owardstay ichwhay ousandsthay areyay owdingcray andyay
endeavouringyay otay ungeplay emay intoyay ethay abyssyay. Illiamway andyay Ustinejay ereway
assassinatedyay, andyay ethay urderermay escapesyay; ehay alksway aboutyay ethay orldway eefray,
andyay erhapspay espectedray. Utbay evenyay ifyay Iyay ereway ondemnedcay otay uffersay onyay ethay
affoldscay orfay ethay amesay imescray, Iyay ouldway otnay angechay acesplay ithway uchsay ayay
etchwray.”

Iyay istenedlay otay isthay iscourseday ithway ethay extremestyay agonyyay. Iyay, otnay inyay eedday,
utbay inyay effectyay, asway ethay uetray urderermay. Elizabethyay eadray ymay anguishyay inyay ymay
ountenancecay, andyay indlykay akingtay ymay andhay, aidsay, y“may earestday iendfray, youyay
ustmay almcay yourselfyay. Esethay eventsyay avehay affectedyay emay, Odgay owsknay owhay
eeplyday; utbay Iyay amyay otnay osay etchedwray asyay youyay areyay. Erethay isyay anyay expressionyay ofyay
espairday, andyay ometimessay ofyay evengeray, inyay youryay ountenancecay atthay akesmay emay
embletray. Earday Ictorvay, anishbay esethay arkday assionspay. Ememberray ethay
iendsfray aroundyay youyay, owhay entrecay allyay eirthay opeshay inyay youyay. Avehay eway ostlay
ethay owerpay ofyay enderingray youyay appyhay? Ahyay! Ilewhay eway ovelay, ilewhay eway areyay
uetray otay eachyay otheryay, erehay inyay isthay andlay ofyay eacepay andyay eautybay, youryay ativenay
ountrycay, eway aymay eapray everyyay anquiltray essing—whatblay ancay isturbday ouryay
eacepay?”

Andyay ouldcay otnay uchsay ordsway omfray erhay omwhay Iyay ondlyfay izedpray eforebay everyyay
otheryay iftgay ofyay ortunefay ufficesay otay asechay awayyay ethay iendfay atthay urkedlay inyay ymay
earthay? Evenyay asyay eshay okespay Iyay ewdray earnay otay erhay, asyay ifyay inyay errortay, estlay atyay
atthay eryvay omentmay ethay estroyerday adhay eenbay earnay otay obray emay ofyay erhay.

Usthay otnay ethay endernesstay ofyay iendshipfray, ornay ethay eautybay ofyay earthyay, ornay ofyay
eavenhay, ouldcay edeemray ymay oulsay omfray oeway; ethay eryvay accentsyay ofyay ovelay ereway
ineffectualyay. Iyay asway encompassedyay ybay ayay oudclay ichwhay onay eneficialbay
influenceyay ouldcay enetratepay. Ethay oundedway eerday aggingdray itsyay aintingfay
imbslay otay omesay untroddenyay akebray, erethay otay azegay uponyay ethay arrowyay ichwhay adhay
iercedpay ityay, andyay otay ieday, asway utbay ayay ypetay ofyay emay.

Ometimessay Iyay ouldcay opecay ithway ethay ullensay espairday atthay overwhelmedyay emay, utbay
ometimessay ethay irlwindwhay assionspay ofyay ymay oulsay ovedray emay otay eeksay, ybay odilybay
exerciseyay andyay ybay angechay ofyay aceplay, omesay eliefray omfray ymay intolerableyay
ensationssay. Ityay asway uringday anyay accessyay ofyay isthay indkay atthay Iyay uddenlysay eftlay
ymay omehay, andyay endingbay ymay epsstay owardstay ethay earnay Alpineyay alleysvay, oughtsay
inyay ethay agnificencemay, ethay eternityyay ofyay uchsay enesscay, otay orgetfay yselfmay andyay
ymay ephemeralyay, ecausebay umanhay, orrowssay. Ymay anderingsway ereway irectedday
owardstay ethay alleyvay ofyay Amounixchay. Iyay adhay isitedvay ityay equentlyfray uringday ymay
oyhoodbay. Ixsay yearsyay adhay assedpay incesay enthay: i_ay_ asway ayay eckwray, utbay oughtnay
adhay angedchay inyay osethay avagesay andyay enduringyay enesscay.

Iyay erformedpay ethay irstfay artpay ofyay ymay ourneyjay onyay orsebackhay. Iyay afterwardsyay
iredhay ayay ulemay, asyay ethay oremay ure-footedsay andyay eastlay iablelay otay eceiveray
injuryyay onyay esethay uggedray oadsray. Ethay eatherway asway inefay; ityay asway aboutyay ethay
iddlemay ofyay ethay onthmay ofyay Augustyay, earlynay otway onthsmay afteryay ethay eathday ofyay
Ustinejay, atthay iserablemay epochyay omfray ichwhay Iyay atedday allyay ymay oeway. Ethay
eightway uponyay ymay iritspay asway ensiblysay ightenedlay asyay Iyay ungedplay yetyay eeperday inyay
ethay avineray ofyay Arveyay. Ethay immenseyay ountainsmay andyay ecipicespray atthay overhungyay
emay onyay everyyay idesay, ethay oundsay ofyay ethay iverray agingray amongyay ethay ocksray, andyay
ethay ashingday ofyay ethay aterfallsway aroundyay okespay ofyay ayay owerpay ightymay asyay
Omnipotence—andyay Iyay easedcay otay earfay oryay otay endbay eforebay anyyay eingbay esslay
almightyyay anthay atthay ichwhay adhay eatedcray andyay uledray ethay elementsyay, erehay
isplayedday inyay eirthay ostmay errifictay uisegay. Illstay, asyay Iyay ascendedyay igherhay,
ethay alleyvay assumedyay ayay oremay agnificentmay andyay astonishingyay aracterchay.
Uinedray astlescay anginghay onyay ethay ecipicespray ofyay inypay ountainsmay, ethay
impetuousyay Arveyay, andyay ottagescay everyyay erehay andyay erethay eepingpay orthfay omfray
amongyay ethay eestray ormedfay ayay enescay ofyay ingularsay eautybay. Utbay ityay asway
augmentedyay andyay enderedray ublimesay ybay ethay ightymay Alpsyay, osewhay itewhay andyay
iningshay yramidspay andyay omesday oweredtay aboveyay allyay, asyay elongingbay otay anotheryay
earthyay, ethay abitationshay ofyay anotheryay aceray ofyay eingsbay.

Iyay assedpay ethay idgebray ofyay Issierpélay, erewhay ethay avineray, ichwhay ethay iverray
ormsfay, openedyay eforebay emay, andyay Iyay eganbay otay ascendyay ethay ountainmay atthay
overhangsyay ityay. Oonsay afteryay, Iyay enteredyay ethay alleyvay ofyay Amounixchay. Isthay
alleyvay isyay oremay onderfulway andyay ublimesay, utbay otnay osay eautifulbay andyay
icturesquepay asyay atthay ofyay Ervoxsay, oughthray ichwhay Iyay adhay ustjay assedpay. Ethay
ighhay andyay owysnay ountainsmay ereway itsyay immediateyay oundariesbay, utbay Iyay awsay onay
oremay uinedray astlescay andyay ertilefay ieldsfay. Immenseyay aciersglay approachedyay
ethay oadray; Iyay eardhay ethay umblingray underthay ofyay ethay allingfay avalancheyay andyay
arkedmay ethay okesmay ofyay itsyay assagepay. Ontmay Ancblay, ethay upremesay andyay
agnificentmay Ontmay Ancblay, aisedray itselfyay omfray ethay urroundingsay aiguilles_ay_,
andyay itsyay emendoustray e_dômay_ overlookedyay ethay alleyvay.

Ayay inglingtay ong-lostlay ensesay ofyay easureplay oftenyay amecay acrossyay emay uringday isthay
ourneyjay. Omesay urntay inyay ethay oadray, omesay ewnay objectyay uddenlysay erceivedpay andyay
ecognisedray, emindedray emay ofyay aysday onegay ybay, andyay ereway associatedyay ithway ethay
ightheartedlay aietygay ofyay oyhoodbay. Ethay eryvay indsway isperedwhay inyay oothingsay
accentsyay, andyay aternalmay Aturenay adebay emay eepway onay oremay. Enthay againyay ethay
indlykay influenceyay easedcay otay act—iyay oundfay yselfmay etteredfay againyay otay iefgray
andyay indulgingyay inyay allyay ethay iserymay ofyay eflectionray. Enthay Iyay urredspay onyay ymay
animalyay, ivingstray osay otay orgetfay ethay orldway, ymay earsfay, andyay oremay anthay allyay,
yself—ormay, inyay ayay oremay esperateday ashionfay, Iyay alightedyay andyay ewthray yselfmay onyay
ethay assgray, eighedway ownday ybay orrorhay andyay espairday.

Atyay engthlay Iyay arrivedyay atyay ethay illagevay ofyay Amounixchay. Exhaustionyay ucceededsay
otay ethay extremeyay atiguefay othbay ofyay odybay andyay ofyay indmay ichwhay Iyay adhay enduredyay.
Orfay ayay ortshay acespay ofyay imetay Iyay emainedray atyay ethay indowway atchingway ethay allidpay
ightningslay atthay ayedplay aboveyay Ontmay Ancblay andyay isteninglay otay ethay ushingray ofyay
ethay Arveyay, ichwhay ursuedpay itsyay oisynay ayway eneathbay. Ethay amesay ullinglay oundssay
actedyay asyay ayay ullabylay otay ymay ootay eenkay ensationssay; enwhay Iyay acedplay ymay eadhay
uponyay ymay illowpay, eepslay eptcray overyay emay; Iyay eltfay ityay asyay ityay amecay andyay essedblay
ethay ivergay ofyay oblivionyay.




Apterchay 10


Iyay entspay ethay ollowingfay ayday oamingray oughthray ethay alleyvay. Iyay oodstay esidebay
ethay ourcessay ofyay ethay Arveironyay, ichwhay aketay eirthay iseray inyay ayay acierglay, atthay
ithway owslay acepay isyay advancingyay ownday omfray ethay ummitsay ofyay ethay illshay otay
arricadebay ethay alleyvay. Ethay abruptyay idessay ofyay astvay ountainsmay ereway eforebay
emay; ethay icyyay allway ofyay ethay acierglay overhungyay emay; ayay ewfay atteredshay inespay ereway
atteredscay aroundyay; andyay ethay olemnsay ilencesay ofyay isthay oriousglay
esence-chamberpray ofyay imperialyay Aturenay asway okenbray onlyyay ybay ethay awlingbray
avesway oryay ethay allfay ofyay omesay astvay agmentfray, ethay underthay oundsay ofyay ethay
avalancheyay oryay ethay ackingcray, everberatedray alongyay ethay ountainsmay, ofyay ethay
accumulatedyay iceyay, ichwhay, oughthray ethay ilentsay orkingway ofyay immutableyay awslay,
asway everyay andyay anonyay entray andyay orntay, asyay ifyay ityay adhay eenbay utbay ayay aythingplay inyay
eirthay andshay. Esethay ublimesay andyay agnificentmay enesscay affordedyay emay ethay
eatestgray onsolationcay atthay Iyay asway apablecay ofyay eceivingray. Eythay elevatedyay emay
omfray allyay ittlenesslay ofyay eelingfay, andyay althoughyay eythay idday otnay emoveray ymay
iefgray, eythay ubduedsay andyay anquillisedtray ityay. Inyay omesay egreeday, alsoyay, eythay
ivertedday ymay indmay omfray ethay oughtsthay overyay ichwhay ityay adhay oodedbray orfay ethay
astlay onthmay. Iyay etiredray otay estray atyay ightnay; ymay umbersslay, asyay ityay ereway,
aitedway onyay andyay inisteredmay otay ybay ethay assemblanceyay ofyay andgray apesshay ichwhay Iyay
adhay ontemplatedcay uringday ethay ayday. Eythay ongregatedcay oundray emay; ethay
unstainedyay owysnay ountain-topmay, ethay itteringglay innaclepay, ethay inepay oodsway,
andyay aggedray arebay avineray, ethay eagleyay, oaringsay amidstyay ethay ouds—theyclay allyay
atheredgay oundray emay andyay adebay emay ebay atyay eacepay.

Erewhay adhay eythay edflay enwhay ethay extnay orningmay Iyay awokeyay? Allyay ofyay
oul-inspiritingsay edflay ithway eepslay, andyay arkday elancholymay oudedclay everyyay
oughtthay. Ethay ainray asway ouringpay inyay orrentstay, andyay ickthay istsmay idhay ethay
ummitssay ofyay ethay ountainsmay, osay atthay Iyay evenyay awsay otnay ethay acesfay ofyay osethay
ightymay iendsfray. Illstay Iyay ouldway enetratepay eirthay istymay eilvay andyay eeksay emthay
inyay eirthay oudyclay etreatsray. Atwhay ereway ainray andyay ormstay otay emay? Ymay ulemay asway
oughtbray otay ethay oorday, andyay Iyay esolvedray otay ascendyay otay ethay ummitsay ofyay
Ontanvertmay. Iyay ememberedray ethay effectyay atthay ethay iewvay ofyay ethay emendoustray
andyay ever-movingyay acierglay adhay oducedpray uponyay ymay indmay enwhay Iyay irstfay awsay ityay.
Ityay adhay enthay illedfay emay ithway ayay ublimesay ecstasyyay atthay avegay ingsway otay ethay
oulsay andyay allowedyay ityay otay oarsay omfray ethay obscureyay orldway otay ightlay andyay oyjay.
Ethay ightsay ofyay ethay awfulyay andyay ajesticmay inyay aturenay adhay indeedyay alwaysyay ethay
effectyay ofyay olemnisingsay ymay indmay andyay ausingcay emay otay orgetfay ethay assingpay
arescay ofyay ifelay. Iyay eterminedday otay ogay ithoutway ayay uidegay, orfay Iyay asway ellway
acquaintedyay ithway ethay athpay, andyay ethay esencepray ofyay anotheryay ouldway estroyday ethay
olitarysay andeurgray ofyay ethay enescay.

Ethay ascentyay isyay ecipitouspray, utbay ethay athpay isyay utcay intoyay ontinualcay andyay ortshay
indingsway, ichwhay enableyay youyay otay urmountsay ethay erpendicularitypay ofyay ethay
ountainmay. Ityay isyay ayay enescay errificallytay esolateday. Inyay ayay ousandthay otsspay
ethay acestray ofyay ethay interway avalancheyay aymay ebay erceivedpay, erewhay eestray ielay
okenbray andyay ewedstray onyay ethay oundgray, omesay entirelyyay estroyedday, othersyay entbay,
eaninglay uponyay ethay uttingjay ocksray ofyay ethay ountainmay oryay ansverselytray uponyay
otheryay eestray. Ethay athpay, asyay youyay ascendyay igherhay, isyay intersectedyay ybay avinesray
ofyay owsnay, ownday ichwhay onesstay ontinuallycay ollray omfray aboveyay; oneyay ofyay emthay isyay
articularlypay angerousday, asyay ethay ightestslay oundsay, uchsay asyay evenyay eakingspay
inyay ayay oudlay oicevay, oducespray ayay oncussioncay ofyay airyay ufficientsay otay awdray
estructionday uponyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay eakerspay. Ethay inespay areyay otnay alltay oryay
uxuriantlay, utbay eythay areyay ombresay andyay addyay anyay airyay ofyay everitysay otay ethay enescay.
Iyay ookedlay onyay ethay alleyvay eneathbay; astvay istsmay ereway isingray omfray ethay iversray
ichwhay anray oughthray ityay andyay urlingcay inyay ickthay eathswray aroundyay ethay oppositeyay
ountainsmay, osewhay ummitssay ereway idhay inyay ethay uniformyay oudsclay, ilewhay ainray
ouredpay omfray ethay arkday yskay andyay addedyay otay ethay elancholymay impressionyay Iyay
eceivedray omfray ethay objectsyay aroundyay emay. Alasyay! Ywhay oesday anmay oastbay ofyay
ensibilitiessay uperiorsay otay osethay apparentyay inyay ethay utebray; ityay onlyyay endersray
emthay oremay ecessarynay eingsbay. Ifyay ouryay impulsesyay ereway onfinedcay otay ungerhay,
irstthay, andyay esireday, eway ightmay ebay earlynay eefray; utbay ownay eway areyay ovedmay ybay
everyyay indway atthay owsblay andyay ayay ancechay ordway oryay enescay atthay atthay ordway aymay
onveycay otay usyay.

  Eway estray; ayay eamdray ashay owerpay otay oisonpay eepslay.
     Eway iseray; oneyay and’ringway oughtthay ollutespay ethay ayday.
  Eway eelfay, onceivecay, oryay easonray; aughlay oryay eepway,
     Embraceyay ondfay oeway, oryay astcay ouryay arescay awayyay;
  Ityay isyay ethay amesay: orfay, ebay ityay oyjay oryay orrowsay,
     Ethay athpay ofyay itsyay epartureday illstay isyay eefray.
  An’smay yesterdayyay aymay e’ernay ebay ikelay ishay orrowmay;
     Oughtnay aymay endureyay utbay utabilitymay!


Ityay asway earlynay oonnay enwhay Iyay arrivedyay atyay ethay optay ofyay ethay ascentyay. Orfay omesay
imetay Iyay atsay uponyay ethay ockray atthay overlooksyay ethay easay ofyay iceyay. Ayay istmay overedcay
othbay atthay andyay ethay urroundingsay ountainsmay. Esentlypray ayay eezebray issipatedday
ethay oudclay, andyay Iyay escendedday uponyay ethay acierglay. Ethay urfacesay isyay eryvay
unevenyay, isingray ikelay ethay avesway ofyay ayay oubledtray easay, escendingday owlay, andyay
interspersedyay ybay iftsray atthay inksay eepday. Ethay ieldfay ofyay iceyay isyay almostyay ayay
eaguelay inyay idthway, utbay Iyay entspay earlynay otway ourshay inyay ossingcray ityay. Ethay
oppositeyay ountainmay isyay ayay arebay erpendicularpay ockray. Omfray ethay idesay erewhay Iyay
ownay oodstay Ontanvertmay asway exactlyyay oppositeyay, atyay ethay istanceday ofyay ayay eaguelay;
andyay aboveyay ityay oseray Ontmay Ancblay, inyay awfulyay ajestymay. Iyay emainedray inyay ayay ecessray
ofyay ethay ockray, azinggay onyay isthay onderfulway andyay upendousstay enescay. Ethay easay,
oryay atherray ethay astvay iverray ofyay iceyay, oundway amongyay itsyay ependentday ountainsmay,
osewhay aerialyay ummitssay unghay overyay itsyay ecessesray. Eirthay icyyay andyay itteringglay
eakspay oneshay inyay ethay unlightsay overyay ethay oudsclay. Ymay earthay, ichwhay asway
eforebay orrowfulsay, ownay elledsway ithway omethingsay ikelay oyjay; Iyay exclaimedyay,
andering“way iritsspay, ifyay indeedyay yeyay anderway, andyay oday otnay estray inyay youryay arrownay
edsbay, allowyay emay isthay aintfay appinesshay, oryay aketay emay, asyay youryay ompanioncay,
awayyay omfray ethay oysjay ofyay ifelay.”

Asyay Iyay aidsay isthay Iyay uddenlysay eheldbay ethay igurefay ofyay ayay anmay, atyay omesay istanceday,
advancingyay owardstay emay ithway uperhumansay eedspay. Ehay oundedbay overyay ethay
evicescray inyay ethay iceyay, amongyay ichwhay Iyay adhay alkedway ithway autioncay; ishay
aturestay, alsoyay, asyay ehay approachedyay, eemedsay otay exceedyay atthay ofyay anmay. Iyay asway
oubledtray; ayay istmay amecay overyay ymay eyesyay, andyay Iyay eltfay ayay aintnessfay eizesay emay,
utbay Iyay asway uicklyqay estoredray ybay ethay oldcay alegay ofyay ethay ountainsmay. Iyay
erceivedpay, asyay ethay apeshay amecay earernay ight(say emendoustray andyay abhorredyay!)
atthay ityay asway ethay etchwray omwhay Iyay adhay eatedcray. Iyay embledtray ithway ageray andyay
orrorhay, esolvingray otay aitway ishay approachyay andyay enthay oseclay ithway imhay inyay
ortalmay ombatcay. Ehay approachedyay; ishay ountenancecay espokebay itterbay anguishyay,
ombinedcay ithway isdainday andyay alignitymay, ilewhay itsyay unearthlyyay uglinessyay
enderedray ityay almostyay ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesyay. Utbay Iyay arcelyscay
observedyay isthay; ageray andyay atredhay adhay atyay irstfay eprivedday emay ofyay utteranceyay,
andyay Iyay ecoveredray onlyyay otay overwhelmyay imhay ithway ordsway expressiveyay ofyay uriousfay
etestationday andyay ontemptcay.

evil“day,” Iyay exclaimedyay, o“day youyay areday approachyay emay? Andyay oday
otnay youyay earfay ethay iercefay engeancevay ofyay ymay armyay eakedwray onyay youryay iserablemay eadhay?
Egonebay, ilevay insectyay! Oryay atherray, aystay, atthay Iyay aymay ampletray youyay otay ustday! Andyay,
ohyay! Atthay Iyay ouldcay, ithway ethay extinctionyay ofyay youryay iserablemay existenceyay, estoreray
osethay ictimsvay omwhay youyay avehay osay iabolicallyday urderedmay!”

i“ay expectedyay isthay eceptionray,” aidsay ethay ondæmay. all“ay enmay atehay ethay
etchedwray; owhay, enthay, ustmay Iyay ebay atedhay, owhay amyay iserablemay eyondbay allyay
ivinglay ingsthay! Yetyay youyay, ymay eatorcray, etestday andyay urnspay emay, ythay eaturecray,
otay omwhay outhay artyay oundbay ybay iestay onlyyay issolubleday ybay ethay annihilationyay ofyay
oneyay ofyay usyay. Youyay urposepay otay illkay emay. Owhay areday youyay ortspay usthay ithway ifelay?
Oday youryay utyday owardstay emay, andyay Iyay illway oday inemay owardstay youyay andyay ethay estray ofyay
ankindmay. Ifyay youyay illway omplycay ithway ymay onditionscay, Iyay illway eavelay emthay andyay
youyay atyay eacepay; utbay ifyay youyay efuseray, Iyay illway utglay ethay awmay ofyay eathday, untilyay ityay
ebay atiatedsay ithway ethay oodblay ofyay youryay emainingray iendsfray.”

abhorred“ay onstermay! Iendfay atthay outhay artyay! Ethay orturestay ofyay ellhay areyay ootay
ildmay ayay engeancevay orfay ythay imescray. Etchedwray evilday! Youyay eproachray emay ithway
youryay eationcray, omecay onyay, enthay, atthay Iyay aymay extinguishyay ethay arkspay ichwhay Iyay
osay egligentlynay estowedbay.”

Ymay ageray asway ithoutway oundsbay; Iyay angspray onyay imhay, impelledyay ybay allyay ethay
eelingsfay ichwhay ancay armyay oneyay eingbay againstyay ethay existenceyay ofyay anotheryay.

Ehay easilyyay eludedyay emay andyay aidsay,

e“bay almcay! Iyay entreatyay youyay otay earhay emay eforebay youyay ivegay entvay otay youryay atredhay
onyay ymay evotedday eadhay. Avehay Iyay otnay ufferedsay enoughyay, atthay youyay eeksay otay
increaseyay ymay iserymay? Ifelay, althoughyay ityay aymay onlyyay ebay anyay accumulationyay ofyay
anguishyay, isyay earday otay emay, andyay Iyay illway efendday ityay. Ememberray, outhay asthay ademay
emay oremay owerfulpay anthay yselfthay; ymay eighthay isyay uperiorsay otay inethay, ymay
ointsjay oremay upplesay. Utbay Iyay illway otnay ebay emptedtay otay etsay yselfmay inyay
oppositionyay otay eethay. Iyay amyay ythay eaturecray, andyay Iyay illway ebay evenyay ildmay andyay
