ocileday otay ymay aturalnay ordlay andyay ingkay ifyay outhay iltway alsoyay erformpay ythay artpay,
ethay ichwhay outhay owestyay emay. Ohyay, Ankensteinfray, ebay otnay equitableyay otay everyyay
otheryay andyay ampletray uponyay emay aloneyay, otay omwhay ythay usticejay, andyay evenyay ythay
emencyclay andyay affectionyay, isyay ostmay ueday. Ememberray atthay Iyay amyay ythay eaturecray;
Iyay oughtyay otay ebay ythay Adamyay, utbay Iyay amyay atherray ethay allenfay angelyay, omwhay outhay
ivestdray omfray oyjay orfay onay isdeedmay. Everywhereyay Iyay eesay issblay, omfray ichwhay Iyay
aloneyay amyay irrevocablyyay excludedyay. Iyay asway enevolentbay andyay oodgay; iserymay ademay
emay ayay iendfay. Akemay emay appyhay, andyay Iyay allshay againyay ebay irtuousvay.”

egone“bay! Iyay illway otnay earhay youyay. Erethay ancay ebay onay ommunitycay etweenbay youyay
andyay emay; eway areyay enemiesyay. Egonebay, oryay etlay usyay ytray ouryay engthstray inyay ayay ightfay,
inyay ichwhay oneyay ustmay allfay.”

ow“hay ancay Iyay ovemay eethay? Illway onay entreatiesyay ausecay eethay otay urntay ayay
avourablefay eyeyay uponyay ythay eaturecray, owhay imploresyay ythay oodnessgay andyay
ompassioncay? Elievebay emay, Ankensteinfray, Iyay asway enevolentbay; ymay oulsay owedglay
ithway ovelay andyay umanityhay; utbay amyay Iyay otnay aloneyay, iserablymay aloneyay? Youyay, ymay
eatorcray, abhoryay emay; atwhay opehay ancay Iyay athergay omfray youryay ellowfay eaturescray,
owhay oweyay emay othingnay? Eythay urnspay andyay atehay emay. Ethay esertday ountainsmay andyay
earydray aciersglay areyay ymay efugeray. Iyay avehay anderedway erehay anymay aysday; ethay
avescay ofyay iceyay, ichwhay Iyay onlyyay oday otnay earfay, areyay ayay ellingdway otay emay, andyay ethay
onlyyay oneyay ichwhay anmay oesday otnay udgegray. Esethay eakblay iesskay Iyay ailhay, orfay eythay
areyay inderkay otay emay anthay youryay ellowfay eingsbay. Ifyay ethay ultitudemay ofyay ankindmay
ewknay ofyay ymay existenceyay, eythay ouldway oday asyay youyay oday, andyay armyay emselvesthay orfay
ymay estructionday. Allshay Iyay otnay enthay atehay emthay owhay abhoryay emay? Iyay illway eepkay
onay ermstay ithway ymay enemiesyay. Iyay amyay iserablemay, andyay eythay allshay areshay ymay
etchednesswray. Yetyay ityay isyay inyay youryay owerpay otay ecompenseray emay, andyay eliverday
emthay omfray anyay evilyay ichwhay ityay onlyyay emainsray orfay youyay otay akemay osay eatgray, atthay
otnay onlyyay youyay andyay youryay amilyfay, utbay ousandsthay ofyay othersyay, allshay ebay
allowedsway upyay inyay ethay irlwindswhay ofyay itsyay ageray. Etlay youryay ompassioncay ebay
ovedmay, andyay oday otnay isdainday emay. Istenlay otay ymay aletay; enwhay youyay avehay eardhay
atthay, abandonyay oryay ommiseratecay emay, asyay youyay allshay udgejay atthay Iyay eserveday.
Utbay earhay emay. Ethay uiltygay areyay allowedyay, ybay umanhay awslay, oodyblay asyay eythay
areyay, otay eakspay inyay eirthay ownyay efenceday eforebay eythay areyay ondemnedcay. Istenlay
otay emay, Ankensteinfray. Youyay accuseyay emay ofyay urdermay, andyay yetyay youyay ouldway, ithway
ayay atisfiedsay onsciencecay, estroyday youryay ownyay eaturecray. Ohyay, aisepray ethay
eternalyay usticejay ofyay anmay! Yetyay Iyay askyay youyay otnay otay arespay emay; istenlay otay emay,
andyay enthay, ifyay youyay ancay, andyay ifyay youyay illway, estroyday ethay orkway ofyay youryay andshay.”

y“whay oday youyay allcay otay ymay emembranceray,” Iyay ejoinedray, ircumstances“cay ofyay
ichwhay Iyay uddershay otay eflectray, atthay Iyay avehay eenbay ethay iserablemay originyay andyay
authoryay? Ursedcay ebay ethay ayday, abhorredyay evilday, inyay ichwhay youyay irstfay awsay
ightlay! Ursedcay although(ay Iyay ursecay yselfmay) ebay ethay andshay atthay ormedfay youyay!
Youyay avehay ademay emay etchedwray eyondbay expressionyay. Youyay avehay eftlay emay onay owerpay
otay onsidercay etherwhay Iyay amyay ustjay otay youyay oryay otnay. Egonebay! Elieveray emay omfray
ethay ightsay ofyay youryay etestedday ormfay.”

us“thay Iyay elieveray eethay, ymay eatorcray,” ehay aidsay, andyay acedplay ishay atedhay andshay
eforebay ymay eyesyay, ichwhay Iyay ungflay omfray emay ithway iolencevay; us“thay Iyay aketay omfray
eethay ayay ightsay ichwhay youyay abhoryay. Illstay outhay anstcay istenlay otay emay andyay antgray
emay ythay ompassioncay. Ybay ethay irtuesvay atthay Iyay onceyay ossessedpay, Iyay emandday isthay
omfray youyay. Earhay ymay aletay; ityay isyay onglay andyay angestray, andyay ethay emperaturetay ofyay
isthay aceplay isyay otnay ittingfay otay youryay inefay ensationssay; omecay otay ethay uthay uponyay
ethay ountainmay. Ethay unsay isyay yetyay ighhay inyay ethay eavenshay; eforebay ityay escendsday
otay idehay itselfyay ehindbay youryay owysnay ecipicespray andyay illuminateyay anotheryay
orldway, youyay illway avehay eardhay ymay orystay andyay ancay ecideday. Onyay youyay ityay estsray,
etherwhay Iyay uitqay orfay everyay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay anmay andyay eadlay ayay armlesshay
ifelay, oryay ecomebay ethay ourgescay ofyay youryay ellowfay eaturescray andyay ethay authoryay ofyay
youryay ownyay eedyspay uinray.”

Asyay ehay aidsay isthay ehay edlay ethay ayway acrossyay ethay iceyay; Iyay ollowedfay. Ymay earthay
asway ullfay, andyay Iyay idday otnay answeryay imhay, utbay asyay Iyay oceededpray, Iyay eighedway ethay
ariousvay argumentsyay atthay ehay adhay usedyay andyay eterminedday atyay eastlay otay istenlay otay
ishay aletay. Iyay asway artlypay urgedyay ybay uriositycay, andyay ompassioncay onfirmedcay ymay
esolutionray. Iyay adhay ithertohay upposedsay imhay otay ebay ethay urderermay ofyay ymay
otherbray, andyay Iyay eagerlyyay oughtsay ayay onfirmationcay oryay enialday ofyay isthay opinionyay.
Orfay ethay irstfay imetay, alsoyay, Iyay eltfay atwhay ethay utiesday ofyay ayay eatorcray owardstay
ishay eaturecray ereway, andyay atthay Iyay oughtyay otay enderray imhay appyhay eforebay Iyay
omplainedcay ofyay ishay ickednessway. Esethay otivesmay urgedyay emay otay omplycay ithway
ishay emandday. Eway ossedcray ethay iceyay, ereforethay, andyay ascendedyay ethay oppositeyay
ockray. Ethay airyay asway oldcay, andyay ethay ainray againyay eganbay otay escendday; eway
enteredyay ethay uthay, ethay iendfay ithway anyay airyay ofyay exultationyay, Iyay ithway ayay eavyhay
earthay andyay epressedday iritsspay. Utbay Iyay onsentedcay otay istenlay, andyay eatingsay
yselfmay ybay ethay irefay ichwhay ymay odiousyay ompanioncay adhay ightedlay, ehay usthay eganbay
ishay aletay.




Apterchay 11


it“ay isyay ithway onsiderablecay ifficultyday atthay Iyay ememberray ethay originalyay erayay ofyay
ymay eingbay; allyay ethay eventsyay ofyay atthay eriodpay appearyay onfusedcay andyay indistinctyay.
Ayay angestray ultiplicitymay ofyay ensationssay eizedsay emay, andyay Iyay awsay, eltfay, eardhay,
andyay eltsmay atyay ethay amesay imetay; andyay ityay asway, indeedyay, ayay onglay imetay eforebay Iyay
earnedlay otay istinguishday etweenbay ethay operationsyay ofyay ymay ariousvay ensessay. Ybay
egreesday, Iyay ememberray, ayay ongerstray ightlay essedpray uponyay ymay ervesnay, osay atthay Iyay
asway obligedyay otay utshay ymay eyesyay. Arknessday enthay amecay overyay emay andyay oubledtray
emay, utbay ardlyhay adhay Iyay eltfay isthay enwhay, ybay openingyay ymay eyesyay, asyay Iyay ownay
upposesay, ethay ightlay ouredpay inyay uponyay emay againyay. Iyay alkedway andyay, Iyay elievebay,
escendedday, utbay Iyay esentlypray oundfay ayay eatgray alterationyay inyay ymay ensationssay.
Eforebay, arkday andyay opaqueyay odiesbay adhay urroundedsay emay, imperviousyay otay ymay
ouchtay oryay ightsay; utbay Iyay ownay oundfay atthay Iyay ouldcay anderway onyay atyay ibertylay, ithway
onay obstaclesyay ichwhay Iyay ouldcay otnay eitheryay urmountsay oryay avoidyay. Ethay ightlay
ecamebay oremay andyay oremay oppressiveyay otay emay, andyay ethay eathay earyingway emay asyay Iyay
alkedway, Iyay oughtsay ayay aceplay erewhay Iyay ouldcay eceiveray adeshay. Isthay asway ethay
orestfay earnay Ingolstadtyay; andyay erehay Iyay aylay ybay ethay idesay ofyay ayay ookbray estingray
omfray ymay atiguefay, untilyay Iyay eltfay ormentedtay ybay ungerhay andyay irstthay. Isthay
ousedray emay omfray ymay earlynay ormantday atestay, andyay Iyay ateyay omesay erriesbay ichwhay Iyay
oundfay anginghay onyay ethay eestray oryay yinglay onyay ethay oundgray. Iyay akedslay ymay irstthay
atyay ethay ookbray, andyay enthay yinglay ownday, asway overcomeyay ybay eepslay.

it“ay asway arkday enwhay Iyay awokeyay; Iyay eltfay oldcay alsoyay, andyay alfhay ightenedfray, asyay ityay
ereway, instinctivelyyay, indingfay yselfmay osay esolateday. Eforebay Iyay adhay uittedqay
youryay apartmentyay, onyay ayay ensationsay ofyay oldcay, Iyay adhay overedcay yselfmay ithway omesay
othesclay, utbay esethay ereway insufficientyay otay ecuresay emay omfray ethay ewsday ofyay
ightnay. Iyay asway ayay oorpay, elplesshay, iserablemay etchwray; Iyay ewknay, andyay ouldcay
istinguishday, othingnay; utbay eelingfay ainpay invadeyay emay onyay allyay idessay, Iyay atsay
ownday andyay eptway.

oon“say ayay entlegay ightlay olestay overyay ethay eavenshay andyay avegay emay ayay ensationsay ofyay
easureplay. Iyay artedstay upyay andyay eheldbay ayay adiantray ormfay iseray omfray amongyay ethay
eestray. e[thay oonmay] Iyay azedgay ithway ayay indkay ofyay onderway. Ityay ovedmay owlyslay,
utbay ityay enlightenedyay ymay athpay, andyay Iyay againyay entway outyay inyay earchsay ofyay erriesbay.
Iyay asway illstay oldcay enwhay underyay oneyay ofyay ethay eestray Iyay oundfay ayay ugehay oakclay, ithway
ichwhay Iyay overedcay yselfmay, andyay atsay ownday uponyay ethay oundgray. Onay istinctday
ideasyay occupiedyay ymay indmay; allyay asway onfusedcay. Iyay eltfay ightlay, andyay ungerhay,
andyay irstthay, andyay arknessday; innumerableyay oundssay angray inyay ymay earsyay, andyay onyay
allyay idessay ariousvay entsscay alutedsay emay; ethay onlyyay objectyay atthay Iyay ouldcay
istinguishday asway ethay ightbray oonmay, andyay Iyay ixedfay ymay eyesyay onyay atthay ithway
easureplay.

everal“say angeschay ofyay ayday andyay ightnay assedpay, andyay ethay orbyay ofyay ightnay adhay
eatlygray essenedlay, enwhay Iyay eganbay otay istinguishday ymay ensationssay omfray eachyay
otheryay. Iyay aduallygray awsay ainlyplay ethay earclay eamstray atthay uppliedsay emay ithway
inkdray andyay ethay eestray atthay adedshay emay ithway eirthay oliagefay. Iyay asway elightedday
enwhay Iyay irstfay iscoveredday atthay ayay easantplay oundsay, ichwhay oftenyay alutedsay ymay
earsyay, oceededpray omfray ethay oatsthray ofyay ethay ittlelay ingedway animalsyay owhay adhay
oftenyay interceptedyay ethay ightlay omfray ymay eyesyay. Iyay eganbay alsoyay otay observeyay,
ithway eatergray accuracyyay, ethay ormsfay atthay urroundedsay emay andyay otay erceivepay ethay
oundariesbay ofyay ethay adiantray oofray ofyay ightlay ichwhay anopiedcay emay. Ometimessay Iyay
iedtray otay imitateyay ethay easantplay ongssay ofyay ethay irdsbay utbay asway unableyay.
Ometimessay Iyay ishedway otay expressyay ymay ensationssay inyay ymay ownyay odemay, utbay ethay
uncouthyay andyay inarticulateyay oundssay ichwhay okebray omfray emay ightenedfray emay intoyay
ilencesay againyay.

e“thay oonmay adhay isappearedday omfray ethay ightnay, andyay againyay, ithway ayay essenedlay
ormfay, owedshay itselfyay, ilewhay Iyay illstay emainedray inyay ethay orestfay. Ymay
ensationssay adhay ybay isthay imetay ecomebay istinctday, andyay ymay indmay eceivedray everyyay
ayday additionalyay ideasyay. Ymay eyesyay ecamebay accustomedyay otay ethay ightlay andyay otay
erceivepay objectsyay inyay eirthay ightray ormsfay; Iyay istinguishedday ethay insectyay omfray
ethay erbhay, andyay ybay egreesday, oneyay erbhay omfray anotheryay. Iyay oundfay atthay ethay
arrowspay utteredyay onenay utbay arshhay otesnay, ilstwhay osethay ofyay ethay ackbirdblay andyay
ushthray ereway eetsway andyay enticingyay.

one“ay ayday, enwhay Iyay asway oppressedyay ybay oldcay, Iyay oundfay ayay irefay ichwhay adhay eenbay
eftlay ybay omesay anderingway eggarsbay, andyay asway overcomeyay ithway elightday atyay ethay
armthway Iyay experiencedyay omfray ityay. Inyay ymay oyjay Iyay ustthray ymay andhay intoyay ethay ivelay
embersyay, utbay uicklyqay ewdray ityay outyay againyay ithway ayay ycray ofyay ainpay. Owhay angestray,
Iyay oughtthay, atthay ethay amesay ausecay ouldshay oducepray uchsay oppositeyay effectsyay! Iyay
examinedyay ethay aterialsmay ofyay ethay irefay, andyay otay ymay oyjay oundfay ityay otay ebay
omposedcay ofyay oodway. Iyay uicklyqay ollectedcay omesay anchesbray, utbay eythay ereway etway
andyay ouldway otnay urnbay. Iyay asway ainedpay atyay isthay andyay atsay illstay atchingway ethay
operationyay ofyay ethay irefay. Ethay etway oodway ichwhay Iyay adhay acedplay earnay ethay eathay
ieddray andyay itselfyay ecamebay inflamedyay. Iyay eflectedray onyay isthay, andyay ybay ouchingtay
ethay ariousvay anchesbray, Iyay iscoveredday ethay ausecay andyay usiedbay yselfmay inyay
ollectingcay ayay eatgray uantityqay ofyay oodway, atthay Iyay ightmay ydray ityay andyay avehay ayay
entifulplay upplysay ofyay irefay. Enwhay ightnay amecay onyay andyay oughtbray eepslay ithway
ityay, Iyay asway inyay ethay eatestgray earfay estlay ymay irefay ouldshay ebay extinguishedyay. Iyay
overedcay ityay arefullycay ithway ydray oodway andyay eaveslay andyay acedplay etway anchesbray
uponyay ityay; andyay enthay, eadingspray ymay oakclay, Iyay aylay onyay ethay oundgray andyay anksay
intoyay eepslay.

it“ay asway orningmay enwhay Iyay awokeyay, andyay ymay irstfay arecay asway otay isitvay ethay irefay.
Iyay uncoveredyay ityay, andyay ayay entlegay eezebray uicklyqay annedfay ityay intoyay ayay ameflay. Iyay
observedyay isthay alsoyay andyay ontrivedcay ayay anfay ofyay anchesbray, ichwhay ousedray ethay
embersyay enwhay eythay ereway earlynay extinguishedyay. Enwhay ightnay amecay againyay Iyay
oundfay, ithway easureplay, atthay ethay irefay avegay ightlay asyay ellway asyay eathay andyay atthay
ethay iscoveryday ofyay isthay elementyay asway usefulyay otay emay inyay ymay oodfay, orfay Iyay oundfay
omesay ofyay ethay offalsyay atthay ethay avellerstray adhay eftlay adhay eenbay oastedray, andyay
astedtay uchmay oremay avourysay anthay ethay erriesbay Iyay atheredgay omfray ethay eestray. Iyay
iedtray, ereforethay, otay essdray ymay oodfay inyay ethay amesay annermay, acingplay ityay onyay
ethay ivelay embersyay. Iyay oundfay atthay ethay erriesbay ereway oiledspay ybay isthay
operationyay, andyay ethay utsnay andyay ootsray uchmay improvedyay.

ood“fay, oweverhay, ecamebay arcescay, andyay Iyay oftenyay entspay ethay olewhay ayday
earchingsay inyay ainvay orfay ayay ewfay acornsyay otay assuageyay ethay angspay ofyay ungerhay. Enwhay
Iyay oundfay isthay, Iyay esolvedray otay uitqay ethay aceplay atthay Iyay adhay ithertohay
inhabitedyay, otay eeksay orfay oneyay erewhay ethay ewfay antsway Iyay experiencedyay ouldway ebay
oremay easilyyay atisfiedsay. Inyay isthay emigrationyay Iyay exceedinglyyay amentedlay ethay
osslay ofyay ethay irefay ichwhay Iyay adhay obtainedyay oughthray accidentyay andyay ewknay otnay owhay
otay eproduceray ityay. Iyay avegay everalsay ourshay otay ethay erioussay onsiderationcay ofyay
isthay ifficultyday, utbay Iyay asway obligedyay otay elinquishray allyay attemptyay otay upplysay
ityay, andyay appingwray yselfmay upyay inyay ymay oakclay, Iyay uckstray acrossyay ethay oodway
owardstay ethay ettingsay unsay. Iyay assedpay eethray aysday inyay esethay amblesray andyay atyay
engthlay iscoveredday ethay openyay ountrycay. Ayay eatgray allfay ofyay owsnay adhay akentay
aceplay ethay ightnay eforebay, andyay ethay ieldsfay ereway ofyay oneyay uniformyay itewhay; ethay
appearanceyay asway isconsolateday, andyay Iyay oundfay ymay eetfay illedchay ybay ethay oldcay
ampday ubstancesay atthay overedcay ethay oundgray.

it“ay asway aboutyay evensay inyay ethay orningmay, andyay Iyay ongedlay otay obtainyay oodfay andyay
eltershay; atyay engthlay Iyay erceivedpay ayay allsmay uthay, onyay ayay isingray oundgray, ichwhay
adhay oubtlessday eenbay uiltbay orfay ethay onveniencecay ofyay omesay epherdshay. Isthay
asway ayay ewnay ightsay otay emay, andyay Iyay examinedyay ethay ucturestray ithway eatgray
uriositycay. Indingfay ethay oorday openyay, Iyay enteredyay. Anyay oldyay anmay atsay inyay ityay,
earnay ayay irefay, overyay ichwhay ehay asway eparingpray ishay eakfastbray. Ehay urnedtay onyay
earinghay ayay oisenay, andyay erceivingpay emay, iekedshray oudlylay, andyay uittingqay ethay
uthay, anray acrossyay ethay ieldsfay ithway ayay eedspay ofyay ichwhay ishay ebilitatedday ormfay
ardlyhay appearedyay apablecay. Ishay appearanceyay, ifferentday omfray anyyay Iyay adhay everyay
eforebay eensay, andyay ishay ightflay omewhatsay urprisedsay emay. Utbay Iyay asway enchantedyay
ybay ethay appearanceyay ofyay ethay uthay; erehay ethay owsnay andyay ainray ouldcay otnay
enetratepay; ethay oundgray asway ydray; andyay ityay esentedpray otay emay enthay asyay exquisiteyay
andyay ivineday ayay etreatray asyay Andæmoniumpay appearedyay otay ethay onsdæmay ofyay ellhay
afteryay eirthay ufferingssay inyay ethay akelay ofyay irefay. Iyay eedilygray evouredday ethay
emnantsray ofyay ethay epherd’sshay eakfastbray, ichwhay onsistedcay ofyay eadbray, eesechay,
ilkmay, andyay ineway; ethay atterlay, oweverhay, Iyay idday otnay ikelay. Enthay, overcomeyay ybay
atiguefay, Iyay aylay ownday amongyay omesay awstray andyay ellfay asleepyay.

it“ay asway oonnay enwhay Iyay awokeyay, andyay alluredyay ybay ethay armthway ofyay ethay unsay, ichwhay
oneshay ightlybray onyay ethay itewhay oundgray, Iyay eterminedday otay ecommenceray ymay
avelstray; andyay, epositingday ethay emainsray ofyay ethay easant’spay eakfastbray inyay ayay
alletway Iyay oundfay, Iyay oceededpray acrossyay ethay ieldsfay orfay everalsay ourshay, untilyay
atyay unsetsay Iyay arrivedyay atyay ayay illagevay. Owhay iraculousmay idday isthay appearyay! Ethay
utshay, ethay eaternay ottagescay, andyay atelystay ouseshay engagedyay ymay admirationyay ybay
urnstay. Ethay egetablesvay inyay ethay ardensgay, ethay ilkmay andyay eesechay atthay Iyay awsay
acedplay atyay ethay indowsway ofyay omesay ofyay ethay ottagescay, alluredyay ymay appetiteyay. Oneyay
ofyay ethay estbay ofyay esethay Iyay enteredyay, utbay Iyay adhay ardlyhay acedplay ymay ootfay ithinway
ethay oorday eforebay ethay ildrenchay iekedshray, andyay oneyay ofyay ethay omenway aintedfay.
Ethay olewhay illagevay asway ousedray; omesay edflay, omesay attackedyay emay, untilyay,
ievouslygray uisedbray ybay onesstay andyay anymay otheryay indskay ofyay issilemay eaponsway, Iyay
escapedyay otay ethay openyay ountrycay andyay earfullyfay ooktay efugeray inyay ayay owlay ovelhay,
uiteqay arebay, andyay akingmay ayay etchedwray appearanceyay afteryay ethay alacespay Iyay adhay
eheldbay inyay ethay illagevay. Isthay ovelhay oweverhay, oinedjay ayay ottagecay ofyay ayay eatnay
andyay easantplay appearanceyay, utbay afteryay ymay atelay earlyday oughtbay experienceyay, Iyay
aredday otnay enteryay ityay. Ymay aceplay ofyay efugeray asway onstructedcay ofyay oodway, utbay osay
owlay atthay Iyay ouldcay ithway ifficultyday itsay uprightyay inyay ityay. Onay oodway, oweverhay,
asway acedplay onyay ethay earthyay, ichwhay ormedfay ethay oorflay, utbay ityay asway ydray; andyay
althoughyay ethay indway enteredyay ityay ybay innumerableyay inkschay, Iyay oundfay ityay anyay
agreeableyay asylumyay omfray ethay owsnay andyay ainray.

ere“hay, enthay, Iyay etreatedray andyay aylay ownday appyhay otay avehay oundfay ayay eltershay,
oweverhay iserablemay, omfray ethay inclemencyyay ofyay ethay easonsay, andyay illstay oremay
omfray ethay arbaritybay ofyay anmay. Asyay oonsay asyay orningmay awnedday Iyay eptcray omfray ymay
ennelkay, atthay Iyay ightmay iewvay ethay adjacentyay ottagecay andyay iscoverday ifyay Iyay ouldcay
emainray inyay ethay abitationhay Iyay adhay oundfay. Ityay asway ituatedsay againstyay ethay ackbay
ofyay ethay ottagecay andyay urroundedsay onyay ethay idessay ichwhay ereway exposedyay ybay ayay igpay
ystay andyay ayay earclay oolpay ofyay aterway. Oneyay artpay asway openyay, andyay ybay atthay Iyay adhay
eptcray inyay; utbay ownay Iyay overedcay everyyay evicecray ybay ichwhay Iyay ightmay ebay erceivedpay
ithway onesstay andyay oodway, yetyay inyay uchsay ayay annermay atthay Iyay ightmay ovemay emthay onyay
occasionyay otay asspay outyay; allyay ethay ightlay Iyay enjoyedyay amecay oughthray ethay ystay, andyay
atthay asway ufficientsay orfay emay.

aving“hay usthay arrangedyay ymay ellingdway andyay arpetedcay ityay ithway eanclay awstray, Iyay
etiredray, orfay Iyay awsay ethay igurefay ofyay ayay anmay atyay ayay istanceday, andyay Iyay ememberedray
ootay ellway ymay eatmenttray ethay ightnay eforebay otay usttray yselfmay inyay ishay owerpay. Iyay
adhay irstfay, oweverhay, ovidedpray orfay ymay ustenancesay orfay atthay ayday ybay ayay oaflay
ofyay oarsecay eadbray, ichwhay Iyay urloinedpay, andyay ayay upcay ithway ichwhay Iyay ouldcay inkdray
oremay onvenientlycay anthay omfray ymay andhay ofyay ethay urepay aterway ichwhay owedflay ybay
ymay etreatray. Ethay oorflay asway ayay ittlelay aisedray, osay atthay ityay asway eptkay
erfectlypay ydray, andyay ybay itsyay icinityvay otay ethay imneychay ofyay ethay ottagecay ityay asway
olerablytay armway.

eing“bay usthay ovidedpray, Iyay esolvedray otay esideray inyay isthay ovelhay untilyay
omethingsay ouldshay occuryay ichwhay ightmay alteryay ymay eterminationday. Ityay asway
indeedyay ayay aradisepay omparedcay otay ethay eakblay orestfay, ymay ormerfay esidenceray,
ethay ain-droppingray anchesbray, andyay ankday earthyay. Iyay ateyay ymay eakfastbray ithway
easureplay andyay asway aboutyay otay emoveray ayay ankplay otay ocurepray yselfmay ayay ittlelay
aterway enwhay Iyay eardhay ayay epstay, andyay ookinglay oughthray ayay allsmay inkchay, Iyay eheldbay
ayay youngyay eaturecray, ithway ayay ailpay onyay erhay eadhay, assingpay eforebay ymay ovelhay. Ethay
irlgay asway youngyay andyay ofyay entlegay emeanourday, unlikeyay atwhay Iyay avehay incesay oundfay
ottagerscay andyay armhousefay ervantssay otay ebay. Yetyay eshay asway eanlymay esseddray, ayay
oarsecay ueblay etticoatpay andyay ayay inenlay acketjay eingbay erhay onlyyay arbgay; erhay airfay
airhay asway aitedplay utbay otnay adornedyay: eshay ookedlay atientpay yetyay adsay. Iyay ostlay
ightsay ofyay erhay, andyay inyay aboutyay ayay uarterqay ofyay anyay ourhay eshay eturnedray earingbay
ethay ailpay, ichwhay asway ownay artlypay illedfay ithway ilkmay. Asyay eshay alkedway alongyay,
eeminglysay incommodedyay ybay ethay urdenbay, ayay youngyay anmay etmay erhay, osewhay
ountenancecay expressedyay ayay eeperday espondenceday. Utteringyay ayay ewfay oundssay ithway
anyay airyay ofyay elancholymay, ehay ooktay ethay ailpay omfray erhay eadhay andyay orebay ityay otay ethay
ottagecay imselfhay. Eshay ollowedfay, andyay eythay isappearedday. Esentlypray Iyay awsay
ethay youngyay anmay againyay, ithway omesay oolstay inyay ishay andhay, osscray ethay ieldfay
ehindbay ethay ottagecay; andyay ethay irlgay asway alsoyay usiedbay, ometimessay inyay ethay
ousehay andyay ometimessay inyay ethay yardyay.

on“ay examiningyay ymay ellingdway, Iyay oundfay atthay oneyay ofyay ethay indowsway ofyay ethay
ottagecay adhay ormerlyfay occupiedyay ayay artpay ofyay ityay, utbay ethay anespay adhay eenbay
illedfay upyay ithway oodway. Inyay oneyay ofyay esethay asway ayay allsmay andyay almostyay
imperceptibleyay inkchay oughthray ichwhay ethay eyeyay ouldcay ustjay enetratepay.
Oughthray isthay evicecray ayay allsmay oomray asway isiblevay, itewashedwhay andyay eanclay
utbay eryvay arebay ofyay urniturefay. Inyay oneyay ornercay, earnay ayay allsmay irefay, atsay anyay
oldyay anmay, eaninglay ishay eadhay onyay ishay andshay inyay ayay isconsolateday attitudeyay. Ethay
youngyay irlgay asway occupiedyay inyay arrangingyay ethay ottagecay; utbay esentlypray eshay
ooktay omethingsay outyay ofyay ayay awerdray, ichwhay employedyay erhay andshay, andyay eshay atsay
ownday esidebay ethay oldyay anmay, owhay, akingtay upyay anyay instrumentyay, eganbay otay ayplay
andyay otay oducepray oundssay eetersway anthay ethay oicevay ofyay ethay ushthray oryay ethay
ightingalenay. Ityay asway ayay ovelylay ightsay, evenyay otay emay, oorpay etchwray owhay adhay
evernay eheldbay aughtyay eautifulbay eforebay. Ethay ilversay airhay andyay enevolentbay
ountenancecay ofyay ethay agedyay ottagercay onway ymay everenceray, ilewhay ethay entlegay
annersmay ofyay ethay irlgay enticedyay ymay ovelay. Ehay ayedplay ayay eetsway ournfulmay airyay
ichwhay Iyay erceivedpay ewdray earstay omfray ethay eyesyay ofyay ishay amiableyay ompanioncay, ofyay
ichwhay ethay oldyay anmay ooktay onay oticenay, untilyay eshay obbedsay audiblyyay; ehay enthay
onouncedpray ayay ewfay oundssay, andyay ethay airfay eaturecray, eavinglay erhay orkway, eltknay
atyay ishay eetfay. Ehay aisedray erhay andyay iledsmay ithway uchsay indnesskay andyay affectionyay
atthay Iyay eltfay ensationssay ofyay ayay eculiarpay andyay overpoweringyay aturenay; eythay ereway
ayay ixturemay ofyay ainpay andyay easureplay, uchsay asyay Iyay adhay evernay eforebay experiencedyay,
eitheryay omfray ungerhay oryay oldcay, armthway oryay oodfay; andyay Iyay ithdrewway omfray ethay
indowway, unableyay otay earbay esethay emotionsyay.

oon“say afteryay isthay ethay youngyay anmay eturnedray, earingbay onyay ishay ouldersshay ayay
oadlay ofyay oodway. Ethay irlgay etmay imhay atyay ethay oorday, elpedhay otay elieveray imhay ofyay
ishay urdenbay, andyay akingtay omesay ofyay ethay uelfay intoyay ethay ottagecay, acedplay ityay onyay
ethay irefay; enthay eshay andyay ethay youthyay entway apartyay intoyay ayay ooknay ofyay ethay ottagecay,
andyay ehay owedshay erhay ayay argelay oaflay andyay ayay iecepay ofyay eesechay. Eshay eemedsay
easedplay andyay entway intoyay ethay ardengay orfay omesay ootsray andyay antsplay, ichwhay eshay
acedplay inyay aterway, andyay enthay uponyay ethay irefay. Eshay afterwardsyay ontinuedcay erhay
orkway, ilstwhay ethay youngyay anmay entway intoyay ethay ardengay andyay appearedyay usilybay
employedyay inyay iggingday andyay ullingpay upyay ootsray. Afteryay ehay adhay eenbay employedyay
usthay aboutyay anyay ourhay, ethay youngyay omanway oinedjay imhay andyay eythay enteredyay ethay
ottagecay ogethertay.

e“thay oldyay anmay adhay, inyay ethay eantimemay, eenbay ensivepay, utbay onyay ethay appearanceyay
ofyay ishay ompanionscay ehay assumedyay ayay oremay eerfulchay airyay, andyay eythay atsay ownday otay
eatyay. Ethay ealmay asway uicklyqay ispatchedday. Ethay youngyay omanway asway againyay
occupiedyay inyay arrangingyay ethay ottagecay, ethay oldyay anmay alkedway eforebay ethay
ottagecay inyay ethay unsay orfay ayay ewfay inutesmay, eaninglay onyay ethay armyay ofyay ethay youthyay.
Othingnay ouldcay exceedyay inyay eautybay ethay ontrastcay etweenbay esethay otway excellentyay
eaturescray. Oneyay asway oldyay, ithway ilversay airshay andyay ayay ountenancecay eamingbay
ithway enevolencebay andyay ovelay; ethay youngeryay asway ightslay andyay acefulgray inyay ishay
igurefay, andyay ishay eaturesfay ereway ouldedmay ithway ethay inestfay ymmetrysay, yetyay ishay
eyesyay andyay attitudeyay expressedyay ethay utmostyay adnesssay andyay espondencyday. Ethay
oldyay anmay eturnedray otay ethay ottagecay, andyay ethay youthyay, ithway oolstay ifferentday
omfray osethay ehay adhay usedyay inyay ethay orningmay, irectedday ishay epsstay acrossyay ethay
ieldsfay.

ight“nay uicklyqay utshay inyay, utbay otay ymay extremeyay onderway, Iyay oundfay atthay ethay
ottagerscay adhay ayay eansmay ofyay olongingpray ightlay ybay ethay useyay ofyay aperstay, andyay asway
elightedday otay indfay atthay ethay ettingsay ofyay ethay unsay idday otnay utpay anyay endyay otay ethay
easureplay Iyay experiencedyay inyay atchingway ymay umanhay eighboursnay. Inyay ethay eveningyay
ethay youngyay irlgay andyay erhay ompanioncay ereway employedyay inyay ariousvay occupationsyay
ichwhay Iyay idday otnay understandyay; andyay ethay oldyay anmay againyay ooktay upyay ethay
instrumentyay ichwhay oducedpray ethay ivineday oundssay atthay adhay enchantedyay emay inyay
ethay orningmay. Osay oonsay asyay ehay adhay inishedfay, ethay youthyay eganbay, otnay otay ayplay,
utbay otay utteryay oundssay atthay ereway onotonousmay, andyay eithernay esemblingray ethay
armonyhay ofyay ethay oldyay an’smay instrumentyay ornay ethay ongssay ofyay ethay irdsbay; Iyay incesay
oundfay atthay ehay eadray aloudyay, utbay atyay atthay imetay Iyay ewknay othingnay ofyay ethay
iencescay ofyay ordsway oryay etterslay.

e“thay amilyfay, afteryay avinghay eenbay usthay occupiedyay orfay ayay ortshay imetay,
extinguishedyay eirthay ightslay andyay etiredray, asyay Iyay onjecturedcay, otay estray.”




Apterchay 12


i“ay aylay onyay ymay awstray, utbay Iyay ouldcay otnay eepslay. Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay
occurrencesyay ofyay ethay ayday. Atwhay ieflychay uckstray emay asway ethay entlegay annersmay
ofyay esethay eoplepay, andyay Iyay ongedlay otay oinjay emthay, utbay aredday otnay. Iyay
ememberedray ootay ellway ethay eatmenttray Iyay adhay ufferedsay ethay ightnay eforebay omfray
ethay arbarousbay illagersvay, andyay esolvedray, ateverwhay oursecay ofyay onductcay Iyay
ightmay ereafterhay inkthay ityay ightray otay ursuepay, atthay orfay ethay esentpray Iyay ouldway
emainray uietlyqay inyay ymay ovelhay, atchingway andyay endeavouringyay otay iscoverday ethay
otivesmay ichwhay influencedyay eirthay actionsyay.

e“thay ottagerscay aroseyay ethay extnay orningmay eforebay ethay unsay. Ethay youngyay omanway
arrangedyay ethay ottagecay andyay eparedpray ethay oodfay, andyay ethay youthyay epartedday
afteryay ethay irstfay ealmay.

is“thay ayday asway assedpay inyay ethay amesay outineray asyay atthay ichwhay ecededpray ityay.
Ethay youngyay anmay asway onstantlycay employedyay outyay ofyay oorsday, andyay ethay irlgay inyay
ariousvay aboriouslay occupationsyay ithinway. Ethay oldyay anmay, omwhay Iyay oonsay
erceivedpay otay ebay indblay, employedyay ishay eisurelay ourshay onyay ishay instrumentyay oryay
inyay ontemplationcay. Othingnay ouldcay exceedyay ethay ovelay andyay espectray ichwhay ethay
youngeryay ottagerscay exhibitedyay owardstay eirthay enerablevay ompanioncay. Eythay
erformedpay owardstay imhay everyyay ittlelay officeyay ofyay affectionyay andyay utyday ithway
entlenessgay, andyay ehay ewardedray emthay ybay ishay enevolentbay ilessmay.

ey“thay ereway otnay entirelyyay appyhay. Ethay youngyay anmay andyay ishay ompanioncay oftenyay
entway apartyay andyay appearedyay otay eepway. Iyay awsay onay ausecay orfay eirthay unhappinessyay,
utbay Iyay asway eeplyday affectedyay ybay ityay. Ifyay uchsay ovelylay eaturescray ereway
iserablemay, ityay asway esslay angestray atthay Iyay, anyay imperfectyay andyay olitarysay eingbay,
ouldshay ebay etchedwray. Yetyay ywhay ereway esethay entlegay eingsbay unhappyyay? Eythay
ossessedpay ayay elightfulday ousehay or(fay uchsay ityay asway inyay ymay eyesyay) andyay everyyay
uxurylay; eythay adhay ayay irefay otay armway emthay enwhay illchay andyay eliciousday iandsvay
enwhay ungryhay; eythay ereway esseddray inyay excellentyay othesclay; andyay, illstay oremay,
eythay enjoyedyay oneyay another’syay ompanycay andyay eechspay, interchangingyay eachyay ayday
ookslay ofyay affectionyay andyay indnesskay. Atwhay idday eirthay earstay implyyay? Idday eythay
eallyray expressyay ainpay? Iyay asway atyay irstfay unableyay otay olvesay esethay uestionsqay,
utbay erpetualpay attentionyay andyay imetay explainedyay otay emay anymay appearancesyay ichwhay
ereway atyay irstfay enigmaticyay.

a“ay onsiderablecay eriodpay elapsedyay eforebay Iyay iscoveredday oneyay ofyay ethay ausescay ofyay
ethay uneasinessyay ofyay isthay amiableyay amilyfay: ityay asway overtypay, andyay eythay
ufferedsay atthay evilyay inyay ayay eryvay istressingday egreeday. Eirthay ourishmentnay
onsistedcay entirelyyay ofyay ethay egetablesvay ofyay eirthay ardengay andyay ethay ilkmay ofyay
oneyay owcay, ichwhay avegay eryvay ittlelay uringday ethay interway, enwhay itsyay astersmay
ouldcay arcelyscay ocurepray oodfay otay upportsay ityay. Eythay oftenyay, Iyay elievebay,
ufferedsay ethay angspay ofyay ungerhay eryvay oignantlypay, especiallyyay ethay otway
youngeryay ottagerscay, orfay everalsay imestay eythay acedplay oodfay eforebay ethay oldyay
anmay enwhay eythay eservedray onenay orfay emselvesthay.

is“thay aittray ofyay indnesskay ovedmay emay ensiblysay. Iyay adhay eenbay accustomedyay,
uringday ethay ightnay, otay ealstay ayay artpay ofyay eirthay orestay orfay ymay ownyay
onsumptioncay, utbay enwhay Iyay oundfay atthay inyay oingday isthay Iyay inflictedyay ainpay onyay
ethay ottagerscay, Iyay abstainedyay andyay atisfiedsay yselfmay ithway erriesbay, utsnay, andyay
ootsray ichwhay Iyay atheredgay omfray ayay eighbouringnay oodway.

i“ay iscoveredday alsoyay anotheryay eansmay oughthray ichwhay Iyay asway enabledyay otay assistyay
eirthay abourslay. Iyay oundfay atthay ethay youthyay entspay ayay eatgray artpay ofyay eachyay ayday
inyay ollectingcay oodway orfay ethay amilyfay irefay, andyay uringday ethay ightnay Iyay oftenyay
ooktay ishay oolstay, ethay useyay ofyay ichwhay Iyay uicklyqay iscoveredday, andyay oughtbray omehay
iringfay ufficientsay orfay ethay onsumptioncay ofyay everalsay aysday.

i“ay ememberray, ethay irstfay imetay atthay Iyay idday isthay, ethay youngyay omanway, enwhay eshay
openedyay ethay oorday inyay ethay orningmay, appearedyay eatlygray astonishedyay onyay eeingsay ayay eatgray
ilepay ofyay oodway onyay ethay outsideyay. Eshay utteredyay omesay ordsway inyay ayay oudlay oicevay, andyay ethay
youthyay oinedjay erhay, owhay alsoyay expressedyay urprisesay. Iyay observedyay, ithway easureplay,
atthay ehay idday otnay ogay otay ethay orestfay atthay ayday, utbay entspay ityay inyay epairingray ethay
ottagecay andyay ultivatingcay ethay ardengay.

y“bay egreesday Iyay ademay ayay iscoveryday ofyay illstay eatergray omentmay. Iyay oundfay atthay
esethay eoplepay ossessedpay ayay ethodmay ofyay ommunicatingcay eirthay experienceyay andyay
eelingsfay otay oneyay anotheryay ybay articulateyay oundssay. Iyay erceivedpay atthay ethay ordsway
eythay okespay ometimessay oducedpray easureplay oryay ainpay, ilessmay oryay adnesssay, inyay ethay
indsmay andyay ountenancescay ofyay ethay earershay. Isthay asway indeedyay ayay odlikegay iencescay,
andyay Iyay ardentlyyay esiredday otay ecomebay acquaintedyay ithway ityay. Utbay Iyay asway affledbay inyay
everyyay attemptyay Iyay ademay orfay isthay urposepay. Eirthay onunciationpray asway uickqay, andyay
ethay ordsway eythay utteredyay, otnay avinghay anyyay apparentyay onnectioncay ithway isiblevay
objectsyay, Iyay asway unableyay otay iscoverday anyyay ueclay ybay ichwhay Iyay ouldcay unravelyay ethay
ysterymay ofyay eirthay eferenceray. Ybay eatgray applicationyay, oweverhay, andyay afteryay avinghay
emainedray uringday ethay acespay ofyay everalsay evolutionsray ofyay ethay oonmay inyay ymay ovelhay, Iyay
iscoveredday ethay amesnay atthay ereway ivengay otay omesay ofyay ethay ostmay amiliarfay objectsyay ofyay
iscourseday; Iyay earnedlay andyay appliedyay ethay ordsway, ire_fay, ilkmay, eadbray,_ andyay
ood_way._ Iyay earnedlay alsoyay ethay amesnay ofyay ethay ottagerscay emselvesthay. Ethay youthyay
andyay ishay ompanioncay adhay eachyay ofyay emthay everalsay amesnay, utbay ethay oldyay anmay adhay onlyyay
oneyay, ichwhay asway ather_fay._ Ethay irlgay asway alledcay ister_say_ oryay
agatha_ay,_ andyay ethay youthyay elix_fay, otherbray,_ oryay on_say_. Iyay annotcay
escribeday ethay elightday Iyay eltfay enwhay Iyay earnedlay ethay ideasyay appropriatedyay otay eachyay ofyay
esethay oundssay andyay asway ableyay otay onouncepray emthay. Iyay istinguishedday everalsay otheryay
ordsway ithoutway eingbay ableyay asyay yetyay otay understandyay oryay applyyay emthay, uchsay asyay ood_gay,
earestday, unhappyyay._

i“ay entspay ethay interway inyay isthay annermay. Ethay entlegay annersmay andyay eautybay ofyay
ethay ottagerscay eatlygray endearedyay emthay otay emay; enwhay eythay ereway unhappyyay, Iyay
eltfay epressedday; enwhay eythay ejoicedray, Iyay ympathisedsay inyay eirthay oysjay. Iyay awsay
ewfay umanhay eingsbay esidesbay emthay, andyay ifyay anyyay otheryay appenedhay otay enteryay ethay
ottagecay, eirthay arshhay annersmay andyay uderay aitgay onlyyay enhancedyay otay emay ethay
uperiorsay accomplishmentsyay ofyay ymay iendsfray. Ethay oldyay anmay, Iyay ouldcay erceivepay,
oftenyay endeavouredyay otay encourageyay ishay ildrenchay, asyay ometimessay Iyay oundfay atthay
ehay alledcay emthay, otay astcay offyay eirthay elancholymay. Ehay ouldway alktay inyay ayay
eerfulchay accentyay, ithway anyay expressionyay ofyay oodnessgay atthay estowedbay easureplay
evenyay uponyay emay. Agathayay istenedlay ithway espectray, erhay eyesyay ometimessay illedfay
ithway earstay, ichwhay eshay endeavouredyay otay ipeway awayyay unperceivedyay; utbay Iyay
enerallygay oundfay atthay erhay ountenancecay andyay onetay ereway oremay eerfulchay afteryay
avinghay istenedlay otay ethay exhortationsyay ofyay erhay atherfay. Ityay asway otnay usthay
ithway Elixfay. Ehay asway alwaysyay ethay addestsay ofyay ethay oupgray, andyay evenyay otay ymay
unpractisedyay ensessay, ehay appearedyay otay avehay ufferedsay oremay eeplyday anthay ishay
iendsfray. Utbay ifyay ishay ountenancecay asway oremay orrowfulsay, ishay oicevay asway oremay
eerfulchay anthay atthay ofyay ishay istersay, especiallyyay enwhay ehay addressedyay ethay oldyay
anmay.

i“ay ouldcay entionmay innumerableyay instancesyay ichwhay, althoughyay ightslay, arkedmay
ethay ispositionsday ofyay esethay amiableyay ottagerscay. Inyay ethay idstmay ofyay overtypay
andyay antway, Elixfay arriedcay ithway easureplay otay ishay istersay ethay irstfay ittlelay
itewhay owerflay atthay eepedpay outyay omfray eneathbay ethay owysnay oundgray. Earlyyay inyay
ethay orningmay, eforebay eshay adhay isenray, ehay earedclay awayyay ethay owsnay atthay
obstructedyay erhay athpay otay ethay ilk-housemay, ewdray aterway omfray ethay ellway, andyay
oughtbray ethay oodway omfray ethay outhouseyay, erewhay, otay ishay erpetualpay
astonishmentyay, ehay oundfay ishay orestay alwaysyay eplenishedray ybay anyay invisibleyay
andhay. Inyay ethay ayday, Iyay elievebay, ehay orkedway ometimessay orfay ayay eighbouringnay
armerfay, ecausebay ehay oftenyay entway orthfay andyay idday otnay eturnray untilyay innerday,
yetyay oughtbray onay oodway ithway imhay. Atyay otheryay imestay ehay orkedway inyay ethay ardengay,
utbay asyay erethay asway ittlelay otay oday inyay ethay ostyfray easonsay, ehay eadray otay ethay oldyay
anmay andyay Agathayay.

is“thay eadingray adhay uzzledpay emay extremelyyay atyay irstfay, utbay ybay egreesday Iyay
iscoveredday atthay ehay utteredyay anymay ofyay ethay amesay oundssay enwhay ehay eadray asyay enwhay
ehay alkedtay. Iyay onjecturedcay, ereforethay, atthay ehay oundfay onyay ethay aperpay ignssay
orfay eechspay ichwhay ehay understoodyay, andyay Iyay ardentlyyay ongedlay otay omprehendcay
esethay alsoyay; utbay owhay asway atthay ossiblepay enwhay Iyay idday otnay evenyay understandyay
ethay oundssay orfay ichwhay eythay oodstay asyay ignssay? Iyay improvedyay, oweverhay,
ensiblysay inyay isthay iencescay, utbay otnay ufficientlysay otay ollowfay upyay anyyay indkay ofyay
onversationcay, althoughyay Iyay appliedyay ymay olewhay indmay otay ethay endeavouryay, orfay Iyay
easilyyay erceivedpay atthay, althoughyay Iyay eagerlyyay ongedlay otay iscoverday yselfmay otay
ethay ottagerscay, Iyay oughtyay otnay otay akemay ethay attemptyay untilyay Iyay adhay irstfay ecomebay
astermay ofyay eirthay anguagelay, ichwhay owledgeknay ightmay enableyay emay otay akemay emthay
overlookyay ethay eformityday ofyay ymay igurefay, orfay ithway isthay alsoyay ethay ontrastcay
erpetuallypay esentedpray otay ymay eyesyay adhay ademay emay acquaintedyay.

i“ay adhay admiredyay ethay erfectpay ormsfay ofyay ymay ottagers—theircay acegray, eautybay,
andyay elicateday omplexionscay; utbay owhay asway Iyay errifiedtay enwhay Iyay iewedvay yselfmay
inyay ayay ansparenttray oolpay! Atyay irstfay Iyay artedstay ackbay, unableyay otay elievebay atthay
ityay asway indeedyay Iyay owhay asway eflectedray inyay ethay irrormay; andyay enwhay Iyay ecamebay
ullyfay onvincedcay atthay Iyay asway inyay ealityray ethay onstermay atthay Iyay amyay, Iyay asway
illedfay ithway ethay itterestbay ensationssay ofyay espondenceday andyay ortificationmay.
Alasyay! Iyay idday otnay yetyay entirelyyay owknay ethay atalfay effectsyay ofyay isthay iserablemay
eformityday.

as“ay ethay unsay ecamebay armerway andyay ethay ightlay ofyay ayday ongerlay, ethay owsnay
anishedvay, andyay Iyay eheldbay ethay arebay eestray andyay ethay ackblay earthyay. Omfray isthay
imetay Elixfay asway oremay employedyay, andyay ethay eart-movinghay indicationsyay ofyay
impendingyay aminefay isappearedday. Eirthay oodfay, asyay Iyay afterwardsyay oundfay, asway
oarsecay, utbay ityay asway olesomewhay; andyay eythay ocuredpray ayay ufficiencysay ofyay ityay.
Everalsay ewnay indskay ofyay antsplay angspray upyay inyay ethay ardengay, ichwhay eythay
esseddray; andyay esethay ignssay ofyay omfortcay increasedyay ailyday asyay ethay easonsay
advancedyay.

e“thay oldyay anmay, eaninglay onyay ishay onsay, alkedway eachyay ayday atyay oonnay, enwhay ityay idday
otnay ainray, asyay Iyay oundfay ityay asway alledcay enwhay ethay eavenshay ouredpay orthfay itsyay
atersway. Isthay equentlyfray ooktay aceplay, utbay ayay ighhay indway uicklyqay ieddray ethay
earthyay, andyay ethay easonsay ecamebay arfay oremay easantplay anthay ityay adhay eenbay.

y“may odemay ofyay ifelay inyay ymay ovelhay asway uniformyay. Uringday ethay orningmay Iyay
attendedyay ethay otionsmay ofyay ethay ottagerscay, andyay enwhay eythay ereway ispersedday inyay
ariousvay occupationsyay, Iyay eptslay; ethay emainderray ofyay ethay ayday asway entspay inyay
observingyay ymay iendsfray. Enwhay eythay adhay etiredray otay estray, ifyay erethay asway anyyay
oonmay oryay ethay ightnay asway ar-lightstay, Iyay entway intoyay ethay oodsway andyay ollectedcay
ymay ownyay oodfay andyay uelfay orfay ethay ottagecay. Enwhay Iyay eturnedray, asyay oftenyay asyay ityay
asway ecessarynay, Iyay earedclay eirthay athpay omfray ethay owsnay andyay erformedpay osethay
officesyay atthay Iyay adhay eensay oneday ybay Elixfay. Iyay afterwardsyay oundfay atthay esethay
abourslay, erformedpay ybay anyay invisibleyay andhay, eatlygray astonishedyay emthay; andyay
onceyay oryay icetway Iyay eardhay emthay, onyay esethay occasionsyay, utteryay ethay ordsway ood_gay
iritspay, onderfulway_; utbay Iyay idday otnay enthay understandyay ethay ignificationsay
ofyay esethay ermstay.

y“may oughtsthay ownay ecamebay oremay activeyay, andyay Iyay ongedlay otay iscoverday ethay
otivesmay andyay eelingsfay ofyay esethay ovelylay eaturescray; Iyay asway inquisitiveyay otay
owknay ywhay Elixfay appearedyay osay iserablemay andyay Agathayay osay adsay. Iyay oughtthay
oolish(fay etchwray!) atthay ityay ightmay ebay inyay ymay owerpay otay estoreray appinesshay otay
esethay eservingday eoplepay. Enwhay Iyay eptslay oryay asway absentyay, ethay ormsfay ofyay ethay
enerablevay indblay atherfay, ethay entlegay Agathayay, andyay ethay excellentyay Elixfay
ittedflay eforebay emay. Iyay ookedlay uponyay emthay asyay uperiorsay eingsbay owhay ouldway ebay
ethay arbitersyay ofyay ymay uturefay estinyday. Iyay ormedfay inyay ymay imaginationyay ayay
ousandthay icturespay ofyay esentingpray yselfmay otay emthay, andyay eirthay eceptionray ofyay
emay. Iyay imaginedyay atthay eythay ouldway ebay isgustedday, untilyay, ybay ymay entlegay
emeanourday andyay onciliatingcay ordsway, Iyay ouldshay irstfay inway eirthay avourfay andyay
afterwardsyay eirthay ovelay.

ese“thay oughtsthay exhilaratedyay emay andyay edlay emay otay applyyay ithway eshfray ardouryay otay
ethay acquiringyay ethay artyay ofyay anguagelay. Ymay organsyay ereway indeedyay arshhay, utbay
upplesay; andyay althoughyay ymay oicevay asway eryvay unlikeyay ethay oftsay usicmay ofyay eirthay
onestay, yetyay Iyay onouncedpray uchsay ordsway asyay Iyay understoodyay ithway olerabletay easeyay.
Ityay asway asyay ethay assyay andyay ethay ap-doglay; yetyay urelysay ethay entlegay assyay osewhay
intentionsyay ereway affectionateyay, althoughyay ishay annersmay ereway uderay, eservedday
etterbay eatmenttray anthay owsblay andyay execrationyay.

e“thay easantplay owersshay andyay enialgay armthway ofyay ingspray eatlygray alteredyay ethay
aspectyay ofyay ethay earthyay. Enmay owhay eforebay isthay angechay eemedsay otay avehay eenbay
idhay inyay avescay ispersedday emselvesthay andyay ereway employedyay inyay ariousvay artsyay ofyay
ultivationcay. Ethay irdsbay angsay inyay oremay eerfulchay otesnay, andyay ethay eaveslay
eganbay otay udbay orthfay onyay ethay eestray. Appyhay, appyhay earthyay! Itfay abitationhay
orfay odsgay, ichwhay, osay ortshay ayay imetay eforebay, asway eakblay, ampday, andyay
unwholesomeyay. Ymay iritsspay ereway elevatedyay ybay ethay enchantingyay appearanceyay ofyay
aturenay; ethay astpay asway ottedblay omfray ymay emorymay, ethay esentpray asway anquiltray,
andyay ethay uturefay ildedgay ybay ightbray aysray ofyay opehay andyay anticipationsyay ofyay oyjay.”




Apterchay 13


i“ay ownay astenhay otay ethay oremay ovingmay artpay ofyay ymay orystay. Iyay allshay elateray
eventsyay atthay impressedyay emay ithway eelingsfay ichwhay, omfray atwhay Iyay adhay eenbay,
avehay ademay emay atwhay Iyay amyay.

ing“spray advancedyay apidlyray; ethay eatherway ecamebay inefay andyay ethay iesskay
oudlessclay. Ityay urprisedsay emay atthay atwhay eforebay asway esertday andyay oomyglay
ouldshay ownay oomblay ithway ethay ostmay eautifulbay owersflay andyay erdurevay. Ymay
ensessay ereway atifiedgray andyay efreshedray ybay ayay ousandthay entsscay ofyay elightday andyay
ayay ousandthay ightssay ofyay eautybay.

it“ay asway onyay oneyay ofyay esethay aysday, enwhay ymay ottagerscay eriodicallypay estedray
omfray abour—thelay oldyay anmay ayedplay onyay ishay uitargay, andyay ethay ildrenchay
istenedlay otay im—thathay Iyay observedyay ethay ountenancecay ofyay Elixfay asway
elancholymay eyondbay expressionyay; ehay ighedsay equentlyfray, andyay onceyay ishay atherfay
ausedpay inyay ishay usicmay, andyay Iyay onjecturedcay ybay ishay annermay atthay ehay inquiredyay
ethay ausecay ofyay ishay on’ssay orrowsay. Elixfay epliedray inyay ayay eerfulchay accentyay, andyay
ethay oldyay anmay asway ecommencingray ishay usicmay enwhay omeonesay appedtay atyay ethay oorday.

it“ay asway ayay adylay onyay orsebackhay, accompaniedyay ybay ayay ountry-mancay asyay ayay uidegay.
Ethay adylay asway esseddray inyay ayay arkday uitsay andyay overedcay ithway ayay ickthay ackblay
eilvay. Agathayay askedyay ayay uestionqay, otay ichwhay ethay angerstray onlyyay epliedray ybay
onouncingpray, inyay ayay eetsway accentyay, ethay amenay ofyay Elixfay. Erhay oicevay asway
usicalmay utbay unlikeyay atthay ofyay eitheryay ofyay ymay iendsfray. Onyay earinghay isthay ordway,
Elixfay amecay upyay astilyhay otay ethay adylay, owhay, enwhay eshay awsay imhay, ewthray upyay erhay
eilvay, andyay Iyay eheldbay ayay ountenancecay ofyay angelicyay eautybay andyay expressionyay. Erhay
airhay ofyay ayay iningshay avenray ackblay, andyay uriouslycay aidedbray; erhay eyesyay ereway
arkday, utbay entlegay, althoughyay animatedyay; erhay eaturesfay ofyay ayay egularray
oportionpray, andyay erhay omplexioncay ondrouslyway airfay, eachyay eekchay ingedtay ithway
ayay ovelylay inkpay.

elix“fay eemedsay avishedray ithway elightday enwhay ehay awsay erhay, everyyay aittray ofyay
orrowsay anishedvay omfray ishay acefay, andyay ityay instantlyyay expressedyay ayay egreeday ofyay
ecstaticyay oyjay, ofyay ichwhay Iyay ouldcay ardlyhay avehay elievedbay ityay apablecay; ishay
eyesyay arkledspay, asyay ishay eekchay ushedflay ithway easureplay; andyay atyay atthay omentmay Iyay
oughtthay imhay asyay eautifulbay asyay ethay angerstray. Eshay appearedyay affectedyay ybay
ifferentday eelingsfay; ipingway ayay ewfay earstay omfray erhay ovelylay eyesyay, eshay eldhay
outyay erhay andhay otay Elixfay, owhay issedkay ityay apturouslyray andyay alledcay erhay, asyay
ellway asyay Iyay ouldcay istinguishday, ishay eetsway Arabianyay. Eshay idday otnay appearyay otay
understandyay imhay, utbay iledsmay. Ehay assistedyay erhay otay ismountday, andyay
ismissingday erhay uidegay, onductedcay erhay intoyay ethay ottagecay. Omesay
onversationcay ooktay aceplay etweenbay imhay andyay ishay atherfay, andyay ethay youngyay
angerstray eltknay atyay ethay oldyay an’smay eetfay andyay ouldway avehay issedkay ishay andhay,
utbay ehay aisedray erhay andyay embracedyay erhay affectionatelyyay.

i“ay oonsay erceivedpay atthay althoughyay ethay angerstray utteredyay articulateyay oundssay
andyay appearedyay otay avehay ayay anguagelay ofyay erhay ownyay, eshay asway eithernay understoodyay
ybay ornay erselfhay understoodyay ethay ottagerscay. Eythay ademay anymay ignssay ichwhay Iyay
idday otnay omprehendcay, utbay Iyay awsay atthay erhay esencepray iffusedday adnessglay
oughthray ethay ottagecay, ispellingday eirthay orrowsay asyay ethay unsay issipatesday ethay
orningmay istsmay. Elixfay eemedsay eculiarlypay appyhay andyay ithway ilessmay ofyay
elightday elcomedway ishay Arabianyay. Agathayay, ethay ever-gentleyay Agathayay, issedkay
ethay andshay ofyay ethay ovelylay angerstray, andyay ointingpay otay erhay otherbray, ademay
ignssay ichwhay appearedyay otay emay otay eanmay atthay ehay adhay eenbay orrowfulsay untilyay eshay
amecay. Omesay ourshay assedpay usthay, ilewhay eythay, ybay eirthay ountenancescay,
expressedyay oyjay, ethay ausecay ofyay ichwhay Iyay idday otnay omprehendcay. Esentlypray Iyay
oundfay, ybay ethay equentfray ecurrenceray ofyay omesay oundsay ichwhay ethay angerstray
epeatedray afteryay emthay, atthay eshay asway endeavouringyay otay earnlay eirthay anguagelay;
andyay ethay ideayay instantlyyay occurredyay otay emay atthay Iyay ouldshay akemay useyay ofyay ethay
amesay instructionsyay otay ethay amesay endyay. Ethay angerstray earnedlay aboutyay entytway
ordsway atyay ethay irstfay essonlay; ostmay ofyay emthay, indeedyay, ereway osethay ichwhay Iyay adhay
eforebay understoodyay, utbay Iyay ofitedpray ybay ethay othersyay.

as“ay ightnay amecay onyay, Agathayay andyay ethay Arabianyay etiredray earlyyay. Enwhay eythay
eparatedsay Elixfay issedkay ethay andhay ofyay ethay angerstray andyay aidsay, ood‘gay ightnay
eetsway Afiesay.’ Ehay atsay upyay uchmay ongerlay, onversingcay ithway ishay atherfay, andyay
ybay ethay equentfray epetitionray ofyay erhay amenay Iyay onjecturedcay atthay eirthay ovelylay
uestgay asway ethay ubjectsay ofyay eirthay onversationcay. Iyay ardentlyyay esiredday otay
understandyay emthay, andyay entbay everyyay acultyfay owardstay atthay urposepay, utbay oundfay
ityay utterlyyay impossibleyay.

e“thay extnay orningmay Elixfay entway outyay otay ishay orkway, andyay afteryay ethay usualyay
occupationsyay ofyay Agathayay ereway inishedfay, ethay Arabianyay atsay atyay ethay eetfay ofyay ethay
oldyay anmay, andyay akingtay ishay uitargay, ayedplay omesay airsyay osay entrancinglyyay
eautifulbay atthay eythay atyay onceyay ewdray earstay ofyay orrowsay andyay elightday omfray ymay
eyesyay. Eshay angsay, andyay erhay oicevay owedflay inyay ayay ichray adencecay, ellingsway oryay
yingday awayyay ikelay ayay ightingalenay ofyay ethay oodsway.

en“whay eshay adhay inishedfay, eshay avegay ethay uitargay otay Agathayay, owhay atyay irstfay
eclinedday ityay. Eshay ayedplay ayay implesay airyay, andyay erhay oicevay accompaniedyay ityay inyay
eetsway accentsyay, utbay unlikeyay ethay ondrousway ainstray ofyay ethay angerstray. Ethay oldyay
anmay appearedyay enrapturedyay andyay aidsay omesay ordsway ichwhay Agathayay endeavouredyay otay
explainyay otay Afiesay, andyay ybay ichwhay ehay appearedyay otay ishway otay expressyay atthay eshay
estowedbay onyay imhay ethay eatestgray elightday ybay erhay usicmay.

e“thay aysday ownay assedpay asyay eaceablypay asyay eforebay, ithway ethay olesay alterationyay
atthay oyjay adhay akentay aceplay ofyay adnesssay inyay ethay ountenancescay ofyay ymay iendsfray.
Afiesay asway alwaysyay aygay andyay appyhay; eshay andyay Iyay improvedyay apidlyray inyay ethay
owledgeknay ofyay anguagelay, osay atthay inyay otway onthsmay Iyay eganbay otay omprehendcay ostmay
ofyay ethay ordsway utteredyay ybay ymay otectorspray.

in“ay ethay eanwhilemay alsoyay ethay ackblay oundgray asway overedcay ithway erbagehay, andyay
ethay eengray anksbay interspersedyay ithway innumerableyay owersflay, eetsway otay ethay
entscay andyay ethay eyesyay, arsstay ofyay alepay adianceray amongyay ethay oonlightmay oodsway;
ethay unsay ecamebay armerway, ethay ightsnay earclay andyay almybay; andyay ymay octurnalnay
amblesray ereway anyay extremeyay easureplay otay emay, althoughyay eythay ereway onsiderablycay
ortenedshay ybay ethay atelay ettingsay andyay earlyyay isingray ofyay ethay unsay, orfay Iyay evernay
enturedvay abroadyay uringday aylightday, earfulfay ofyay eetingmay ithway ethay amesay
eatmenttray Iyay adhay ormerlyfay enduredyay inyay ethay irstfay illagevay ichwhay Iyay enteredyay.

y“may aysday ereway entspay inyay oseclay attentionyay, atthay Iyay ightmay oremay eedilyspay
astermay ethay anguagelay; andyay Iyay aymay oastbay atthay Iyay improvedyay oremay apidlyray anthay
ethay Arabianyay, owhay understoodyay eryvay ittlelay andyay onversedcay inyay okenbray
accentsyay, ilstwhay Iyay omprehendedcay andyay ouldcay imitateyay almostyay everyyay ordway atthay
asway okenspay.

ile“whay Iyay improvedyay inyay eechspay, Iyay alsoyay earnedlay ethay iencescay ofyay etterslay asyay
ityay asway aughttay otay ethay angerstray, andyay isthay openedyay eforebay emay ayay ideway ieldfay
orfay onderway andyay elightday.

e“thay ookbay omfray ichwhay Elixfay instructedyay Afiesay asway Olney’svay uins_ray
ofyay Empiresyay_. Iyay ouldshay otnay avehay understoodyay ethay urportpay ofyay isthay ookbay adhay otnay
Elixfay, inyay eadingray ityay, ivengay eryvay inutemay explanationsyay. Ehay adhay osenchay isthay
orkway, ehay aidsay, ecausebay ethay eclamatoryday ylestay asway amedfray inyay imitationyay ofyay ethay
Easternyay authorsyay. Oughthray isthay orkway Iyay obtainedyay ayay ursorycay owledgeknay ofyay istoryhay
andyay ayay iewvay ofyay ethay everalsay empiresyay atyay esentpray existingyay inyay ethay orldway; ityay avegay
emay anyay insightyay intoyay ethay annersmay, overnmentsgay, andyay eligionsray ofyay ethay ifferentday
ationsnay ofyay ethay earthyay. Iyay eardhay ofyay ethay othfulslay Asiaticsyay, ofyay ethay upendousstay
eniusgay andyay entalmay activityyay ofyay ethay Eciansgray, ofyay ethay arsway andyay onderfulway irtuevay
ofyay ethay earlyyay Omans—ofray eirthay ubsequentsay egenerating—ofday ethay
eclineday ofyay atthay ightymay empireyay, ofyay ivalrychay, Istianitychray, andyay ingskay. Iyay eardhay
ofyay ethay iscoveryday ofyay ethay Americanyay emispherehay andyay eptway ithway Afiesay overyay ethay
aplesshay atefay ofyay itsyay originalyay inhabitantsyay.

ese“thay onderfulway arrationsnay inspiredyay emay ithway angestray eelingsfay. Asway
anmay, indeedyay, atyay onceyay osay owerfulpay, osay irtuousvay andyay agnificentmay, yetyay osay
iciousvay andyay asebay? Ehay appearedyay atyay oneyay imetay ayay eremay ionscay ofyay ethay evilyay
inciplepray andyay atyay anotheryay asyay allyay atthay ancay ebay onceivedcay ofyay oblenay andyay
odlikegay. Otay ebay ayay eatgray andyay irtuousvay anmay appearedyay ethay ighesthay onourhay
atthay ancay efallbay ayay ensitivesay eingbay; otay ebay asebay andyay iciousvay, asyay anymay onyay
ecordray avehay eenbay, appearedyay ethay owestlay egradationday, ayay onditioncay oremay
abjectyay anthay atthay ofyay ethay indblay olemay oryay armlesshay ormway. Orfay ayay onglay imetay Iyay
ouldcay otnay onceivecay owhay oneyay anmay ouldcay ogay orthfay otay urdermay ishay ellowfay, oryay
evenyay ywhay erethay ereway awslay andyay overnmentsgay; utbay enwhay Iyay eardhay etailsday ofyay
icevay andyay oodshedblay, ymay onderway easedcay andyay Iyay urnedtay awayyay ithway isgustday andyay
oathinglay.

every“ay onversationcay ofyay ethay ottagerscay ownay openedyay ewnay ondersway otay emay.
Ilewhay Iyay istenedlay otay ethay instructionsyay ichwhay Elixfay estowedbay uponyay ethay
Arabianyay, ethay angestray ystemsay ofyay umanhay ocietysay asway explainedyay otay emay. Iyay
eardhay ofyay ethay ivisionday ofyay opertypray, ofyay immenseyay ealthway andyay ualidsqay
overtypay, ofyay ankray, escentday, andyay oblenay oodblay.

e“thay ordsway inducedyay emay otay urntay owardstay yselfmay. Iyay earnedlay atthay ethay
ossessionspay ostmay esteemedyay ybay youryay ellowfay eaturescray ereway ighhay andyay
unsulliedyay escentday unitedyay ithway ichesray. Ayay anmay ightmay ebay espectedray ithway
onlyyay oneyay ofyay esethay advantagesyay, utbay ithoutway eitheryay ehay asway onsideredcay,
exceptyay inyay eryvay areray instancesyay, asyay ayay agabondvay andyay ayay aveslay, oomedday otay
asteway ishay owerspay orfay ethay ofitspray ofyay ethay osenchay ewfay! Andyay atwhay asway Iyay? Ofyay
ymay eationcray andyay eatorcray Iyay asway absolutelyyay ignorantyay, utbay Iyay ewknay atthay Iyay
ossessedpay onay oneymay, onay iendsfray, onay indkay ofyay opertypray. Iyay asway, esidesbay,
enduedyay ithway ayay igurefay ideouslyhay eformedday andyay oathsomelay; Iyay asway otnay evenyay
ofyay ethay amesay aturenay asyay anmay. Iyay asway oremay agileyay anthay eythay andyay ouldcay
ubsistsay uponyay oarsercay ietday; Iyay orebay ethay extremesyay ofyay eathay andyay oldcay ithway
esslay injuryyay otay ymay amefray; ymay aturestay arfay exceededyay eirsthay. Enwhay Iyay ookedlay
aroundyay Iyay awsay andyay eardhay ofyay onenay ikelay emay. Asway Iyay, enthay, ayay onstermay, ayay otblay
uponyay ethay earthyay, omfray ichwhay allyay enmay edflay andyay omwhay allyay enmay isownedday?

i“ay annotcay escribeday otay youyay ethay agonyyay atthay esethay eflectionsray inflictedyay
uponyay emay; Iyay iedtray otay ispelday emthay, utbay orrowsay onlyyay increasedyay ithway
owledgeknay. Ohyay, atthay Iyay adhay orfay everyay emainedray inyay ymay ativenay oodway, ornay
ownknay ornay eltfay eyondbay ethay ensationssay ofyay ungerhay, irstthay, andyay eathay!

of“ay atwhay ayay angestray aturenay isyay owledgeknay! Ityay ingsclay otay ethay indmay enwhay ityay
ashay onceyay eizedsay onyay ityay ikelay ayay ichenlay onyay ethay ockray. Iyay ishedway ometimessay otay
akeshay offyay allyay oughtthay andyay eelingfay, utbay Iyay earnedlay atthay erethay asway utbay oneyay
eansmay otay overcomeyay ethay ensationsay ofyay ainpay, andyay atthay asway eath—aday atestay
ichwhay Iyay earedfay yetyay idday otnay understandyay. Iyay admiredyay irtuevay andyay oodgay
eelingsfay andyay ovedlay ethay entlegay annersmay andyay amiableyay ualitiesqay ofyay ymay
ottagerscay, utbay Iyay asway utshay outyay omfray intercourseyay ithway emthay, exceptyay
oughthray eansmay ichwhay Iyay obtainedyay ybay ealthstay, enwhay Iyay asway unseenyay andyay
unknownyay, andyay ichwhay atherray increasedyay anthay atisfiedsay ethay esireday Iyay adhay ofyay
ecomingbay oneyay amongyay ymay ellowsfay. Ethay entlegay ordsway ofyay Agathayay andyay ethay
animatedyay ilessmay ofyay ethay armingchay Arabianyay ereway otnay orfay emay. Ethay ildmay
exhortationsyay ofyay ethay oldyay anmay andyay ethay ivelylay onversationcay ofyay ethay ovedlay
Elixfay ereway otnay orfay emay. Iserablemay, unhappyyay etchwray!

other“ay essonslay ereway impressedyay uponyay emay evenyay oremay eeplyday. Iyay eardhay ofyay ethay
ifferenceday ofyay exessay, andyay ethay irthbay andyay owthgray ofyay ildrenchay, owhay ethay
atherfay otedday onyay ethay ilessmay ofyay ethay infantyay, andyay ethay ivelylay alliessay ofyay ethay
olderyay ildchay, owhay allyay ethay ifelay andyay arescay ofyay ethay othermay ereway appedwray upyay
inyay ethay eciouspray argechay, owhay ethay indmay ofyay youthyay expandedyay andyay ainedgay
owledgeknay, ofyay otherbray, istersay, andyay allyay ethay ariousvay elationshipsray ichwhay
indbay oneyay umanhay eingbay otay anotheryay inyay utualmay ondsbay.

ut“bay erewhay ereway ymay iendsfray andyay elationsray? Onay atherfay adhay atchedway ymay
infantyay aysday, onay othermay adhay essedblay emay ithway ilessmay andyay aressescay; oryay ifyay
eythay adhay, allyay ymay astpay ifelay asway ownay ayay otblay, ayay indblay acancyvay inyay ichwhay Iyay
istinguishedday othingnay. Omfray ymay earliestyay emembranceray Iyay adhay eenbay asyay Iyay
enthay asway inyay eighthay andyay oportionpray. Iyay adhay evernay yetyay eensay ayay eingbay
esemblingray emay oryay owhay aimedclay anyyay intercourseyay ithway emay. Atwhay asway Iyay? Ethay
uestionqay againyay ecurredray, otay ebay answeredyay onlyyay ithway oansgray.

i“ay illway oonsay explainyay otay atwhay esethay eelingsfay endedtay, utbay allowyay emay ownay otay
eturnray otay ethay ottagerscay, osewhay orystay excitedyay inyay emay uchsay ariousvay
eelingsfay ofyay indignationyay, elightday, andyay onderway, utbay ichwhay allyay erminatedtay
inyay additionalyay ovelay andyay everenceray orfay ymay otectorspray or(fay osay Iyay ovedlay, inyay
anyay innocentyay, alf-painfulhay elf-deceitsay, otay allcay emthay).”




Apterchay 14


ome“say imetay elapsedyay eforebay Iyay earnedlay ethay istoryhay ofyay ymay iendsfray. Ityay asway
oneyay ichwhay ouldcay otnay ailfay otay impressyay itselfyay eeplyday onyay ymay indmay, unfoldingyay
asyay ityay idday ayay umbernay ofyay ircumstancescay, eachyay interestingyay andyay onderfulway otay
oneyay osay utterlyyay inexperiencedyay asyay Iyay asway.

e“thay amenay ofyay ethay oldyay anmay asway Eday Aceylay. Ehay asway escendedday omfray ayay oodgay
amilyfay inyay Ancefray, erewhay ehay adhay ivedlay orfay anymay yearsyay inyay affluenceyay,
espectedray ybay ishay uperiorssay andyay elovedbay ybay ishay equalsyay. Ishay onsay asway edbray
inyay ethay ervicesay ofyay ishay ountrycay, andyay Agathayay adhay ankedray ithway adieslay ofyay ethay
ighesthay istinctionday. Ayay ewfay onthsmay eforebay ymay arrivalyay eythay adhay ivedlay inyay
ayay argelay andyay uxuriouslay itycay alledcay Arispay, urroundedsay ybay iendsfray andyay
ossessedpay ofyay everyyay enjoymentyay ichwhay irtuevay, efinementray ofyay intellectyay, oryay
astetay, accompaniedyay ybay ayay oderatemay ortunefay, ouldcay affordyay.

e“thay atherfay ofyay Afiesay adhay eenbay ethay ausecay ofyay eirthay uinray. Ehay asway ayay
Urkishtay erchantmay andyay adhay inhabitedyay Arispay orfay anymay yearsyay, enwhay, orfay omesay
easonray ichwhay Iyay ouldcay otnay earnlay, ehay ecamebay obnoxiousyay otay ethay overnmentgay.
Ehay asway eizedsay andyay astcay intoyay isonpray ethay eryvay ayday atthay Afiesay arrivedyay omfray
Onstantinoplecay otay oinjay imhay. Ehay asway iedtray andyay ondemnedcay otay eathday. Ethay
injusticeyay ofyay ishay entencesay asway eryvay agrantflay; allyay Arispay asway indignantyay;
andyay ityay asway udgedjay atthay ishay eligionray andyay ealthway atherray anthay ethay imecray
allegedyay againstyay imhay adhay eenbay ethay ausecay ofyay ishay ondemnationcay.

elix“fay adhay accidentallyyay eenbay esentpray atyay ethay ialtray; ishay orrorhay andyay
indignationyay ereway uncontrollableyay enwhay ehay eardhay ethay ecisionday ofyay ethay
ourtcay. Ehay ademay, atyay atthay omentmay, ayay olemnsay owvay otay eliverday imhay andyay enthay
ookedlay aroundyay orfay ethay eansmay. Afteryay anymay uitlessfray attemptsyay otay aingay
admittanceyay otay ethay isonpray, ehay oundfay ayay onglystray atedgray indowway inyay anyay
unguardedyay artpay ofyay ethay uildingbay, ichwhay ightedlay ethay ungeonday ofyay ethay
unfortunateyay Uhammadanmay, owhay, oadedlay ithway ainschay, aitedway inyay espairday ethay
executionyay ofyay ethay arbarousbay entencesay. Elixfay isitedvay ethay ategray atyay ightnay
andyay ademay ownknay otay ethay isonerpray ishay intentionsyay inyay ishay avourfay. Ethay Urktay,
amazedyay andyay elightedday, endeavouredyay otay indlekay ethay ealzay ofyay ishay elivererday
ybay omisespray ofyay ewardray andyay ealthway. Elixfay ejectedray ishay offersyay ithway
ontemptcay, yetyay enwhay ehay awsay ethay ovelylay Afiesay, owhay asway allowedyay otay isitvay
erhay atherfay andyay owhay ybay erhay esturesgay expressedyay erhay ivelylay atitudegray, ethay
youthyay ouldcay otnay elphay owningyay otay ishay ownyay indmay atthay ethay aptivecay ossessedpay
ayay easuretray ichwhay ouldway ullyfay ewardray ishay oiltay andyay azardhay.

e“thay Urktay uicklyqay erceivedpay ethay impressionyay atthay ishay aughterday adhay ademay
onyay ethay earthay ofyay Elixfay andyay endeavouredyay otay ecuresay imhay oremay entirelyyay inyay
ishay interestsyay ybay ethay omisepray ofyay erhay andhay inyay arriagemay osay oonsay asyay ehay
ouldshay ebay onveyedcay otay ayay aceplay ofyay afetysay. Elixfay asway ootay elicateday otay
acceptyay isthay offeryay, yetyay ehay ookedlay orwardfay otay ethay obabilitypray ofyay ethay
eventyay asyay otay ethay onsummationcay ofyay ishay appinesshay.

uring“day ethay ensuingyay aysday, ilewhay ethay eparationspray ereway oinggay orwardfay orfay
ethay escapeyay ofyay ethay erchantmay, ethay ealzay ofyay Elixfay asway armedway ybay everalsay
etterslay atthay ehay eceivedray omfray isthay ovelylay irlgay, owhay oundfay eansmay otay
expressyay erhay oughtsthay inyay ethay anguagelay ofyay erhay overlay ybay ethay aidyay ofyay anyay oldyay
anmay, ayay ervantsay ofyay erhay atherfay owhay understoodyay Enchfray. Eshay ankedthay imhay inyay
ethay ostmay ardentyay ermstay orfay ishay intendedyay ervicessay owardstay erhay arentpay, andyay
atyay ethay amesay imetay eshay entlygay eploredday erhay ownyay atefay.

i“ay avehay opiescay ofyay esethay etterslay, orfay Iyay oundfay eansmay, uringday ymay esidenceray
inyay ethay ovelhay, otay ocurepray ethay implementsyay ofyay itingwray; andyay ethay etterslay
ereway oftenyay inyay ethay andshay ofyay Elixfay oryay Agathayay. Eforebay Iyay epartday Iyay illway
ivegay emthay otay youyay; eythay illway ovepray ethay uthtray ofyay ymay aletay; utbay atyay esentpray,
asyay ethay unsay isyay alreadyyay arfay eclinedday, Iyay allshay onlyyay avehay imetay otay epeatray
ethay ubstancesay ofyay emthay otay youyay.

afie“say elatedray atthay erhay othermay asway ayay Istianchray Arabyay, eizedsay andyay ademay ayay
aveslay ybay ethay Urkstay; ecommendedray ybay erhay eautybay, eshay adhay onway ethay earthay ofyay
ethay atherfay ofyay Afiesay, owhay arriedmay erhay. Ethay youngyay irlgay okespay inyay ighhay andyay
enthusiasticyay ermstay ofyay erhay othermay, owhay, ornbay inyay eedomfray, urnedspay ethay
ondagebay otay ichwhay eshay asway ownay educedray. Eshay instructedyay erhay aughterday inyay
ethay enetstay ofyay erhay eligionray andyay aughttay erhay otay aspireyay otay igherhay owerspay ofyay
intellectyay andyay anyay independenceyay ofyay iritspay orbiddenfay otay ethay emalefay
ollowersfay ofyay Uhammadmay. Isthay adylay iedday, utbay erhay essonslay ereway indeliblyyay
impressedyay onyay ethay indmay ofyay Afiesay, owhay ickenedsay atyay ethay ospectpray ofyay againyay
eturningray otay Asiayay andyay eingbay immuredyay ithinway ethay allsway ofyay ayay aremhay,
allowedyay onlyyay otay occupyyay erselfhay ithway infantileyay amusementsyay, ill-suitedyay otay
ethay empertay ofyay erhay oulsay, ownay accustomedyay otay andgray ideasyay andyay ayay oblenay
emulationyay orfay irtuevay. Ethay ospectpray ofyay arryingmay ayay Istianchray andyay
emainingray inyay ayay ountrycay erewhay omenway ereway allowedyay otay aketay ayay ankray inyay
ocietysay asway enchantingyay otay erhay.

e“thay ayday orfay ethay executionyay ofyay ethay Urktay asway ixedfay, utbay onyay ethay ightnay
eviouspray otay ityay ehay uittedqay ishay isonpray andyay eforebay orningmay asway istantday
anymay eagueslay omfray Arispay. Elixfay adhay ocuredpray assportspay inyay ethay amenay ofyay
ishay atherfay, istersay, andyay imselfhay. Ehay adhay eviouslypray ommunicatedcay ishay
anplay otay ethay ormerfay, owhay aidedyay ethay eceitday ybay uittingqay ishay ousehay, underyay
ethay etencepray ofyay ayay ourneyjay andyay oncealedcay imselfhay, ithway ishay aughterday, inyay
anyay obscureyay artpay ofyay Arispay.

elix“fay onductedcay ethay ugitivesfay oughthray Ancefray otay Yonslay andyay acrossyay Ontmay
Eniscay otay Eghornlay, erewhay ethay erchantmay adhay ecidedday otay aitway ayay avourablefay
opportunityyay ofyay assingpay intoyay omesay artpay ofyay ethay Urkishtay ominionsday.

afie“say esolvedray otay emainray ithway erhay atherfay untilyay ethay omentmay ofyay ishay
epartureday, eforebay ichwhay imetay ethay Urktay enewedray ishay omisepray atthay eshay
ouldshay ebay unitedyay otay ishay elivererday; andyay Elixfay emainedray ithway emthay inyay
expectationyay ofyay atthay eventyay; andyay inyay ethay eantimemay ehay enjoyedyay ethay ocietysay
ofyay ethay Arabianyay, owhay exhibitedyay owardstay imhay ethay implestsay andyay enderesttay
affectionyay. Eythay onversedcay ithway oneyay anotheryay oughthray ethay eansmay ofyay anyay
interpreteryay, andyay ometimessay ithway ethay interpretationyay ofyay ookslay; andyay Afiesay
angsay otay imhay ethay ivineday airsyay ofyay erhay ativenay ountrycay.

e“thay Urktay allowedyay isthay intimacyyay otay aketay aceplay andyay encouragedyay ethay opeshay
ofyay ethay youthfulyay overslay, ilewhay inyay ishay earthay ehay adhay ormedfay arfay otheryay
ansplay. Ehay oathedlay ethay ideayay atthay ishay aughterday ouldshay ebay unitedyay otay ayay
Istianchray, utbay ehay earedfay ethay esentmentray ofyay Elixfay ifyay ehay ouldshay appearyay
ukewarmlay, orfay ehay ewknay atthay ehay asway illstay inyay ethay owerpay ofyay ishay elivererday
ifyay ehay ouldshay oosechay otay etraybay imhay otay ethay Italianyay atestay ichwhay eythay
inhabitedyay. Ehay evolvedray ayay ousandthay ansplay ybay ichwhay ehay ouldshay ebay enabledyay
otay olongpray ethay eceitday untilyay ityay ightmay ebay onay ongerlay ecessarynay, andyay
ecretlysay otay aketay ishay aughterday ithway imhay enwhay ehay epartedday. Ishay ansplay
ereway acilitatedfay ybay ethay ewsnay ichwhay arrivedyay omfray Arispay.

e“thay overnmentgay ofyay Ancefray ereway eatlygray enragedyay atyay ethay escapeyay ofyay eirthay
ictimvay andyay aredspay onay ainspay otay etectday andyay unishpay ishay elivererday. Ethay
otplay ofyay Elixfay asway uicklyqay iscoveredday, andyay Eday Aceylay andyay Agathayay ereway
ownthray intoyay isonpray. Ethay ewsnay eachedray Elixfay andyay ousedray imhay omfray ishay
eamdray ofyay easureplay. Ishay indblay andyay agedyay atherfay andyay ishay entlegay istersay aylay
inyay ayay oisomenay ungeonday ilewhay ehay enjoyedyay ethay eefray airyay andyay ethay ocietysay ofyay
erhay omwhay ehay ovedlay. Isthay ideayay asway orturetay otay imhay. Ehay uicklyqay arrangedyay
ithway ethay Urktay atthay ifyay ethay atterlay ouldshay indfay ayay avourablefay opportunityyay
orfay escapeyay eforebay Elixfay ouldcay eturnray otay Italyyay, Afiesay ouldshay emainray asyay ayay
oarderbay atyay ayay onventcay atyay Eghornlay; andyay enthay, uittingqay ethay ovelylay Arabianyay,
ehay astenedhay otay Arispay andyay eliveredday imselfhay upyay otay ethay engeancevay ofyay ethay
awlay, opinghay otay eefray Eday Aceylay andyay Agathayay ybay isthay oceedingpray.

e“hay idday otnay ucceedsay. Eythay emainedray onfinedcay orfay ivefay onthsmay eforebay ethay
ialtray ooktay aceplay, ethay esultray ofyay ichwhay eprivedday emthay ofyay eirthay ortunefay
andyay ondemnedcay emthay otay ayay erpetualpay exileyay omfray eirthay ativenay ountrycay.

ey“thay oundfay ayay iserablemay asylumyay inyay ethay ottagecay inyay Ermanygay, erewhay Iyay
iscoveredday emthay. Elixfay oonsay earnedlay atthay ethay eacheroustray Urktay, orfay
omwhay ehay andyay ishay amilyfay enduredyay uchsay unheard-ofyay oppressionyay, onyay
iscoveringday atthay ishay elivererday asway usthay educedray otay overtypay andyay uinray,
ecamebay ayay aitortray otay oodgay eelingfay andyay onourhay andyay adhay uittedqay Italyyay ithway
ishay aughterday, insultinglyyay endingsay Elixfay ayay ittancepay ofyay oneymay otay aidyay imhay,
asyay ehay aidsay, inyay omesay anplay ofyay uturefay aintenancemay.

uch“say ereway ethay eventsyay atthay eyedpray onyay ethay earthay ofyay Elixfay andyay enderedray
imhay, enwhay Iyay irstfay awsay imhay, ethay ostmay iserablemay ofyay ishay amilyfay. Ehay ouldcay
avehay enduredyay overtypay, andyay ilewhay isthay istressday adhay eenbay ethay eedmay ofyay ishay
irtuevay, ehay oriedglay inyay ityay; utbay ethay ingratitudeyay ofyay ethay Urktay andyay ethay osslay
ofyay ishay elovedbay Afiesay ereway isfortunesmay oremay itterbay andyay irreparableyay. Ethay
arrivalyay ofyay ethay Arabianyay ownay infusedyay ewnay ifelay intoyay ishay oulsay.

en“whay ethay ewsnay eachedray Eghornlay atthay Elixfay asway eprivedday ofyay ishay ealthway
andyay ankray, ethay erchantmay ommandedcay ishay aughterday otay inkthay onay oremay ofyay erhay
overlay, utbay otay eparepray otay eturnray otay erhay ativenay ountrycay. Ethay enerousgay
aturenay ofyay Afiesay asway outragedyay ybay isthay ommandcay; eshay attemptedyay otay
expostulateyay ithway erhay atherfay, utbay ehay eftlay erhay angrilyyay, eiteratingray ishay
yrannicaltay andatemay.

a“ay ewfay aysday afteryay, ethay Urktay enteredyay ishay aughter’sday apartmentyay andyay oldtay
erhay astilyhay atthay ehay adhay easonray otay elievebay atthay ishay esidenceray atyay Eghornlay
adhay eenbay ivulgedday andyay atthay ehay ouldshay eedilyspay ebay eliveredday upyay otay ethay
Enchfray overnmentgay; ehay adhay onsequentlycay iredhay ayay esselvay otay onveycay imhay otay
Onstantinoplecay, orfay ichwhay itycay ehay ouldshay ailsay inyay ayay ewfay ourshay. Ehay
intendedyay otay eavelay ishay aughterday underyay ethay arecay ofyay ayay onfidentialcay
ervantsay, otay ollowfay atyay erhay eisurelay ithway ethay eatergray artpay ofyay ishay
opertypray, ichwhay adhay otnay yetyay arrivedyay atyay Eghornlay.

en“whay aloneyay, Afiesay esolvedray inyay erhay ownyay indmay ethay anplay ofyay onductcay atthay ityay
ouldway ecomebay erhay otay ursuepay inyay isthay emergencyyay. Ayay esidenceray inyay Urkeytay
asway abhorrentyay otay erhay; erhay eligionray andyay erhay eelingsfay ereway alikeyay averseyay
otay ityay. Ybay omesay aperspay ofyay erhay atherfay ichwhay ellfay intoyay erhay andshay eshay
eardhay ofyay ethay exileyay ofyay erhay overlay andyay earntlay ethay amenay ofyay ethay otspay erewhay
ehay enthay esidedray. Eshay esitatedhay omesay imetay, utbay atyay engthlay eshay ormedfay erhay
eterminationday. Akingtay ithway erhay omesay ewelsjay atthay elongedbay otay erhay andyay ayay
umsay ofyay oneymay, eshay uittedqay Italyyay ithway anyay attendantyay, ayay ativenay ofyay Eghornlay,
utbay owhay understoodyay ethay ommoncay anguagelay ofyay Urkeytay, andyay epartedday orfay
Ermanygay.

e“shay arrivedyay inyay afetysay atyay ayay owntay aboutyay entytway eagueslay omfray ethay ottagecay
ofyay Eday Aceylay, enwhay erhay attendantyay ellfay angerouslyday illyay. Afiesay ursednay erhay
ithway ethay ostmay evotedday affectionyay, utbay ethay oorpay irlgay iedday, andyay ethay
Arabianyay asway eftlay aloneyay, unacquaintedyay ithway ethay anguagelay ofyay ethay ountrycay
andyay utterlyyay ignorantyay ofyay ethay ustomscay ofyay ethay orldway. Eshay ellfay, oweverhay,
intoyay oodgay andshay. Ethay Italianyay adhay entionedmay ethay amenay ofyay ethay otspay orfay
ichwhay eythay ereway oundbay, andyay afteryay erhay eathday ethay omanway ofyay ethay ousehay inyay
ichwhay eythay adhay ivedlay ooktay arecay atthay Afiesay ouldshay arriveyay inyay afetysay atyay
ethay ottagecay ofyay erhay overlay.”




Apterchay 15


uch“say asway ethay istoryhay ofyay ymay elovedbay ottagerscay. Ityay impressedyay emay eeplyday.
Iyay earnedlay, omfray ethay iewsvay ofyay ocialsay ifelay ichwhay ityay evelopedday, otay admireyay
eirthay irtuesvay andyay otay eprecateday ethay icesvay ofyay ankindmay.

as“ay yetyay Iyay ookedlay uponyay imecray asyay ayay istantday evilyay, enevolencebay andyay
enerositygay ereway everyay esentpray eforebay emay, incitingyay ithinway emay ayay esireday otay
ecomebay anyay actoryay inyay ethay usybay enescay erewhay osay anymay admirableyay ualitiesqay
ereway alledcay orthfay andyay isplayedday. Utbay inyay ivinggay anyay accountyay ofyay ethay
ogresspray ofyay ymay intellectyay, Iyay ustmay otnay omityay ayay ircumstancecay ichwhay occurredyay
inyay ethay eginningbay ofyay ethay onthmay ofyay Augustyay ofyay ethay amesay yearyay.

one“ay ightnay uringday ymay accustomedyay isitvay otay ethay eighbouringnay oodway erewhay Iyay
ollectedcay ymay ownyay oodfay andyay oughtbray omehay iringfay orfay ymay otectorspray, Iyay oundfay onyay
ethay oundgray ayay eathernlay ortmanteaupay ontainingcay everalsay articlesyay ofyay essdray andyay
omesay ooksbay. Iyay eagerlyyay eizedsay ethay izepray andyay eturnedray ithway ityay otay ymay ovelhay. 
Ortunatelyfay ethay ooksbay ereway ittenwray inyay ethay anguagelay, ethay elementsyay ofyay ichwhay Iyay
adhay acquiredyay atyay ethay ottagecay; eythay onsistedcay ofyay aradise_pay Ostlay_, ayay olumevay
ofyay utarch’s_play Iveslay_, andyay ethay orrows_say ofyay Erterway_. Ethay
ossessionpay ofyay esethay easurestray avegay emay extremeyay elightday; Iyay ownay ontinuallycay
udiedstay andyay exercisedyay ymay indmay uponyay esethay istorieshay, ilstwhay ymay iendsfray ereway
employedyay inyay eirthay ordinaryyay occupationsyay.

i“ay ancay ardlyhay escribeday otay youyay ethay effectyay ofyay esethay ooksbay. Eythay oducedpray
inyay emay anyay infinityyay ofyay ewnay imagesyay andyay eelingsfay, atthay ometimessay aisedray emay
otay ecstasyyay, utbay oremay equentlyfray unksay emay intoyay ethay owestlay ejectionday. Inyay
ethay orrows_say ofyay Erterway_, esidesbay ethay interestyay ofyay itsyay implesay andyay affectingyay
orystay, osay anymay opinionsyay areyay anvassedcay andyay osay anymay ightslay ownthray uponyay
atwhay adhay ithertohay eenbay otay emay obscureyay ubjectssay atthay Iyay oundfay inyay ityay ayay
ever-endingnay ourcesay ofyay eculationspay andyay astonishmentyay. Ethay entlegay andyay
omesticday annersmay ityay escribedday, ombinedcay ithway oftylay entimentssay andyay
eelingsfay, ichwhay adhay orfay eirthay objectyay omethingsay outyay ofyay elfsay, accordedyay
ellway ithway ymay experienceyay amongyay ymay otectorspray andyay ithway ethay antsway ichwhay
ereway orfay everyay aliveyay inyay ymay ownyay osombay. Utbay Iyay oughtthay Erterway imselfhay ayay
oremay ivineday eingbay anthay Iyay adhay everyay eheldbay oryay imaginedyay; ishay aracterchay
