ontainedcay onay etensionpray, utbay ityay anksay eepday. Ethay isquisitionsday uponyay
eathday andyay uicidesay ereway alculatedcay otay illfay emay ithway onderway. Iyay idday otnay
etendpray otay enteryay intoyay ethay eritsmay ofyay ethay asecay, yetyay Iyay inclinedyay owardstay
ethay opinionsyay ofyay ethay erohay, osewhay extinctionyay Iyay eptway, ithoutway eciselypray
understandingyay ityay.

as“ay Iyay eadray, oweverhay, Iyay appliedyay uchmay ersonallypay otay ymay ownyay eelingsfay andyay
onditioncay. Iyay oundfay yselfmay imilarsay yetyay atyay ethay amesay imetay angelystray
unlikeyay otay ethay eingsbay oncerningcay omwhay Iyay eadray andyay otay osewhay onversationcay Iyay
asway ayay istenerlay. Iyay ympathisedsay ithway andyay artlypay understoodyay emthay, utbay Iyay
asway unformedyay inyay indmay; Iyay asway ependentday onyay onenay andyay elatedray otay onenay.
e‘thay athpay ofyay ymay epartureday asway eefray,’ andyay erethay asway onenay otay amentlay ymay
annihilationyay. Ymay ersonpay asway ideoushay andyay ymay aturestay iganticgay. Atwhay idday
isthay eanmay? Owhay asway Iyay? Atwhay asway Iyay? Encewhay idday Iyay omecay? Atwhay asway ymay
estinationday? Esethay uestionsqay ontinuallycay ecurredray, utbay Iyay asway unableyay otay
olvesay emthay.

e“thay olumevay ofyay utarch’s_play Iveslay_ ichwhay Iyay ossessedpay ontainedcay ethay
istorieshay ofyay ethay irstfay oundersfay ofyay ethay ancientyay epublicsray. Isthay ookbay
adhay ayay arfay ifferentday effectyay uponyay emay omfray ethay orrows_say ofyay Erterway_. Iyay
earnedlay omfray Erter’sway imaginationsyay espondencyday andyay oomglay, utbay Utarchplay
aughttay emay ighhay oughtsthay; ehay elevatedyay emay aboveyay ethay etchedwray eresphay ofyay ymay
ownyay eflectionsray, otay admireyay andyay ovelay ethay eroeshay ofyay astpay agesyay. Anymay
ingsthay Iyay eadray urpassedsay ymay understandingyay andyay experienceyay. Iyay adhay ayay eryvay
onfusedcay owledgeknay ofyay ingdomskay, ideway extentsyay ofyay ountrycay, ightymay iversray,
andyay oundlessbay eassay. Utbay Iyay asway erfectlypay unacquaintedyay ithway ownstay andyay
argelay assemblagesyay ofyay enmay. Ethay ottagecay ofyay ymay otectorspray adhay eenbay ethay
onlyyay oolschay inyay ichwhay Iyay adhay udiedstay umanhay aturenay, utbay isthay ookbay
evelopedday ewnay andyay ightiermay enesscay ofyay actionyay. Iyay eadray ofyay enmay oncernedcay
inyay ublicpay affairsyay, overninggay oryay assacringmay eirthay eciesspay. Iyay eltfay ethay
eatestgray ardouryay orfay irtuevay iseray ithinway emay, andyay abhorrenceyay orfay icevay, asyay
arfay asyay Iyay understoodyay ethay ignificationsay ofyay osethay ermstay, elativeray asyay eythay
ereway, asyay Iyay appliedyay emthay, otay easureplay andyay ainpay aloneyay. Inducedyay ybay esethay
eelingsfay, Iyay asway ofyay oursecay edlay otay admireyay eaceablepay awgiverslay, Umanay,
Olonsay, andyay Ycurguslay, inyay eferencepray otay Omulusray andyay Eseusthay. Ethay
atriarchalpay iveslay ofyay ymay otectorspray ausedcay esethay impressionsyay otay aketay ayay
irmfay oldhay onyay ymay indmay; erhapspay, ifyay ymay irstfay introductionyay otay umanityhay adhay
eenbay ademay ybay ayay youngyay oldiersay, urningbay orfay oryglay andyay aughterslay, Iyay ouldshay
avehay eenbay imbuedyay ithway ifferentday ensationssay.

ut“bay aradise_pay Ostlay_ excitedyay ifferentday andyay arfay eeperday emotionsyay. Iyay eadray
ityay, asyay Iyay adhay eadray ethay otheryay olumesvay ichwhay adhay allenfay intoyay ymay andshay, asyay
ayay uetray istoryhay. Ityay ovedmay everyyay eelingfay ofyay onderway andyay aweyay atthay ethay
icturepay ofyay anyay omnipotentyay Odgay arringway ithway ishay eaturescray asway apablecay ofyay
excitingyay. Iyay oftenyay eferredray ethay everalsay ituationssay, asyay eirthay imilaritysay
uckstray emay, otay ymay ownyay. Ikelay Adamyay, Iyay asway apparentlyyay unitedyay ybay onay inklay otay
anyyay otheryay eingbay inyay existenceyay; utbay ishay atestay asway arfay ifferentday omfray inemay
inyay everyyay otheryay espectray. Ehay adhay omecay orthfay omfray ethay andshay ofyay Odgay ayay
erfectpay eaturecray, appyhay andyay osperouspray, uardedgay ybay ethay especialyay arecay ofyay
ishay Eatorcray; ehay asway allowedyay otay onversecay ithway andyay acquireyay owledgeknay omfray
eingsbay ofyay ayay uperiorsay aturenay, utbay Iyay asway etchedwray, elplesshay, andyay aloneyay.
Anymay imestay Iyay onsideredcay Atansay asyay ethay itterfay emblemyay ofyay ymay onditioncay, orfay
oftenyay, ikelay imhay, enwhay Iyay iewedvay ethay issblay ofyay ymay otectorspray, ethay itterbay
allgay ofyay envyyay oseray ithinway emay.

another“ay ircumstancecay engthenedstray andyay onfirmedcay esethay eelingsfay. Oonsay
afteryay ymay arrivalyay inyay ethay ovelhay Iyay iscoveredday omesay aperspay inyay ethay ocketpay ofyay
ethay essdray ichwhay Iyay adhay akentay omfray youryay aboratorylay. Atyay irstfay Iyay adhay
eglectednay emthay, utbay ownay atthay Iyay asway ableyay otay ecipherday ethay aracterschay inyay
ichwhay eythay ereway ittenwray, Iyay eganbay otay udystay emthay ithway iligenceday. Ityay asway
youryay ournaljay ofyay ethay ourfay onthsmay atthay ecededpray ymay eationcray. Youyay
inutelymay escribedday inyay esethay aperspay everyyay epstay youyay ooktay inyay ethay ogresspray
ofyay youryay orkway; isthay istoryhay asway ingledmay ithway accountsyay ofyay omesticday
occurrencesyay. Youyay oubtlessday ecollectray esethay aperspay. Erehay eythay areyay.
Everythingyay isyay elatedray inyay emthay ichwhay earsbay eferenceray otay ymay accursedyay
originyay; ethay olewhay etailday ofyay atthay eriessay ofyay isgustingday ircumstancescay
ichwhay oducedpray ityay isyay etsay inyay iewvay; ethay inutestmay escriptionday ofyay ymay odiousyay
andyay oathsomelay ersonpay isyay ivengay, inyay anguagelay ichwhay aintedpay youryay ownyay
orrorshay andyay enderedray inemay indelibleyay. Iyay ickenedsay asyay Iyay eadray. ateful‘hay
ayday enwhay Iyay eceivedray ifelay!’ Iyay exclaimedyay inyay agonyyay. accursed‘ay eatorcray!
Ywhay idday youyay ormfay ayay onstermay osay ideoushay atthay evenyay you_ay_ urnedtay omfray emay inyay
isgustday? Odgay, inyay itypay, ademay anmay eautifulbay andyay alluringyay, afteryay ishay ownyay
imageyay; utbay ymay ormfay isyay ayay ilthyfay ypetay ofyay yoursyay, oremay orridhay evenyay omfray ethay
eryvay esemblanceray. Atansay adhay ishay ompanionscay, ellowfay evilsday, otay admireyay
andyay encourageyay imhay, utbay Iyay amyay olitarysay andyay abhorredyay.’

ese“thay ereway ethay eflectionsray ofyay ymay ourshay ofyay espondencyday andyay olitudesay;
utbay enwhay Iyay ontemplatedcay ethay irtuesvay ofyay ethay ottagerscay, eirthay amiableyay andyay
enevolentbay ispositionsday, Iyay ersuadedpay yselfmay atthay enwhay eythay ouldshay
ecomebay acquaintedyay ithway ymay admirationyay ofyay eirthay irtuesvay eythay ouldway
ompassionatecay emay andyay overlookyay ymay ersonalpay eformityday. Ouldcay eythay urntay
omfray eirthay oorday oneyay, oweverhay onstrousmay, owhay olicitedsay eirthay ompassioncay
andyay iendshipfray? Iyay esolvedray, atyay eastlay, otnay otay espairday, utbay inyay everyyay ayway
otay itfay yselfmay orfay anyay interviewyay ithway emthay ichwhay ouldway ecideday ymay atefay. Iyay
ostponedpay isthay attemptyay orfay omesay onthsmay ongerlay, orfay ethay importanceyay
attachedyay otay itsyay uccesssay inspiredyay emay ithway ayay eaddray estlay Iyay ouldshay ailfay.
Esidesbay, Iyay oundfay atthay ymay understandingyay improvedyay osay uchmay ithway everyyay
ay’sday experienceyay atthay Iyay asway unwillingyay otay ommencecay isthay undertakingyay
untilyay ayay ewfay oremay onthsmay ouldshay avehay addedyay otay ymay agacitysay.

everal“say angeschay, inyay ethay eantimemay, ooktay aceplay inyay ethay ottagecay. Ethay
esencepray ofyay Afiesay iffusedday appinesshay amongyay itsyay inhabitantsyay, andyay Iyay alsoyay
oundfay atthay ayay eatergray egreeday ofyay entyplay eignedray erethay. Elixfay andyay Agathayay
entspay oremay imetay inyay amusementyay andyay onversationcay, andyay ereway assistedyay inyay
eirthay abourslay ybay ervantssay. Eythay idday otnay appearyay ichray, utbay eythay ereway
ontentedcay andyay appyhay; eirthay eelingsfay ereway erenesay andyay eacefulpay, ilewhay
inemay ecamebay everyyay ayday oremay umultuoustay. Increaseyay ofyay owledgeknay onlyyay
iscoveredday otay emay oremay earlyclay atwhay ayay etchedwray outcastyay Iyay asway. Iyay
erishedchay opehay, ityay isyay uetray, utbay ityay anishedvay enwhay Iyay eheldbay ymay ersonpay
eflectedray inyay aterway oryay ymay adowshay inyay ethay oonshinemay, evenyay asyay atthay ailfray
imageyay andyay atthay inconstantyay adeshay.

i“ay endeavouredyay otay ushcray esethay earsfay andyay otay ortifyfay yselfmay orfay ethay ialtray
ichwhay inyay ayay ewfay onthsmay Iyay esolvedray otay undergoyay; andyay ometimessay Iyay allowedyay ymay
oughtsthay, uncheckedyay ybay easonray, otay ambleray inyay ethay ieldsfay ofyay Aradisepay, andyay
aredday otay ancyfay amiableyay andyay ovelylay eaturescray ympathisingsay ithway ymay
eelingsfay andyay eeringchay ymay oomglay; eirthay angelicyay ountenancescay eathedbray
ilessmay ofyay onsolationcay. Utbay ityay asway allyay ayay eamdray; onay Eveyay oothedsay ymay
orrowssay ornay aredshay ymay oughtsthay; Iyay asway aloneyay. Iyay ememberedray Adam’syay
upplicationsay otay ishay Eatorcray. Utbay erewhay asway inemay? Ehay adhay abandonedyay emay,
andyay inyay ethay itternessbay ofyay ymay earthay Iyay ursedcay imhay.

autumn“ay assedpay usthay. Iyay awsay, ithway urprisesay andyay iefgray, ethay eaveslay ecayday
andyay allfay, andyay aturenay againyay assumeyay ethay arrenbay andyay eakblay appearanceyay ityay
adhay ornway enwhay Iyay irstfay eheldbay ethay oodsway andyay ethay ovelylay oonmay. Yetyay Iyay idday
otnay eedhay ethay eaknessblay ofyay ethay eatherway; Iyay asway etterbay ittedfay ybay ymay
onformationcay orfay ethay enduranceyay ofyay oldcay anthay eathay. Utbay ymay iefchay
elightsday ereway ethay ightsay ofyay ethay owersflay, ethay irdsbay, andyay allyay ethay aygay
apparelyay ofyay ummersay; enwhay osethay esertedday emay, Iyay urnedtay ithway oremay attentionyay
owardstay ethay ottagerscay. Eirthay appinesshay asway otnay ecreasedday ybay ethay
absenceyay ofyay ummersay. Eythay ovedlay andyay ympathisedsay ithway oneyay anotheryay; andyay
eirthay oysjay, ependingday onyay eachyay otheryay, ereway otnay interruptedyay ybay ethay
asualtiescay atthay ooktay aceplay aroundyay emthay. Ethay oremay Iyay awsay ofyay emthay, ethay
eatergray ecamebay ymay esireday otay aimclay eirthay otectionpray andyay indnesskay; ymay
earthay yearnedyay otay ebay ownknay andyay ovedlay ybay esethay amiableyay eaturescray; otay eesay
eirthay eetsway ookslay irectedday owardstay emay ithway affectionyay asway ethay utmostyay
imitlay ofyay ymay ambitionyay. Iyay aredday otnay inkthay atthay eythay ouldway urntay emthay omfray
emay ithway isdainday andyay orrorhay. Ethay oorpay atthay oppedstay atyay eirthay oorday ereway
evernay ivendray awayyay. Iyay askedyay, ityay isyay uetray, orfay eatergray easurestray anthay ayay
ittlelay oodfay oryay estray: Iyay equiredray indnesskay andyay ympathysay; utbay Iyay idday otnay
elievebay yselfmay utterlyyay unworthyyay ofyay ityay.

e“thay interway advancedyay, andyay anyay entireyay evolutionray ofyay ethay easonssay adhay akentay
aceplay incesay Iyay awokeyay intoyay ifelay. Ymay attentionyay atyay isthay imetay asway olelysay
irectedday owardstay ymay anplay ofyay introducingyay yselfmay intoyay ethay ottagecay ofyay ymay
otectorspray. Iyay evolvedray anymay ojectspray, utbay atthay onyay ichwhay Iyay inallyfay
ixedfay asway otay enteryay ethay ellingdway enwhay ethay indblay oldyay anmay ouldshay ebay aloneyay.
Iyay adhay agacitysay enoughyay otay iscoverday atthay ethay unnaturalyay ideousnesshay ofyay ymay
ersonpay asway ethay iefchay objectyay ofyay orrorhay ithway osethay owhay adhay ormerlyfay
eheldbay emay. Ymay oicevay, althoughyay arshhay, adhay othingnay erribletay inyay ityay; Iyay
oughtthay, ereforethay, atthay ifyay inyay ethay absenceyay ofyay ishay ildrenchay Iyay ouldcay aingay
ethay oodgay illway andyay ediationmay ofyay ethay oldyay Eday Aceylay, Iyay ightmay ybay ishay eansmay
ebay oleratedtay ybay ymay youngeryay otectorspray.

one“ay ayday, enwhay ethay unsay oneshay onyay ethay edray eaveslay atthay ewedstray ethay oundgray
andyay iffusedday eerfulnesschay, althoughyay ityay eniedday armthway, Afiesay, Agathayay,
andyay Elixfay epartedday onyay ayay onglay ountrycay alkway, andyay ethay oldyay anmay, atyay ishay ownyay
esireday, asway eftlay aloneyay inyay ethay ottagecay. Enwhay ishay ildrenchay adhay epartedday,
ehay ooktay upyay ishay uitargay andyay ayedplay everalsay ournfulmay utbay eetsway airsyay, oremay
eetsway andyay ournfulmay anthay Iyay adhay everyay eardhay imhay ayplay eforebay. Atyay irstfay ishay
ountenancecay asway illuminatedyay ithway easureplay, utbay asyay ehay ontinuedcay,
oughtfulnessthay andyay adnesssay ucceededsay; atyay engthlay, ayinglay asideyay ethay
instrumentyay, ehay atsay absorbedyay inyay eflectionray.

y“may earthay eatbay uickqay; isthay asway ethay ourhay andyay omentmay ofyay ialtray, ichwhay
ouldway ecideday ymay opeshay oryay ealiseray ymay earsfay. Ethay ervantssay ereway onegay otay ayay
eighbouringnay airfay. Allyay asway ilentsay inyay andyay aroundyay ethay ottagecay; ityay asway anyay
excellentyay opportunityyay; yetyay, enwhay Iyay oceededpray otay executeyay ymay anplay, ymay
imbslay ailedfay emay andyay Iyay anksay otay ethay oundgray. Againyay Iyay oseray, andyay exertingyay
allyay ethay irmnessfay ofyay ichwhay Iyay asway astermay, emovedray ethay anksplay ichwhay Iyay adhay
acedplay eforebay ymay ovelhay otay oncealcay ymay etreatray. Ethay eshfray airyay evivedray
emay, andyay ithway enewedray eterminationday Iyay approachedyay ethay oorday ofyay eirthay
ottagecay.

i“ay ockedknay. o‘whay isyay erethay?’ aidsay ethay oldyay anmay. ome‘cay inyay.’

i“ay enteredyay. ardon‘pay isthay intrusionyay,’ aidsay Iyay; i‘ay amyay
ayay avellertray inyay antway ofyay ayay ittlelay estray; youyay ouldway eatlygray obligeyay emay ifyay youyay
ouldway allowyay emay otay emainray ayay ewfay inutesmay eforebay ethay irefay.’

enter“‘ay,’ aidsay Eday Aceylay, and‘ay Iyay illway ytray inyay atwhay
annermay Iyay ancay otay elieveray youryay antsway; utbay, unfortunatelyyay, ymay ildrenchay areyay
omfray omehay, andyay asyay Iyay amyay indblay, Iyay amyay afraidyay Iyay allshay indfay ityay ifficultday otay
ocurepray oodfay orfay youyay.’

o“‘day otnay oubletray yourselfyay, ymay indkay osthay; Iyay avehay oodfay; ityay isyay
armthway andyay estray onlyyay atthay Iyay eednay.’

i“ay atsay ownday, andyay ayay ilencesay ensuedyay. Iyay ewknay atthay everyyay inutemay asway
eciouspray otay emay, yetyay Iyay emainedray irresoluteyay inyay atwhay annermay otay ommencecay
ethay interviewyay, enwhay ethay oldyay anmay addressedyay emay.

y‘bay youryay anguagelay, angerstray, Iyay upposesay youyay areyay ymay ountrymancay; areyay youyay
Enchfray?’

o“‘nay; utbay Iyay asway educatedyay ybay ayay Enchfray amilyfay andyay understandyay atthay
anguagelay onlyyay. Iyay amyay ownay oinggay otay aimclay ethay otectionpray ofyay omesay iendsfray,
omwhay Iyay incerelysay ovelay, andyay ofyay osewhay avourfay Iyay avehay omesay opeshay.’

are“‘ay eythay Ermansgay?’

o“‘nay, eythay areyay Enchfray. Utbay etlay usyay angechay ethay ubjectsay. Iyay amyay anyay
unfortunateyay andyay esertedday eaturecray, Iyay ooklay aroundyay andyay Iyay avehay onay elationray
oryay iendfray uponyay earthyay. Esethay amiableyay eoplepay otay omwhay Iyay ogay avehay evernay
eensay emay andyay owknay ittlelay ofyay emay. Iyay amyay ullfay ofyay earsfay, orfay ifyay Iyay ailfay
erethay, Iyay amyay anyay outcastyay inyay ethay orldway orfay everyay.’

o“‘day otnay espairday. Otay ebay iendlessfray isyay indeedyay otay ebay unfortunateyay, utbay
ethay eartshay ofyay enmay, enwhay unprejudicedyay ybay anyyay obviousyay elf-interestsay, areyay
ullfay ofyay otherlybray ovelay andyay aritychay. Elyray, ereforethay, onyay youryay opeshay;
andyay ifyay esethay iendsfray areyay oodgay andyay amiableyay, oday otnay espairday.’

ey“‘thay areyay ind—theykay areyay ethay ostmay excellentyay eaturescray inyay ethay orldway;
utbay, unfortunatelyyay, eythay areyay ejudicedpray againstyay emay. Iyay avehay oodgay
ispositionsday; ymay ifelay ashay eenbay ithertohay armlesshay andyay inyay omesay egreeday
eneficialbay; utbay ayay atalfay ejudicepray oudsclay eirthay eyesyay, andyay erewhay eythay
oughtyay otay eesay ayay eelingfay andyay indkay iendfray, eythay eholdbay onlyyay ayay etestableday
onstermay.’

at“‘thay isyay indeedyay unfortunateyay; utbay ifyay youyay areyay eallyray amelessblay, annotcay
youyay undeceiveyay emthay?’

i“‘ay amyay aboutyay otay undertakeyay atthay asktay; andyay ityay isyay onyay atthay accountyay atthay Iyay
eelfay osay anymay overwhelmingyay errorstay. Iyay enderlytay ovelay esethay iendsfray; Iyay
avehay, unknownyay otay emthay, eenbay orfay anymay onthsmay inyay ethay abitshay ofyay ailyday
indnesskay owardstay emthay; utbay eythay elievebay atthay Iyay ishway otay injureyay emthay, andyay
ityay isyay atthay ejudicepray ichwhay Iyay ishway otay overcomeyay.’

ere“‘whay oday esethay iendsfray esideray?’

ear“‘nay isthay otspay.’

e“thay oldyay anmay ausedpay andyay enthay ontinuedcay, if‘ay youyay illway unreservedlyyay
onfidecay otay emay ethay articularspay ofyay youryay aletay, Iyay erhapspay aymay ebay ofyay useyay inyay
undeceivingyay emthay. Iyay amyay indblay andyay annotcay udgejay ofyay youryay ountenancecay, utbay
erethay isyay omethingsay inyay youryay ordsway ichwhay ersuadespay emay atthay youyay areyay
inceresay. Iyay amyay oorpay andyay anyay exileyay, utbay ityay illway affordyay emay uetray easureplay
otay ebay inyay anyyay ayway erviceablesay otay ayay umanhay eaturecray.’

excellent“‘ay anmay! Iyay ankthay youyay andyay acceptyay youryay enerousgay offeryay. Youyay
aiseray emay omfray ethay ustday ybay isthay indnesskay; andyay Iyay usttray atthay, ybay youryay aidyay,
Iyay allshay otnay ebay ivendray omfray ethay ocietysay andyay ympathysay ofyay youryay ellowfay
eaturescray.’

eaven“‘hay orbidfay! Evenyay ifyay youyay ereway eallyray iminalcray, orfay atthay ancay onlyyay
ivedray youyay otay esperationday, andyay otnay instigateyay youyay otay irtuevay. Iyay alsoyay amyay
unfortunateyay; Iyay andyay ymay amilyfay avehay eenbay ondemnedcay, althoughyay innocentyay;
udgejay, ereforethay, ifyay Iyay oday otnay eelfay orfay youryay isfortunesmay.’

ow“‘hay ancay Iyay ankthay youyay, ymay estbay andyay onlyyay enefactorbay? Omfray youryay ipslay
irstfay avehay Iyay eardhay ethay oicevay ofyay indnesskay irectedday owardstay emay; Iyay allshay
ebay orfay everyay atefulgray; andyay youryay esentpray umanityhay assuresyay emay ofyay uccesssay
ithway osethay iendsfray omwhay Iyay amyay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay eetingmay.’

ay“‘may Iyay owknay ethay amesnay andyay esidenceray ofyay osethay iendsfray?’

i“ay ausedpay. Isthay, Iyay oughtthay, asway ethay omentmay ofyay ecisionday, ichwhay asway otay
obray emay ofyay oryay estowbay appinesshay onyay emay orfay everyay. Iyay uggledstray ainlyvay orfay
irmnessfay ufficientsay otay answeryay imhay, utbay ethay effortyay estroyedday allyay ymay
emainingray engthstray; Iyay anksay onyay ethay airchay andyay obbedsay aloudyay. Atyay atthay
omentmay Iyay eardhay ethay epsstay ofyay ymay youngeryay otectorspray. Iyay adhay otnay ayay omentmay
otay oselay, utbay eizingsay ethay andhay ofyay ethay oldyay anmay, Iyay iedcray, ow‘nay isyay ethay
imetay! Avesay andyay otectpray emay! Youyay andyay youryay amilyfay areyay ethay iendsfray omwhay Iyay
eeksay. Oday otnay youyay esertday emay inyay ethay ourhay ofyay ialtray!’

eat“‘gray Odgay!’ exclaimedyay ethay oldyay anmay. o‘whay areyay youyay?’

at“ay atthay instantyay ethay ottagecay oorday asway openedyay, andyay Elixfay, Afiesay, andyay
Agathayay enteredyay. Owhay ancay escribeday eirthay orrorhay andyay onsternationcay onyay
eholdingbay emay? Agathayay aintedfay, andyay Afiesay, unableyay otay attendyay otay erhay
iendfray, ushedray outyay ofyay ethay ottagecay. Elixfay artedday orwardfay, andyay ithway
upernaturalsay orcefay oretay emay omfray ishay atherfay, otay osewhay eesknay Iyay ungclay, inyay
ayay ansporttray ofyay uryfay, ehay ashedday emay otay ethay oundgray andyay uckstray emay iolentlyvay
ithway ayay ickstay. Iyay ouldcay avehay orntay imhay imblay omfray imblay, asyay ethay ionlay endsray
ethay antelopeyay. Utbay ymay earthay anksay ithinway emay asyay ithway itterbay icknesssay, andyay
Iyay efrainedray. Iyay awsay imhay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay epeatingray ishay owblay, enwhay,
overcomeyay ybay ainpay andyay anguishyay, Iyay uittedqay ethay ottagecay, andyay inyay ethay eneralgay
umulttay escapedyay unperceivedyay otay ymay ovelhay.”




Apterchay 16


ursed“cay, ursedcay eatorcray! Ywhay idday Iyay ivelay? Ywhay, inyay atthay instantyay, idday Iyay
otnay extinguishyay ethay arkspay ofyay existenceyay ichwhay youyay adhay osay antonlyway
estowedbay? Iyay owknay otnay; espairday adhay otnay yetyay akentay ossessionpay ofyay emay; ymay
eelingsfay ereway osethay ofyay ageray andyay evengeray. Iyay ouldcay ithway easureplay avehay
estroyedday ethay ottagecay andyay itsyay inhabitantsyay andyay avehay uttedglay yselfmay ithway
eirthay ieksshray andyay iserymay.

en“whay ightnay amecay Iyay uittedqay ymay etreatray andyay anderedway inyay ethay oodway; andyay
ownay, onay ongerlay estrainedray ybay ethay earfay ofyay iscoveryday, Iyay avegay entvay otay ymay
anguishyay inyay earfulfay owlingshay. Iyay asway ikelay ayay ildway eastbay atthay adhay okenbray
ethay oilstay, estroyingday ethay objectsyay atthay obstructedyay emay andyay angingray
oughthray ethay oodway ithway ayay ag-likestay iftnesssway. Ohyay! Atwhay ayay iserablemay
ightnay Iyay assedpay! Ethay oldcay arsstay oneshay inyay ockerymay, andyay ethay arebay eestray
avedway eirthay anchesbray aboveyay emay; ownay andyay enthay ethay eetsway oicevay ofyay ayay irdbay
urstbay orthfay amidstyay ethay universalyay illnessstay. Allyay, avesay Iyay, ereway atyay estray
oryay inyay enjoymentyay; Iyay, ikelay ethay arch-fiendyay, orebay ayay ellhay ithinway emay, andyay
indingfay yselfmay unsympathisedyay ithway, ishedway otay eartay upyay ethay eestray, eadspray
avochay andyay estructionday aroundyay emay, andyay enthay otay avehay atsay ownday andyay enjoyedyay
ethay uinray.

ut“bay isthay asway ayay uxurylay ofyay ensationsay atthay ouldcay otnay endureyay; Iyay ecamebay
atiguedfay ithway excessyay ofyay odilybay exertionyay andyay anksay onyay ethay ampday assgray inyay
ethay icksay impotenceyay ofyay espairday. Erethay asway onenay amongyay ethay yriadsmay ofyay enmay
atthay existedyay owhay ouldway itypay oryay assistyay emay; andyay ouldshay Iyay eelfay indnesskay
owardstay ymay enemiesyay? Onay; omfray atthay omentmay Iyay eclaredday everlastingyay arway
againstyay ethay eciesspay, andyay oremay anthay allyay, againstyay imhay owhay adhay ormedfay emay
andyay entsay emay orthfay otay isthay insupportableyay iserymay.

e“thay unsay oseray; Iyay eardhay ethay oicesvay ofyay enmay andyay ewknay atthay ityay asway
impossibleyay otay eturnray otay ymay etreatray uringday atthay ayday. Accordinglyyay Iyay idhay
yselfmay inyay omesay ickthay underwoodyay, eterminingday otay evoteday ethay ensuingyay ourshay
otay eflectionray onyay ymay ituationsay.

e“thay easantplay unshinesay andyay ethay urepay airyay ofyay ayday estoredray emay otay omesay
egreeday ofyay anquillitytray; andyay enwhay Iyay onsideredcay atwhay adhay assedpay atyay ethay
ottagecay, Iyay ouldcay otnay elphay elievingbay atthay Iyay adhay eenbay ootay astyhay inyay ymay
onclusionscay. Iyay adhay ertainlycay actedyay imprudentlyyay. Ityay asway apparentyay atthay
ymay onversationcay adhay interestedyay ethay atherfay inyay ymay ehalfbay, andyay Iyay asway ayay
oolfay inyay avinghay exposedyay ymay ersonpay otay ethay orrorhay ofyay ishay ildrenchay. Iyay
oughtyay otay avehay amiliarisedfay ethay oldyay Eday Aceylay otay emay, andyay ybay egreesday otay
avehay iscoveredday yselfmay otay ethay estray ofyay ishay amilyfay, enwhay eythay ouldshay avehay
eenbay eparedpray orfay ymay approachyay. Utbay Iyay idday otnay elievebay ymay errorsyay otay ebay
irretrievableyay, andyay afteryay uchmay onsiderationcay Iyay esolvedray otay eturnray otay ethay
ottagecay, eeksay ethay oldyay anmay, andyay ybay ymay epresentationsray inway imhay otay ymay
artypay.

ese“thay oughtsthay almedcay emay, andyay inyay ethay afternoonyay Iyay anksay intoyay ayay ofoundpray
eepslay; utbay ethay everfay ofyay ymay oodblay idday otnay allowyay emay otay ebay isitedvay ybay
eacefulpay eamsdray. Ethay orriblehay enescay ofyay ethay ecedingpray ayday asway orfay everyay
actingyay eforebay ymay eyesyay; ethay emalesfay ereway yingflay andyay ethay enragedyay Elixfay
earingtay emay omfray ishay ather’sfay eetfay. Iyay awokeyay exhaustedyay, andyay indingfay atthay
ityay asway alreadyyay ightnay, Iyay eptcray orthfay omfray ymay iding-placehay, andyay entway inyay
earchsay ofyay oodfay.

en“whay ymay ungerhay asway appeasedyay, Iyay irectedday ymay epsstay owardstay ethay
ell-knownway athpay atthay onductedcay otay ethay ottagecay. Allyay erethay asway atyay eacepay.
Iyay eptcray intoyay ymay ovelhay andyay emainedray inyay ilentsay expectationyay ofyay ethay
accustomedyay ourhay enwhay ethay amilyfay aroseyay. Atthay ourhay assedpay, ethay unsay
ountedmay ighhay inyay ethay eavenshay, utbay ethay ottagerscay idday otnay appearyay. Iyay
embledtray iolentlyvay, apprehendingyay omesay eadfuldray isfortunemay. Ethay insideyay
ofyay ethay ottagecay asway arkday, andyay Iyay eardhay onay otionmay; Iyay annotcay escribeday ethay
agonyyay ofyay isthay uspensesay.

esently“pray otway ountrymencay assedpay ybay, utbay ausingpay earnay ethay ottagecay, eythay
enteredyay intoyay onversationcay, usingyay iolentvay esticulationsgay; utbay Iyay idday otnay
understandyay atwhay eythay aidsay, asyay eythay okespay ethay anguagelay ofyay ethay ountrycay,
ichwhay ifferedday omfray atthay ofyay ymay otectorspray. Oonsay afteryay, oweverhay, Elixfay
approachedyay ithway anotheryay anmay; Iyay asway urprisedsay, asyay Iyay ewknay atthay ehay adhay otnay
uittedqay ethay ottagecay atthay orningmay, andyay aitedway anxiouslyyay otay iscoverday omfray
ishay iscourseday ethay eaningmay ofyay esethay unusualyay appearancesyay.

o“‘day youyay onsidercay,’ aidsay ishay ompanioncay otay imhay,
at‘thay youyay illway ebay obligedyay otay aypay eethray onthsmay’ entray andyay otay oselay
ethay oducepray ofyay youryay ardengay? Iyay oday otnay ishway otay aketay anyyay unfairyay advantageyay, andyay
Iyay egbay ereforethay atthay youyay illway aketay omesay aysday otay onsidercay ofyay youryay
eterminationday.’

it“‘ay isyay utterlyyay uselessyay,’ epliedray Elixfay; e‘way ancay
evernay againyay inhabityay youryay ottagecay. Ethay ifelay ofyay ymay atherfay isyay inyay ethay eatestgray
angerday, owingyay otay ethay eadfuldray ircumstancecay atthay Iyay avehay elatedray. Ymay ifeway andyay
ymay istersay illway evernay ecoverray omfray eirthay orrorhay. Iyay entreatyay youyay otnay otay easonray
ithway emay anyyay oremay. Aketay ossessionpay ofyay youryay enementtay andyay etlay emay yflay omfray isthay
aceplay.’

elix“fay embledtray iolentlyvay asyay ehay aidsay isthay. Ehay andyay ishay ompanioncay
enteredyay ethay ottagecay, inyay ichwhay eythay emainedray orfay ayay ewfay inutesmay, andyay enthay
epartedday. Iyay evernay awsay anyyay ofyay ethay amilyfay ofyay Eday Aceylay oremay.

i“ay ontinuedcay orfay ethay emainderray ofyay ethay ayday inyay ymay ovelhay inyay ayay atestay ofyay
utteryay andyay upidstay espairday. Ymay otectorspray adhay epartedday andyay adhay okenbray
ethay onlyyay inklay atthay eldhay emay otay ethay orldway. Orfay ethay irstfay imetay ethay
eelingsfay ofyay evengeray andyay atredhay illedfay ymay osombay, andyay Iyay idday otnay ivestray otay
ontrolcay emthay, utbay allowingyay yselfmay otay ebay ornebay awayyay ybay ethay eamstray, Iyay
entbay ymay indmay owardstay injuryyay andyay eathday. Enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay ymay iendsfray,
ofyay ethay ildmay oicevay ofyay Eday Aceylay, ethay entlegay eyesyay ofyay Agathayay, andyay ethay
exquisiteyay eautybay ofyay ethay Arabianyay, esethay oughtsthay anishedvay andyay ayay ushgay ofyay
earstay omewhatsay oothedsay emay. Utbay againyay enwhay Iyay eflectedray atthay eythay adhay
urnedspay andyay esertedday emay, angeryay eturnedray, ayay ageray ofyay angeryay, andyay unableyay otay
injureyay anythingyay umanhay, Iyay urnedtay ymay uryfay owardstay inanimateyay objectsyay. Asyay
ightnay advancedyay, Iyay acedplay ayay arietyvay ofyay ombustiblescay aroundyay ethay ottagecay,
andyay afteryay avinghay estroyedday everyyay estigevay ofyay ultivationcay inyay ethay ardengay,
Iyay aitedway ithway orcedfay impatienceyay untilyay ethay oonmay adhay unksay otay ommencecay ymay
operationsyay.

as“ay ethay ightnay advancedyay, ayay iercefay indway aroseyay omfray ethay oodsway andyay uicklyqay
ispersedday ethay oudsclay atthay adhay oiteredlay inyay ethay eavenshay; ethay astblay oretay
alongyay ikelay ayay ightymay avalancheyay andyay oducedpray ayay indkay ofyay insanityyay inyay ymay
iritsspay atthay urstbay allyay oundsbay ofyay easonray andyay eflectionray. Iyay ightedlay ethay
ydray anchbray ofyay ayay eetray andyay ancedday ithway uryfay aroundyay ethay evotedday ottagecay,
ymay eyesyay illstay ixedfay onyay ethay esternway orizonhay, ethay edgeyay ofyay ichwhay ethay oonmay
earlynay ouchedtay. Ayay artpay ofyay itsyay orbyay asway atyay engthlay idhay, andyay Iyay avedway ymay
andbray; ityay anksay, andyay ithway ayay oudlay eamscray Iyay iredfay ethay awstray, andyay eathhay,
andyay ushesbay, ichwhay Iyay adhay ollectedcay. Ethay indway annedfay ethay irefay, andyay ethay
ottagecay asway uicklyqay envelopedyay ybay ethay amesflay, ichwhay ungclay otay ityay andyay
ickedlay ityay ithway eirthay orkedfay andyay estroyingday onguestay.

as“ay oonsay asyay Iyay asway onvincedcay atthay onay assistanceyay ouldcay avesay anyyay artpay ofyay
ethay abitationhay, Iyay uittedqay ethay enescay andyay oughtsay orfay efugeray inyay ethay oodsway.

and“ay ownay, ithway ethay orldway eforebay emay, itherwhay ouldshay Iyay endbay ymay epsstay? Iyay
esolvedray otay yflay arfay omfray ethay enescay ofyay ymay isfortunesmay; utbay otay emay, atedhay
andyay espisedday, everyyay ountrycay ustmay ebay equallyyay orriblehay. Atyay engthlay ethay
oughtthay ofyay youyay ossedcray ymay indmay. Iyay earnedlay omfray youryay aperspay atthay youyay
ereway ymay atherfay, ymay eatorcray; andyay otay omwhay ouldcay Iyay applyyay ithway oremay itnessfay
anthay otay imhay owhay adhay ivengay emay ifelay? Amongyay ethay essonslay atthay Elixfay adhay
estowedbay uponyay Afiesay, eographygay adhay otnay eenbay omittedyay; Iyay adhay earnedlay omfray
esethay ethay elativeray ituationssay ofyay ethay ifferentday ountriescay ofyay ethay earthyay.
Youyay adhay entionedmay Enevagay asyay ethay amenay ofyay youryay ativenay owntay, andyay owardstay
isthay aceplay Iyay esolvedray otay oceedpray.

ut“bay owhay asway Iyay otay irectday yselfmay? Iyay ewknay atthay Iyay ustmay aveltray inyay ayay
outhwesterlysay irectionday otay eachray ymay estinationday, utbay ethay unsay asway ymay
onlyyay uidegay. Iyay idday otnay owknay ethay amesnay ofyay ethay ownstay atthay Iyay asway otay asspay
oughthray, ornay ouldcay Iyay askyay informationyay omfray ayay inglesay umanhay eingbay; utbay Iyay
idday otnay espairday. Omfray youyay onlyyay ouldcay Iyay opehay orfay uccoursay, althoughyay
owardstay youyay Iyay eltfay onay entimentsay utbay atthay ofyay atredhay. Unfeelingyay,
eartlesshay eatorcray! Youyay adhay endowedyay emay ithway erceptionspay andyay assionspay
andyay enthay astcay emay abroadyay anyay objectyay orfay ethay ornscay andyay orrorhay ofyay ankindmay.
Utbay onyay youyay onlyyay adhay Iyay anyyay aimclay orfay itypay andyay edressray, andyay omfray youyay Iyay
eterminedday otay eeksay atthay usticejay ichwhay Iyay ainlyvay attemptedyay otay aingay omfray
anyyay otheryay eingbay atthay oreway ethay umanhay ormfay.

y“may avelstray ereway onglay andyay ethay ufferingssay Iyay enduredyay intenseyay. Ityay asway
atelay inyay autumnyay enwhay Iyay uittedqay ethay istrictday erewhay Iyay adhay osay onglay esidedray.
Iyay avelledtray onlyyay atyay ightnay, earfulfay ofyay encounteringyay ethay isagevay ofyay ayay
umanhay eingbay. Aturenay ecayedday aroundyay emay, andyay ethay unsay ecamebay eatlesshay;
ainray andyay owsnay ouredpay aroundyay emay; ightymay iversray ereway ozenfray; ethay urfacesay
ofyay ethay earthyay asway ardhay andyay illchay, andyay arebay, andyay Iyay oundfay onay eltershay. Ohyay,
earthyay! Owhay oftenyay idday Iyay imprecateyay ursescay onyay ethay ausecay ofyay ymay eingbay! Ethay
ildnessmay ofyay ymay aturenay adhay edflay, andyay allyay ithinway emay asway urnedtay otay allgay
andyay itternessbay. Ethay earernay Iyay approachedyay otay youryay abitationhay, ethay oremay
eeplyday idday Iyay eelfay ethay iritspay ofyay evengeray enkindledyay inyay ymay earthay. Owsnay
ellfay, andyay ethay atersway ereway ardenedhay, utbay Iyay estedray otnay. Ayay ewfay incidentsyay
ownay andyay enthay irectedday emay, andyay Iyay ossessedpay ayay apmay ofyay ethay ountrycay; utbay Iyay
oftenyay anderedway ideway omfray ymay athpay. Ethay agonyyay ofyay ymay eelingsfay allowedyay emay
onay espiteray; onay incidentyay occurredyay omfray ichwhay ymay ageray andyay iserymay ouldcay
otnay extractyay itsyay oodfay; utbay ayay ircumstancecay atthay appenedhay enwhay Iyay arrivedyay
onyay ethay onfinescay ofyay Itzerlandsway, enwhay ethay unsay adhay ecoveredray itsyay armthway
andyay ethay earthyay againyay eganbay otay ooklay eengray, onfirmedcay inyay anyay especialyay
annermay ethay itternessbay andyay orrorhay ofyay ymay eelingsfay.

i“ay enerallygay estedray uringday ethay ayday andyay avelledtray onlyyay enwhay Iyay asway
ecuredsay ybay ightnay omfray ethay iewvay ofyay anmay. Oneyay orningmay, oweverhay, indingfay
atthay ymay athpay aylay oughthray ayay eepday oodway, Iyay enturedvay otay ontinuecay ymay ourneyjay
afteryay ethay unsay adhay isenray; ethay ayday, ichwhay asway oneyay ofyay ethay irstfay ofyay ingspray,
eeredchay evenyay emay ybay ethay ovelinesslay ofyay itsyay unshinesay andyay ethay alminessbay ofyay
ethay airyay. Iyay eltfay emotionsyay ofyay entlenessgay andyay easureplay, atthay adhay onglay
appearedyay eadday, eviveray ithinway emay. Alfhay urprisedsay ybay ethay oveltynay ofyay
esethay ensationssay, Iyay allowedyay yselfmay otay ebay ornebay awayyay ybay emthay, andyay
orgettingfay ymay olitudesay andyay eformityday, aredday otay ebay appyhay. Oftsay earstay
againyay edewedbay ymay eekschay, andyay Iyay evenyay aisedray ymay umidhay eyesyay ithway
ankfulnessthay owardstay ethay essedblay unsay, ichwhay estowedbay uchsay oyjay uponyay emay.

i“ay ontinuedcay otay indway amongyay ethay athspay ofyay ethay oodway, untilyay Iyay amecay otay itsyay
oundarybay, ichwhay asway irtedskay ybay ayay eepday andyay apidray iverray, intoyay ichwhay anymay
ofyay ethay eestray entbay eirthay anchesbray, ownay uddingbay ithway ethay eshfray ingspray.
Erehay Iyay ausedpay, otnay exactlyyay owingknay atwhay athpay otay ursuepay, enwhay Iyay eardhay
ethay oundsay ofyay oicesvay, atthay inducedyay emay otay oncealcay yselfmay underyay ethay adeshay
ofyay ayay ypresscay. Iyay asway arcelyscay idhay enwhay ayay youngyay irlgay amecay unningray
owardstay ethay otspay erewhay Iyay asway oncealedcay, aughinglay, asyay ifyay eshay anray omfray
omeonesay inyay ortspay. Eshay ontinuedcay erhay oursecay alongyay ethay ecipitouspray idessay
ofyay ethay iverray, enwhay uddenlysay erhay ootfay ippedslay, andyay eshay ellfay intoyay ethay
apidray eamstray. Iyay ushedray omfray ymay iding-placehay andyay ithway extremeyay abourlay,
omfray ethay orcefay ofyay ethay urrentcay, avedsay erhay andyay aggeddray erhay otay oreshay. Eshay
asway enselesssay, andyay Iyay endeavouredyay ybay everyyay eansmay inyay ymay owerpay otay estoreray
animationyay, enwhay Iyay asway uddenlysay interruptedyay ybay ethay approachyay ofyay ayay usticray,
owhay asway obablypray ethay ersonpay omfray omwhay eshay adhay ayfullyplay edflay. Onyay
eeingsay emay, ehay artedday owardstay emay, andyay earingtay ethay irlgay omfray ymay armsyay,
astenedhay owardstay ethay eeperday artspay ofyay ethay oodway. Iyay ollowedfay eedilyspay, Iyay
ardlyhay ewknay ywhay; utbay enwhay ethay anmay awsay emay awdray earnay, ehay aimedyay ayay ungay,
ichwhay ehay arriedcay, atyay ymay odybay andyay iredfay. Iyay anksay otay ethay oundgray, andyay ymay
injureryay, ithway increasedyay iftnesssway, escapedyay intoyay ethay oodway.

is“thay asway enthay ethay ewardray ofyay ymay enevolencebay! Iyay adhay avedsay ayay umanhay eingbay
omfray estructionday, andyay asyay ayay ecompenseray Iyay ownay ithedwray underyay ethay iserablemay
ainpay ofyay ayay oundway ichwhay atteredshay ethay eshflay andyay onebay. Ethay eelingsfay ofyay
indnesskay andyay entlenessgay ichwhay Iyay adhay entertainedyay utbay ayay ewfay omentsmay
eforebay avegay aceplay otay ellishhay ageray andyay ashinggnay ofyay eethtay. Inflamedyay ybay
ainpay, Iyay owedvay eternalyay atredhay andyay engeancevay otay allyay ankindmay. Utbay ethay
agonyyay ofyay ymay oundway overcameyay emay; ymay ulsespay ausedpay, andyay Iyay aintedfay.

or“fay omesay eeksway Iyay edlay ayay iserablemay ifelay inyay ethay oodsway, endeavouringyay otay
urecay ethay oundway ichwhay Iyay adhay eceivedray. Ethay allbay adhay enteredyay ymay ouldershay,
andyay Iyay ewknay otnay etherwhay ityay adhay emainedray erethay oryay assedpay oughthray; atyay anyyay
ateray Iyay adhay onay eansmay ofyay extractingyay ityay. Ymay ufferingssay ereway augmentedyay
alsoyay ybay ethay oppressiveyay ensesay ofyay ethay injusticeyay andyay ingratitudeyay ofyay eirthay
inflictionyay. Ymay ailyday owsvay oseray orfay evenge—aray eepday andyay eadlyday evengeray,
uchsay asyay ouldway aloneyay ompensatecay orfay ethay outragesyay andyay anguishyay Iyay adhay
enduredyay.

after“ay omesay eeksway ymay oundway ealedhay, andyay Iyay ontinuedcay ymay ourneyjay. Ethay
abourslay Iyay enduredyay ereway onay ongerlay otay ebay alleviatedyay ybay ethay ightbray unsay oryay
entlegay eezesbray ofyay ingspray; allyay oyjay asway utbay ayay ockerymay ichwhay insultedyay ymay
esolateday atestay andyay ademay emay eelfay oremay ainfullypay atthay Iyay asway otnay ademay orfay
ethay enjoymentyay ofyay easureplay.

ut“bay ymay oilstay ownay ewdray earnay ayay oseclay, andyay inyay otway onthsmay omfray isthay imetay Iyay
eachedray ethay environsyay ofyay Enevagay.

it“ay asway eveningyay enwhay Iyay arrivedyay, andyay Iyay etiredray otay ayay iding-placehay amongyay
ethay ieldsfay atthay urroundsay ityay otay editatemay inyay atwhay annermay Iyay ouldshay applyyay
otay youyay. Iyay asway oppressedyay ybay atiguefay andyay ungerhay andyay arfay ootay unhappyyay otay
enjoyyay ethay entlegay eezesbray ofyay eveningyay oryay ethay ospectpray ofyay ethay unsay ettingsay
ehindbay ethay upendousstay ountainsmay ofyay Urajay.

at“ay isthay imetay ayay ightslay eepslay elievedray emay omfray ethay ainpay ofyay eflectionray,
ichwhay asway isturbedday ybay ethay approachyay ofyay ayay eautifulbay ildchay, owhay amecay
unningray intoyay ethay ecessray Iyay adhay osenchay, ithway allyay ethay ortivenessspay ofyay
infancyyay. Uddenlysay, asyay Iyay azedgay onyay imhay, anyay ideayay eizedsay emay atthay isthay
ittlelay eaturecray asway unprejudicedyay andyay adhay ivedlay ootay ortshay ayay imetay otay avehay
imbibedyay ayay orrorhay ofyay eformityday. Ifyay, ereforethay, Iyay ouldcay eizesay imhay andyay
educateyay imhay asyay ymay ompanioncay andyay iendfray, Iyay ouldshay otnay ebay osay esolateday inyay
isthay eopledpay earthyay.

urged“ay ybay isthay impulseyay, Iyay eizedsay onyay ethay oybay asyay ehay assedpay andyay ewdray imhay
owardstay emay. Asyay oonsay asyay ehay eheldbay ymay ormfay, ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay
ishay eyesyay andyay utteredyay ayay illshray eamscray; Iyay ewdray ishay andhay orciblyfay omfray ishay
acefay andyay aidsay, ild‘chay, atwhay isyay ethay eaningmay ofyay isthay? Iyay oday otnay intendyay otay
urthay youyay; istenlay otay emay.’

e“hay uggledstray iolentlyvay. et‘lay emay ogay,’ ehay iedcray;
onster‘may! Uglyyay etchwray! Youyay ishway otay eatyay emay andyay eartay emay otay iecespay. Youyay
areyay anyay ogreyay. Etlay emay ogay, oryay Iyay illway elltay ymay apapay.’

oy“‘bay, youyay illway evernay eesay youryay atherfay againyay; youyay ustmay omecay ithway emay.’

ideous“‘hay onstermay! Etlay emay ogay. Ymay apapay isyay ayay yndic—hesay isyay May.
Ankenstein—hefray illway unishpay youyay. Youyay areday otnay eepkay emay.’

ankenstein“‘fray! youyay elongbay enthay otay ymay enemy—toyay imhay owardstay omwhay Iyay avehay
ornsway eternalyay evengeray; youyay allshay ebay ymay irstfay ictimvay.’

e“thay ildchay illstay uggledstray andyay oadedlay emay ithway epithetsyay ichwhay arriedcay
espairday otay ymay earthay; Iyay aspedgray ishay oatthray otay ilencesay imhay, andyay inyay ayay
omentmay ehay aylay eadday atyay ymay eetfay.

i“ay azedgay onyay ymay ictimvay, andyay ymay earthay elledsway ithway exultationyay andyay ellishhay
iumphtray; appingclay ymay andshay, Iyay exclaimedyay, i‘ay ootay ancay eatecray esolationday;
ymay enemyyay isyay otnay invulnerableyay; isthay eathday illway arrycay espairday otay imhay, andyay
ayay ousandthay otheryay iseriesmay allshay ormenttay andyay estroyday imhay.’

as“ay Iyay ixedfay ymay eyesyay onyay ethay ildchay, Iyay awsay omethingsay itteringglay onyay ishay
eastbray. Iyay ooktay ityay; ityay asway ayay ortraitpay ofyay ayay ostmay ovelylay omanway. Inyay itespay
ofyay ymay alignitymay, ityay oftenedsay andyay attractedyay emay. Orfay ayay ewfay omentsmay Iyay
azedgay ithway elightday onyay erhay arkday eyesyay, ingedfray ybay eepday asheslay, andyay erhay
ovelylay ipslay; utbay esentlypray ymay ageray eturnedray; Iyay ememberedray atthay Iyay asway
orfay everyay eprivedday ofyay ethay elightsday atthay uchsay eautifulbay eaturescray ouldcay
estowbay andyay atthay eshay osewhay esemblanceray Iyay ontemplatedcay ouldway, inyay
egardingray emay, avehay angedchay atthay airyay ofyay ivineday enignitybay otay oneyay
expressiveyay ofyay isgustday andyay affrightyay.

an“cay youyay onderway atthay uchsay oughtsthay ansportedtray emay ithway ageray? Iyay onlyyay
onderway atthay atyay atthay omentmay, insteadyay ofyay entingvay ymay ensationssay inyay
exclamationsyay andyay agonyyay, Iyay idday otnay ushray amongyay ankindmay andyay erishpay inyay ethay
attemptyay otay estroyday emthay.

ile“whay Iyay asway overcomeyay ybay esethay eelingsfay, Iyay eftlay ethay otspay erewhay Iyay adhay
ommittedcay ethay urdermay, andyay eekingsay ayay oremay ecludedsay iding-placehay, Iyay
enteredyay ayay arnbay ichwhay adhay appearedyay otay emay otay ebay emptyyay. Ayay omanway asway
eepingslay onyay omesay awstray; eshay asway youngyay, otnay indeedyay osay eautifulbay asyay erhay
osewhay ortraitpay Iyay eldhay, utbay ofyay anyay agreeableyay aspectyay andyay oomingblay inyay ethay
ovelinesslay ofyay youthyay andyay ealthhay. Erehay, Iyay oughtthay, isyay oneyay ofyay osethay osewhay
oy-impartingjay ilessmay areyay estowedbay onyay allyay utbay emay. Andyay enthay Iyay entbay overyay
erhay andyay isperedwhay, awake‘ay, airestfay, ythay overlay isyay ear—henay owhay ouldway
ivegay ishay ifelay utbay otay obtainyay oneyay ooklay ofyay affectionyay omfray inethay eyesyay; ymay
elovedbay, awakeyay!’

e“thay eeperslay irredstay; ayay illthray ofyay errortay anray oughthray emay. Ouldshay eshay
indeedyay awakeyay, andyay eesay emay, andyay ursecay emay, andyay enounceday ethay urderermay? Usthay
ouldway eshay assuredlyyay actyay ifyay erhay arkenedday eyesyay openedyay andyay eshay eheldbay emay.
Ethay oughtthay asway adnessmay; ityay irredstay ethay iendfay ithinway e—notmay Iyay, utbay
eshay, allshay uffersay; ethay urdermay Iyay avehay ommittedcay ecausebay Iyay amyay orfay everyay
obbedray ofyay allyay atthay eshay ouldcay ivegay emay, eshay allshay atoneyay. Ethay imecray adhay
itsyay ourcesay inyay erhay; ebay ershay ethay unishmentpay! Anksthay otay ethay essonslay ofyay
Elixfay andyay ethay anguinarysay awslay ofyay anmay, Iyay adhay earnedlay ownay otay orkway
ischiefmay. Iyay entbay overyay erhay andyay acedplay ethay ortraitpay ecurelysay inyay oneyay ofyay
ethay oldsfay ofyay erhay essdray. Eshay ovedmay againyay, andyay Iyay edflay.

or“fay omesay aysday Iyay auntedhay ethay otspay erewhay esethay enesscay adhay akentay aceplay,
ometimessay ishingway otay eesay youyay, ometimessay esolvedray otay uitqay ethay orldway andyay
itsyay iseriesmay orfay everyay. Atyay engthlay Iyay anderedway owardstay esethay ountainsmay,
andyay avehay angedray oughthray eirthay immenseyay ecessesray, onsumedcay ybay ayay urningbay
assionpay ichwhay youyay aloneyay ancay atifygray. Eway aymay otnay artpay untilyay youyay avehay
omisedpray otay omplycay ithway ymay equisitionray. Iyay amyay aloneyay andyay iserablemay; anmay
illway otnay associateyay ithway emay; utbay oneyay asyay eformedday andyay orriblehay asyay yselfmay
ouldway otnay enyday erselfhay otay emay. Ymay ompanioncay ustmay ebay ofyay ethay amesay eciesspay
andyay avehay ethay amesay efectsday. Isthay eingbay youyay ustmay eatecray.”




Apterchay 17


Ethay eingbay inishedfay eakingspay andyay ixedfay ishay ookslay uponyay emay inyay ethay
expectationyay ofyay ayay eplyray. Utbay Iyay asway ewilderedbay, erplexedpay, andyay unableyay otay
arrangeyay ymay ideasyay ufficientlysay otay understandyay ethay ullfay extentyay ofyay ishay
opositionpray. Ehay ontinuedcay,

you“ay ustmay eatecray ayay emalefay orfay emay ithway omwhay Iyay ancay ivelay inyay ethay
interchangeyay ofyay osethay ympathiessay ecessarynay orfay ymay eingbay. Isthay youyay aloneyay
ancay oday, andyay Iyay emandday ityay ofyay youyay asyay ayay ightray ichwhay youyay ustmay otnay efuseray otay
oncedecay.”

Ethay atterlay artpay ofyay ishay aletay adhay indledkay anewyay inyay emay ethay angeryay atthay adhay
iedday awayyay ilewhay ehay arratednay ishay eacefulpay ifelay amongyay ethay ottagerscay, andyay
asyay ehay aidsay isthay Iyay ouldcay onay ongerlay uppresssay ethay ageray atthay urnedbay ithinway
emay.

i“ay oday efuseray ityay,” Iyay epliedray; and“ay onay orturetay allshay everyay extortyay ayay
onsentcay omfray emay. Youyay aymay enderray emay ethay ostmay iserablemay ofyay enmay, utbay youyay
allshay evernay akemay emay asebay inyay ymay ownyay eyesyay. Allshay Iyay eatecray anotheryay ikelay
yourselfyay, osewhay ointjay ickednessway ightmay esolateday ethay orldway. Egonebay! Iyay
avehay answeredyay youyay; youyay aymay orturetay emay, utbay Iyay illway evernay onsentcay.”

you“ay areyay inyay ethay ongwray,” epliedray ethay iendfay; and“ay insteadyay
ofyay eateningthray, Iyay amyay ontentcay otay easonray ithway youyay. Iyay amyay aliciousmay ecausebay Iyay
amyay iserablemay. Amyay Iyay otnay unnedshay andyay atedhay ybay allyay ankindmay? Youyay, ymay eatorcray,
ouldway eartay emay otay iecespay andyay iumphtray; ememberray atthay, andyay elltay emay ywhay Iyay
ouldshay itypay anmay oremay anthay ehay itiespay emay? Youyay ouldway otnay allcay ityay urdermay ifyay youyay
ouldcay ecipitatepray emay intoyay oneyay ofyay osethay ice-riftsyay andyay estroyday ymay amefray, ethay
orkway ofyay youryay ownyay andshay. Allshay Iyay espectray anmay enwhay ehay ondemnscay emay? Etlay imhay
ivelay ithway emay inyay ethay interchangeyay ofyay indnesskay, andyay insteadyay ofyay injuryyay Iyay ouldway
estowbay everyyay enefitbay uponyay imhay ithway earstay ofyay atitudegray atyay ishay acceptanceyay.
Utbay atthay annotcay ebay; ethay umanhay ensessay areyay insurmountableyay arriersbay otay ouryay
unionyay. Yetyay inemay allshay otnay ebay ethay ubmissionsay ofyay abjectyay averyslay. Iyay illway
evengeray ymay injuriesyay; ifyay Iyay annotcay inspireyay ovelay, Iyay illway ausecay earfay, andyay
ieflychay owardstay youyay ymay arch-enemyyay, ecausebay ymay eatorcray, oday Iyay earsway
inextinguishableyay atredhay. Avehay ayay arecay; Iyay illway orkway atyay youryay estructionday, ornay
inishfay untilyay Iyay esolateday youryay earthay, osay atthay youyay allshay ursecay ethay ourhay ofyay
youryay irthbay.”

Ayay iendishfay ageray animatedyay imhay asyay ehay aidsay isthay; ishay acefay asway inkledwray
intoyay ontortionscay ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesyay otay eholdbay; utbay esentlypray
ehay almedcay imselfhay andyay oceededpray—

i“ay intendedyay otay easonray. Isthay assionpay isyay etrimentalday otay emay, orfay youyay oday
otnay eflectray atthay you_ay_ areyay ethay ausecay ofyay itsyay excessyay. Ifyay anyyay eingbay eltfay
emotionsyay ofyay enevolencebay owardstay emay, Iyay ouldshay eturnray emthay ayay undredhay andyay ayay
undredfoldhay; orfay atthay oneyay eature’scray akesay Iyay ouldway akemay eacepay ithway ethay
olewhay indkay! Utbay Iyay ownay indulgeyay inyay eamsdray ofyay issblay atthay annotcay ebay ealisedray.
Atwhay Iyay askyay ofyay youyay isyay easonableray andyay oderatemay; Iyay emandday ayay eaturecray ofyay
anotheryay exsay, utbay asyay ideoushay asyay yselfmay; ethay atificationgray isyay allsmay, utbay ityay
isyay allyay atthay Iyay ancay eceiveray, andyay ityay allshay ontentcay emay. Ityay isyay uetray, eway allshay ebay
onstersmay, utcay offyay omfray allyay ethay orldway; utbay onyay atthay accountyay eway allshay ebay oremay
attachedyay otay oneyay anotheryay. Ouryay iveslay illway otnay ebay appyhay, utbay eythay illway ebay
armlesshay andyay eefray omfray ethay iserymay Iyay ownay eelfay. Ohyay! Ymay eatorcray, akemay emay
appyhay; etlay emay eelfay atitudegray owardstay youyay orfay oneyay enefitbay! Etlay emay eesay atthay Iyay
exciteyay ethay ympathysay ofyay omesay existingyay ingthay; oday otnay enyday emay ymay
equestray!”

Iyay asway ovedmay. Iyay udderedshay enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay ossiblepay onsequencescay
ofyay ymay onsentcay, utbay Iyay eltfay atthay erethay asway omesay usticejay inyay ishay argumentyay.
Ishay aletay andyay ethay eelingsfay ehay ownay expressedyay ovedpray imhay otay ebay ayay eaturecray
ofyay inefay ensationssay, andyay idday Iyay otnay asyay ishay akermay oweyay imhay allyay ethay ortionpay
ofyay appinesshay atthay ityay asway inyay ymay owerpay otay estowbay? Ehay awsay ymay angechay ofyay
eelingfay andyay ontinuedcay,

if“ay youyay onsentcay, eithernay youyay ornay anyyay otheryay umanhay eingbay allshay everyay eesay
usyay againyay; Iyay illway ogay otay ethay astvay ildsway ofyay Outhsay Americayay. Ymay oodfay isyay otnay
atthay ofyay anmay; Iyay oday otnay estroyday ethay amblay andyay ethay idkay otay utglay ymay appetiteyay;
acornsyay andyay erriesbay affordyay emay ufficientsay ourishmentnay. Ymay ompanioncay illway
ebay ofyay ethay amesay aturenay asyay yselfmay andyay illway ebay ontentcay ithway ethay amesay arefay.
Eway allshay akemay ouryay edbay ofyay ieddray eaveslay; ethay unsay illway ineshay onyay usyay asyay onyay
anmay andyay illway ipenray ouryay oodfay. Ethay icturepay Iyay esentpray otay youyay isyay eacefulpay
andyay umanhay, andyay youyay ustmay eelfay atthay youyay ouldcay enyday ityay onlyyay inyay ethay
antonnessway ofyay owerpay andyay ueltycray. Itilesspay asyay youyay avehay eenbay owardstay emay,
Iyay ownay eesay ompassioncay inyay youryay eyesyay; etlay emay eizesay ethay avourablefay omentmay
andyay ersuadepay youyay otay omisepray atwhay Iyay osay ardentlyyay esireday.”

you“ay oposepray,” epliedray Iyay, o“tay yflay omfray ethay abitationshay ofyay
anmay, otay elldway inyay osethay ildsway erewhay ethay eastsbay ofyay ethay ieldfay illway ebay youryay
onlyyay ompanionscay. Owhay ancay youyay, owhay onglay orfay ethay ovelay andyay ympathysay ofyay anmay,
erseverepay inyay isthay exileyay? Youyay illway eturnray andyay againyay eeksay eirthay indnesskay, andyay
youyay illway eetmay ithway eirthay etestationday; youryay evilyay assionspay illway ebay enewedray,
andyay youyay illway enthay avehay ayay ompanioncay otay aidyay youyay inyay ethay asktay ofyay estructionday.
Isthay aymay otnay ebay; easecay otay argueyay ethay ointpay, orfay Iyay annotcay onsentcay.”

ow“hay inconstantyay areyay youryay eelingsfay! Utbay ayay omentmay agoyay youyay ereway ovedmay ybay
ymay epresentationsray, andyay ywhay oday youyay againyay ardenhay yourselfyay otay ymay omplaintscay?
Iyay earsway otay youyay, ybay ethay earthyay ichwhay Iyay inhabityay, andyay ybay youyay atthay ademay emay, atthay
ithway ethay ompanioncay youyay estowbay, Iyay illway uitqay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay anmay andyay
elldway, asyay ityay aymay ancechay, inyay ethay ostmay avagesay ofyay acesplay. Ymay evilyay assionspay
illway avehay edflay, orfay Iyay allshay eetmay ithway ympathysay! Ymay ifelay illway owflay uietlyqay
awayyay, andyay inyay ymay yingday omentsmay Iyay allshay otnay ursecay ymay akermay.”

Ishay ordsway adhay ayay angestray effectyay uponyay emay. Iyay ompassionatedcay imhay andyay
ometimessay eltfay ayay ishway otay onsolecay imhay, utbay enwhay Iyay ookedlay uponyay imhay, enwhay
Iyay awsay ethay ilthyfay assmay atthay ovedmay andyay alkedtay, ymay earthay ickenedsay andyay ymay
eelingsfay ereway alteredyay otay osethay ofyay orrorhay andyay atredhay. Iyay iedtray otay iflestay
esethay ensationssay; Iyay oughtthay atthay asyay Iyay ouldcay otnay ympathisesay ithway imhay, Iyay
adhay onay ightray otay ithholdway omfray imhay ethay allsmay ortionpay ofyay appinesshay ichwhay
asway yetyay inyay ymay owerpay otay estowbay.

you“ay earsway,” Iyay aidsay, o“tay ebay armlesshay; utbay avehay youyay otnay
alreadyyay ownshay ayay egreeday ofyay alicemay atthay ouldshay easonablyray akemay emay istrustday
youyay? Aymay otnay evenyay isthay ebay ayay eintfay atthay illway increaseyay youryay iumphtray ybay
affordingyay ayay iderway opescay orfay youryay evengeray?”

ow“hay isyay isthay? Iyay ustmay otnay ebay ifledtray ithway, andyay Iyay emandday anyay answeryay. Ifyay
Iyay avehay onay iestay andyay onay affectionsyay, atredhay andyay icevay ustmay ebay ymay ortionpay;
ethay ovelay ofyay anotheryay illway estroyday ethay ausecay ofyay ymay imescray, andyay Iyay allshay
ecomebay ayay ingthay ofyay osewhay existenceyay everyoneyay illway ebay ignorantyay. Ymay icesvay
areyay ethay ildrenchay ofyay ayay orcedfay olitudesay atthay Iyay abhoryay, andyay ymay irtuesvay illway
ecessarilynay ariseyay enwhay Iyay ivelay inyay ommunioncay ithway anyay equalyay. Iyay allshay eelfay
ethay affectionsyay ofyay ayay ensitivesay eingbay andyay ecomebay inkedlay otay ethay ainchay ofyay
existenceyay andyay eventsyay omfray ichwhay Iyay amyay ownay excludedyay.”

Iyay ausedpay omesay imetay otay eflectray onyay allyay ehay adhay elatedray andyay ethay ariousvay
argumentsyay ichwhay ehay adhay employedyay. Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay omisepray ofyay irtuesvay ichwhay
ehay adhay isplayedday onyay ethay openingyay ofyay ishay existenceyay andyay ethay ubsequentsay ightblay
ofyay allyay indlykay eelingfay ybay ethay oathinglay andyay ornscay ichwhay ishay otectorspray adhay
anifestedmay owardstay imhay. Ishay owerpay andyay eatsthray ereway otnay omittedyay inyay ymay
alculationscay; ayay eaturecray owhay ouldcay existyay inyay ethay ice-cavesyay ofyay ethay aciersglay
andyay idehay imselfhay omfray ursuitpay amongyay ethay idgesray ofyay inaccessibleyay ecipicespray
asway ayay eingbay ossessingpay acultiesfay ityay ouldway ebay ainvay otay opecay ithway. Afteryay ayay
onglay ausepay ofyay eflectionray Iyay oncludedcay atthay ethay usticejay ueday othbay otay imhay andyay
ymay ellowfay eaturescray emandedday ofyay emay atthay Iyay ouldshay omplycay ithway ishay equestray.
Urningtay otay imhay, ereforethay, Iyay aidsay,

i“ay onsentcay otay youryay emandday, onyay youryay olemnsay oathyay otay uitqay Europeyay orfay everyay,
andyay everyyay otheryay aceplay inyay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay anmay, asyay oonsay asyay Iyay allshay
eliverday intoyay youryay andshay ayay emalefay owhay illway accompanyyay youyay inyay youryay exileyay.”

i“ay earsway,” ehay iedcray, y“bay ethay unsay, andyay ybay ethay ueblay yskay ofyay
eavenhay, andyay ybay ethay irefay ofyay ovelay atthay urnsbay ymay earthay, atthay ifyay youyay antgray ymay
ayerpray, ilewhay eythay existyay youyay allshay evernay eholdbay emay againyay. Epartday otay youryay
omehay andyay ommencecay youryay abourslay; Iyay allshay atchway eirthay ogresspray ithway
unutterableyay anxietyyay; andyay earfay otnay utbay atthay enwhay youyay areyay eadyray Iyay allshay
appearyay.”

Ayingsay isthay, ehay uddenlysay uittedqay emay, earfulfay, erhapspay, ofyay anyyay angechay inyay
ymay entimentssay. Iyay awsay imhay escendday ethay ountainmay ithway eatergray eedspay anthay
ethay ightflay ofyay anyay eagleyay, andyay uicklyqay ostlay amongyay ethay undulationsyay ofyay ethay
easay ofyay iceyay.

Ishay aletay adhay occupiedyay ethay olewhay ayday, andyay ethay unsay asway uponyay ethay ergevay ofyay
ethay orizonhay enwhay ehay epartedday. Iyay ewknay atthay Iyay oughtyay otay astenhay ymay escentday
owardstay ethay alleyvay, asyay Iyay ouldshay oonsay ebay encompassedyay inyay arknessday; utbay ymay
earthay asway eavyhay, andyay ymay epsstay owslay. Ethay abourlay ofyay indingway amongyay ethay
ittlelay athspay ofyay ethay ountainmay andyay ixingfay ymay eetfay irmlyfay asyay Iyay advancedyay
erplexedpay emay, occupiedyay asyay Iyay asway ybay ethay emotionsyay ichwhay ethay occurrencesyay
ofyay ethay ayday adhay oducedpray. Ightnay asway arfay advancedyay enwhay Iyay amecay otay ethay
alfwayhay esting-placeray andyay eatedsay yselfmay esidebay ethay ountainfay. Ethay arsstay
oneshay atyay intervalsyay asyay ethay oudsclay assedpay omfray overyay emthay; ethay arkday inespay
oseray eforebay emay, andyay everyyay erehay andyay erethay ayay okenbray eetray aylay onyay ethay
oundgray; ityay asway ayay enescay ofyay onderfulway olemnitysay andyay irredstay angestray
oughtsthay ithinway emay. Iyay eptway itterlybay, andyay aspingclay ymay andshay inyay agonyyay, Iyay
exclaimedyay, oh“ay! arsstay andyay oudsclay andyay indsway, yeyay areyay allyay aboutyay otay ockmay
emay; ifyay yeyay eallyray itypay emay, ushcray ensationsay andyay emorymay; etlay emay ecomebay asyay
oughtnay; utbay ifyay otnay, epartday, epartday, andyay eavelay emay inyay arknessday.”

Esethay ereway ildway andyay iserablemay oughtsthay, utbay Iyay annotcay escribeday otay youyay
owhay ethay eternalyay inklingtway ofyay ethay arsstay eighedway uponyay emay andyay owhay Iyay
istenedlay otay everyyay astblay ofyay indway asyay ifyay ityay ereway ayay ullday uglyyay irocsay onyay itsyay
ayway otay onsumecay emay.

Orningmay awnedday eforebay Iyay arrivedyay atyay ethay illagevay ofyay Amounixchay; Iyay ooktay onay
estray, utbay eturnedray immediatelyyay otay Enevagay. Evenyay inyay ymay ownyay earthay Iyay ouldcay
ivegay onay expressionyay otay ymay ensations—theysay eighedway onyay emay ithway ayay
ountain’smay eightway andyay eirthay excessyay estroyedday ymay agonyyay eneathbay emthay.
Usthay Iyay eturnedray omehay, andyay enteringyay ethay ousehay, esentedpray yselfmay otay ethay
amilyfay. Ymay aggardhay andyay ildway appearanceyay awokeyay intenseyay alarmyay, utbay Iyay
answeredyay onay uestionqay, arcelyscay idday Iyay eakspay. Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay Iyay ereway acedplay
underyay ayay an—asbay ifyay Iyay adhay onay ightray otay aimclay eirthay ympathies—assay ifyay
evernay oremay ightmay Iyay enjoyyay ompanionshipcay ithway emthay. Yetyay evenyay usthay Iyay
ovedlay emthay otay adorationyay; andyay otay avesay emthay, Iyay esolvedray otay edicateday
yselfmay otay ymay ostmay abhorredyay asktay. Ethay ospectpray ofyay uchsay anyay occupationyay
ademay everyyay otheryay ircumstancecay ofyay existenceyay asspay eforebay emay ikelay ayay eamdray,
andyay atthay oughtthay onlyyay adhay otay emay ethay ealityray ofyay ifelay.




Apterchay 18


Ayday afteryay ayday, eekway afteryay eekway, assedpay awayyay onyay ymay eturnray otay Enevagay; andyay
Iyay ouldcay otnay ollectcay ethay ouragecay otay ecommenceray ymay orkway. Iyay earedfay ethay
engeancevay ofyay ethay isappointedday iendfay, yetyay Iyay asway unableyay otay overcomeyay ymay
epugnanceray otay ethay asktay ichwhay asway enjoinedyay emay. Iyay oundfay atthay Iyay ouldcay otnay
omposecay ayay emalefay ithoutway againyay evotingday everalsay onthsmay otay ofoundpray
udystay andyay aboriouslay isquisitionday. Iyay adhay eardhay ofyay omesay iscoveriesday
avinghay eenbay ademay ybay anyay Englishyay ilosopherphay, ethay owledgeknay ofyay ichwhay asway
aterialmay otay ymay uccesssay, andyay Iyay ometimessay oughtthay ofyay obtainingyay ymay
ather’sfay onsentcay otay isitvay Englandyay orfay isthay urposepay; utbay Iyay ungclay otay
everyyay etencepray ofyay elayday andyay ankshray omfray akingtay ethay irstfay epstay inyay anyay
undertakingyay osewhay immediateyay ecessitynay eganbay otay appearyay esslay absoluteyay otay
emay. Ayay angechay indeedyay adhay akentay aceplay inyay emay; ymay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay
ithertohay eclinedday, asway ownay uchmay estoredray; andyay ymay iritsspay, enwhay
uncheckedyay ybay ethay emorymay ofyay ymay unhappyyay omisepray, oseray oportionablypray. Ymay
atherfay awsay isthay angechay ithway easureplay, andyay ehay urnedtay ishay oughtsthay
owardstay ethay estbay ethodmay ofyay eradicatingyay ethay emainsray ofyay ymay elancholymay,
ichwhay everyyay ownay andyay enthay ouldway eturnray ybay itsfay, andyay ithway ayay evouringday
acknessblay overcastyay ethay approachingyay unshinesay. Atyay esethay omentsmay Iyay ooktay
efugeray inyay ethay ostmay erfectpay olitudesay. Iyay assedpay olewhay aysday onyay ethay akelay
aloneyay inyay ayay ittlelay oatbay, atchingway ethay oudsclay andyay isteninglay otay ethay
ipplingray ofyay ethay avesway, ilentsay andyay istlesslay. Utbay ethay eshfray airyay andyay
ightbray unsay eldomsay ailedfay otay estoreray emay otay omesay egreeday ofyay omposurecay, andyay
onyay ymay eturnray Iyay etmay ethay alutationssay ofyay ymay iendsfray ithway ayay eadierray ilesmay
andyay ayay oremay eerfulchay earthay.

Ityay asway afteryay ymay eturnray omfray oneyay ofyay esethay amblesray atthay ymay atherfay,
allingcay emay asideyay, usthay addressedyay emay,

i“ay amyay appyhay otay emarkray, ymay earday onsay, atthay youyay avehay esumedray youryay ormerfay
easuresplay andyay eemsay otay ebay eturningray otay yourselfyay. Andyay yetyay youyay areyay illstay
unhappyyay andyay illstay avoidyay ouryay ocietysay. Orfay omesay imetay Iyay asway ostlay inyay
onjecturecay asyay otay ethay ausecay ofyay isthay, utbay yesterdayyay anyay ideayay uckstray emay,
andyay ifyay ityay isyay ellway oundedfay, Iyay onjurecay youyay otay avowyay ityay. Eserveray onyay uchsay ayay
ointpay ouldway ebay otnay onlyyay uselessyay, utbay awdray ownday ebletray iserymay onyay usyay allyay.”

Iyay embledtray iolentlyvay atyay ishay exordiumyay, andyay ymay atherfay ontinuedcay—

i“ay onfesscay, ymay onsay, atthay Iyay avehay alwaysyay ookedlay orwardfay otay youryay
arriagemay ithway ouryay earday Elizabethyay asyay ethay ietay ofyay ouryay omesticday omfortcay andyay ethay
aystay ofyay ymay ecliningday yearsyay. Youyay ereway attachedyay otay eachyay otheryay omfray youryay
earliestyay infancyyay; youyay udiedstay ogethertay, andyay appearedyay, inyay ispositionsday andyay
astestay, entirelyyay uitedsay otay oneyay anotheryay. Utbay osay indblay isyay ethay experienceyay ofyay
anmay atthay atwhay Iyay onceivedcay otay ebay ethay estbay assistantsyay otay ymay anplay aymay avehay
entirelyyay estroyedday ityay. Youyay, erhapspay, egardray erhay asyay youryay istersay, ithoutway anyyay
ishway atthay eshay ightmay ecomebay youryay ifeway. Aynay, youyay aymay avehay etmay ithway anotheryay
omwhay youyay aymay ovelay; andyay onsideringcay yourselfyay asyay oundbay inyay onourhay otay
Elizabethyay, isthay ugglestray aymay occasionyay ethay oignantpay iserymay ichwhay youyay appearyay
otay eelfay.”

y“may earday atherfay, eassureray yourselfyay. Iyay ovelay ymay ousincay enderlytay andyay
incerelysay. Iyay evernay awsay anyyay omanway owhay excitedyay, asyay Elizabethyay oesday, ymay
armestway admirationyay andyay affectionyay. Ymay uturefay opeshay andyay ospectspray areyay
entirelyyay oundbay upyay inyay ethay expectationyay ofyay ouryay unionyay.”

e“thay expressionyay ofyay youryay entimentssay ofyay isthay ubjectsay, ymay earday Ictorvay,
ivesgay emay oremay easureplay anthay Iyay avehay orfay omesay imetay experiencedyay. Ifyay youyay
eelfay usthay, eway allshay assuredlyyay ebay appyhay, oweverhay esentpray eventsyay aymay astcay
ayay oomglay overyay usyay. Utbay ityay isyay isthay oomglay ichwhay appearsyay otay avehay akentay osay
ongstray ayay oldhay ofyay youryay indmay atthay Iyay ishway otay issipateday. Elltay emay,
ereforethay, etherwhay youyay objectyay otay anyay immediateyay olemnisationsay ofyay ethay
arriagemay. Eway avehay eenbay unfortunateyay, andyay ecentray eventsyay avehay awndray usyay
omfray atthay everydayyay anquillitytray efittingbay ymay yearsyay andyay infirmitiesyay. Youyay
areyay youngeryay; yetyay Iyay oday otnay upposesay, ossessedpay asyay youyay areyay ofyay ayay ompetentcay
ortunefay, atthay anyay earlyyay arriagemay ouldway atyay allyay interfereyay ithway anyyay uturefay
ansplay ofyay onourhay andyay utilityyay atthay youyay aymay avehay ormedfay. Oday otnay upposesay,
oweverhay, atthay Iyay ishway otay ictateday appinesshay otay youyay oryay atthay ayay elayday onyay
youryay artpay ouldway ausecay emay anyyay erioussay uneasinessyay. Interpretyay ymay ordsway
ithway andourcay andyay answeryay emay, Iyay onjurecay youyay, ithway onfidencecay andyay
inceritysay.”

Iyay istenedlay otay ymay atherfay inyay ilencesay andyay emainedray orfay omesay imetay incapableyay
ofyay offeringyay anyyay eplyray. Iyay evolvedray apidlyray inyay ymay indmay ayay ultitudemay ofyay
oughtsthay andyay endeavouredyay otay arriveyay atyay omesay onclusioncay. Alasyay! Otay emay
ethay ideayay ofyay anyay immediateyay unionyay ithway ymay Elizabethyay asway oneyay ofyay orrorhay andyay
ismayday. Iyay asway oundbay ybay ayay olemnsay omisepray ichwhay Iyay adhay otnay yetyay ulfilledfay
andyay aredday otnay eakbray, oryay ifyay Iyay idday, atwhay anifoldmay iseriesmay ightmay otnay
impendyay overyay emay andyay ymay evotedday amilyfay! Ouldcay Iyay enteryay intoyay ayay estivalfay
ithway isthay eadlyday eightway yetyay anginghay oundray ymay ecknay andyay owingbay emay otay ethay
oundgray? Iyay ustmay erformpay ymay engagementyay andyay etlay ethay onstermay epartday ithway
ishay atemay eforebay Iyay allowedyay yselfmay otay enjoyyay ethay elightday ofyay ayay unionyay omfray
ichwhay Iyay expectedyay eacepay.

Iyay ememberedray alsoyay ethay ecessitynay imposedyay uponyay emay ofyay eitheryay ourneyingjay otay
Englandyay oryay enteringyay intoyay ayay onglay orrespondencecay ithway osethay ilosophersphay
ofyay atthay ountrycay osewhay owledgeknay andyay iscoveriesday ereway ofyay indispensableyay
useyay otay emay inyay ymay esentpray undertakingyay. Ethay atterlay ethodmay ofyay obtainingyay
ethay esiredday intelligenceyay asway ilatoryday andyay unsatisfactoryyay; esidesbay, Iyay
adhay anyay insurmountableyay aversionyay otay ethay ideayay ofyay engagingyay yselfmay inyay ymay
oathsomelay asktay inyay ymay ather’sfay ousehay ilewhay inyay abitshay ofyay amiliarfay
intercourseyay ithway osethay Iyay ovedlay. Iyay ewknay atthay ayay ousandthay earfulfay
accidentsyay ightmay occuryay, ethay ightestslay ofyay ichwhay ouldway iscloseday ayay aletay otay
illthray allyay onnectedcay ithway emay ithway orrorhay. Iyay asway awareyay alsoyay atthay Iyay
ouldshay oftenyay oselay allyay elf-commandsay, allyay apacitycay ofyay idinghay ethay
arrowinghay ensationssay atthay ouldway ossesspay emay uringday ethay ogresspray ofyay ymay
unearthlyyay occupationyay. Iyay ustmay absentyay yselfmay omfray allyay Iyay ovedlay ilewhay usthay
employedyay. Onceyay ommencedcay, ityay ouldway uicklyqay ebay achievedyay, andyay Iyay ightmay ebay
estoredray otay ymay amilyfay inyay eacepay andyay appinesshay. Ymay omisepray ulfilledfay,
ethay onstermay ouldway epartday orfay everyay. Oryay o(say ymay ondfay ancyfay imagedyay) omesay
accidentyay ightmay eanwhilemay occuryay otay estroyday imhay andyay utpay anyay endyay otay ymay
averyslay orfay everyay.

Esethay eelingsfay ictatedday ymay answeryay otay ymay atherfay. Iyay expressedyay ayay ishway otay
isitvay Englandyay, utbay oncealingcay ethay uetray easonsray ofyay isthay equestray, Iyay
othedclay ymay esiresday underyay ayay uisegay ichwhay excitedyay onay uspicionsay, ilewhay Iyay
urgedyay ymay esireday ithway anyay earnestnessyay atthay easilyyay inducedyay ymay atherfay otay
omplycay. Afteryay osay onglay ayay eriodpay ofyay anyay absorbingyay elancholymay atthay
esembledray adnessmay inyay itsyay intensityyay andyay effectsyay, ehay asway adglay otay indfay
atthay Iyay asway apablecay ofyay akingtay easureplay inyay ethay ideayay ofyay uchsay ayay ourneyjay,
andyay ehay opedhay atthay angechay ofyay enescay andyay ariedvay amusementyay ouldway, eforebay ymay
eturnray, avehay estoredray emay entirelyyay otay yselfmay.

Ethay urationday ofyay ymay absenceyay asway eftlay otay ymay ownyay oicechay; ayay ewfay onthsmay, oryay
atyay ostmay ayay yearyay, asway ethay eriodpay ontemplatedcay. Oneyay aternalpay indkay
ecautionpray ehay adhay akentay otay ensureyay ymay avinghay ayay ompanioncay. Ithoutway
eviouslypray ommunicatingcay ithway emay, ehay adhay, inyay oncertcay ithway Elizabethyay,
arrangedyay atthay Ervalclay ouldshay oinjay emay atyay Asburghstray. Isthay interferedyay
ithway ethay olitudesay Iyay ovetedcay orfay ethay osecutionpray ofyay ymay asktay; yetyay atyay ethay
ommencementcay ofyay ymay ourneyjay ethay esencepray ofyay ymay iendfray ouldcay inyay onay ayway ebay
anyay impedimentyay, andyay ulytray Iyay ejoicedray atthay usthay Iyay ouldshay ebay avedsay anymay
ourshay ofyay onelylay, addeningmay eflectionray. Aynay, Enryhay ightmay andstay etweenbay
emay andyay ethay intrusionyay ofyay ymay oefay. Ifyay Iyay ereway aloneyay, ouldway ehay otnay atyay imestay
orcefay ishay abhorredyay esencepray onyay emay otay emindray emay ofyay ymay asktay oryay otay
ontemplatecay itsyay ogresspray?

Otay Englandyay, ereforethay, Iyay asway oundbay, andyay ityay asway understoodyay atthay ymay unionyay
ithway Elizabethyay ouldshay aketay aceplay immediatelyyay onyay ymay eturnray. Ymay ather’sfay
ageyay enderedray imhay extremelyyay averseyay otay elayday. Orfay yselfmay, erethay asway oneyay
ewardray Iyay omisedpray yselfmay omfray ymay etestedday oils—onetay onsolationcay orfay ymay
unparalleledyay ufferingssay; ityay asway ethay ospectpray ofyay atthay ayday enwhay,
enfranchisedyay omfray ymay iserablemay averyslay, Iyay ightmay aimclay Elizabethyay andyay
orgetfay ethay astpay inyay ymay unionyay ithway erhay.

Iyay ownay ademay arrangementsyay orfay ymay ourneyjay, utbay oneyay eelingfay auntedhay emay
ichwhay illedfay emay ithway earfay andyay agitationyay. Uringday ymay absenceyay Iyay ouldshay
eavelay ymay iendsfray unconsciousyay ofyay ethay existenceyay ofyay eirthay enemyyay andyay
unprotectedyay omfray ishay attacksyay, exasperatedyay asyay ehay ightmay ebay ybay ymay
epartureday. Utbay ehay adhay omisedpray otay ollowfay emay ereverwhay Iyay ightmay ogay, andyay
ouldway ehay otnay accompanyyay emay otay Englandyay? Isthay imaginationyay asway eadfuldray inyay
itselfyay, utbay oothingsay inasmuchyay asyay ityay upposedsay ethay afetysay ofyay ymay iendsfray.
Iyay asway agonisedyay ithway ethay ideayay ofyay ethay ossibilitypay atthay ethay everseray ofyay
isthay ightmay appenhay. Utbay oughthray ethay olewhay eriodpay uringday ichwhay Iyay asway ethay
aveslay ofyay ymay eaturecray Iyay allowedyay yselfmay otay ebay overnedgay ybay ethay impulsesyay ofyay
ethay omentmay; andyay ymay esentpray ensationssay onglystray intimatedyay atthay ethay iendfay
ouldway ollowfay emay andyay exemptyay ymay amilyfay omfray ethay angerday ofyay ishay
achinationsmay.

Ityay asway inyay ethay atterlay endyay ofyay Eptembersay atthay Iyay againyay uittedqay ymay ativenay
ountrycay. Ymay ourneyjay adhay eenbay ymay ownyay uggestionsay, andyay Elizabethyay
ereforethay acquiescedyay, utbay eshay asway illedfay ithway isquietday atyay ethay ideayay ofyay
ymay ufferingsay, awayyay omfray erhay, ethay inroadsyay ofyay iserymay andyay iefgray. Ityay adhay
eenbay erhay arecay ichwhay ovidedpray emay ayay ompanioncay inyay Erval—andclay yetyay ayay anmay
isyay indblay otay ayay ousandthay inutemay ircumstancescay ichwhay allcay orthfay ayay oman’sway
eduloussay attentionyay. Eshay ongedlay otay idbay emay astenhay ymay eturnray; ayay ousandthay
onflictingcay emotionsyay enderedray erhay utemay asyay eshay adebay emay ayay earfultay, ilentsay
arewellfay.

Iyay ewthray yselfmay intoyay ethay arriagecay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayyay, ardlyhay
owingknay itherwhay Iyay asway oinggay, andyay arelesscay ofyay atwhay asway assingpay aroundyay.
Iyay ememberedray onlyyay, andyay ityay asway ithway ayay itterbay anguishyay atthay Iyay eflectedray onyay
ityay, otay orderyay atthay ymay emicalchay instrumentsyay ouldshay ebay ackedpay otay ogay ithway
emay. Illedfay ithway earydray imaginationsyay, Iyay assedpay oughthray anymay eautifulbay
andyay ajesticmay enesscay, utbay ymay eyesyay ereway ixedfay andyay unobservingyay. Iyay ouldcay
onlyyay inkthay ofyay ethay ournebay ofyay ymay avelstray andyay ethay orkway ichwhay asway otay occupyyay
emay ilstwhay eythay enduredyay.

Afteryay omesay aysday entspay inyay istlesslay indolenceyay, uringday ichwhay Iyay aversedtray
anymay eagueslay, Iyay arrivedyay atyay Asburghstray, erewhay Iyay aitedway otway aysday orfay
Ervalclay. Ehay amecay. Alasyay, owhay eatgray asway ethay ontrastcay etweenbay usyay! Ehay
asway aliveyay otay everyyay ewnay enescay, oyfuljay enwhay ehay awsay ethay eautiesbay ofyay ethay
ettingsay unsay, andyay oremay appyhay enwhay ehay eheldbay ityay iseray andyay ecommenceray ayay ewnay
ayday. Ehay ointedpay outyay otay emay ethay iftingshay olourscay ofyay ethay andscapelay andyay
ethay appearancesyay ofyay ethay yskay. is“thay isyay atwhay ityay isyay otay ivelay,” ehay iedcray;
ow“nay Iyay enjoyyay existenceyay! Utbay youyay, ymay earday Ankensteinfray, ereforewhay areyay
youyay espondingday andyay orrowfulsay!” Inyay uthtray, Iyay asway occupiedyay ybay oomyglay
oughtsthay andyay eithernay awsay ethay escentday ofyay ethay eveningyay arstay ornay ethay oldengay
unrisesay eflectedray inyay ethay Inerhay. Andyay youyay, ymay iendfray, ouldway ebay arfay oremay
amusedyay ithway ethay ournaljay ofyay Ervalclay, owhay observedyay ethay eneryscay ithway anyay
eyeyay ofyay eelingfay andyay elightday, anthay inyay isteninglay otay ymay eflectionsray. Iyay, ayay
iserablemay etchwray, auntedhay ybay ayay ursecay atthay utshay upyay everyyay avenueyay otay
enjoymentyay.

Eway adhay agreedyay otay escendday ethay Inerhay inyay ayay oatbay omfray Asburghstray otay
Otterdamray, encewhay eway ightmay aketay ippingshay orfay Ondonlay. Uringday isthay
oyagevay eway assedpay anymay illowyway islandsyay andyay awsay everalsay eautifulbay ownstay.
Eway ayedstay ayay ayday atyay Annheimmay, andyay onyay ethay ifthfay omfray ouryay epartureday omfray
Asburghstray, arrivedyay atyay Ainzmay. Ethay oursecay ofyay ethay Inerhay elowbay Ainzmay
ecomesbay uchmay oremay icturesquepay. Ethay iverray escendsday apidlyray andyay indsway
etweenbay illshay, otnay ighhay, utbay eepstay, andyay ofyay eautifulbay ormsfay. Eway awsay
anymay uinedray astlescay andingstay onyay ethay edgesyay ofyay ecipicespray, urroundedsay ybay
ackblay oodsway, ighhay andyay inaccessibleyay. Isthay artpay ofyay ethay Inerhay, indeedyay,
esentspray ayay ingularlysay ariegatedvay andscapelay. Inyay oneyay otspay youyay iewvay
uggedray illshay, uinedray astlescay overlookingyay emendoustray ecipicespray, ithway
ethay arkday Inerhay ushingray eneathbay; andyay onyay ethay uddensay urntay ofyay ayay omontorypray,
ourishingflay ineyardsvay ithway eengray opingslay anksbay andyay ayay eanderingmay iverray
andyay opulouspay ownstay occupyyay ethay enescay.

Eway avelledtray atyay ethay imetay ofyay ethay intagevay andyay eardhay ethay ongsay ofyay ethay abourerslay
asyay eway idedglay ownday ethay eamstray. Evenyay Iyay, epressedday inyay indmay, andyay ymay iritsspay
ontinuallycay agitatedyay ybay oomyglay eelingsfay, evenyay Iyay asway easedplay. Iyay aylay atyay ethay
ottombay ofyay ethay oatbay, andyay asyay Iyay azedgay onyay ethay oudlessclay ueblay yskay, Iyay eemedsay otay
inkdray inyay ayay anquillitytray otay ichwhay Iyay adhay onglay eenbay ayay angerstray. Andyay ifyay esethay
ereway ymay ensationssay, owhay ancay escribeday osethay ofyay Enryhay? Ehay eltfay asyay ifyay ehay adhay
eenbay ansportedtray otay Airy-landfay andyay enjoyedyay ayay appinesshay eldomsay astedtay ybay
anmay. i“ay avehay eensay,” ehay aidsay, e“thay ostmay eautifulbay enesscay
ofyay ymay ownyay ountrycay; Iyay avehay isitedvay ethay akeslay ofyay Ucernelay andyay Uriyay, erewhay ethay
owysnay ountainsmay escendday almostyay erpendicularlypay otay ethay aterway, astingcay ackblay
andyay impenetrableyay adesshay, ichwhay ouldway ausecay ayay oomyglay andyay ournfulmay appearanceyay
ereway ityay otnay orfay ethay ostmay erdantvay islandsyay atthay elieveray ethay eyeyay ybay eirthay aygay
appearanceyay; Iyay avehay eensay isthay akelay agitatedyay ybay ayay empesttay, enwhay ethay indway oretay
upyay irlwindswhay ofyay aterway andyay avegay youyay anyay ideayay ofyay atwhay ethay ater-spoutway ustmay ebay
onyay ethay eatgray oceanyay; andyay ethay avesway ashday ithway uryfay ethay asebay ofyay ethay ountainmay,
erewhay ethay iestpray andyay ishay istressmay ereway overwhelmedyay ybay anyay avalancheyay andyay
erewhay eirthay yingday oicesvay areyay illstay aidsay otay ebay eardhay amidyay ethay ausespay ofyay ethay
ightlynay indway; Iyay avehay eensay ethay ountainsmay ofyay Alay Alaisvay, andyay ethay Ayspay eday Audvay;
utbay isthay ountrycay, Ictorvay, easesplay emay oremay anthay allyay osethay ondersway. Ethay
ountainsmay ofyay Itzerlandsway areyay oremay ajesticmay andyay angestray, utbay erethay isyay ayay
armchay inyay ethay anksbay ofyay isthay ivineday iverray atthay Iyay evernay eforebay awsay equalledyay.
Ooklay atyay atthay astlecay ichwhay overhangsyay yonyay ecipicepray; andyay atthay alsoyay onyay ethay
islandyay, almostyay oncealedcay amongstyay ethay oliagefay ofyay osethay ovelylay eestray; andyay ownay
atthay oupgray ofyay abourerslay omingcay omfray amongyay eirthay inesvay; andyay atthay illagevay
alfhay idhay inyay ethay ecessray ofyay ethay ountainmay. Ohyay, urelysay ethay iritspay atthay inhabitsyay
andyay uardsgay isthay aceplay ashay ayay oulsay oremay inyay armonyhay ithway anmay anthay osethay owhay
