ilepay ethay acierglay oryay etireray otay ethay inaccessibleyay eakspay ofyay ethay ountainsmay ofyay
ouryay ownyay ountrycay.”

Ervalclay! Elovedbay iendfray! Evenyay ownay ityay elightsday emay otay ecordray youryay ordsway andyay
otay elldway onyay ethay aisepray ofyay ichwhay youyay areyay osay eminentlyyay eservingday. Ehay asway ayay
eingbay ormedfay inyay ethay ery“vay oetrypay ofyay aturenay.” Ishay ildway andyay
enthusiasticyay imaginationyay asway astenedchay ybay ethay ensibilitysay ofyay ishay earthay. Ishay
oulsay overflowedyay ithway ardentyay affectionsyay, andyay ishay iendshipfray asway ofyay atthay
evotedday andyay ondrousway aturenay atthay ethay orldly-mindedway eachtay usyay otay ooklay orfay onlyyay
inyay ethay imaginationyay. Utbay evenyay umanhay ympathiessay ereway otnay ufficientsay otay
atisfysay ishay eageryay indmay. Ethay eneryscay ofyay externalyay aturenay, ichwhay othersyay egardray
onlyyay ithway admirationyay, ehay ovedlay ithway ardouryay:—

    e——thay oundingsay ataractcay
    Auntedhay imhay ikelay ayay assionpay: ethay alltay ockray,
    Ethay ountainmay, andyay ethay eepday andyay oomyglay oodway,
    Eirthay olourscay andyay eirthay ormsfay, ereway enthay otay imhay
    Anyay appetiteyay; ayay eelingfay, andyay ayay ovelay,
    Atthay adhay onay eednay ofyay ayay emoterray armchay,
    Ybay oughtthay uppliedsay, oryay anyyay interestyay
    Unborrow’dyay omfray ethay eyeyay.

          ordsworth’s[way intern“tay Abbeyyay”.]

Andyay erewhay oesday ehay ownay existyay? Isyay isthay entlegay andyay ovelylay eingbay ostlay
orfay everyay? Ashay isthay indmay, osay epleteray ithway ideasyay, imaginationsyay ancifulfay
andyay agnificentmay, ichwhay ormedfay ayay orldway, osewhay existenceyay ependedday onyay ethay
ifelay ofyay itsyay eator;—hascray isthay indmay erishedpay? Oesday ityay ownay onlyyay existyay
inyay ymay emorymay? Onay, ityay isyay otnay usthay; youryay ormfay osay ivinelyday oughtwray, andyay
eamingbay ithway eautybay, ashay ecayedday, utbay youryay iritspay illstay isitsvay andyay
onsolescay youryay unhappyyay iendfray.

Ardonpay isthay ushgay ofyay orrowsay; esethay ineffectualyay ordsway areyay utbay ayay ightslay
ibutetray otay ethay unexampledyay orthway ofyay Enryhay, utbay eythay oothesay ymay earthay,
overflowingyay ithway ethay anguishyay ichwhay ishay emembranceray eatescray. Iyay illway
oceedpray ithway ymay aletay.

Eyondbay Olognecay eway escendedday otay ethay ainsplay ofyay Ollandhay; andyay eway esolvedray otay
ostpay ethay emainderray ofyay ouryay ayway, orfay ethay indway asway ontrarycay andyay ethay eamstray ofyay
ethay iverray asway ootay entlegay otay aidyay usyay.

Ouryay ourneyjay erehay ostlay ethay interestyay arisingyay omfray eautifulbay eneryscay, utbay eway
arrivedyay inyay ayay ewfay aysday atyay Otterdamray, encewhay eway oceededpray ybay easay otay Englandyay.
Ityay asway onyay ayay earclay orningmay, inyay ethay atterlay aysday ofyay Ecemberday, atthay Iyay irstfay awsay
ethay itewhay iffsclay ofyay Itainbray. Ethay anksbay ofyay ethay Amesthay esentedpray ayay ewnay enescay;
eythay ereway atflay utbay ertilefay, andyay almostyay everyyay owntay asway arkedmay ybay ethay
emembranceray ofyay omesay orystay. Eway awsay Ilburytay Ortfay andyay ememberedray ethay Anishspay
Armadayay, Avesendgray, Oolwichway, andyay Eenwich—placesgray ichwhay Iyay adhay eardhay
ofyay evenyay inyay ymay ountrycay.

Atyay engthlay eway awsay ethay umerousnay eeplesstay ofyay Ondonlay, Stay. Aul’spay oweringtay
aboveyay allyay, andyay ethay Owertay amedfay inyay Englishyay istoryhay.




Apterchay 19


Ondonlay asway ouryay esentpray ointpay ofyay estray; eway eterminedday otay emainray everalsay
onthsmay inyay isthay onderfulway andyay elebratedcay itycay. Ervalclay esiredday ethay
intercourseyay ofyay ethay enmay ofyay eniusgay andyay alenttay owhay ourishedflay atyay isthay
imetay, utbay isthay asway ithway emay ayay econdarysay objectyay; Iyay asway incipallypray
occupiedyay ithway ethay eansmay ofyay obtainingyay ethay informationyay ecessarynay orfay ethay
ompletioncay ofyay ymay omisepray andyay uicklyqay availedyay yselfmay ofyay ethay etterslay ofyay
introductionyay atthay Iyay adhay oughtbray ithway emay, addressedyay otay ethay ostmay
istinguishedday aturalnay ilosophersphay.

Ifyay isthay ourneyjay adhay akentay aceplay uringday ymay aysday ofyay udystay andyay appinesshay,
ityay ouldway avehay affordedyay emay inexpressibleyay easureplay. Utbay ayay ightblay adhay
omecay overyay ymay existenceyay, andyay Iyay onlyyay isitedvay esethay eoplepay orfay ethay akesay ofyay
ethay informationyay eythay ightmay ivegay emay onyay ethay ubjectsay inyay ichwhay ymay interestyay
asway osay erriblytay ofoundpray. Ompanycay asway irksomeyay otay emay; enwhay aloneyay, Iyay
ouldcay illfay ymay indmay ithway ethay ightssay ofyay eavenhay andyay earthyay; ethay oicevay ofyay
Enryhay oothedsay emay, andyay Iyay ouldcay usthay eatchay yselfmay intoyay ayay ansitorytray
eacepay. Utbay usybay, uninterestingyay, oyousjay acesfay oughtbray ackbay espairday otay
ymay earthay. Iyay awsay anyay insurmountableyay arrierbay acedplay etweenbay emay andyay ymay
ellowfay enmay; isthay arrierbay asway ealedsay ithway ethay oodblay ofyay Illiamway andyay
Ustinejay, andyay otay eflectray onyay ethay eventsyay onnectedcay ithway osethay amesnay illedfay
ymay oulsay ithway anguishyay.

Utbay inyay Ervalclay Iyay awsay ethay imageyay ofyay ymay ormerfay elfsay; ehay asway inquisitiveyay
andyay anxiousyay otay aingay experienceyay andyay instructionyay. Ethay ifferenceday ofyay
annersmay ichwhay ehay observedyay asway otay imhay anyay inexhaustibleyay ourcesay ofyay
instructionyay andyay amusementyay. Ehay asway alsoyay ursuingpay anyay objectyay ehay adhay onglay
adhay inyay iewvay. Ishay esignday asway otay isitvay Indiayay, inyay ethay eliefbay atthay ehay adhay
inyay ishay owledgeknay ofyay itsyay ariousvay anguageslay, andyay inyay ethay iewsvay ehay adhay
akentay ofyay itsyay ocietysay, ethay eansmay ofyay ateriallymay assistingyay ethay ogresspray ofyay
Europeanyay olonizationcay andyay adetray. Inyay Itainbray onlyyay ouldcay ehay urtherfay ethay
executionyay ofyay ishay anplay. Ehay asway orfay everyay usybay, andyay ethay onlyyay eckchay otay ishay
enjoymentsyay asway ymay orrowfulsay andyay ejectedday indmay. Iyay iedtray otay oncealcay isthay
asyay uchmay asyay ossiblepay, atthay Iyay ightmay otnay ebarday imhay omfray ethay easuresplay
aturalnay otay oneyay owhay asway enteringyay onyay ayay ewnay enescay ofyay ifelay, undisturbedyay ybay
anyyay arecay oryay itterbay ecollectionray. Iyay oftenyay efusedray otay accompanyyay imhay,
allegingyay anotheryay engagementyay, atthay Iyay ightmay emainray aloneyay. Iyay ownay alsoyay
eganbay otay ollectcay ethay aterialsmay ecessarynay orfay ymay ewnay eationcray, andyay isthay
asway otay emay ikelay ethay orturetay ofyay inglesay opsdray ofyay aterway ontinuallycay allingfay
onyay ethay eadhay. Everyyay oughtthay atthay asway evotedday otay ityay asway anyay extremeyay
anguishyay, andyay everyyay ordway atthay Iyay okespay inyay allusionyay otay ityay ausedcay ymay ipslay
otay uiverqay, andyay ymay earthay otay alpitatepay.

Afteryay assingpay omesay onthsmay inyay Ondonlay, eway eceivedray ayay etterlay omfray ayay ersonpay inyay
Otlandscay owhay adhay ormerlyfay eenbay ouryay isitorvay atyay Enevagay. Ehay entionedmay ethay
eautiesbay ofyay ishay ativenay ountrycay andyay askedyay usyay ifyay osethay ereway otnay ufficientsay
allurementsyay otay induceyay usyay otay olongpray ouryay ourneyjay asyay arfay orthnay asyay Erthpay,
erewhay ehay esidedray. Ervalclay eagerlyyay esiredday otay acceptyay isthay invitationyay, andyay Iyay,
althoughyay Iyay abhorredyay ocietysay, ishedway otay iewvay againyay ountainsmay andyay eamsstray andyay
allyay ethay ondrousway orksway ithway ichwhay Aturenay adornsyay erhay osenchay elling-placesdway.

Eway adhay arrivedyay inyay Englandyay atyay ethay eginningbay ofyay Octoberyay, andyay ityay asway ownay
Ebruaryfay. Eway accordinglyyay eterminedday otay ommencecay ouryay ourneyjay owardstay ethay
orthnay atyay ethay expirationyay ofyay anotheryay onthmay. Inyay isthay expeditionyay eway idday otnay
intendyay otay ollowfay ethay eatgray oadray otay Edinburghyay, utbay otay isitvay Indsorway, Oxfordyay,
Atlockmay, andyay ethay Umberlandcay akeslay, esolvingray otay arriveyay atyay ethay ompletioncay ofyay
isthay ourtay aboutyay ethay endyay ofyay Ulyjay. Iyay ackedpay upyay ymay emicalchay instrumentsyay andyay
ethay aterialsmay Iyay adhay ollectedcay, esolvingray otay inishfay ymay abourslay inyay omesay
obscureyay ooknay inyay ethay orthernnay ighlandshay ofyay Otlandscay.

Eway uittedqay Ondonlay onyay ethay 27th ofyay Archmay andyay emainedray ayay ewfay aysday atyay
Indsorway, amblingray inyay itsyay eautifulbay orestfay. Isthay asway ayay ewnay enescay otay usyay
ountaineersmay; ethay ajesticmay oaksyay, ethay uantityqay ofyay amegay, andyay ethay erdshay ofyay
atelystay eerday ereway allyay oveltiesnay otay usyay.

Omfray encethay eway oceededpray otay Oxfordyay. Asyay eway enteredyay isthay itycay, ouryay indsmay
ereway illedfay ithway ethay emembranceray ofyay ethay eventsyay atthay adhay eenbay ansactedtray
erethay oremay anthay ayay enturycay andyay ayay alfhay eforebay. Ityay asway erehay atthay Arleschay
Iyay. adhay ollectedcay ishay orcesfay. Isthay itycay adhay emainedray aithfulfay otay imhay,
afteryay ethay olewhay ationnay adhay orsakenfay ishay ausecay otay oinjay ethay andardstay ofyay
Arliamentpay andyay ibertylay. Ethay emorymay ofyay atthay unfortunateyay ingkay andyay ishay
ompanionscay, ethay amiableyay Alklandfay, ethay insolentyay Oringgay, ishay ueenqay, andyay
onsay, avegay ayay eculiarpay interestyay otay everyyay artpay ofyay ethay itycay ichwhay eythay
ightmay ebay upposedsay otay avehay inhabitedyay. Ethay iritspay ofyay elderyay aysday oundfay ayay
ellingdway erehay, andyay eway elightedday otay acetray itsyay ootstepsfay. Ifyay esethay
eelingsfay adhay otnay oundfay anyay imaginaryyay atificationgray, ethay appearanceyay ofyay
ethay itycay adhay yetyay inyay itselfyay ufficientsay eautybay otay obtainyay ouryay admirationyay.
Ethay ollegescay areyay ancientyay andyay icturesquepay; ethay eetsstray areyay almostyay
agnificentmay; andyay ethay ovelylay Isisyay, ichwhay owsflay esidebay ityay oughthray eadowsmay
ofyay exquisiteyay erdurevay, isyay eadspray orthfay intoyay ayay acidplay expanseyay ofyay atersway,
ichwhay eflectsray itsyay ajesticmay assemblageyay ofyay owerstay, andyay iresspay, andyay
omesday, embosomedyay amongyay agedyay eestray.

Iyay enjoyedyay isthay enescay, andyay yetyay ymay enjoymentyay asway embitteredyay othbay ybay ethay
emorymay ofyay ethay astpay andyay ethay anticipationyay ofyay ethay uturefay. Iyay asway ormedfay
orfay eacefulpay appinesshay. Uringday ymay youthfulyay aysday iscontentday evernay
isitedvay ymay indmay, andyay ifyay Iyay asway everyay overcomeyay ybay ennui_ay_, ethay ightsay ofyay atwhay
isyay eautifulbay inyay aturenay oryay ethay udystay ofyay atwhay isyay excellentyay andyay ublimesay inyay
ethay oductionspray ofyay anmay ouldcay alwaysyay interestyay ymay earthay andyay ommunicatecay
elasticityyay otay ymay iritsspay. Utbay Iyay amyay ayay astedblay eetray; ethay oltbay ashay
enteredyay ymay oulsay; andyay Iyay eltfay enthay atthay Iyay ouldshay urvivesay otay exhibityay atwhay
Iyay allshay oonsay easecay otay e—abay iserablemay ectaclespay ofyay eckedwray umanityhay,
itiablepay otay othersyay andyay intolerableyay otay yselfmay.

Eway assedpay ayay onsiderablecay eriodpay atyay Oxfordyay, amblingray amongyay itsyay environsyay
andyay endeavouringyay otay identifyyay everyyay otspay ichwhay ightmay elateray otay ethay ostmay
animatingyay epochyay ofyay Englishyay istoryhay. Ouryay ittlelay oyagesvay ofyay iscoveryday
ereway oftenyay olongedpray ybay ethay uccessivesay objectsyay atthay esentedpray
emselvesthay. Eway isitedvay ethay ombtay ofyay ethay illustriousyay Ampdenhay andyay ethay
ieldfay onyay ichwhay atthay atriotpay ellfay. Orfay ayay omentmay ymay oulsay asway elevatedyay
omfray itsyay ebasingday andyay iserablemay earsfay otay ontemplatecay ethay ivineday ideasyay
ofyay ibertylay andyay elf-sacrificesay ofyay ichwhay esethay ightssay ereway ethay onumentsmay
andyay ethay emembrancersray. Orfay anyay instantyay Iyay aredday otay akeshay offyay ymay ainschay
andyay ooklay aroundyay emay ithway ayay eefray andyay oftylay iritspay, utbay ethay ironyay adhay eatenyay
intoyay ymay eshflay, andyay Iyay anksay againyay, emblingtray andyay opelesshay, intoyay ymay
iserablemay elfsay.

Eway eftlay Oxfordyay ithway egretray andyay oceededpray otay Atlockmay, ichwhay asway ouryay extnay
aceplay ofyay estray. Ethay ountrycay inyay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay isthay illagevay
esembledray, otay ayay eatergray egreeday, ethay eneryscay ofyay Itzerlandsway; utbay
everythingyay isyay onyay ayay owerlay alescay, andyay ethay eengray illshay antway ethay owncray ofyay
istantday itewhay Alpsyay ichwhay alwaysyay attendyay onyay ethay inypay ountainsmay ofyay ymay
ativenay ountrycay. Eway isitedvay ethay ondrousway avecay andyay ethay ittlelay abinetscay
ofyay aturalnay istoryhay, erewhay ethay uriositiescay areyay isposedday inyay ethay amesay
annermay asyay inyay ethay ollectionscay atyay Ervoxsay andyay Amounixchay. Ethay atterlay amenay
ademay emay embletray enwhay onouncedpray ybay Enryhay, andyay Iyay astenedhay otay uitqay
Atlockmay, ithway ichwhay atthay erribletay enescay asway usthay associatedyay.

Omfray Erbyday, illstay ourneyingjay orthwardsnay, eway assedpay otway onthsmay inyay
Umberlandcay andyay Estmorlandway. Iyay ouldcay ownay almostyay ancyfay yselfmay amongyay ethay
Isssway ountainsmay. Ethay ittlelay atchespay ofyay owsnay ichwhay yetyay ingeredlay onyay ethay
orthernnay idessay ofyay ethay ountainsmay, ethay akeslay, andyay ethay ashingday ofyay ethay
ockyray eamsstray ereway allyay amiliarfay andyay earday ightssay otay emay. Erehay alsoyay eway
ademay omesay acquaintancesyay, owhay almostyay ontrivedcay otay eatchay emay intoyay
appinesshay. Ethay elightday ofyay Ervalclay asway oportionablypray eatergray anthay
inemay; ishay indmay expandedyay inyay ethay ompanycay ofyay enmay ofyay alenttay, andyay ehay oundfay
inyay ishay ownyay aturenay eatergray apacitiescay andyay esourcesray anthay ehay ouldcay avehay
imaginedyay imselfhay otay avehay ossessedpay ilewhay ehay associatedyay ithway ishay
inferiorsyay. i“ay ouldcay asspay ymay ifelay erehay,” aidsay ehay otay emay; and“ay amongyay
esethay ountainsmay Iyay ouldshay arcelyscay egretray Itzerlandsway andyay ethay Inerhay.”

Utbay ehay oundfay atthay ayay aveller’stray ifelay isyay oneyay atthay includesyay uchmay ainpay
amidstyay itsyay enjoymentsyay. Ishay eelingsfay areyay orfay everyay onyay ethay etchstray; andyay
enwhay ehay eginsbay otay inksay intoyay eposeray, ehay indsfay imselfhay obligedyay otay uitqay
atthay onyay ichwhay ehay estsray inyay easureplay orfay omethingsay ewnay, ichwhay againyay
engagesyay ishay attentionyay, andyay ichwhay alsoyay ehay orsakesfay orfay otheryay oveltiesnay.

Eway adhay arcelyscay isitedvay ethay ariousvay akeslay ofyay Umberlandcay andyay Estmorlandway
andyay onceivedcay anyay affectionyay orfay omesay ofyay ethay inhabitantsyay enwhay ethay eriodpay
ofyay ouryay appointmentyay ithway ouryay Otchscay iendfray approachedyay, andyay eway eftlay emthay
otay aveltray onyay. Orfay ymay ownyay artpay Iyay asway otnay orrysay. Iyay adhay ownay eglectednay ymay
omisepray orfay omesay imetay, andyay Iyay earedfay ethay effectsyay ofyay ethay on’sdæmay
isappointmentday. Ehay ightmay emainray inyay Itzerlandsway andyay eakwray ishay engeancevay
onyay ymay elativesray. Isthay ideayay ursuedpay emay andyay ormentedtay emay atyay everyyay omentmay
omfray ichwhay Iyay ightmay otherwiseyay avehay atchedsnay eposeray andyay eacepay. Iyay aitedway
orfay ymay etterslay ithway everishfay impatienceyay; ifyay eythay ereway elayedday Iyay asway
iserablemay andyay overcomeyay ybay ayay ousandthay earsfay; andyay enwhay eythay arrivedyay andyay Iyay
awsay ethay uperscriptionsay ofyay Elizabethyay oryay ymay atherfay, Iyay ardlyhay aredday otay
eadray andyay ascertainyay ymay atefay. Ometimessay Iyay oughtthay atthay ethay iendfay
ollowedfay emay andyay ightmay expediteyay ymay emissnessray ybay urderingmay ymay ompanioncay.
Enwhay esethay oughtsthay ossessedpay emay, Iyay ouldway otnay uitqay Enryhay orfay ayay omentmay,
utbay ollowedfay imhay asyay ishay adowshay, otay otectpray imhay omfray ethay anciedfay ageray ofyay
ishay estroyerday. Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay Iyay adhay ommittedcay omesay eatgray imecray, ethay
onsciousnesscay ofyay ichwhay auntedhay emay. Iyay asway uiltlessgay, utbay Iyay adhay indeedyay
awndray ownday ayay orriblehay ursecay uponyay ymay eadhay, asyay ortalmay asyay atthay ofyay imecray.

Iyay isitedvay Edinburghyay ithway anguidlay eyesyay andyay indmay; andyay yetyay atthay itycay ightmay
avehay interestedyay ethay ostmay unfortunateyay eingbay. Ervalclay idday otnay ikelay ityay osay ellway
asyay Oxfordyay, orfay ethay antiquityyay ofyay ethay atterlay itycay asway oremay easingplay otay imhay.
Utbay ethay eautybay andyay egularityray ofyay ethay ewnay owntay ofyay Edinburghyay, itsyay omanticray
astlecay andyay itsyay environsyay, ethay ostmay elightfulday inyay ethay orldway, Arthur’syay
Eatsay, Stay. Ernard’sbay Ellway, andyay ethay Entlandpay Illshay, ompensatedcay imhay orfay
ethay angechay andyay illedfay imhay ithway eerfulnesschay andyay admirationyay. Utbay Iyay asway
impatientyay otay arriveyay atyay ethay erminationtay ofyay ymay ourneyjay.

Eway eftlay Edinburghyay inyay ayay eekway, assingpay oughthray Ouparcay, Stay. Andrew’syay, andyay
alongyay ethay anksbay ofyay ethay Aytay, otay Erthpay, erewhay ouryay iendfray expectedyay usyay.
Utbay Iyay asway inyay onay oodmay otay aughlay andyay alktay ithway angersstray oryay enteryay intoyay
eirthay eelingsfay oryay ansplay ithway ethay oodgay umourhay expectedyay omfray ayay uestgay; andyay
accordinglyyay Iyay oldtay Ervalclay atthay Iyay ishedway otay akemay ethay ourtay ofyay Otlandscay
aloneyay. o“day youyay,” aidsay Iyay, enjoy“ay yourselfyay, andyay etlay isthay ebay ouryay
endezvousray. Iyay aymay ebay absentyay ayay onthmay oryay otway; utbay oday otnay interfereyay ithway
ymay otionsmay, Iyay entreatyay youyay; eavelay emay otay eacepay andyay olitudesay orfay ayay ortshay
imetay; andyay enwhay Iyay eturnray, Iyay opehay ityay illway ebay ithway ayay ighterlay earthay, oremay
ongenialcay otay youryay ownyay empertay.”

Enryhay ishedway otay issuadeday emay, utbay eeingsay emay entbay onyay isthay anplay, easedcay otay
emonstrateray. Ehay entreatedyay emay otay itewray oftenyay. i“ay adhay atherray ebay ithway
youyay,” ehay aidsay, in“ay youryay olitarysay amblesray, anthay ithway esethay Otchscay
eoplepay, omwhay Iyay oday otnay owknay; astenhay, enthay, ymay earday iendfray, otay eturnray,
atthay Iyay aymay againyay eelfay yselfmay omewhatsay atyay omehay, ichwhay Iyay annotcay oday inyay
youryay absenceyay.”

Avinghay artedpay omfray ymay iendfray, Iyay eterminedday otay isitvay omesay emoteray otspay ofyay
Otlandscay andyay inishfay ymay orkway inyay olitudesay. Iyay idday otnay oubtday utbay atthay ethay
onstermay ollowedfay emay andyay ouldway iscoverday imselfhay otay emay enwhay Iyay ouldshay avehay
inishedfay, atthay ehay ightmay eceiveray ishay ompanioncay.

Ithway isthay esolutionray Iyay aversedtray ethay orthernnay ighlandshay andyay ixedfay onyay oneyay ofyay
ethay emotestray ofyay ethay Orkneysyay asyay ethay enescay ofyay ymay abourslay. Ityay asway ayay aceplay
ittedfay orfay uchsay ayay orkway, eingbay ardlyhay oremay anthay ayay ockray osewhay ighhay idessay ereway
ontinuallycay eatenbay uponyay ybay ethay avesway. Ethay oilsay asway arrenbay, arcelyscay
affordingyay asturepay orfay ayay ewfay iserablemay owscay, andyay oatmealyay orfay itsyay
inhabitantsyay, ichwhay onsistedcay ofyay ivefay ersonspay, osewhay auntgay andyay aggyscray imbslay
avegay okenstay ofyay eirthay iserablemay arefay. Egetablesvay andyay eadbray, enwhay eythay
indulgedyay inyay uchsay uxurieslay, andyay evenyay eshfray aterway, asway otay ebay ocuredpray omfray
ethay ainlandmay, ichwhay asway aboutyay ivefay ilesmay istantday.

Onyay ethay olewhay islandyay erethay ereway utbay eethray iserablemay utshay, andyay oneyay ofyay
esethay asway acantvay enwhay Iyay arrivedyay. Isthay Iyay iredhay. Ityay ontainedcay utbay otway
oomsray, andyay esethay exhibitedyay allyay ethay ualidnesssqay ofyay ethay ostmay iserablemay
enurypay. Ethay atchthay adhay allenfay inyay, ethay allsway ereway unplasteredyay, andyay ethay
oorday asway offyay itsyay ingeshay. Iyay orderedyay ityay otay ebay epairedray, oughtbay omesay
urniturefay, andyay ooktay ossessionpay, anyay incidentyay ichwhay ouldway oubtlessday avehay
occasionedyay omesay urprisesay adhay otnay allyay ethay ensessay ofyay ethay ottagerscay eenbay
enumbedbay ybay antway andyay ualidsqay overtypay. Asyay ityay asway, Iyay ivedlay ungazedyay atyay
andyay unmolestedyay, ardlyhay ankedthay orfay ethay ittancepay ofyay oodfay andyay othesclay
ichwhay Iyay avegay, osay uchmay oesday ufferingsay untblay evenyay ethay oarsestcay ensationssay
ofyay enmay.

Inyay isthay etreatray Iyay evotedday ethay orningmay otay abourlay; utbay inyay ethay eveningyay,
enwhay ethay eatherway ermittedpay, Iyay alkedway onyay ethay onystay eachbay ofyay ethay easay otay
istenlay otay ethay avesway asyay eythay oaredray andyay ashedday atyay ymay eetfay. Ityay asway ayay
onotonousmay yetyay ever-changingyay enescay. Iyay oughtthay ofyay Itzerlandsway; ityay asway
arfay ifferentday omfray isthay esolateday andyay appallingyay andscapelay. Itsyay illshay
areyay overedcay ithway inesvay, andyay itsyay ottagescay areyay atteredscay icklythay inyay ethay
ainsplay. Itsyay airfay akeslay eflectray ayay ueblay andyay entlegay yskay, andyay enwhay
oubledtray ybay ethay indsway, eirthay umulttay isyay utbay asyay ethay ayplay ofyay ayay ivelylay
infantyay enwhay omparedcay otay ethay oaringsray ofyay ethay iantgay oceanyay.

Inyay isthay annermay Iyay istributedday ymay occupationsyay enwhay Iyay irstfay arrivedyay, utbay
asyay Iyay oceededpray inyay ymay abourlay, ityay ecamebay everyyay ayday oremay orriblehay andyay
irksomeyay otay emay. Ometimessay Iyay ouldcay otnay evailpray onyay yselfmay otay enteryay ymay
aboratorylay orfay everalsay aysday, andyay atyay otheryay imestay Iyay oiledtay ayday andyay ightnay
inyay orderyay otay ompletecay ymay orkway. Ityay asway, indeedyay, ayay ilthyfay ocesspray inyay
ichwhay Iyay asway engagedyay. Uringday ymay irstfay experimentyay, ayay indkay ofyay
enthusiasticyay enzyfray adhay indedblay emay otay ethay orrorhay ofyay ymay employmentyay; ymay
indmay asway intentlyyay ixedfay onyay ethay onsummationcay ofyay ymay abourlay, andyay ymay eyesyay
ereway utshay otay ethay orrorhay ofyay ymay oceedingspray. Utbay ownay Iyay entway otay ityay inyay
oldcay oodblay, andyay ymay earthay oftenyay ickenedsay atyay ethay orkway ofyay ymay andshay.

Usthay ituatedsay, employedyay inyay ethay ostmay etestableday occupationyay, immersedyay inyay
ayay olitudesay erewhay othingnay ouldcay orfay anyay instantyay allcay ymay attentionyay omfray
ethay actualyay enescay inyay ichwhay Iyay asway engagedyay, ymay iritsspay ecamebay unequalyay; Iyay
ewgray estlessray andyay ervousnay. Everyyay omentmay Iyay earedfay otay eetmay ymay
ersecutorpay. Ometimessay Iyay atsay ithway ymay eyesyay ixedfay onyay ethay oundgray, earingfay
otay aiseray emthay estlay eythay ouldshay encounteryay ethay objectyay ichwhay Iyay osay uchmay
eadeddray otay eholdbay. Iyay earedfay otay anderway omfray ethay ightsay ofyay ymay ellowfay
eaturescray estlay enwhay aloneyay ehay ouldshay omecay otay aimclay ishay ompanioncay.

Inyay ethay eanmay imetay Iyay orkedway onyay, andyay ymay abourlay asway alreadyyay onsiderablycay
advancedyay. Iyay ookedlay owardstay itsyay ompletioncay ithway ayay emuloustray andyay eageryay
opehay, ichwhay Iyay aredday otnay usttray yselfmay otay uestionqay utbay ichwhay asway
intermixedyay ithway obscureyay orebodingsfay ofyay evilyay atthay ademay ymay earthay ickensay
inyay ymay osombay.




Apterchay 20


Iyay atsay oneyay eveningyay inyay ymay aboratorylay; ethay unsay adhay etsay, andyay ethay oonmay asway ustjay
isingray omfray ethay easay; Iyay adhay otnay ufficientsay ightlay orfay ymay employmentyay, andyay Iyay
emainedray idleyay, inyay ayay ausepay ofyay onsiderationcay ofyay etherwhay Iyay ouldshay eavelay ymay
abourlay orfay ethay ightnay oryay astenhay itsyay onclusioncay ybay anyay unremittingyay attentionyay
otay ityay. Asyay Iyay atsay, ayay aintray ofyay eflectionray occurredyay otay emay ichwhay edlay emay otay
onsidercay ethay effectsyay ofyay atwhay Iyay asway ownay oingday. Eethray yearsyay eforebay, Iyay asway
engagedyay inyay ethay amesay annermay andyay adhay eatedcray ayay iendfay osewhay unparalleledyay
arbaritybay adhay esolatedday ymay earthay andyay illedfay ityay orfay everyay ithway ethay itterestbay
emorseray. Iyay asway ownay aboutyay otay ormfay anotheryay eingbay ofyay osewhay ispositionsday Iyay asway
alikeyay ignorantyay; eshay ightmay ecomebay entay ousandthay imestay oremay alignantmay anthay erhay
atemay andyay elightday, orfay itsyay ownyay akesay, inyay urdermay andyay etchednesswray. Ehay adhay
ornsway otay uitqay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay anmay andyay idehay imselfhay inyay esertsday, utbay eshay
adhay otnay; andyay eshay, owhay inyay allyay obabilitypray asway otay ecomebay ayay inkingthay andyay
easoningray animalyay, ightmay efuseray otay omplycay ithway ayay ompactcay ademay eforebay erhay
eationcray. Eythay ightmay evenyay atehay eachyay otheryay; ethay eaturecray owhay alreadyyay ivedlay
oathedlay ishay ownyay eformityday, andyay ightmay ehay otnay onceivecay ayay eatergray abhorrenceyay
orfay ityay enwhay ityay amecay eforebay ishay eyesyay inyay ethay emalefay ormfay? Eshay alsoyay ightmay urntay
ithway isgustday omfray imhay otay ethay uperiorsay eautybay ofyay anmay; eshay ightmay uitqay imhay,
andyay ehay ebay againyay aloneyay, exasperatedyay ybay ethay eshfray ovocationpray ofyay eingbay
esertedday ybay oneyay ofyay ishay ownyay eciesspay.

Evenyay ifyay eythay ereway otay eavelay Europeyay andyay inhabityay ethay esertsday ofyay ethay ewnay orldway,
yetyay oneyay ofyay ethay irstfay esultsray ofyay osethay ympathiessay orfay ichwhay ethay ondæmay
irstedthay ouldway ebay ildrenchay, andyay ayay aceray ofyay evilsday ouldway ebay opagatedpray uponyay
ethay earthyay owhay ightmay akemay ethay eryvay existenceyay ofyay ethay eciesspay ofyay anmay ayay
onditioncay ecariouspray andyay ullfay ofyay errortay. Adhay Iyay ightray, orfay ymay ownyay enefitbay,
otay inflictyay isthay ursecay uponyay everlastingyay enerationsgay? Iyay adhay eforebay eenbay ovedmay
ybay ethay ophismssay ofyay ethay eingbay Iyay adhay eatedcray; Iyay adhay eenbay uckstray enselesssay ybay
ishay iendishfay eatsthray; utbay ownay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, ethay ickednessway ofyay ymay
omisepray urstbay uponyay emay; Iyay udderedshay otay inkthay atthay uturefay agesyay ightmay ursecay emay
asyay eirthay estpay, osewhay elfishnesssay adhay otnay esitatedhay otay uybay itsyay ownyay eacepay atyay
ethay icepray, erhapspay, ofyay ethay existenceyay ofyay ethay olewhay umanhay aceray.

Iyay embledtray andyay ymay earthay ailedfay ithinway emay, enwhay, onyay ookinglay upyay, Iyay awsay ybay
ethay ightlay ofyay ethay oonmay ethay ondæmay atyay ethay asementcay. Ayay astlyghay ingray
inkledwray ishay ipslay asyay ehay azedgay onyay emay, erewhay Iyay atsay ulfillingfay ethay asktay
ichwhay ehay adhay allottedyay otay emay. Yesyay, ehay adhay ollowedfay emay inyay ymay avelstray; ehay
adhay oiteredlay inyay orestsfay, idhay imselfhay inyay avescay, oryay akentay efugeray inyay ideway
andyay esertday eathshay; andyay ehay ownay amecay otay arkmay ymay ogresspray andyay aimclay ethay
ulfilmentfay ofyay ymay omisepray.

Asyay Iyay ookedlay onyay imhay, ishay ountenancecay expressedyay ethay utmostyay extentyay ofyay
alicemay andyay eacherytray. Iyay oughtthay ithway ayay ensationsay ofyay adnessmay onyay ymay
omisepray ofyay eatingcray anotheryay ikelay otay imhay, andyay emblingtray ithway assionpay,
oretay otay iecespay ethay ingthay onyay ichwhay Iyay asway engagedyay. Ethay etchwray awsay emay
estroyday ethay eaturecray onyay osewhay uturefay existenceyay ehay ependedday orfay
appinesshay, andyay ithway ayay owlhay ofyay evilishday espairday andyay evengeray, ithdrewway.

Iyay eftlay ethay oomray, andyay ockinglay ethay oorday, ademay ayay olemnsay owvay inyay ymay ownyay
earthay evernay otay esumeray ymay abourslay; andyay enthay, ithway emblingtray epsstay, Iyay
oughtsay ymay ownyay apartmentyay. Iyay asway aloneyay; onenay ereway earnay emay otay issipateday
ethay oomglay andyay elieveray emay omfray ethay ickeningsay oppressionyay ofyay ethay ostmay
erribletay everiesray.

Everalsay ourshay assedpay, andyay Iyay emainedray earnay ymay indowway azinggay onyay ethay easay;
ityay asway almostyay otionlessmay, orfay ethay indsway ereway ushedhay, andyay allyay aturenay
eposedray underyay ethay eyeyay ofyay ethay uietqay oonmay. Ayay ewfay ishingfay esselsvay aloneyay
eckedspay ethay aterway, andyay ownay andyay enthay ethay entlegay eezebray aftedway ethay oundsay
ofyay oicesvay asyay ethay ishermenfay alledcay otay oneyay anotheryay. Iyay eltfay ethay ilencesay,
althoughyay Iyay asway ardlyhay onsciouscay ofyay itsyay extremeyay ofunditypray, untilyay ymay earyay
asway uddenlysay arrestedyay ybay ethay addlingpay ofyay oarsyay earnay ethay oreshay, andyay ayay
ersonpay andedlay oseclay otay ymay ousehay.

Inyay ayay ewfay inutesmay afteryay, Iyay eardhay ethay eakingcray ofyay ymay oorday, asyay ifyay omesay oneyay
endeavouredyay otay openyay ityay oftlysay. Iyay embledtray omfray eadhay otay ootfay; Iyay eltfay ayay
esentimentpray ofyay owhay ityay asway andyay ishedway otay ouseray oneyay ofyay ethay easantspay owhay
eltdway inyay ayay ottagecay otnay arfay omfray inemay; utbay Iyay asway overcomeyay ybay ethay ensationsay
ofyay elplessnesshay, osay oftenyay eltfay inyay ightfulfray eamsdray, enwhay youyay inyay ainvay
endeavouryay otay yflay omfray anyay impendingyay angerday, andyay asway ootedray otay ethay otspay.

Esentlypray Iyay eardhay ethay oundsay ofyay ootstepsfay alongyay ethay assagepay; ethay oorday
openedyay, andyay ethay etchwray omwhay Iyay eadeddray appearedyay. Uttingshay ethay oorday, ehay
approachedyay emay andyay aidsay inyay ayay otheredsmay oicevay,

you“ay avehay estroyedday ethay orkway ichwhay youyay eganbay; atwhay isyay ityay atthay youyay
intendyay? Oday youyay areday otay eakbray youryay omisepray? Iyay avehay enduredyay oiltay andyay iserymay;
Iyay eftlay Itzerlandsway ithway youyay; Iyay eptcray alongyay ethay oresshay ofyay ethay Inerhay, amongyay
itsyay illowway islandsyay andyay overyay ethay ummitssay ofyay itsyay illshay. Iyay avehay eltdway anymay
onthsmay inyay ethay eathshay ofyay Englandyay andyay amongyay ethay esertsday ofyay Otlandscay. Iyay avehay
enduredyay incalculableyay atiguefay, andyay oldcay, andyay ungerhay; oday youyay areday estroyday ymay
opeshay?”

egone“bay! Iyay oday eakbray ymay omisepray; evernay illway Iyay eatecray anotheryay ikelay
yourselfyay, equalyay inyay eformityday andyay ickednessway.”

ave“slay, Iyay eforebay easonedray ithway youyay, utbay youyay avehay ovedpray yourselfyay
unworthyyay ofyay ymay ondescensioncay. Ememberray atthay Iyay avehay owerpay; youyay elievebay
yourselfyay iserablemay, utbay Iyay ancay akemay youyay osay etchedwray atthay ethay ightlay ofyay
ayday illway ebay atefulhay otay youyay. Youyay areyay ymay eatorcray, utbay Iyay amyay youryay astermay;
obeyyay!”

e“thay ourhay ofyay ymay irresolutionyay isyay astpay, andyay ethay eriodpay ofyay youryay owerpay isyay
arrivedyay. Youryay eatsthray annotcay ovemay emay otay oday anyay actyay ofyay ickednessway; utbay
eythay onfirmcay emay inyay ayay eterminationday ofyay otnay eatingcray youyay ayay ompanioncay inyay
icevay. Allshay Iyay, inyay oolcay oodblay, etsay ooselay uponyay ethay earthyay ayay ondæmay osewhay
elightday isyay inyay eathday andyay etchednesswray? Egonebay! Iyay amyay irmfay, andyay youryay
ordsway illway onlyyay exasperateyay ymay ageray.”

Ethay onstermay awsay ymay eterminationday inyay ymay acefay andyay ashedgnay ishay eethtay inyay ethay
impotenceyay ofyay angeryay. all“shay eachyay anmay,” iedcray ehay, ind“fay ayay
ifeway orfay ishay osombay, andyay eachyay eastbay avehay ishay atemay, andyay Iyay ebay aloneyay? Iyay adhay
eelingsfay ofyay affectionyay, andyay eythay ereway equitedray ybay etestationday andyay ornscay.
Anmay! Youyay aymay atehay, utbay ewarebay! Youryay ourshay illway asspay inyay eaddray andyay iserymay,
andyay oonsay ethay oltbay illway allfay ichwhay ustmay avishray omfray youyay youryay appinesshay orfay
everyay. Areyay youyay otay ebay appyhay ilewhay Iyay ovelgray inyay ethay intensityyay ofyay ymay
etchednesswray? Youyay ancay astblay ymay otheryay assionspay, utbay evengeray
emains—revengeray, enceforthhay earerday anthay ightlay oryay oodfay! Iyay aymay ieday, utbay
irstfay youyay, ymay yranttay andyay ormentortay, allshay ursecay ethay unsay atthay azesgay onyay youryay
iserymay. Ewarebay, orfay Iyay amyay earlessfay andyay ereforethay owerfulpay. Iyay illway atchway ithway
ethay ilinessway ofyay ayay akesnay, atthay Iyay aymay ingstay ithway itsyay enomvay. Anmay, youyay allshay
epentray ofyay ethay injuriesyay youyay inflictyay.”

evil“day, easecay; andyay oday otnay oisonpay ethay airyay ithway esethay oundssay ofyay alicemay.
Iyay avehay eclaredday ymay esolutionray otay youyay, andyay Iyay amyay onay owardcay otay endbay
eneathbay ordsway. Eavelay emay; Iyay amyay inexorableyay.”

it“ay isyay ellway. Iyay ogay; utbay ememberray, Iyay allshay ebay ithway youyay onyay youryay
edding-nightway.”

Iyay artedstay orwardfay andyay exclaimedyay, illain“vay! Eforebay youyay ignsay ymay
eath-warrantday, ebay uresay atthay youyay areyay yourselfyay afesay.”

Iyay ouldway avehay eizedsay imhay, utbay ehay eludedyay emay andyay uittedqay ethay ousehay ithway
ecipitationpray. Inyay ayay ewfay omentsmay Iyay awsay imhay inyay ishay oatbay, ichwhay otshay
acrossyay ethay atersway ithway anyay arrowyyay iftnesssway andyay asway oonsay ostlay amidstyay ethay
avesway.

Allyay asway againyay ilentsay, utbay ishay ordsway angray inyay ymay earsyay. Iyay urnedbay ithway ageray otay
ursuepay ethay urderermay ofyay ymay eacepay andyay ecipitatepray imhay intoyay ethay oceanyay. Iyay
alkedway upyay andyay ownday ymay oomray astilyhay andyay erturbedpay, ilewhay ymay imaginationyay
onjuredcay upyay ayay ousandthay imagesyay otay ormenttay andyay ingstay emay. Ywhay adhay Iyay otnay
ollowedfay imhay andyay osedclay ithway imhay inyay ortalmay ifestray? Utbay Iyay adhay ufferedsay imhay
otay epartday, andyay ehay adhay irectedday ishay oursecay owardstay ethay ainlandmay. Iyay udderedshay
otay inkthay owhay ightmay ebay ethay extnay ictimvay acrificedsay otay ishay insatiateyay evengeray.
Andyay enthay Iyay oughtthay againyay ofyay ishay ords—“_iway illway ebay ithway youyay onyay
youryay edding-nightway._” Atthay, enthay, asway ethay eriodpay ixedfay orfay ethay
ulfilmentfay ofyay ymay estinyday. Inyay atthay ourhay Iyay ouldshay ieday andyay atyay onceyay atisfysay andyay
extinguishyay ishay alicemay. Ethay ospectpray idday otnay ovemay emay otay earfay; yetyay enwhay Iyay
oughtthay ofyay ymay elovedbay Elizabethyay, ofyay erhay earstay andyay endlessyay orrowsay, enwhay eshay
ouldshay indfay erhay overlay osay arbarouslybay atchedsnay omfray erhay, earstay, ethay irstfay Iyay
adhay edshay orfay anymay onthsmay, eamedstray omfray ymay eyesyay, andyay Iyay esolvedray otnay otay allfay
eforebay ymay enemyyay ithoutway ayay itterbay ugglestray.

Ethay ightnay assedpay awayyay, andyay ethay unsay oseray omfray ethay oceanyay; ymay eelingsfay ecamebay
almercay, ifyay ityay aymay ebay alledcay almnesscay enwhay ethay iolencevay ofyay ageray inkssay intoyay
ethay epthsday ofyay espairday. Iyay eftlay ethay ousehay, ethay orridhay enescay ofyay ethay astlay
ight’snay ontentioncay, andyay alkedway onyay ethay eachbay ofyay ethay easay, ichwhay Iyay
almostyay egardedray asyay anyay insuperableyay arrierbay etweenbay emay andyay ymay ellowfay
eaturescray; aynay, ayay ishway atthay uchsay ouldshay ovepray ethay actfay olestay acrossyay emay. Iyay
esiredday atthay Iyay ightmay asspay ymay ifelay onyay atthay arrenbay ockray, earilyway, ityay isyay uetray,
utbay uninterruptedyay ybay anyyay uddensay ockshay ofyay iserymay. Ifyay Iyay eturnedray, ityay asway otay
ebay acrificedsay oryay otay eesay osethay omwhay Iyay ostmay ovedlay ieday underyay ethay aspgray ofyay ayay
ondæmay omwhay Iyay adhay yselfmay eatedcray.

Iyay alkedway aboutyay ethay isleyay ikelay ayay estlessray ectrespay, eparatedsay omfray allyay ityay
ovedlay andyay iserablemay inyay ethay eparationsay. Enwhay ityay ecamebay oonnay, andyay ethay
unsay oseray igherhay, Iyay aylay ownday onyay ethay assgray andyay asway overpoweredyay ybay ayay eepday
eepslay. Iyay adhay eenbay awakeyay ethay olewhay ofyay ethay ecedingpray ightnay, ymay ervesnay
ereway agitatedyay, andyay ymay eyesyay inflamedyay ybay atchingway andyay iserymay. Ethay eepslay
intoyay ichwhay Iyay ownay anksay efreshedray emay; andyay enwhay Iyay awokeyay, Iyay againyay eltfay asyay
ifyay Iyay elongedbay otay ayay aceray ofyay umanhay eingsbay ikelay yselfmay, andyay Iyay eganbay otay
eflectray uponyay atwhay adhay assedpay ithway eatergray omposurecay; yetyay illstay ethay
ordsway ofyay ethay iendfay angray inyay ymay earsyay ikelay ayay eath-knellday; eythay appearedyay
ikelay ayay eamdray, yetyay istinctday andyay oppressiveyay asyay ayay ealityray.

Ethay unsay adhay arfay escendedday, andyay Iyay illstay atsay onyay ethay oreshay, atisfyingsay ymay
appetiteyay, ichwhay adhay ecomebay avenousray, ithway anyay oatenyay akecay, enwhay Iyay awsay ayay
ishing-boatfay andlay oseclay otay emay, andyay oneyay ofyay ethay enmay oughtbray emay ayay acketpay;
ityay ontainedcay etterslay omfray Enevagay, andyay oneyay omfray Ervalclay entreatingyay emay otay
oinjay imhay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay asway earingway awayyay ishay imetay uitlesslyfray erewhay
ehay asway, atthay etterslay omfray ethay iendsfray ehay adhay ormedfay inyay Ondonlay esiredday
ishay eturnray otay ompletecay ethay egotiationnay eythay adhay enteredyay intoyay orfay ishay
Indianyay enterpriseyay. Ehay ouldcay otnay anyyay ongerlay elayday ishay epartureday; utbay asyay
ishay ourneyjay otay Ondonlay ightmay ebay ollowedfay, evenyay oonersay anthay ehay ownay
onjecturedcay, ybay ishay ongerlay oyagevay, ehay entreatedyay emay otay estowbay asyay uchmay ofyay
ymay ocietysay onyay imhay asyay Iyay ouldcay arespay. Ehay esoughtbay emay, ereforethay, otay
eavelay ymay olitarysay isleyay andyay otay eetmay imhay atyay Erthpay, atthay eway ightmay oceedpray
outhwardssay ogethertay. Isthay etterlay inyay ayay egreeday ecalledray emay otay ifelay, andyay
Iyay eterminedday otay uitqay ymay islandyay atyay ethay expirationyay ofyay otway aysday.

Yetyay, eforebay Iyay epartedday, erethay asway ayay asktay otay erformpay, onyay ichwhay Iyay udderedshay
otay eflectray; Iyay ustmay ackpay upyay ymay emicalchay instrumentsyay, andyay orfay atthay urposepay Iyay
ustmay enteryay ethay oomray ichwhay adhay eenbay ethay enescay ofyay ymay odiousyay orkway, andyay Iyay ustmay
andlehay osethay utensilsyay ethay ightsay ofyay ichwhay asway ickeningsay otay emay. Ethay extnay
orningmay, atyay aybreakday, Iyay ummonedsay ufficientsay ouragecay andyay unlockedyay ethay oorday
ofyay ymay aboratorylay. Ethay emainsray ofyay ethay alf-finishedhay eaturecray, omwhay Iyay adhay
estroyedday, aylay atteredscay onyay ethay oorflay, andyay Iyay almostyay eltfay asyay ifyay Iyay adhay
angledmay ethay ivinglay eshflay ofyay ayay umanhay eingbay. Iyay ausedpay otay ollectcay yselfmay andyay
enthay enteredyay ethay amberchay. Ithway emblingtray andhay Iyay onveyedcay ethay instrumentsyay
outyay ofyay ethay oomray, utbay Iyay eflectedray atthay Iyay oughtyay otnay otay eavelay ethay elicsray ofyay ymay
orkway otay exciteyay ethay orrorhay andyay uspicionsay ofyay ethay easantspay; andyay Iyay accordinglyyay
utpay emthay intoyay ayay asketbay, ithway ayay eatgray uantityqay ofyay onesstay, andyay ayinglay emthay
upyay, eterminedday otay owthray emthay intoyay ethay easay atthay eryvay ightnay; andyay inyay ethay
eantimemay Iyay atsay uponyay ethay eachbay, employedyay inyay eaningclay andyay arrangingyay ymay
emicalchay apparatusyay.

Othingnay ouldcay ebay oremay ompletecay anthay ethay alterationyay atthay adhay akentay aceplay
inyay ymay eelingsfay incesay ethay ightnay ofyay ethay appearanceyay ofyay ethay ondæmay. Iyay adhay
eforebay egardedray ymay omisepray ithway ayay oomyglay espairday asyay ayay ingthay atthay, ithway
ateverwhay onsequencescay, ustmay ebay ulfilledfay; utbay Iyay ownay eltfay asyay ifyay ayay ilmfay
adhay eenbay akentay omfray eforebay ymay eyesyay andyay atthay Iyay orfay ethay irstfay imetay awsay
earlyclay. Ethay ideayay ofyay enewingray ymay abourslay idday otnay orfay oneyay instantyay occuryay
otay emay; ethay eatthray Iyay adhay eardhay eighedway onyay ymay oughtsthay, utbay Iyay idday otnay
eflectray atthay ayay oluntaryvay actyay ofyay inemay ouldcay avertyay ityay. Iyay adhay esolvedray inyay
ymay ownyay indmay atthay otay eatecray anotheryay ikelay ethay iendfay Iyay adhay irstfay ademay
ouldway ebay anyay actyay ofyay ethay asestbay andyay ostmay atrociousyay elfishnesssay, andyay Iyay
anishedbay omfray ymay indmay everyyay oughtthay atthay ouldcay eadlay otay ayay ifferentday
onclusioncay.

Etweenbay otway andyay eethray inyay ethay orningmay ethay oonmay oseray; andyay Iyay enthay, uttingpay ymay
asketbay aboardyay ayay ittlelay iffskay, ailedsay outyay aboutyay ourfay ilesmay omfray ethay oreshay.
Ethay enescay asway erfectlypay olitarysay; ayay ewfay oatsbay ereway eturningray owardstay andlay,
utbay Iyay ailedsay awayyay omfray emthay. Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay Iyay asway aboutyay ethay ommissioncay ofyay ayay
eadfuldray imecray andyay avoidedyay ithway udderingshay anxietyyay anyyay encounteryay ithway ymay
ellowfay eaturescray. Atyay oneyay imetay ethay oonmay, ichwhay adhay eforebay eenbay earclay, asway
uddenlysay overspreadyay ybay ayay ickthay oudclay, andyay Iyay ooktay advantageyay ofyay ethay omentmay ofyay
arknessday andyay astcay ymay asketbay intoyay ethay easay; Iyay istenedlay otay ethay urglinggay oundsay
asyay ityay anksay andyay enthay ailedsay awayyay omfray ethay otspay. Ethay yskay ecamebay oudedclay, utbay
ethay airyay asway urepay, althoughyay illedchay ybay ethay ortheastnay eezebray atthay asway enthay
isingray. Utbay ityay efreshedray emay andyay illedfay emay ithway uchsay agreeableyay ensationssay
atthay Iyay esolvedray otay olongpray ymay aystay onyay ethay aterway, andyay ixingfay ethay udderray inyay ayay
irectday ositionpay, etchedstray yselfmay atyay ethay ottombay ofyay ethay oatbay. Oudsclay idhay ethay
oonmay, everythingyay asway obscureyay, andyay Iyay eardhay onlyyay ethay oundsay ofyay ethay oatbay asyay itsyay
eelkay utcay oughthray ethay avesway; ethay urmurmay ulledlay emay, andyay inyay ayay ortshay imetay Iyay
eptslay oundlysay.

Iyay oday otnay owknay owhay onglay Iyay emainedray inyay isthay ituationsay, utbay enwhay Iyay awokeyay Iyay
oundfay atthay ethay unsay adhay alreadyyay ountedmay onsiderablycay. Ethay indway asway ighhay, andyay
ethay avesway ontinuallycay eatenedthray ethay afetysay ofyay ymay ittlelay iffskay. Iyay oundfay
atthay ethay indway asway ortheastnay andyay ustmay avehay ivendray emay arfay omfray ethay oastcay omfray
ichwhay Iyay adhay embarkedyay. Iyay endeavouredyay otay angechay ymay oursecay utbay uicklyqay oundfay
atthay ifyay Iyay againyay ademay ethay attemptyay ethay oatbay ouldway ebay instantlyyay illedfay ithway
aterway. Usthay ituatedsay, ymay onlyyay esourceray asway otay ivedray eforebay ethay indway. Iyay
onfesscay atthay Iyay eltfay ayay ewfay ensationssay ofyay errortay. Iyay adhay onay ompasscay ithway emay
andyay asway osay enderlyslay acquaintedyay ithway ethay eographygay ofyay isthay artpay ofyay ethay
orldway atthay ethay unsay asway ofyay ittlelay enefitbay otay emay. Iyay ightmay ebay ivendray intoyay ethay
ideway Atlanticyay andyay eelfay allyay ethay orturestay ofyay arvationstay oryay ebay allowedsway upyay inyay
ethay immeasurableyay atersway atthay oaredray andyay uffetedbay aroundyay emay. Iyay adhay alreadyyay
eenbay outyay anymay ourshay andyay eltfay ethay ormenttay ofyay ayay urningbay irstthay, ayay eludepray otay
ymay otheryay ufferingssay. Iyay ookedlay onyay ethay eavenshay, ichwhay ereway overedcay ybay oudsclay
atthay ewflay eforebay ethay indway, onlyyay otay ebay eplacedray ybay othersyay; Iyay ookedlay uponyay ethay
easay; ityay asway otay ebay ymay avegray. iend“fay,” Iyay exclaimedyay, your“ay
asktay isyay alreadyyay ulfilledfay!” Iyay oughtthay ofyay Elizabethyay, ofyay ymay atherfay, andyay
ofyay Erval—allclay eftlay ehindbay, onyay omwhay ethay onstermay ightmay atisfysay ishay
anguinarysay andyay ercilessmay assionspay. Isthay ideayay ungedplay emay intoyay ayay everieray osay
espairingday andyay ightfulfray atthay evenyay ownay, enwhay ethay enescay isyay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay
osingclay eforebay emay orfay everyay, Iyay uddershay otay eflectray onyay ityay.

Omesay ourshay assedpay usthay; utbay ybay egreesday, asyay ethay unsay eclinedday owardstay ethay
orizonhay, ethay indway iedday awayyay intoyay ayay entlegay eezebray andyay ethay easay ecamebay
eefray omfray eakersbray. Utbay esethay avegay aceplay otay ayay eavyhay ellsway; Iyay eltfay icksay
andyay ardlyhay ableyay otay oldhay ethay udderray, enwhay uddenlysay Iyay awsay ayay inelay ofyay ighhay
andlay owardstay ethay outhsay.

Almostyay entspay, asyay Iyay asway, ybay atiguefay andyay ethay eadfuldray uspensesay Iyay enduredyay
orfay everalsay ourshay, isthay uddensay ertaintycay ofyay ifelay ushedray ikelay ayay oodflay ofyay
armway oyjay otay ymay earthay, andyay earstay ushedgay omfray ymay eyesyay.

Owhay utablemay areyay ouryay eelingsfay, andyay owhay angestray isyay atthay ingingclay ovelay eway avehay
ofyay ifelay evenyay inyay ethay excessyay ofyay iserymay! Iyay onstructedcay anotheryay ailsay ithway ayay
artpay ofyay ymay essdray andyay eagerlyyay eeredstay ymay oursecay owardstay ethay andlay. Ityay adhay ayay
ildway andyay ockyray appearanceyay, utbay asyay Iyay approachedyay earernay Iyay easilyyay erceivedpay
ethay acestray ofyay ultivationcay. Iyay awsay esselsvay earnay ethay oreshay andyay oundfay yselfmay
uddenlysay ansportedtray ackbay otay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofyay ivilisedcay anmay. Iyay
arefullycay acedtray ethay indingsway ofyay ethay andlay andyay ailedhay ayay eeplestay ichwhay Iyay atyay
engthlay awsay issuingyay omfray ehindbay ayay allsmay omontorypray. Asyay Iyay asway inyay ayay atestay ofyay
extremeyay ebilityday, Iyay esolvedray otay ailsay irectlyday owardstay ethay owntay, asyay ayay aceplay
erewhay Iyay ouldcay ostmay easilyyay ocurepray ourishmentnay. Ortunatelyfay Iyay adhay oneymay ithway
emay. Asyay Iyay urnedtay ethay omontorypray Iyay erceivedpay ayay allsmay eatnay owntay andyay ayay oodgay
arbourhay, ichwhay Iyay enteredyay, ymay earthay oundingbay ithway oyjay atyay ymay unexpectedyay
escapeyay.

Asyay Iyay asway occupiedyay inyay ixingfay ethay oatbay andyay arrangingyay ethay ailssay, everalsay
eoplepay owdedcray owardstay ethay otspay. Eythay eemedsay uchmay urprisedsay atyay ymay
appearanceyay, utbay insteadyay ofyay offeringyay emay anyyay assistanceyay, isperedwhay
ogethertay ithway esturesgay atthay atyay anyyay otheryay imetay ightmay avehay oducedpray inyay emay
ayay ightslay ensationsay ofyay alarmyay. Asyay ityay asway, Iyay erelymay emarkedray atthay eythay
okespay Englishyay, andyay Iyay ereforethay addressedyay emthay inyay atthay anguagelay. y“may
oodgay iendsfray,” aidsay Iyay, ill“way youyay ebay osay indkay asyay otay elltay emay ethay amenay ofyay
isthay owntay andyay informyay emay erewhay Iyay amyay?”

you“ay illway owknay atthay oonsay enoughyay,” epliedray ayay anmay ithway ayay oarsehay oicevay.
aybe“may youyay areyay omecay otay ayay aceplay atthay illway otnay ovepray uchmay otay youryay astetay,
utbay youyay illway otnay ebay onsultedcay asyay otay youryay uartersqay, Iyay omisepray youyay.”

Iyay asway exceedinglyyay urprisedsay onyay eceivingray osay uderay anyay answeryay omfray ayay
angerstray, andyay Iyay asway alsoyay isconcertedday onyay erceivingpay ethay owningfray andyay
angryyay ountenancescay ofyay ishay ompanionscay. y“whay oday youyay answeryay emay osay
oughlyray?” Iyay epliedray. urely“say ityay isyay otnay ethay ustomcay ofyay Englishmenyay otay
eceiveray angersstray osay inhospitablyyay.”

i“ay oday otnay owknay,” aidsay ethay anmay, at“whay ethay ustomcay ofyay ethay
Englishyay aymay ebay, utbay ityay isyay ethay ustomcay ofyay ethay Irishyay otay atehay illainsvay.”

Ilewhay isthay angestray ialogueday ontinuedcay, Iyay erceivedpay ethay owdcray apidlyray
increaseyay. Eirthay acesfay expressedyay ayay ixturemay ofyay uriositycay andyay angeryay, ichwhay
annoyedyay andyay inyay omesay egreeday alarmedyay emay. Iyay inquiredyay ethay ayway otay ethay innyay, utbay
onay oneyay epliedray. Iyay enthay ovedmay orwardfay, andyay ayay urmuringmay oundsay aroseyay omfray ethay
owdcray asyay eythay ollowedfay andyay urroundedsay emay, enwhay anyay ill-lookingyay anmay
approachingyay appedtay emay onyay ethay ouldershay andyay aidsay, ome“cay, irsay, youyay ustmay
ollowfay emay otay Mray. Irwin’skay otay ivegay anyay accountyay ofyay yourselfyay.”

o“whay isyay Mray. Irwinkay? Ywhay amyay Iyay otay ivegay anyay accountyay ofyay yselfmay? Isyay otnay
isthay ayay eefray ountrycay?”

ay“ay, irsay, eefray enoughyay orfay onesthay olksfay. Mray. Irwinkay isyay ayay agistratemay,
andyay youyay areyay otay ivegay anyay accountyay ofyay ethay eathday ofyay ayay entlemangay owhay asway
oundfay urderedmay erehay astlay ightnay.”

Isthay answeryay artledstay emay, utbay Iyay esentlypray ecoveredray yselfmay. Iyay asway innocentyay;
atthay ouldcay easilyyay ebay ovedpray; accordinglyyay Iyay ollowedfay ymay onductorcay inyay ilencesay
andyay asway edlay otay oneyay ofyay ethay estbay ouseshay inyay ethay owntay. Iyay asway eadyray otay inksay omfray
atiguefay andyay ungerhay, utbay eingbay urroundedsay ybay ayay owdcray, Iyay oughtthay ityay oliticpay
otay ouseray allyay ymay engthstray, atthay onay ysicalphay ebilityday ightmay ebay onstruedcay intoyay
apprehensionyay oryay onsciouscay uiltgay. Ittlelay idday Iyay enthay expectyay ethay alamitycay atthay
asway inyay ayay ewfay omentsmay otay overwhelmyay emay andyay extinguishyay inyay orrorhay andyay espairday
allyay earfay ofyay ignominyyay oryay eathday.

Iyay ustmay ausepay erehay, orfay ityay equiresray allyay ymay ortitudefay otay ecallray ethay emorymay ofyay
ethay ightfulfray eventsyay ichwhay Iyay amyay aboutyay otay elateray, inyay operpray etailday, otay ymay
ecollectionray.




Apterchay 21


Iyay asway oonsay introducedyay intoyay ethay esencepray ofyay ethay agistratemay, anyay oldyay
enevolentbay anmay ithway almcay andyay ildmay annersmay. Ehay ookedlay uponyay emay, oweverhay,
ithway omesay egreeday ofyay everitysay, andyay enthay, urningtay owardstay ymay onductorscay,
ehay askedyay owhay appearedyay asyay itnessesway onyay isthay occasionyay.

Aboutyay alfhay ayay ozenday enmay amecay orwardfay; andyay, oneyay eingbay electedsay ybay ethay
agistratemay, ehay eposedday atthay ehay adhay eenbay outyay ishingfay ethay ightnay eforebay ithway
ishay onsay andyay other-in-lawbray, Anielday Ugentnay, enwhay, aboutyay entay o’clockyay,
eythay observedyay ayay ongstray ortherlynay astblay isingray, andyay eythay accordinglyyay utpay inyay
orfay ortpay. Ityay asway ayay eryvay arkday ightnay, asyay ethay oonmay adhay otnay yetyay isenray; eythay idday
otnay andlay atyay ethay arbourhay, utbay, asyay eythay adhay eenbay accustomedyay, atyay ayay eekcray aboutyay
otway ilesmay elowbay. Ehay alkedway onyay irstfay, arryingcay ayay artpay ofyay ethay ishingfay ackletay,
andyay ishay ompanionscay ollowedfay imhay atyay omesay istanceday. Asyay ehay asway oceedingpray
alongyay ethay andssay, ehay uckstray ishay ootfay againstyay omethingsay andyay ellfay atyay ishay
engthlay onyay ethay oundgray. Ishay ompanionscay amecay upyay otay assistyay imhay, andyay ybay ethay
ightlay ofyay eirthay anternlay eythay oundfay atthay ehay adhay allenfay onyay ethay odybay ofyay ayay anmay,
owhay asway otay allyay appearanceyay eadday. Eirthay irstfay uppositionsay asway atthay ityay asway ethay
orpsecay ofyay omesay ersonpay owhay adhay eenbay owneddray andyay asway ownthray onyay oreshay ybay ethay
avesway, utbay onyay examinationyay eythay oundfay atthay ethay othesclay ereway otnay etway andyay evenyay
atthay ethay odybay asway otnay enthay oldcay. Eythay instantlyyay arriedcay ityay otay ethay ottagecay
ofyay anyay oldyay omanway earnay ethay otspay andyay endeavouredyay, utbay inyay ainvay, otay estoreray ityay
otay ifelay. Ityay appearedyay otay ebay ayay andsomehay youngyay anmay, aboutyay ivefay andyay entytway
yearsyay ofyay ageyay. Ehay adhay apparentlyyay eenbay angledstray, orfay erethay asway onay ignsay ofyay
anyyay iolencevay exceptyay ethay ackblay arkmay ofyay ingersfay onyay ishay ecknay.

Ethay irstfay artpay ofyay isthay epositionday idday otnay inyay ethay eastlay interestyay emay, utbay
enwhay ethay arkmay ofyay ethay ingersfay asway entionedmay Iyay ememberedray ethay urdermay ofyay
ymay otherbray andyay eltfay yselfmay extremelyyay agitatedyay; ymay imbslay embledtray, andyay ayay
istmay amecay overyay ymay eyesyay, ichwhay obligedyay emay otay eanlay onyay ayay airchay orfay
upportsay. Ethay agistratemay observedyay emay ithway ayay eenkay eyeyay andyay ofyay oursecay ewdray
anyay unfavourableyay auguryyay omfray ymay annermay.

Ethay onsay onfirmedcay ishay ather’sfay accountyay, utbay enwhay Anielday Ugentnay asway
alledcay ehay oresway ositivelypay atthay ustjay eforebay ethay allfay ofyay ishay ompanioncay, ehay
awsay ayay oatbay, ithway ayay inglesay anmay inyay ityay, atyay ayay ortshay istanceday omfray ethay oreshay;
andyay asyay arfay asyay ehay ouldcay udgejay ybay ethay ightlay ofyay ayay ewfay arsstay, ityay asway ethay amesay
oatbay inyay ichwhay Iyay adhay ustjay andedlay.

Ayay omanway eposedday atthay eshay ivedlay earnay ethay eachbay andyay asway andingstay atyay ethay oorday
ofyay erhay ottagecay, aitingway orfay ethay eturnray ofyay ethay ishermenfay, aboutyay anyay ourhay
eforebay eshay eardhay ofyay ethay iscoveryday ofyay ethay odybay, enwhay eshay awsay ayay oatbay ithway
onlyyay oneyay anmay inyay ityay ushpay offyay omfray atthay artpay ofyay ethay oreshay erewhay ethay orpsecay
asway afterwardsyay oundfay.

Anotheryay omanway onfirmedcay ethay accountyay ofyay ethay ishermenfay avinghay oughtbray ethay
odybay intoyay erhay ousehay; ityay asway otnay oldcay. Eythay utpay ityay intoyay ayay edbay andyay
ubbedray ityay, andyay Anielday entway otay ethay owntay orfay anyay apothecaryyay, utbay ifelay asway
uiteqay onegay.

Everalsay otheryay enmay ereway examinedyay oncerningcay ymay andinglay, andyay eythay agreedyay
atthay, ithway ethay ongstray orthnay indway atthay adhay arisenyay uringday ethay ightnay, ityay
asway eryvay obablepray atthay Iyay adhay eatenbay aboutyay orfay anymay ourshay andyay adhay eenbay
obligedyay otay eturnray earlynay otay ethay amesay otspay omfray ichwhay Iyay adhay epartedday.
Esidesbay, eythay observedyay atthay ityay appearedyay atthay Iyay adhay oughtbray ethay odybay
omfray anotheryay aceplay, andyay ityay asway ikelylay atthay asyay Iyay idday otnay appearyay otay owknay
ethay oreshay, Iyay ightmay avehay utpay intoyay ethay arbourhay ignorantyay ofyay ethay istanceday
ofyay ethay owntay ofyay —— omfray ethay aceplay erewhay Iyay adhay epositedday ethay orpsecay.

Mray. Irwinkay, onyay earinghay isthay evidenceyay, esiredday atthay Iyay ouldshay ebay akentay intoyay
ethay oomray erewhay ethay odybay aylay orfay intermentyay, atthay ityay ightmay ebay observedyay atwhay
effectyay ethay ightsay ofyay ityay ouldway oducepray uponyay emay. Isthay ideayay asway obablypray
uggestedsay ybay ethay extremeyay agitationyay Iyay adhay exhibitedyay enwhay ethay odemay ofyay ethay
urdermay adhay eenbay escribedday. Iyay asway accordinglyyay onductedcay, ybay ethay agistratemay
andyay everalsay otheryay ersonspay, otay ethay innyay. Iyay ouldcay otnay elphay eingbay uckstray ybay ethay
angestray oincidencescay atthay adhay akentay aceplay uringday isthay eventfulyay ightnay; utbay,
owingknay atthay Iyay adhay eenbay onversingcay ithway everalsay ersonspay inyay ethay islandyay Iyay adhay
inhabitedyay aboutyay ethay imetay atthay ethay odybay adhay eenbay oundfay, Iyay asway erfectlypay
anquiltray asyay otay ethay onsequencescay ofyay ethay affairyay.

Iyay enteredyay ethay oomray erewhay ethay orpsecay aylay andyay asway edlay upyay otay ethay offincay. Owhay
ancay Iyay escribeday ymay ensationssay onyay eholdingbay ityay? Iyay eelfay yetyay archedpay ithway
orrorhay, ornay ancay Iyay eflectray onyay atthay erribletay omentmay ithoutway udderingshay andyay
agonyyay. Ethay examinationyay, ethay esencepray ofyay ethay agistratemay andyay itnessesway,
assedpay ikelay ayay eamdray omfray ymay emorymay enwhay Iyay awsay ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofyay Enryhay
Ervalclay etchedstray eforebay emay. Iyay aspedgay orfay eathbray, andyay owingthray yselfmay onyay
ethay odybay, Iyay exclaimedyay, ave“hay ymay urderousmay achinationsmay eprivedday youyay
alsoyay, ymay earestday Enryhay, ofyay ifelay? Otway Iyay avehay alreadyyay estroyedday; otheryay
ictimsvay awaityay eirthay estinyday; utbay youyay, Ervalclay, ymay iendfray, ymay
enefactorbay—”

Ethay umanhay amefray ouldcay onay ongerlay upportsay ethay agoniesyay atthay Iyay enduredyay, andyay
Iyay asway arriedcay outyay ofyay ethay oomray inyay ongstray onvulsionscay.

Ayay everfay ucceededsay otay isthay. Iyay aylay orfay otway onthsmay onyay ethay ointpay ofyay eathday; ymay
avingsray, asyay Iyay afterwardsyay eardhay, ereway ightfulfray; Iyay alledcay yselfmay ethay
urderermay ofyay Illiamway, ofyay Ustinejay, andyay ofyay Ervalclay. Ometimessay Iyay entreatedyay ymay
attendantsyay otay assistyay emay inyay ethay estructionday ofyay ethay iendfay ybay omwhay Iyay asway
ormentedtay; andyay atyay othersyay Iyay eltfay ethay ingersfay ofyay ethay onstermay alreadyyay aspinggray
ymay ecknay, andyay eamedscray aloudyay ithway agonyyay andyay errortay. Ortunatelyfay, asyay Iyay okespay
ymay ativenay anguagelay, Mray. Irwinkay aloneyay understoodyay emay; utbay ymay esturesgay andyay
itterbay iescray ereway ufficientsay otay affrightyay ethay otheryay itnessesway.

Ywhay idday Iyay otnay ieday? Oremay iserablemay anthay anmay everyay asway eforebay, ywhay idday Iyay otnay
inksay intoyay orgetfulnessfay andyay estray? Eathday atchessnay awayyay anymay oomingblay
ildrenchay, ethay onlyyay opeshay ofyay eirthay otingday arentspay; owhay anymay idesbray andyay
youthfulyay overslay avehay eenbay oneyay ayday inyay ethay oomblay ofyay ealthhay andyay opehay, andyay ethay
extnay ayay eypray orfay ormsway andyay ethay ecayday ofyay ethay ombtay! Ofyay atwhay aterialsmay asway Iyay
ademay atthay Iyay ouldcay usthay esistray osay anymay ocksshay, ichwhay, ikelay ethay urningtay ofyay
ethay eelwhay, ontinuallycay enewedray ethay orturetay?

Utbay Iyay asway oomedday otay ivelay andyay inyay otway onthsmay oundfay yselfmay asyay awakingyay omfray
ayay eamdray, inyay ayay isonpray, etchedstray onyay ayay etchedwray edbay, urroundedsay ybay
aolersgay, urnkeystay, oltsbay, andyay allyay ethay iserablemay apparatusyay ofyay ayay ungeonday.
Ityay asway orningmay, Iyay ememberray, enwhay Iyay usthay awokeyay otay understandingyay; Iyay adhay
orgottenfay ethay articularspay ofyay atwhay adhay appenedhay andyay onlyyay eltfay asyay ifyay omesay
eatgray isfortunemay adhay uddenlysay overwhelmedyay emay; utbay enwhay Iyay ookedlay aroundyay
andyay awsay ethay arredbay indowsway andyay ethay ualidnesssqay ofyay ethay oomray inyay ichwhay Iyay
asway, allyay ashedflay acrossyay ymay emorymay andyay Iyay oanedgray itterlybay.

Isthay oundsay isturbedday anyay oldyay omanway owhay asway eepingslay inyay ayay airchay esidebay
emay. Eshay asway ayay iredhay ursenay, ethay ifeway ofyay oneyay ofyay ethay urnkeystay, andyay erhay
ountenancecay expressedyay allyay osethay adbay ualitiesqay ichwhay oftenyay aracterisechay
atthay assclay. Ethay ineslay ofyay erhay acefay ereway ardhay andyay uderay, ikelay atthay ofyay
ersonspay accustomedyay otay eesay ithoutway ympathisingsay inyay ightssay ofyay iserymay. Erhay
onetay expressedyay erhay entireyay indifferenceyay; eshay addressedyay emay inyay Englishyay,
andyay ethay oicevay uckstray emay asyay oneyay atthay Iyay adhay eardhay uringday ymay ufferingssay.

are“ay youyay etterbay ownay, irsay?” aidsay eshay.

Iyay epliedray inyay ethay amesay anguagelay, ithway ayay eeblefay oicevay, i“ay elievebay Iyay amyay;
utbay ifyay ityay ebay allyay uetray, ifyay indeedyay Iyay idday otnay eamdray, Iyay amyay orrysay atthay Iyay amyay
illstay aliveyay otay eelfay isthay iserymay andyay orrorhay.”

or“fay atthay attermay,” epliedray ethay oldyay omanway, if“ay youyay eanmay aboutyay ethay
entlemangay youyay urderedmay, Iyay elievebay atthay ityay ereway etterbay orfay youyay ifyay youyay
ereway eadday, orfay Iyay ancyfay ityay illway ogay ardhay ithway youyay! Oweverhay, at’sthay onenay
ofyay ymay usinessbay; Iyay amyay entsay otay ursenay youyay andyay etgay youyay ellway; Iyay oday ymay utyday
ithway ayay afesay onsciencecay; ityay ereway ellway ifyay everybodyyay idday ethay amesay.”

Iyay urnedtay ithway oathinglay omfray ethay omanway owhay ouldcay utteryay osay unfeelingyay ayay
eechspay otay ayay ersonpay ustjay avedsay, onyay ethay eryvay edgeyay ofyay eathday; utbay Iyay eltfay
anguidlay andyay unableyay otay eflectray onyay allyay atthay adhay assedpay. Ethay olewhay eriessay
ofyay ymay ifelay appearedyay otay emay asyay ayay eamdray; Iyay ometimessay oubtedday ifyay indeedyay ityay
ereway allyay uetray, orfay ityay evernay esentedpray itselfyay otay ymay indmay ithway ethay orcefay
ofyay ealityray.

Asyay ethay imagesyay atthay oatedflay eforebay emay ecamebay oremay istinctday, Iyay ewgray
everishfay; ayay arknessday essedpray aroundyay emay; onay oneyay asway earnay emay owhay oothedsay
emay ithway ethay entlegay oicevay ofyay ovelay; onay earday andhay upportedsay emay. Ethay
ysicianphay amecay andyay escribedpray edicinesmay, andyay ethay oldyay omanway eparedpray
emthay orfay emay; utbay utteryay arelessnesscay asway isiblevay inyay ethay irstfay, andyay ethay
expressionyay ofyay utalitybray asway onglystray arkedmay inyay ethay isagevay ofyay ethay
econdsay. Owhay ouldcay ebay interestedyay inyay ethay atefay ofyay ayay urderermay utbay ethay
angmanhay owhay ouldway aingay ishay eefay?

Esethay ereway ymay irstfay eflectionsray, utbay Iyay oonsay earnedlay atthay Mray. Irwinkay adhay
ownshay emay extremeyay indnesskay. Ehay adhay ausedcay ethay estbay oomray inyay ethay isonpray
otay ebay eparedpray orfay emay etched(wray indeedyay asway ethay estbay); andyay ityay asway ehay owhay
adhay ovidedpray ayay ysicianphay andyay ayay ursenay. Ityay isyay uetray, ehay eldomsay amecay otay
eesay emay, orfay althoughyay ehay ardentlyyay esiredday otay elieveray ethay ufferingssay ofyay
everyyay umanhay eaturecray, ehay idday otnay ishway otay ebay esentpray atyay ethay agoniesyay andyay
iserablemay avingsray ofyay ayay urderermay. Ehay amecay, ereforethay, ometimessay otay eesay
atthay Iyay asway otnay eglectednay, utbay ishay isitsvay ereway ortshay andyay ithway onglay
intervalsyay.

Oneyay ayday, ilewhay Iyay asway aduallygray ecoveringray, Iyay asway eatedsay inyay ayay airchay, ymay eyesyay
alfhay openyay andyay ymay eekschay ividlay ikelay osethay inyay eathday. Iyay asway overcomeyay ybay oomglay
andyay iserymay andyay oftenyay eflectedray Iyay adhay etterbay eeksay eathday anthay esireday otay
emainray inyay ayay orldway ichwhay otay emay asway epleteray ithway etchednesswray. Atyay oneyay imetay Iyay
onsideredcay etherwhay Iyay ouldshay otnay eclareday yselfmay uiltygay andyay uffersay ethay
enaltypay ofyay ethay awlay, esslay innocentyay anthay oorpay Ustinejay adhay eenbay. Uchsay ereway ymay
oughtsthay enwhay ethay oorday ofyay ymay apartmentyay asway openedyay andyay Mray. Irwinkay enteredyay.
Ishay ountenancecay expressedyay ympathysay andyay ompassioncay; ehay ewdray ayay airchay oseclay otay
inemay andyay addressedyay emay inyay Enchfray,

i“ay earfay atthay isthay aceplay isyay eryvay ockingshay otay youyay; ancay Iyay oday anythingyay otay
akemay youyay oremay omfortablecay?”

i“ay ankthay youyay, utbay allyay atthay youyay entionmay isyay othingnay otay emay; onyay ethay olewhay
earthyay erethay isyay onay omfortcay ichwhay Iyay amyay apablecay ofyay eceivingray.”

i“ay owknay atthay ethay ympathysay ofyay ayay angerstray ancay ebay utbay ofyay ittlelay eliefray otay
oneyay ornebay ownday asyay youyay areyay ybay osay angestray ayay isfortunemay. Utbay youyay illway, Iyay
opehay, oonsay uitqay isthay elancholymay abodeyay, orfay oubtlessday evidenceyay ancay
easilyyay ebay oughtbray otay eefray youyay omfray ethay iminalcray argechay.”

at“thay isyay ymay eastlay oncerncay; Iyay amyay, ybay ayay oursecay ofyay angestray eventsyay, ecomebay
ethay ostmay iserablemay ofyay ortalsmay. Ersecutedpay andyay orturedtay asyay Iyay amyay andyay
avehay eenbay, ancay eathday ebay anyyay evilyay otay emay?”

othing“nay indeedyay ouldcay ebay oremay unfortunateyay andyay agonisingyay anthay ethay
angestray anceschay atthay avehay atelylay occurredyay. Youyay ereway ownthray, ybay omesay
urprisingsay accidentyay, onyay isthay oreshay, enownedray orfay itsyay ospitalityhay,
eizedsay immediatelyyay, andyay argedchay ithway urdermay. Ethay irstfay ightsay atthay asway
esentedpray otay youryay eyesyay asway ethay odybay ofyay youryay iendfray, urderedmay inyay osay
unaccountableyay ayay annermay andyay acedplay, asyay ityay ereway, ybay omesay iendfay acrossyay
youryay athpay.”

Asyay Mray. Irwinkay aidsay isthay, otwithstandingnay ethay agitationyay Iyay enduredyay onyay
isthay etrospectray ofyay ymay ufferingssay, Iyay alsoyay eltfay onsiderablecay urprisesay atyay
ethay owledgeknay ehay eemedsay otay ossesspay oncerningcay emay. Iyay upposesay omesay
astonishmentyay asway exhibitedyay inyay ymay ountenancecay, orfay Mray. Irwinkay astenedhay
otay aysay,

immediately“ay uponyay youryay eingbay akentay illyay, allyay ethay aperspay atthay ereway onyay
youryay ersonpay ereway oughtbray emay, andyay Iyay examinedyay emthay atthay Iyay ightmay iscoverday omesay
acetray ybay ichwhay Iyay ouldcay endsay otay youryay elationsray anyay accountyay ofyay youryay isfortunemay
andyay illnessyay. Iyay oundfay everalsay etterslay, andyay, amongyay othersyay, oneyay ichwhay Iyay
iscoveredday omfray itsyay ommencementcay otay ebay omfray youryay atherfay. Iyay instantlyyay otewray
otay Enevagay; earlynay otway onthsmay avehay elapsedyay incesay ethay epartureday ofyay ymay etterlay.
Utbay youyay areyay illyay; evenyay ownay youyay embletray; youyay areyay unfityay orfay agitationyay ofyay anyyay
indkay.”

is“thay uspensesay isyay ayay ousandthay imestay orseway anthay ethay ostmay orriblehay eventyay;
elltay emay atwhay ewnay enescay ofyay eathday ashay eenbay actedyay, andyay osewhay urdermay Iyay amyay
ownay otay amentlay?”

your“ay amilyfay isyay erfectlypay ellway,” aidsay Mray. Irwinkay ithway
entlenessgay; and“ay omeonesay, ayay iendfray, isyay omecay otay isitvay youyay.”

Iyay owknay otnay ybay atwhay ainchay ofyay oughtthay ethay ideayay esentedpray itselfyay, utbay ityay
instantlyyay artedday intoyay ymay indmay atthay ethay urderermay adhay omecay otay ockmay atyay ymay
iserymay andyay aunttay emay ithway ethay eathday ofyay Ervalclay, asyay ayay ewnay incitementyay orfay
emay otay omplycay ithway ishay ellishhay esiresday. Iyay utpay ymay andhay eforebay ymay eyesyay,
andyay iedcray outyay inyay agonyyay,

oh“ay! Aketay imhay awayyay! Iyay annotcay eesay imhay; orfay Od’sgay akesay, oday otnay
etlay imhay enteryay!”

Mray. Irwinkay egardedray emay ithway ayay oubledtray ountenancecay. Ehay ouldcay otnay elphay
egardingray ymay exclamationyay asyay ayay esumptionpray ofyay ymay uiltgay andyay aidsay inyay
atherray ayay everesay onetay,

i“ay ouldshay avehay oughtthay, youngyay anmay, atthay ethay esencepray ofyay youryay atherfay
ouldway avehay eenbay elcomeway insteadyay ofyay inspiringyay uchsay iolentvay epugnanceray.”

y“may atherfay!” iedcray Iyay, ilewhay everyyay eaturefay andyay everyyay usclemay asway elaxedray
omfray anguishyay otay easureplay. is“ay ymay atherfay indeedyay omecay? Owhay indkay, owhay
eryvay indkay! Utbay erewhay isyay ehay, ywhay oesday ehay otnay astenhay otay emay?”

Ymay angechay ofyay annermay urprisedsay andyay easedplay ethay agistratemay; erhapspay ehay
oughtthay atthay ymay ormerfay exclamationyay asway ayay omentarymay eturnray ofyay eliriumday,
andyay ownay ehay instantlyyay esumedray ishay ormerfay enevolencebay. Ehay oseray andyay
uittedqay ethay oomray ithway ymay ursenay, andyay inyay ayay omentmay ymay atherfay enteredyay ityay.

Othingnay, atyay isthay omentmay, ouldcay avehay ivengay emay eatergray easureplay anthay ethay
arrivalyay ofyay ymay atherfay. Iyay etchedstray outyay ymay andhay otay imhay andyay iedcray,

are“ay youyay enthay afe—andsay Elizabeth—andyay Ernestyay?”

Ymay atherfay almedcay emay ithway assurancesyay ofyay eirthay elfareway andyay endeavouredyay, ybay
ellingdway onyay esethay ubjectssay osay interestingyay otay ymay earthay, otay aiseray ymay
espondingday iritsspay; utbay ehay oonsay eltfay atthay ayay isonpray annotcay ebay ethay abodeyay ofyay
eerfulnesschay. at“whay ayay aceplay isyay isthay atthay youyay inhabityay, ymay onsay!”
aidsay ehay, ookinglay ournfullymay atyay ethay arredbay indowsway andyay etchedwray appearanceyay
ofyay ethay oomray. you“ay avelledtray otay eeksay appinesshay, utbay ayay atalityfay eemssay
otay ursuepay youyay. Andyay oorpay Ervalclay—”

Ethay amenay ofyay ymay unfortunateyay andyay urderedmay iendfray asway anyay agitationyay ootay
eatgray otay ebay enduredyay inyay ymay eakway atestay; Iyay edshay earstay.

alas“ay! Yesyay, ymay atherfay,” epliedray Iyay; ome“say estinyday ofyay ethay
ostmay orriblehay indkay angshay overyay emay, andyay Iyay ustmay ivelay otay ulfilfay ityay, oryay urelysay Iyay
ouldshay avehay iedday onyay ethay offincay ofyay Enryhay.”

Eway ereway otnay allowedyay otay onversecay orfay anyyay engthlay ofyay imetay, orfay ethay
ecariouspray atestay ofyay ymay ealthhay enderedray everyyay ecautionpray ecessarynay atthay
ouldcay ensureyay anquillitytray. Mray. Irwinkay amecay inyay andyay insistedyay atthay ymay
engthstray ouldshay otnay ebay exhaustedyay ybay ootay uchmay exertionyay. Utbay ethay
appearanceyay ofyay ymay atherfay asway otay emay ikelay atthay ofyay ymay oodgay angelyay, andyay Iyay
aduallygray ecoveredray ymay ealthhay.

Asyay ymay icknesssay uittedqay emay, Iyay asway absorbedyay ybay ayay oomyglay andyay ackblay
elancholymay atthay othingnay ouldcay issipateday. Ethay imageyay ofyay Ervalclay asway
orfay everyay eforebay emay, astlyghay andyay urderedmay. Oremay anthay onceyay ethay agitationyay
intoyay ichwhay esethay eflectionsray ewthray emay ademay ymay iendsfray eaddray ayay angerousday
elapseray. Alasyay! Ywhay idday eythay eservepray osay iserablemay andyay etestedday ayay
ifelay? Ityay asway urelysay atthay Iyay ightmay ulfilfay ymay estinyday, ichwhay isyay ownay
awingdray otay ayay oseclay. Oonsay, ohyay, eryvay oonsay, illway eathday extinguishyay esethay
obbingsthray andyay elieveray emay omfray ethay ightymay eightway ofyay anguishyay atthay earsbay
emay otay ethay ustday; andyay, inyay executingyay ethay awardyay ofyay usticejay, Iyay allshay alsoyay
inksay otay estray. Enthay ethay appearanceyay ofyay eathday asway istantday, althoughyay ethay
ishway asway everyay esentpray otay ymay oughtsthay; andyay Iyay oftenyay atsay orfay ourshay
otionlessmay andyay eechlessspay, ishingway orfay omesay ightymay evolutionray atthay
ightmay urybay emay andyay ymay estroyerday inyay itsyay uinsray.

Ethay easonsay ofyay ethay assizesyay approachedyay. Iyay adhay alreadyyay eenbay eethray onthsmay
inyay isonpray, andyay althoughyay Iyay asway illstay eakway andyay inyay ontinualcay angerday ofyay ayay
elapseray, Iyay asway obligedyay otay aveltray earlynay ayay undredhay ilesmay otay ethay ountrycay
owntay erewhay ethay ourtcay asway eldhay. Mray. Irwinkay argedchay imselfhay ithway everyyay
arecay ofyay ollectingcay itnessesway andyay arrangingyay ymay efenceday. Iyay asway aredspay
ethay isgraceday ofyay appearingyay ubliclypay asyay ayay iminalcray, asyay ethay asecay asway otnay
oughtbray eforebay ethay ourtcay atthay ecidesday onyay ifelay andyay eathday. Ethay andgray
uryjay ejectedray ethay illbay, onyay itsyay eingbay ovedpray atthay Iyay asway onyay ethay Orkneyyay
Islandsyay atyay ethay ourhay ethay odybay ofyay ymay iendfray asway oundfay; andyay ayay ortnightfay
afteryay ymay emovalray Iyay asway iberatedlay omfray isonpray.

Ymay atherfay asway enrapturedyay onyay indingfay emay eedfray omfray ethay exationsvay ofyay ayay
iminalcray argechay, atthay Iyay asway againyay allowedyay otay eathebray ethay eshfray
atmosphereyay andyay ermittedpay otay eturnray otay ymay ativenay ountrycay. Iyay idday otnay
articipatepay inyay esethay eelingsfay, orfay otay emay ethay allsway ofyay ayay ungeonday oryay ayay
alacepay ereway alikeyay atefulhay. Ethay upcay ofyay ifelay asway oisonedpay orfay everyay, andyay
althoughyay ethay unsay oneshay uponyay emay, asyay uponyay ethay appyhay andyay aygay ofyay earthay, Iyay
awsay aroundyay emay othingnay utbay ayay enseday andyay ightfulfray arknessday, enetratedpay ybay
onay ightlay utbay ethay immerglay ofyay otway eyesyay atthay aredglay uponyay emay. Ometimessay
eythay ereway ethay expressiveyay eyesyay ofyay Enryhay, anguishinglay inyay eathday, ethay arkday
orbsyay earlynay overedcay ybay ethay idslay andyay ethay onglay ackblay asheslay atthay ingedfray
emthay; ometimessay ityay asway ethay ateryway, oudedclay eyesyay ofyay ethay onstermay, asyay Iyay
irstfay awsay emthay inyay ymay amberchay atyay Ingolstadtyay.

Ymay atherfay iedtray otay awakenyay inyay emay ethay eelingsfay ofyay affectionyay. Ehay alkedtay
ofyay Enevagay, ichwhay Iyay ouldshay oonsay isitvay, ofyay Elizabethyay andyay Ernestyay; utbay
esethay ordsway onlyyay ewdray eepday oansgray omfray emay. Ometimessay, indeedyay, Iyay eltfay ayay
ishway orfay appinesshay andyay oughtthay ithway elancholymay elightday ofyay ymay elovedbay
ousincay oryay ongedlay, ithway ayay evouringday aladie_may uday ayspay_, otay eesay onceyay oremay
ethay ueblay akelay andyay apidray Onerhay, atthay adhay eenbay osay earday otay emay inyay earlyyay
ildhoodchay; utbay ymay eneralgay atestay ofyay eelingfay asway ayay orportay inyay ichwhay ayay
isonpray asway asyay elcomeway ayay esidenceray asyay ethay ivinestday enescay inyay aturenay; andyay
esethay itsfay ereway eldomsay interruptedyay utbay ybay aroxysmspay ofyay anguishyay andyay
espairday. Atyay esethay omentsmay Iyay oftenyay endeavouredyay otay utpay anyay endyay otay ethay
existenceyay Iyay oathedlay, andyay ityay equiredray unceasingyay attendanceyay andyay igilancevay
otay estrainray emay omfray ommittingcay omesay eadfuldray actyay ofyay iolencevay.

Yetyay oneyay utyday emainedray otay emay, ethay ecollectionray ofyay ichwhay inallyfay
iumphedtray overyay ymay elfishsay espairday. Ityay asway ecessarynay atthay Iyay ouldshay
eturnray ithoutway elayday otay Enevagay, erethay otay atchway overyay ethay iveslay ofyay osethay
Iyay osay ondlyfay ovedlay andyay otay ielay inyay aitway orfay ethay urderermay, atthay ifyay anyyay
ancechay edlay emay otay ethay aceplay ofyay ishay oncealmentcay, oryay ifyay ehay aredday againyay otay
astblay emay ybay ishay esencepray, Iyay ightmay, ithway unfailingyay aimyay, utpay anyay endyay otay
ethay existenceyay ofyay ethay onstrousmay imageyay ichwhay Iyay adhay enduedyay ithway ethay
ockerymay ofyay ayay oulsay illstay oremay onstrousmay. Ymay atherfay illstay esiredday otay
elayday ouryay epartureday, earfulfay atthay Iyay ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay atiguesfay ofyay ayay
ourneyjay, orfay Iyay asway ayay atteredshay eck—thewray adowshay ofyay ayay umanhay eingbay. Ymay
engthstray asway onegay. Iyay asway ayay eremay eletonskay, andyay everfay ightnay andyay ayday
eyedpray uponyay ymay astedway amefray.

Illstay, asyay Iyay urgedyay ouryay eavinglay Irelandyay ithway uchsay inquietudeyay andyay impatienceyay,
ymay atherfay oughtthay ityay estbay otay yieldyay. Eway ooktay ouryay assagepay onyay oardbay ayay esselvay
oundbay orfay Avre-de-gracehay andyay ailedsay ithway ayay airfay indway omfray ethay Irishyay oresshay.
Ityay asway idnightmay. Iyay aylay onyay ethay eckday ookinglay atyay ethay arsstay andyay isteninglay otay
ethay ashingday ofyay ethay avesway. Iyay ailedhay ethay arknessday atthay utshay Irelandyay omfray ymay
ightsay, andyay ymay ulsepay eatbay ithway ayay everishfay oyjay enwhay Iyay eflectedray atthay Iyay ouldshay
oonsay eesay Enevagay. Ethay astpay appearedyay otay emay inyay ethay ightlay ofyay ayay ightfulfray eamdray;
yetyay ethay esselvay inyay ichwhay Iyay asway, ethay indway atthay ewblay emay omfray ethay etestedday
oreshay ofyay Irelandyay, andyay ethay easay ichwhay urroundedsay emay, oldtay emay ootay orciblyfay
atthay Iyay asway eceivedday ybay onay isionvay andyay atthay Ervalclay, ymay iendfray andyay earestday
ompanioncay, adhay allenfay ayay ictimvay otay emay andyay ethay onstermay ofyay ymay eationcray. Iyay
epassedray, inyay ymay emorymay, ymay olewhay ifelay; ymay uietqay appinesshay ilewhay esidingray
ithway ymay amilyfay inyay Enevagay, ethay eathday ofyay ymay othermay, andyay ymay epartureday orfay
Ingolstadtyay. Iyay ememberedray, udderingshay, ethay admay enthusiasmyay atthay urriedhay emay onyay
otay ethay eationcray ofyay ymay ideoushay enemyyay, andyay Iyay alledcay otay indmay ethay ightnay inyay
ichwhay ehay irstfay ivedlay. Iyay asway unableyay otay ursuepay ethay aintray ofyay oughtthay; ayay
ousandthay eelingsfay essedpray uponyay emay, andyay Iyay eptway itterlybay.

Everyay incesay ymay ecoveryray omfray ethay everfay, Iyay adhay eenbay inyay ethay ustomcay ofyay akingtay
everyyay ightnay ayay allsmay uantityqay ofyay audanumlay, orfay ityay asway ybay eansmay ofyay isthay ugdray
onlyyay atthay Iyay asway enabledyay otay aingay ethay estray ecessarynay orfay ethay eservationpray ofyay
ifelay. Oppressedyay ybay ethay ecollectionray ofyay ymay ariousvay isfortunesmay, Iyay ownay
allowedsway oubleday ymay usualyay uantityqay andyay oonsay eptslay ofoundlypray. Utbay eepslay idday
otnay affordyay emay espiteray omfray oughtthay andyay iserymay; ymay eamsdray esentedpray ayay
