ousandthay objectsyay atthay aredscay emay. Owardstay orningmay Iyay asway ossessedpay ybay ayay indkay
ofyay ightmarenay; Iyay eltfay ethay iend’sfay aspgray inyay ymay ecknay andyay ouldcay otnay eefray
yselfmay omfray ityay; oansgray andyay iescray angray inyay ymay earsyay. Ymay atherfay, owhay asway
atchingway overyay emay, erceivingpay ymay estlessnessray, awokeyay emay; ethay ashingday avesway
ereway aroundyay, ethay oudyclay yskay aboveyay, ethay iendfay asway otnay erehay: ayay ensesay ofyay
ecuritysay, ayay eelingfay atthay ayay ucetray asway establishedyay etweenbay ethay esentpray ourhay
andyay ethay irresistibleyay, isastrousday uturefay impartedyay otay emay ayay indkay ofyay almcay
orgetfulnessfay, ofyay ichwhay ethay umanhay indmay isyay ybay itsyay ucturestray eculiarlypay
usceptiblesay.




Apterchay 22


Ethay oyagevay amecay otay anyay endyay. Eway andedlay, andyay oceededpray otay Arispay. Iyay oonsay
oundfay atthay Iyay adhay overtaxedyay ymay engthstray andyay atthay Iyay ustmay eposeray eforebay Iyay
ouldcay ontinuecay ymay ourneyjay. Ymay ather’sfay arecay andyay attentionsyay ereway
indefatigableyay, utbay ehay idday otnay owknay ethay originyay ofyay ymay ufferingssay andyay
oughtsay erroneousyay ethodsmay otay emedyray ethay incurableyay illyay. Ehay ishedway emay otay
eeksay amusementyay inyay ocietysay. Iyay abhorredyay ethay acefay ofyay anmay. Ohyay, otnay
abhorredyay! Eythay ereway ymay ethrenbray, ymay ellowfay eingsbay, andyay Iyay eltfay
attractedyay evenyay otay ethay ostmay epulsiveray amongyay emthay, asyay otay eaturescray ofyay anyay
angelicyay aturenay andyay elestialcay echanismmay. Utbay Iyay eltfay atthay Iyay adhay onay ightray
otay areshay eirthay intercourseyay. Iyay adhay unchainedyay anyay enemyyay amongyay emthay osewhay
oyjay ityay asway otay edshay eirthay oodblay andyay otay evelray inyay eirthay oansgray. Owhay eythay
ouldway, eachyay andyay allyay, abhoryay emay andyay unthay emay omfray ethay orldway, idday eythay owknay
ymay unhallowedyay actsyay andyay ethay imescray ichwhay adhay eirthay ourcesay inyay emay!

Ymay atherfay yieldedyay atyay engthlay otay ymay esireday otay avoidyay ocietysay andyay ovestray ybay
ariousvay argumentsyay otay anishbay ymay espairday. Ometimessay ehay oughtthay atthay Iyay
eltfay eeplyday ethay egradationday ofyay eingbay obligedyay otay answeryay ayay argechay ofyay
urdermay, andyay ehay endeavouredyay otay ovepray otay emay ethay utilityfay ofyay idepray.

alas“ay! Ymay atherfay,” aidsay Iyay, ow“hay ittlelay oday youyay owknay emay. 
Umanhay eingsbay, eirthay eelingsfay andyay assionspay, ouldway indeedyay ebay egradedday ifyay uchsay
ayay etchwray asyay Iyay eltfay idepray. Ustinejay, oorpay unhappyyay Ustinejay, asway asyay innocentyay
asyay Iyay, andyay eshay ufferedsay ethay amesay argechay; eshay iedday orfay ityay; andyay Iyay amyay ethay ausecay
ofyay is—ithay urderedmay erhay. Illiamway, Ustinejay, andyay Enry—theyhay allyay
iedday ybay ymay andshay.”

Ymay atherfay adhay oftenyay, uringday ymay imprisonmentyay, eardhay emay akemay ethay amesay
assertionyay; enwhay Iyay usthay accusedyay yselfmay, ehay ometimessay eemedsay otay esireday anyay
explanationyay, andyay atyay othersyay ehay appearedyay otay onsidercay ityay asyay ethay offspringyay ofyay
eliriumday, andyay atthay, uringday ymay illnessyay, omesay ideayay ofyay isthay indkay adhay esentedpray
itselfyay otay ymay imaginationyay, ethay emembranceray ofyay ichwhay Iyay eservedpray inyay ymay
onvalescencecay. Iyay avoidedyay explanationyay andyay aintainedmay ayay ontinualcay ilencesay
oncerningcay ethay etchwray Iyay adhay eatedcray. Iyay adhay ayay ersuasionpay atthay Iyay ouldshay ebay
upposedsay admay, andyay isthay inyay itselfyay ouldway orfay everyay avehay ainedchay ymay onguetay. Utbay,
esidesbay, Iyay ouldcay otnay ingbray yselfmay otay iscloseday ayay ecretsay ichwhay ouldway illfay ymay
earerhay ithway onsternationcay andyay akemay earfay andyay unnaturalyay orrorhay ethay inmatesyay ofyay
ishay eastbray. Iyay eckedchay, ereforethay, ymay impatientyay irstthay orfay ympathysay andyay asway
ilentsay enwhay Iyay ouldway avehay ivengay ethay orldway otay avehay onfidedcay ethay atalfay ecretsay.
Yetyay, illstay, ordsway ikelay osethay Iyay avehay ecordedray ouldway urstbay uncontrollablyyay
omfray emay. Iyay ouldcay offeryay onay explanationyay ofyay emthay, utbay eirthay uthtray inyay artpay
elievedray ethay urdenbay ofyay ymay ysteriousmay oeway.

Uponyay isthay occasionyay ymay atherfay aidsay, ithway anyay expressionyay ofyay unboundedyay onderway,
y“may earestday Ictorvay, atwhay infatuationyay isyay isthay? Ymay earday onsay, Iyay entreatyay
youyay evernay otay akemay uchsay anyay assertionyay againyay.”

i“ay amyay otnay admay,” Iyay iedcray energeticallyyay; e“thay unsay andyay ethay eavenshay, owhay
avehay iewedvay ymay operationsyay, ancay earbay itnessway ofyay ymay uthtray. Iyay amyay ethay
assassinyay ofyay osethay ostmay innocentyay ictimsvay; eythay iedday ybay ymay achinationsmay.
Ayay ousandthay imestay ouldway Iyay avehay edshay ymay ownyay oodblay, opdray ybay opdray, otay avehay
avedsay eirthay iveslay; utbay Iyay ouldcay otnay, ymay atherfay, indeedyay Iyay ouldcay otnay
acrificesay ethay olewhay umanhay aceray.”

Ethay onclusioncay ofyay isthay eechspay onvincedcay ymay atherfay atthay ymay ideasyay ereway
erangedday, andyay ehay instantlyyay angedchay ethay ubjectsay ofyay ouryay onversationcay andyay
endeavouredyay otay alteryay ethay oursecay ofyay ymay oughtsthay. Ehay ishedway asyay uchmay asyay
ossiblepay otay obliterateyay ethay emorymay ofyay ethay enesscay atthay adhay akentay aceplay inyay
Irelandyay andyay evernay alludedyay otay emthay oryay ufferedsay emay otay eakspay ofyay ymay
isfortunesmay.

Asyay imetay assedpay awayyay Iyay ecamebay oremay almcay; iserymay adhay erhay ellingdway inyay ymay
earthay, utbay Iyay onay ongerlay alkedtay inyay ethay amesay incoherentyay annermay ofyay ymay ownyay
imescray; ufficientsay orfay emay asway ethay onsciousnesscay ofyay emthay. Ybay ethay utmostyay
elf-violencesay Iyay urbedcay ethay imperiousyay oicevay ofyay etchednesswray, ichwhay
ometimessay esiredday otay eclareday itselfyay otay ethay olewhay orldway, andyay ymay annersmay
ereway almercay andyay oremay omposedcay anthay eythay adhay everyay eenbay incesay ymay ourneyjay
otay ethay easay ofyay iceyay.

Ayay ewfay aysday eforebay eway eftlay Arispay onyay ouryay ayway otay Itzerlandsway, Iyay eceivedray ethay
ollowingfay etterlay omfray Elizabethyay:

y“may earday Iendfray,

it“ay avegay emay ethay eatestgray easureplay otay eceiveray ayay etterlay omfray ymay uncleyay
atedday atyay Arispay; youyay areyay onay ongerlay atyay ayay ormidablefay istanceday, andyay Iyay aymay
opehay otay eesay youyay inyay esslay anthay ayay ortnightfay. Ymay oorpay ousincay, owhay uchmay youyay
ustmay avehay ufferedsay! Iyay expectyay otay eesay youyay ookinglay evenyay oremay illyay anthay
enwhay youyay uittedqay Enevagay. Isthay interway ashay eenbay assedpay ostmay iserablymay,
orturedtay asyay Iyay avehay eenbay ybay anxiousyay uspensesay; yetyay Iyay opehay otay eesay eacepay inyay
youryay ountenancecay andyay otay indfay atthay youryay earthay isyay otnay otallytay oidvay ofyay
omfortcay andyay anquillitytray.

yet“ay Iyay earfay atthay ethay amesay eelingsfay ownay existyay atthay ademay youyay osay iserablemay
ayay yearyay agoyay, evenyay erhapspay augmentedyay ybay imetay. Iyay ouldway otnay isturbday youyay atyay
isthay eriodpay, enwhay osay anymay isfortunesmay eighway uponyay youyay, utbay ayay
onversationcay atthay Iyay adhay ithway ymay uncleyay eviouspray otay ishay epartureday endersray
omesay explanationyay ecessarynay eforebay eway eetmay.

Explanationyay! Youyay aymay ossiblypay aysay, Atwhay ancay Elizabethyay avehay otay explainyay? Ifyay
youyay eallyray aysay isthay, ymay uestionsqay areyay answeredyay andyay allyay ymay oubtsday atisfiedsay.
Utbay youyay areyay istantday omfray emay, andyay ityay isyay ossiblepay atthay youyay aymay eaddray andyay yetyay
ebay easedplay ithway isthay explanationyay; andyay inyay ayay obabilitypray ofyay isthay eingbay ethay
asecay, Iyay areday otnay anyyay ongerlay ostponepay itingwray atwhay, uringday youryay absenceyay, Iyay
avehay oftenyay ishedway otay expressyay otay youyay utbay avehay evernay adhay ethay ouragecay otay eginbay.

you“ay ellway owknay, Ictorvay, atthay ouryay unionyay adhay eenbay ethay avouritefay anplay ofyay
youryay arentspay everyay incesay ouryay infancyyay. Eway ereway oldtay isthay enwhay youngyay, andyay
aughttay otay ooklay orwardfay otay ityay asyay anyay eventyay atthay ouldway ertainlycay aketay
aceplay. Eway ereway affectionateyay ayfellowsplay uringday ildhoodchay, andyay, Iyay
elievebay, earday andyay aluedvay iendsfray otay oneyay anotheryay asyay eway ewgray olderyay. Utbay
asyay otherbray andyay istersay oftenyay entertainyay ayay ivelylay affectionyay owardstay eachyay
otheryay ithoutway esiringday ayay oremay intimateyay unionyay, aymay otnay uchsay alsoyay ebay ouryay
asecay? Elltay emay, earestday Ictorvay. Answeryay emay, Iyay onjurecay youyay ybay ouryay utualmay
appinesshay, ithway implesay uth—dotray youyay otnay ovelay anotheryay?

you“ay avehay avelledtray; youyay avehay entspay everalsay yearsyay ofyay youryay ifelay atyay
Ingolstadtyay; andyay Iyay onfesscay otay youyay, ymay iendfray, atthay enwhay Iyay awsay youyay astlay
autumnyay osay unhappyyay, yingflay otay olitudesay omfray ethay ocietysay ofyay everyyay
eaturecray, Iyay ouldcay otnay elphay upposingsay atthay youyay ightmay egretray ouryay
onnectioncay andyay elievebay yourselfyay oundbay inyay onourhay otay ulfilfay ethay ishesway ofyay
youryay arentspay, althoughyay eythay opposedyay emselvesthay otay youryay inclinationsyay.
Utbay isthay isyay alsefay easoningray. Iyay onfesscay otay youyay, ymay iendfray, atthay Iyay ovelay
youyay andyay atthay inyay ymay airyyay eamsdray ofyay uturityfay youyay avehay eenbay ymay onstantcay
iendfray andyay ompanioncay. Utbay ityay isyay youryay appinesshay Iyay esireday asyay ellway asyay ymay
ownyay enwhay Iyay eclareday otay youyay atthay ouryay arriagemay ouldway enderray emay eternallyyay
iserablemay unlessyay ityay ereway ethay ictateday ofyay youryay ownyay eefray oicechay. Evenyay ownay
Iyay eepway otay inkthay atthay, ornebay ownday asyay youyay areyay ybay ethay uellestcray
isfortunesmay, youyay aymay iflestay, ybay ethay ordway onour_hay_, allyay opehay ofyay atthay
ovelay andyay appinesshay ichwhay ouldway aloneyay estoreray youyay otay yourselfyay. Iyay, owhay
avehay osay isinterestedday anyay affectionyay orfay youyay, aymay increaseyay youryay iseriesmay
enfoldtay ybay eingbay anyay obstacleyay otay youryay ishesway. Ahyay! Ictorvay, ebay assuredyay
atthay youryay ousincay andyay aymateplay ashay ootay inceresay ayay ovelay orfay youyay otnay otay ebay
ademay iserablemay ybay isthay uppositionsay. Ebay appyhay, ymay iendfray; andyay ifyay youyay
obeyyay emay inyay isthay oneyay equestray, emainray atisfiedsay atthay othingnay onyay earthyay
illway avehay ethay owerpay otay interruptyay ymay anquillitytray.

o“day otnay etlay isthay etterlay isturbday youyay; oday otnay answeryay omorrowtay, oryay ethay
extnay ayday, oryay evenyay untilyay youyay omecay, ifyay ityay illway ivegay youyay ainpay. Ymay uncleyay
illway endsay emay ewsnay ofyay youryay ealthhay, andyay ifyay Iyay eesay utbay oneyay ilesmay onyay youryay
ipslay enwhay eway eetmay, occasionedyay ybay isthay oryay anyyay otheryay exertionyay ofyay inemay, Iyay
allshay eednay onay otheryay appinesshay.

elizabeth“ay Avenzalay.



eneva“gay, Aymay 18th, 17—”



Isthay etterlay evivedray inyay ymay emorymay atwhay Iyay adhay eforebay orgottenfay, ethay eatthray ofyay
ethay iend—“_ifay illway ebay ithway youyay onyay youryay
edding-nightway!_” Uchsay asway ymay entencesay, andyay onyay atthay ightnay ouldway ethay
ondæmay employyay everyyay artyay otay estroyday emay andyay eartay emay omfray ethay impseglay ofyay
appinesshay ichwhay omisedpray artlypay otay onsolecay ymay ufferingssay. Onyay atthay ightnay ehay
adhay eterminedday otay onsummatecay ishay imescray ybay ymay eathday. Ellway, ebay ityay osay; ayay
eadlyday ugglestray ouldway enthay assuredlyyay aketay aceplay, inyay ichwhay ifyay ehay ereway
ictoriousvay Iyay ouldshay ebay atyay eacepay andyay ishay owerpay overyay emay ebay atyay anyay endyay. Ifyay ehay
ereway anquishedvay, Iyay ouldshay ebay ayay eefray anmay. Alasyay! Atwhay eedomfray? Uchsay asyay ethay
easantpay enjoysyay enwhay ishay amilyfay avehay eenbay assacredmay eforebay ishay eyesyay, ishay
ottagecay urntbay, ishay andslay aidlay asteway, andyay ehay isyay urnedtay adriftyay, omelesshay,
ennilesspay, andyay aloneyay, utbay eefray. Uchsay ouldway ebay ymay ibertylay exceptyay atthay inyay ymay
Elizabethyay Iyay ossessedpay ayay easuretray, alasyay, alancedbay ybay osethay orrorshay ofyay
emorseray andyay uiltgay ichwhay ouldway ursuepay emay untilyay eathday.

Eetsway andyay elovedbay Elizabethyay! Iyay eadray andyay ereadray erhay etterlay, andyay omesay
oftenedsay eelingsfay olestay intoyay ymay earthay andyay aredday otay isperwhay aradisiacalpay
eamsdray ofyay ovelay andyay oyjay; utbay ethay appleyay asway alreadyyay eatenyay, andyay ethay
angel’syay armyay aredbay otay ivedray emay omfray allyay opehay. Yetyay Iyay ouldway ieday otay akemay
erhay appyhay. Ifyay ethay onstermay executedyay ishay eatthray, eathday asway inevitableyay; yetyay,
againyay, Iyay onsideredcay etherwhay ymay arriagemay ouldway astenhay ymay atefay. Ymay
estructionday ightmay indeedyay arriveyay ayay ewfay onthsmay oonersay, utbay ifyay ymay orturertay
ouldshay uspectsay atthay Iyay ostponedpay ityay, influencedyay ybay ishay enacesmay, ehay ouldway
urelysay indfay otheryay andyay erhapspay oremay eadfuldray eansmay ofyay evengeray. Ehay adhay owedvay
o_tay ebay ithway emay onyay ymay edding-nightway_, yetyay ehay idday otnay onsidercay atthay
eatthray asyay indingbay imhay otay eacepay inyay ethay eantimemay, orfay asyay ifyay otay owshay emay atthay
ehay asway otnay yetyay atiatedsay ithway oodblay, ehay adhay urderedmay Ervalclay immediatelyyay
afteryay ethay enunciationyay ofyay ishay eatsthray. Iyay esolvedray, ereforethay, atthay ifyay ymay
immediateyay unionyay ithway ymay ousincay ouldway onducecay eitheryay otay ershay oryay ymay
ather’sfay appinesshay, ymay adversary’syay esignsday againstyay ymay ifelay
ouldshay otnay etardray ityay ayay inglesay ourhay.

Inyay isthay atestay ofyay indmay Iyay otewray otay Elizabethyay. Ymay etterlay asway almcay andyay
affectionateyay. i“ay earfay, ymay elovedbay irlgay,” Iyay aidsay, ittle“lay appinesshay
emainsray orfay usyay onyay earthyay; yetyay allyay atthay Iyay aymay oneyay ayday enjoyyay isyay entredcay inyay
youyay. Asechay awayyay youryay idleyay earsfay; otay youyay aloneyay oday Iyay onsecratecay ymay ifelay
andyay ymay endeavoursyay orfay ontentmentcay. Iyay avehay oneyay ecretsay, Elizabethyay, ayay
eadfuldray oneyay; enwhay evealedray otay youyay, ityay illway illchay youryay amefray ithway
orrorhay, andyay enthay, arfay omfray eingbay urprisedsay atyay ymay iserymay, youyay illway onlyyay
onderway atthay Iyay urvivesay atwhay Iyay avehay enduredyay. Iyay illway onfidecay isthay aletay ofyay
iserymay andyay errortay otay youyay ethay ayday afteryay ouryay arriagemay allshay aketay aceplay,
orfay, ymay eetsway ousincay, erethay ustmay ebay erfectpay onfidencecay etweenbay usyay. Utbay
untilyay enthay, Iyay onjurecay youyay, oday otnay entionmay oryay alludeyay otay ityay. Isthay Iyay ostmay
earnestlyyay entreatyay, andyay Iyay owknay youyay illway omplycay.”

Inyay aboutyay ayay eekway afteryay ethay arrivalyay ofyay Elizabeth’syay etterlay eway eturnedray
otay Enevagay. Ethay eetsway irlgay elcomedway emay ithway armway affectionyay, yetyay earstay ereway
inyay erhay eyesyay asyay eshay eheldbay ymay emaciatedyay amefray andyay everishfay eekschay. Iyay awsay ayay
angechay inyay erhay alsoyay. Eshay asway innerthay andyay adhay ostlay uchmay ofyay atthay eavenlyhay
ivacityvay atthay adhay eforebay armedchay emay; utbay erhay entlenessgay andyay oftsay ookslay ofyay
ompassioncay ademay erhay ayay oremay itfay ompanioncay orfay oneyay astedblay andyay iserablemay asyay Iyay
asway.

Ethay anquillitytray ichwhay Iyay ownay enjoyedyay idday otnay endureyay. Emorymay oughtbray adnessmay
ithway ityay, andyay enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay atwhay adhay assedpay, ayay ealray insanityyay ossessedpay
emay; ometimessay Iyay asway uriousfay andyay urntbay ithway ageray, ometimessay owlay andyay
espondentday. Iyay eithernay okespay ornay ookedlay atyay anyoneyay, utbay atsay otionlessmay,
ewilderedbay ybay ethay ultitudemay ofyay iseriesmay atthay overcameyay emay.

Elizabethyay aloneyay adhay ethay owerpay otay awdray emay omfray esethay itsfay; erhay entlegay oicevay
ouldway oothesay emay enwhay ansportedtray ybay assionpay andyay inspireyay emay ithway umanhay
eelingsfay enwhay unksay inyay orportay. Eshay eptway ithway emay andyay orfay emay. Enwhay easonray
eturnedray, eshay ouldway emonstrateray andyay endeavouryay otay inspireyay emay ithway
esignationray. Ahyay! Ityay isyay ellway orfay ethay unfortunateyay otay ebay esignedray, utbay orfay ethay
uiltygay erethay isyay onay eacepay. Ethay agoniesyay ofyay emorseray oisonpay ethay uxurylay erethay isyay
otherwiseyay ometimessay oundfay inyay indulgingyay ethay excessyay ofyay iefgray.

Oonsay afteryay ymay arrivalyay ymay atherfay okespay ofyay ymay immediateyay arriagemay ithway
Elizabethyay. Iyay emainedray ilentsay.

ave“hay youyay, enthay, omesay otheryay attachmentyay?”

one“nay onyay earthyay. Iyay ovelay Elizabethyay andyay ooklay orwardfay otay ouryay unionyay ithway
elightday. Etlay ethay ayday ereforethay ebay ixedfay; andyay onyay ityay Iyay illway onsecratecay
yselfmay, inyay ifelay oryay eathday, otay ethay appinesshay ofyay ymay ousincay.”

y“may earday Ictorvay, oday otnay eakspay usthay. Eavyhay isfortunesmay avehay efallenbay
usyay, utbay etlay usyay onlyyay ingclay oserclay otay atwhay emainsray andyay ansfertray ouryay ovelay
orfay osethay omwhay eway avehay ostlay otay osethay owhay yetyay ivelay. Ouryay irclecay illway ebay
allsmay utbay oundbay oseclay ybay ethay iestay ofyay affectionyay andyay utualmay isfortunemay.
Andyay enwhay imetay allshay avehay oftenedsay youryay espairday, ewnay andyay earday objectsyay ofyay
arecay illway ebay ornbay otay eplaceray osethay ofyay omwhay eway avehay eenbay osay uellycray
eprivedday.”

Uchsay ereway ethay essonslay ofyay ymay atherfay. Utbay otay emay ethay emembranceray ofyay ethay
eatthray eturnedray; ornay ancay youyay onderway atthay, omnipotentyay asyay ethay iendfay adhay
yetyay eenbay inyay ishay eedsday ofyay oodblay, Iyay ouldshay almostyay egardray imhay asyay
invincibleyay, andyay atthay enwhay ehay adhay onouncedpray ethay ordsway i“_ay allshay ebay ithway
youyay onyay youryay edding-nightway_,” Iyay ouldshay egardray ethay eatenedthray atefay asyay
unavoidableyay. Utbay eathday asway onay evilyay otay emay ifyay ethay osslay ofyay Elizabethyay ereway
alancedbay ithway ityay, andyay Iyay ereforethay, ithway ayay ontentedcay andyay evenyay eerfulchay
ountenancecay, agreedyay ithway ymay atherfay atthay ifyay ymay ousincay ouldway onsentcay, ethay
eremonycay ouldshay aketay aceplay inyay entay aysday, andyay usthay utpay, asyay Iyay imaginedyay,
ethay ealsay otay ymay atefay.

Eatgray Odgay! Ifyay orfay oneyay instantyay Iyay adhay oughtthay atwhay ightmay ebay ethay ellishhay
intentionyay ofyay ymay iendishfay adversaryyay, Iyay ouldway atherray avehay anishedbay yselfmay
orfay everyay omfray ymay ativenay ountrycay andyay anderedway ayay iendlessfray outcastyay overyay
ethay earthyay anthay avehay onsentedcay otay isthay iserablemay arriagemay. Utbay, asyay ifyay
ossessedpay ofyay agicmay owerspay, ethay onstermay adhay indedblay emay otay ishay ealray
intentionsyay; andyay enwhay Iyay oughtthay atthay Iyay adhay eparedpray onlyyay ymay ownyay eathday, Iyay
astenedhay atthay ofyay ayay arfay earerday ictimvay.

Asyay ethay eriodpay ixedfay orfay ouryay arriagemay ewdray earernay, etherwhay omfray owardicecay oryay
ayay opheticpray eelingfay, Iyay eltfay ymay earthay inksay ithinway emay. Utbay Iyay oncealedcay ymay
eelingsfay ybay anyay appearanceyay ofyay ilarityhay atthay oughtbray ilessmay andyay oyjay otay ethay
ountenancecay ofyay ymay atherfay, utbay ardlyhay eceivedday ethay ever-watchfulyay andyay icernay
eyeyay ofyay Elizabethyay. Eshay ookedlay orwardfay otay ouryay unionyay ithway acidplay ontentmentcay,
otnay unmingledyay ithway ayay ittlelay earfay, ichwhay astpay isfortunesmay adhay impressedyay,
atthay atwhay ownay appearedyay ertaincay andyay angibletay appinesshay ightmay oonsay issipateday
intoyay anyay airyyay eamdray andyay eavelay onay acetray utbay eepday andyay everlastingyay egretray.

Eparationspray ereway ademay orfay ethay eventyay, ongratulatorycay isitsvay ereway eceivedray,
andyay allyay oreway ayay ilingsmay appearanceyay. Iyay utshay upyay, asyay ellway asyay Iyay ouldcay, inyay ymay ownyay
earthay ethay anxietyyay atthay eyedpray erethay andyay enteredyay ithway eemingsay earnestnessyay
intoyay ethay ansplay ofyay ymay atherfay, althoughyay eythay ightmay onlyyay ervesay asyay ethay
ecorationsday ofyay ymay agedytray. Oughthray ymay ather’sfay exertionsyay ayay artpay ofyay
ethay inheritanceyay ofyay Elizabethyay adhay eenbay estoredray otay erhay ybay ethay Austrianyay
overnmentgay. Ayay allsmay ossessionpay onyay ethay oresshay ofyay Omocay elongedbay otay erhay. Ityay
asway agreedyay atthay, immediatelyyay afteryay ouryay unionyay, eway ouldshay oceedpray otay Illavay
Avenzalay andyay endspay ouryay irstfay aysday ofyay appinesshay esidebay ethay eautifulbay akelay
earnay ichwhay ityay oodstay.

Inyay ethay eantimemay Iyay ooktay everyyay ecautionpray otay efendday ymay ersonpay inyay asecay ethay
iendfay ouldshay openlyyay attackyay emay. Iyay arriedcay istolspay andyay ayay aggerday
onstantlycay aboutyay emay andyay asway everyay onyay ethay atchway otay eventpray artificeyay, andyay
ybay esethay eansmay ainedgay ayay eatergray egreeday ofyay anquillitytray. Indeedyay, asyay ethay
eriodpay approachedyay, ethay eatthray appearedyay oremay asyay ayay elusionday, otnay otay ebay
egardedray asyay orthyway otay isturbday ymay eacepay, ilewhay ethay appinesshay Iyay opedhay orfay
inyay ymay arriagemay oreway ayay eatergray appearanceyay ofyay ertaintycay asyay ethay ayday ixedfay
orfay itsyay olemnisationsay ewdray earernay andyay Iyay eardhay ityay ontinuallycay okenspay ofyay
asyay anyay occurrenceyay ichwhay onay accidentyay ouldcay ossiblypay eventpray.

Elizabethyay eemedsay appyhay; ymay anquiltray emeanourday ontributedcay eatlygray otay
almcay erhay indmay. Utbay onyay ethay ayday atthay asway otay ulfilfay ymay ishesway andyay ymay
estinyday, eshay asway elancholymay, andyay ayay esentimentpray ofyay evilyay ervadedpay erhay;
andyay erhapspay alsoyay eshay oughtthay ofyay ethay eadfuldray ecretsay ichwhay Iyay adhay
omisedpray otay evealray otay erhay onyay ethay ollowingfay ayday. Ymay atherfay asway inyay ethay
eantimemay overjoyedyay, andyay, inyay ethay ustlebay ofyay eparationpray, onlyyay ecognisedray inyay
ethay elancholymay ofyay ishay iecenay ethay iffidenceday ofyay ayay idebray.

Afteryay ethay eremonycay asway erformedpay ayay argelay artypay assembledyay atyay ymay
ather’sfay, utbay ityay asway agreedyay atthay Elizabethyay andyay Iyay ouldshay ommencecay ouryay
ourneyjay ybay aterway, eepingslay atthay ightnay atyay Evianyay andyay ontinuingcay ouryay
oyagevay onyay ethay ollowingfay ayday. Ethay ayday asway airfay, ethay indway avourablefay;
allyay iledsmay onyay ouryay uptialnay embarkationyay.

Osethay ereway ethay astlay omentsmay ofyay ymay ifelay uringday ichwhay Iyay enjoyedyay ethay
eelingfay ofyay appinesshay. Eway assedpay apidlyray alongyay; ethay unsay asway othay, utbay eway
ereway elteredshay omfray itsyay aysray ybay ayay indkay ofyay anopycay ilewhay eway enjoyedyay ethay
eautybay ofyay ethay enescay, ometimessay onyay oneyay idesay ofyay ethay akelay, erewhay eway awsay
Ontmay Alêvesay, ethay easantplay anksbay ofyay Ontalègremay, andyay atyay ayay istanceday,
urmountingsay allyay, ethay eautifulbay Ontmay Ancblay, andyay ethay assemblageyay ofyay owysnay
ountainsmay atthay inyay ainvay endeavouryay otay emulateyay erhay; ometimessay oastingcay ethay
oppositeyay anksbay, eway awsay ethay ightymay Urajay opposingyay itsyay arkday idesay otay ethay
ambitionyay atthay ouldway uitqay itsyay ativenay ountrycay, andyay anyay almostyay
insurmountableyay arrierbay otay ethay invaderyay owhay ouldshay ishway otay enslaveyay ityay.

Iyay ooktay ethay andhay ofyay Elizabethyay. you“ay areyay orrowfulsay, ymay ovelay. Ahyay! Ifyay
youyay ewknay atwhay Iyay avehay ufferedsay andyay atwhay Iyay aymay yetyay endureyay, youyay ouldway
endeavouryay otay etlay emay astetay ethay uietqay andyay eedomfray omfray espairday atthay isthay
oneyay ayday atyay eastlay ermitspay emay otay enjoyyay.”

e“bay appyhay, ymay earday Ictorvay,” epliedray Elizabethyay; ere“thay isyay, Iyay opehay,
othingnay otay istressday youyay; andyay ebay assuredyay atthay ifyay ayay ivelylay oyjay isyay otnay
aintedpay inyay ymay acefay, ymay earthay isyay ontentedcay. Omethingsay isperswhay otay emay
otnay otay ependday ootay uchmay onyay ethay ospectpray atthay isyay openedyay eforebay usyay, utbay Iyay
illway otnay istenlay otay uchsay ayay inistersay oicevay. Observeyay owhay astfay eway ovemay
alongyay andyay owhay ethay oudsclay, ichwhay ometimessay obscureyay andyay ometimessay iseray
aboveyay ethay omeday ofyay Ontmay Ancblay, enderray isthay enescay ofyay eautybay illstay oremay
interestingyay. Ooklay alsoyay atyay ethay innumerableyay ishfay atthay areyay immingsway inyay
ethay earclay atersway, erewhay eway ancay istinguishday everyyay ebblepay atthay ieslay atyay
ethay ottombay. Atwhay ayay ivineday ayday! Owhay appyhay andyay erenesay allyay aturenay
appearsyay!”

Usthay Elizabethyay endeavouredyay otay ivertday erhay oughtsthay andyay inemay omfray allyay
eflectionray uponyay elancholymay ubjectssay. Utbay erhay empertay asway uctuatingflay;
oyjay orfay ayay ewfay instantsyay oneshay inyay erhay eyesyay, utbay ityay ontinuallycay avegay aceplay
otay istractionday andyay everieray.

Ethay unsay anksay owerlay inyay ethay eavenshay; eway assedpay ethay iverray Ancedray andyay
observedyay itsyay athpay oughthray ethay asmschay ofyay ethay igherhay andyay ethay ensglay ofyay ethay
owerlay illshay. Ethay Alpsyay erehay omecay oserclay otay ethay akelay, andyay eway approachedyay
ethay amphitheatreyay ofyay ountainsmay ichwhay ormsfay itsyay easternyay oundarybay. Ethay
irespay ofyay Evianyay oneshay underyay ethay oodsway atthay urroundedsay ityay andyay ethay angeray
ofyay ountainmay aboveyay ountainmay ybay ichwhay ityay asway overhungyay.

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay ithertohay arriedcay usyay alongyay ithway amazingyay apidityray,
anksay atyay unsetsay otay ayay ightlay eezebray; ethay oftsay airyay ustjay uffledray ethay aterway
andyay ausedcay ayay easantplay otionmay amongyay ethay eestray asyay eway approachedyay ethay
oreshay, omfray ichwhay ityay aftedway ethay ostmay elightfulday entscay ofyay owersflay andyay
ayhay. Ethay unsay anksay eneathbay ethay orizonhay asyay eway andedlay, andyay asyay Iyay ouchedtay
ethay oreshay Iyay eltfay osethay arescay andyay earsfay eviveray ichwhay oonsay ereway otay aspclay
emay andyay ingclay otay emay orfay everyay.




Apterchay 23


Ityay asway eightyay o’clockyay enwhay eway andedlay; eway alkedway orfay ayay ortshay imetay onyay ethay
oreshay, enjoyingyay ethay ansitorytray ightlay, andyay enthay etiredray otay ethay innyay andyay
ontemplatedcay ethay ovelylay enescay ofyay atersway, oodsway, andyay ountainsmay, obscuredyay
inyay arknessday, yetyay illstay isplayingday eirthay ackblay outlinesyay.

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay allenfay inyay ethay outhsay, ownay oseray ithway eatgray iolencevay
inyay ethay estway. Ethay oonmay adhay eachedray erhay ummitsay inyay ethay eavenshay andyay asway
eginningbay otay escendday; ethay oudsclay eptsway acrossyay ityay iftersway anthay ethay
ightflay ofyay ethay ulturevay andyay immedday erhay aysray, ilewhay ethay akelay eflectedray ethay
enescay ofyay ethay usybay eavenshay, enderedray illstay usierbay ybay ethay estlessray avesway
atthay ereway eginningbay otay iseray. Uddenlysay ayay eavyhay ormstay ofyay ainray escendedday.

Iyay adhay eenbay almcay uringday ethay ayday, utbay osay oonsay asyay ightnay obscuredyay ethay
apesshay ofyay objectsyay, ayay ousandthay earsfay aroseyay inyay ymay indmay. Iyay asway anxiousyay
andyay atchfulway, ilewhay ymay ightray andhay aspedgray ayay istolpay ichwhay asway iddenhay inyay
ymay osombay; everyyay oundsay errifiedtay emay, utbay Iyay esolvedray atthay Iyay ouldway ellsay ymay
ifelay earlyday andyay otnay inkshray omfray ethay onflictcay untilyay ymay ownyay ifelay oryay atthay
ofyay ymay adversaryyay asway extinguishedyay.

Elizabethyay observedyay ymay agitationyay orfay omesay imetay inyay imidtay andyay earfulfay ilencesay,
utbay erethay asway omethingsay inyay ymay anceglay ichwhay ommunicatedcay errortay otay erhay, andyay
emblingtray, eshay askedyay, at“whay isyay ityay atthay agitatesyay youyay, ymay earday Ictorvay?
Atwhay isyay ityay youyay earfay?”

oh“ay! Eacepay, eacepay, ymay ovelay,” epliedray Iyay; is“thay ightnay, andyay
allyay illway ebay afesay; utbay isthay ightnay isyay eadfuldray, eryvay eadfuldray.”

Iyay assedpay anyay ourhay inyay isthay atestay ofyay indmay, enwhay uddenlysay Iyay eflectedray owhay
earfulfay ethay ombatcay ichwhay Iyay omentarilymay expectedyay ouldway ebay otay ymay ifeway,
andyay Iyay earnestlyyay entreatedyay erhay otay etireray, esolvingray otnay otay oinjay erhay
untilyay Iyay adhay obtainedyay omesay owledgeknay asyay otay ethay ituationsay ofyay ymay enemyyay.

Eshay eftlay emay, andyay Iyay ontinuedcay omesay imetay alkingway upyay andyay ownday ethay assagespay
ofyay ethay ousehay andyay inspectingyay everyyay ornercay atthay ightmay affordyay ayay etreatray otay
ymay adversaryyay. Utbay Iyay iscoveredday onay acetray ofyay imhay andyay asway eginningbay otay
onjecturecay atthay omesay ortunatefay ancechay adhay intervenedyay otay eventpray ethay
executionyay ofyay ishay enacesmay enwhay uddenlysay Iyay eardhay ayay illshray andyay eadfuldray
eamscray. Ityay amecay omfray ethay oomray intoyay ichwhay Elizabethyay adhay etiredray. Asyay Iyay
eardhay ityay, ethay olewhay uthtray ushedray intoyay ymay indmay, ymay armsyay oppeddray, ethay
otionmay ofyay everyyay usclemay andyay ibrefay asway uspendedsay; Iyay ouldcay eelfay ethay oodblay
icklingtray inyay ymay einsvay andyay inglingtay inyay ethay extremitiesyay ofyay ymay imbslay. Isthay
atestay astedlay utbay orfay anyay instantyay; ethay eamscray asway epeatedray, andyay Iyay ushedray
intoyay ethay oomray.

Eatgray Odgay! Ywhay idday Iyay otnay enthay expireyay! Ywhay amyay Iyay erehay otay elateray ethay
estructionday ofyay ethay estbay opehay andyay ethay urestpay eaturecray onyay earthyay? Eshay asway
erethay, ifelesslay andyay inanimateyay, ownthray acrossyay ethay edbay, erhay eadhay anginghay ownday
andyay erhay alepay andyay istortedday eaturesfay alfhay overedcay ybay erhay airhay. Everywhereyay Iyay
urntay Iyay eesay ethay amesay igure—herfay oodlessblay armsyay andyay elaxedray ormfay ungflay
ybay ethay urderermay onyay itsyay idalbray ierbay. Ouldcay Iyay eholdbay isthay andyay ivelay? Alasyay!
Ifelay isyay obstinateyay andyay ingsclay osestclay erewhay ityay isyay ostmay atedhay. Orfay ayay omentmay
onlyyay idday Iyay oselay ecollectionray; Iyay ellfay enselesssay onyay ethay oundgray.

Enwhay Iyay ecoveredray Iyay oundfay yselfmay urroundedsay ybay ethay eoplepay ofyay ethay innyay; eirthay
ountenancescay expressedyay ayay eathlessbray errortay, utbay ethay orrorhay ofyay othersyay
appearedyay onlyyay asyay ayay ockerymay, ayay adowshay ofyay ethay eelingsfay atthay oppressedyay emay. Iyay
escapedyay omfray emthay otay ethay oomray erewhay aylay ethay odybay ofyay Elizabethyay, ymay ovelay, ymay
ifeway, osay atelylay ivinglay, osay earday, osay orthyway. Eshay adhay eenbay ovedmay omfray ethay
osturepay inyay ichwhay Iyay adhay irstfay eheldbay erhay, andyay ownay, asyay eshay aylay, erhay eadhay uponyay
erhay armyay andyay ayay andkerchiefhay ownthray acrossyay erhay acefay andyay ecknay, Iyay ightmay avehay
upposedsay erhay asleepyay. Iyay ushedray owardstay erhay andyay embracedyay erhay ithway ardouryay, utbay
ethay eadlyday anguorlay andyay oldnesscay ofyay ethay imbslay oldtay emay atthay atwhay Iyay ownay eldhay
inyay ymay armsyay adhay easedcay otay ebay ethay Elizabethyay omwhay Iyay adhay ovedlay andyay erishedchay.
Ethay urderousmay arkmay ofyay ethay iend’sfay aspgray asway onyay erhay ecknay, andyay ethay
eathbray adhay easedcay otay issueyay omfray erhay ipslay.

Ilewhay Iyay illstay unghay overyay erhay inyay ethay agonyyay ofyay espairday, Iyay appenedhay otay ooklay upyay.
Ethay indowsway ofyay ethay oomray adhay eforebay eenbay arkenedday, andyay Iyay eltfay ayay indkay ofyay
anicpay onyay eeingsay ethay alepay yellowyay ightlay ofyay ethay oonmay illuminateyay ethay amberchay.
Ethay uttersshay adhay eenbay ownthray ackbay, andyay ithway ayay ensationsay ofyay orrorhay otnay otay ebay
escribedday, Iyay awsay atyay ethay openyay indowway ayay igurefay ethay ostmay ideoushay andyay abhorredyay.
Ayay ingray asway onyay ethay acefay ofyay ethay onstermay; ehay eemedsay otay eerjay, asyay ithway ishay
iendishfay ingerfay ehay ointedpay owardstay ethay orpsecay ofyay ymay ifeway. Iyay ushedray owardstay
ethay indowway, andyay awingdray ayay istolpay omfray ymay osombay, iredfay; utbay ehay eludedyay emay,
eapedlay omfray ishay ationstay, andyay unningray ithway ethay iftnesssway ofyay ightninglay,
ungedplay intoyay ethay akelay.

Ethay eportray ofyay ethay istolpay oughtbray ayay owdcray intoyay ethay oomray. Iyay ointedpay otay
ethay otspay erewhay ehay adhay isappearedday, andyay eway ollowedfay ethay acktray ithway
oatsbay; etsnay ereway astcay, utbay inyay ainvay. Afteryay assingpay everalsay ourshay, eway
eturnedray opelesshay, ostmay ofyay ymay ompanionscay elievingbay ityay otay avehay eenbay ayay
ormfay onjuredcay upyay ybay ymay ancyfay. Afteryay avinghay andedlay, eythay oceededpray otay
earchsay ethay ountrycay, artiespay oinggay inyay ifferentday irectionsday amongyay ethay
oodsway andyay inesvay.

Iyay attemptedyay otay accompanyyay emthay andyay oceededpray ayay ortshay istanceday omfray ethay
ousehay, utbay ymay eadhay irledwhay oundray, ymay epsstay ereway ikelay osethay ofyay ayay unkendray
anmay, Iyay ellfay atyay astlay inyay ayay atestay ofyay utteryay exhaustionyay; ayay ilmfay overedcay ymay
eyesyay, andyay ymay inskay asway archedpay ithway ethay eathay ofyay everfay. Inyay isthay atestay Iyay
asway arriedcay ackbay andyay acedplay onyay ayay edbay, ardlyhay onsciouscay ofyay atwhay adhay
appenedhay; ymay eyesyay anderedway oundray ethay oomray asyay ifyay otay eeksay omethingsay atthay
Iyay adhay ostlay.

Afteryay anyay intervalyay Iyay aroseyay, andyay asyay ifyay ybay instinctyay, awledcray intoyay ethay oomray
erewhay ethay orpsecay ofyay ymay elovedbay aylay. Erethay ereway omenway eepingway aroundyay; Iyay
unghay overyay ityay andyay oinedjay ymay adsay earstay otay eirsthay; allyay isthay imetay onay
istinctday ideayay esentedpray itselfyay otay ymay indmay, utbay ymay oughtsthay ambledray otay
ariousvay ubjectssay, eflectingray onfusedlycay onyay ymay isfortunesmay andyay eirthay
ausecay. Iyay asway ewilderedbay, inyay ayay oudclay ofyay onderway andyay orrorhay. Ethay eathday
ofyay Illiamway, ethay executionyay ofyay Ustinejay, ethay urdermay ofyay Ervalclay, andyay astlylay
ofyay ymay ifeway; evenyay atyay atthay omentmay Iyay ewknay otnay atthay ymay onlyyay emainingray
iendsfray ereway afesay omfray ethay alignitymay ofyay ethay iendfay; ymay atherfay evenyay ownay
ightmay ebay ithingwray underyay ishay aspgray, andyay Ernestyay ightmay ebay eadday atyay ishay
eetfay. Isthay ideayay ademay emay uddershay andyay ecalledray emay otay actionyay. Iyay artedstay
upyay andyay esolvedray otay eturnray otay Enevagay ithway allyay ossiblepay eedspay.

Erethay ereway onay orseshay otay ebay ocuredpray, andyay Iyay ustmay eturnray ybay ethay akelay; utbay ethay
indway asway unfavourableyay, andyay ethay ainray ellfay inyay orrentstay. Oweverhay, ityay asway
ardlyhay orningmay, andyay Iyay ightmay easonablyray opehay otay arriveyay ybay ightnay. Iyay iredhay enmay
otay owray andyay ooktay anyay oaryay yselfmay, orfay Iyay adhay alwaysyay experiencedyay eliefray omfray
entalmay ormenttay inyay odilybay exerciseyay. Utbay ethay overflowingyay iserymay Iyay ownay eltfay,
andyay ethay excessyay ofyay agitationyay atthay Iyay enduredyay enderedray emay incapableyay ofyay anyyay
exertionyay. Iyay ewthray ownday ethay oaryay, andyay eaninglay ymay eadhay uponyay ymay andshay, avegay ayway
otay everyyay oomyglay ideayay atthay aroseyay. Ifyay Iyay ookedlay upyay, Iyay awsay enesscay ichwhay ereway
amiliarfay otay emay inyay ymay appierhay imetay andyay ichwhay Iyay adhay ontemplatedcay utbay ethay ayday
eforebay inyay ethay ompanycay ofyay erhay owhay asway ownay utbay ayay adowshay andyay ayay ecollectionray.
Earstay eamedstray omfray ymay eyesyay. Ethay ainray adhay easedcay orfay ayay omentmay, andyay Iyay awsay
ethay ishfay ayplay inyay ethay atersway asyay eythay adhay oneday ayay ewfay ourshay eforebay; eythay adhay
enthay eenbay observedyay ybay Elizabethyay. Othingnay isyay osay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay asyay
ayay eatgray andyay uddensay angechay. Ethay unsay ightmay ineshay oryay ethay oudsclay ightmay owerlay,
utbay othingnay ouldcay appearyay otay emay asyay ityay adhay oneday ethay ayday eforebay. Ayay iendfay adhay
atchedsnay omfray emay everyyay opehay ofyay uturefay appinesshay; onay eaturecray adhay everyay eenbay
osay iserablemay asyay Iyay asway; osay ightfulfray anyay eventyay isyay inglesay inyay ethay istoryhay ofyay
anmay.

Utbay ywhay ouldshay Iyay elldway uponyay ethay incidentsyay atthay ollowedfay isthay astlay
overwhelmingyay eventyay? Inemay ashay eenbay ayay aletay ofyay orrorshay; Iyay avehay eachedray eirthay
acme_ay_, andyay atwhay Iyay ustmay ownay elateray ancay utbay ebay edioustay otay youyay. Owknay
atthay, oneyay ybay oneyay, ymay iendsfray ereway atchedsnay awayyay; Iyay asway eftlay esolateday. Ymay
ownyay engthstray isyay exhaustedyay, andyay Iyay ustmay elltay, inyay ayay ewfay ordsway, atwhay emainsray ofyay
ymay ideoushay arrationnay.

Iyay arrivedyay atyay Enevagay. Ymay atherfay andyay Ernestyay yetyay ivedlay, utbay ethay ormerfay unksay
underyay ethay idingstay atthay Iyay orebay. Iyay eesay imhay ownay, excellentyay andyay enerablevay oldyay
anmay! Ishay eyesyay anderedway inyay acancyvay, orfay eythay adhay ostlay eirthay armchay andyay eirthay
elight—hisday Elizabethyay, ishay oremay anthay aughterday, omwhay ehay otedday onyay ithway
allyay atthay affectionyay ichwhay ayay anmay eelsfay, owhay inyay ethay eclineday ofyay ifelay, avinghay
ewfay affectionsyay, ingsclay oremay earnestlyyay otay osethay atthay emainray. Ursedcay, ursedcay
ebay ethay iendfay atthay oughtbray iserymay onyay ishay eygray airshay andyay oomedday imhay otay asteway
inyay etchednesswray! Ehay ouldcay otnay ivelay underyay ethay orrorshay atthay ereway accumulatedyay
aroundyay imhay; ethay ingsspray ofyay existenceyay uddenlysay avegay ayway; ehay asway unableyay otay
iseray omfray ishay edbay, andyay inyay ayay ewfay aysday ehay iedday inyay ymay armsyay.

Atwhay enthay ecamebay ofyay emay? Iyay owknay otnay; Iyay ostlay ensationsay, andyay ainschay andyay
arknessday ereway ethay onlyyay objectsyay atthay essedpray uponyay emay. Ometimessay,
indeedyay, Iyay eamtdray atthay Iyay anderedway inyay oweryflay eadowsmay andyay easantplay alesvay
ithway ethay iendsfray ofyay ymay youthyay, utbay Iyay awokeyay andyay oundfay yselfmay inyay ayay
ungeonday. Elancholymay ollowedfay, utbay ybay egreesday Iyay ainedgay ayay earclay
onceptioncay ofyay ymay iseriesmay andyay ituationsay andyay asway enthay eleasedray omfray ymay
isonpray. Orfay eythay adhay alledcay emay admay, andyay uringday anymay onthsmay, asyay Iyay
understoodyay, ayay olitarysay ellcay adhay eenbay ymay abitationhay.

Ibertylay, oweverhay, adhay eenbay ayay uselessyay iftgay otay emay, adhay Iyay otnay, asyay Iyay
awakenedyay otay easonray, atyay ethay amesay imetay awakenedyay otay evengeray. Asyay ethay
emorymay ofyay astpay isfortunesmay essedpray uponyay emay, Iyay eganbay otay eflectray onyay eirthay
ause—thecay onstermay omwhay Iyay adhay eatedcray, ethay iserablemay ondæmay omwhay Iyay adhay
entsay abroadyay intoyay ethay orldway orfay ymay estructionday. Iyay asway ossessedpay ybay ayay
addeningmay ageray enwhay Iyay oughtthay ofyay imhay, andyay esiredday andyay ardentlyyay ayedpray
atthay Iyay ightmay avehay imhay ithinway ymay aspgray otay eakwray ayay eatgray andyay ignalsay
evengeray onyay ishay ursedcay eadhay.

Ornay idday ymay atehay onglay onfinecay itselfyay otay uselessyay ishesway; Iyay eganbay otay
eflectray onyay ethay estbay eansmay ofyay ecuringsay imhay; andyay orfay isthay urposepay, aboutyay
ayay onthmay afteryay ymay eleaseray, Iyay epairedray otay ayay iminalcray udgejay inyay ethay owntay
andyay oldtay imhay atthay Iyay adhay anyay accusationyay otay akemay, atthay Iyay ewknay ethay
estroyerday ofyay ymay amilyfay, andyay atthay Iyay equiredray imhay otay exertyay ishay olewhay
authorityyay orfay ethay apprehensionyay ofyay ethay urderermay.

Ethay agistratemay istenedlay otay emay ithway attentionyay andyay indnesskay. e“bay
assuredyay, irsay,” aidsay ehay, o“nay ainspay oryay exertionsyay onyay ymay artpay allshay
ebay aredspay otay iscoverday ethay illainvay.”

i“ay ankthay youyay,” epliedray Iyay; isten“lay, ereforethay, otay ethay
epositionday atthay Iyay avehay otay akemay. Ityay isyay indeedyay ayay aletay osay angestray atthay Iyay
ouldshay earfay youyay ouldway otnay editcray ityay ereway erethay otnay omethingsay inyay uthtray
ichwhay, oweverhay onderfulway, orcesfay onvictioncay. Ethay orystay isyay ootay onnectedcay otay
ebay istakenmay orfay ayay eamdray, andyay Iyay avehay onay otivemay orfay alsehoodfay.” Ymay
annermay asyay Iyay usthay addressedyay imhay asway impressiveyay utbay almcay; Iyay adhay ormedfay inyay ymay
ownyay earthay ayay esolutionray otay ursuepay ymay estroyerday otay eathday, andyay isthay urposepay
uietedqay ymay agonyyay andyay orfay anyay intervalyay econciledray emay otay ifelay. Iyay ownay elatedray
ymay istoryhay ieflybray utbay ithway irmnessfay andyay ecisionpray, arkingmay ethay atesday ithway
accuracyyay andyay evernay eviatingday intoyay invectiveyay oryay exclamationyay.

Ethay agistratemay appearedyay atyay irstfay erfectlypay incredulousyay, utbay asyay Iyay ontinuedcay
ehay ecamebay oremay attentiveyay andyay interestedyay; Iyay awsay imhay ometimessay uddershay ithway
orrorhay; atyay othersyay ayay ivelylay urprisesay, unmingledyay ithway isbeliefday, asway aintedpay
onyay ishay ountenancecay.

Enwhay Iyay adhay oncludedcay ymay arrationnay, Iyay aidsay, is“thay isyay ethay eingbay omwhay Iyay
accuseyay andyay orfay osewhay eizuresay andyay unishmentpay Iyay allcay uponyay youyay otay exertyay youryay
olewhay owerpay. Ityay isyay youryay utyday asyay ayay agistratemay, andyay Iyay elievebay andyay opehay atthay
youryay eelingsfay asyay ayay anmay illway otnay evoltray omfray ethay executionyay ofyay osethay
unctionsfay onyay isthay occasionyay.”

Isthay addressyay ausedcay ayay onsiderablecay angechay inyay ethay ysiognomyphay ofyay ymay ownyay
auditoryay. Ehay adhay eardhay ymay orystay ithway atthay alfhay indkay ofyay eliefbay atthay isyay ivengay
otay ayay aletay ofyay iritsspay andyay upernaturalsay eventsyay; utbay enwhay ehay asway alledcay uponyay
otay actyay officiallyyay inyay onsequencecay, ethay olewhay idetay ofyay ishay incredulityyay
eturnedray. Ehay, oweverhay, answeredyay ildlymay, i“ay ouldway illinglyway affordyay youyay
everyyay aidyay inyay youryay ursuitpay, utbay ethay eaturecray ofyay omwhay youyay eakspay appearsyay otay
avehay owerspay ichwhay ouldway utpay allyay ymay exertionsyay otay efianceday. Owhay ancay ollowfay anyay
animalyay ichwhay ancay aversetray ethay easay ofyay iceyay andyay inhabityay avescay andyay ensday erewhay
onay anmay ouldway enturevay otay intrudeyay? Esidesbay, omesay onthsmay avehay elapsedyay incesay
ethay ommissioncay ofyay ishay imescray, andyay onay oneyay ancay onjecturecay otay atwhay aceplay ehay
ashay anderedway oryay atwhay egionray ehay aymay ownay inhabityay.”

i“ay oday otnay oubtday atthay ehay overshay earnay ethay otspay ichwhay Iyay inhabityay, andyay ifyay
ehay ashay indeedyay akentay efugeray inyay ethay Alpsyay, ehay aymay ebay untedhay ikelay ethay amoischay
andyay estroyedday asyay ayay eastbay ofyay eypray. Utbay Iyay erceivepay youryay oughtsthay; youyay oday otnay
editcray ymay arrativenay andyay oday otnay intendyay otay ursuepay ymay enemyyay ithway ethay
unishmentpay ichwhay isyay ishay esertday.”

Asyay Iyay okespay, ageray arkledspay inyay ymay eyesyay; ethay agistratemay asway intimidatedyay.
you“ay areyay istakenmay,” aidsay ehay. i“ay illway exertyay yselfmay, andyay ifyay
ityay isyay inyay ymay owerpay otay eizesay ethay onstermay, ebay assuredyay atthay ehay allshay uffersay
unishmentpay oportionatepray otay ishay imescray. Utbay Iyay earfay, omfray atwhay youyay avehay
yourselfyay escribedday otay ebay ishay opertiespray, atthay isthay illway ovepray
impracticableyay; andyay usthay, ilewhay everyyay operpray easuremay isyay ursuedpay, youyay ouldshay
akemay upyay youryay indmay otay isappointmentday.”

at“thay annotcay ebay; utbay allyay atthay Iyay ancay aysay illway ebay ofyay ittlelay availyay. Ymay
evengeray isyay ofyay onay omentmay otay youyay; yetyay, ilewhay Iyay allowyay ityay otay ebay ayay icevay, Iyay
onfesscay atthay ityay isyay ethay evouringday andyay onlyyay assionpay ofyay ymay oulsay. Ymay ageray
isyay unspeakableyay enwhay Iyay eflectray atthay ethay urderermay, omwhay Iyay avehay urnedtay
ooselay uponyay ocietysay, illstay existsyay. Youyay efuseray ymay ustjay emandday; Iyay avehay
utbay oneyay esourceray, andyay Iyay evoteday yselfmay, eitheryay inyay ymay ifelay oryay eathday, otay
ishay estructionday.”

Iyay embledtray ithway excessyay ofyay agitationyay asyay Iyay aidsay isthay; erethay asway ayay enzyfray
inyay ymay annermay, andyay omethingsay, Iyay oubtday otnay, ofyay atthay aughtyhay iercenessfay
ichwhay ethay artyrsmay ofyay oldyay areyay aidsay otay avehay ossessedpay. Utbay otay ayay Enevangay
agistratemay, osewhay indmay asway occupiedyay ybay arfay otheryay ideasyay anthay osethay ofyay
evotionday andyay eroismhay, isthay elevationyay ofyay indmay adhay uchmay ethay appearanceyay ofyay
adnessmay. Ehay endeavouredyay otay oothesay emay asyay ayay ursenay oesday ayay ildchay andyay
evertedray otay ymay aletay asyay ethay effectsyay ofyay eliriumday.

an“may,” Iyay iedcray, ow“hay ignorantyay artyay outhay inyay ythay idepray ofyay
isdomway! Easecay; youyay owknay otnay atwhay ityay isyay youyay aysay.”

Iyay okebray omfray ethay ousehay angryyay andyay isturbedday andyay etiredray otay editatemay onyay
omesay otheryay odemay ofyay actionyay.




Apterchay 24


Ymay esentpray ituationsay asway oneyay inyay ichwhay allyay oluntaryvay oughtthay asway
allowedsway upyay andyay ostlay. Iyay asway urriedhay awayyay ybay uryfay; evengeray aloneyay
endowedyay emay ithway engthstray andyay omposurecay; ityay ouldedmay ymay eelingsfay andyay
allowedyay emay otay ebay alculatingcay andyay almcay atyay eriodspay enwhay otherwiseyay
eliriumday oryay eathday ouldway avehay eenbay ymay ortionpay.

Ymay irstfay esolutionray asway otay uitqay Enevagay orfay everyay; ymay ountrycay, ichwhay, enwhay Iyay
asway appyhay andyay elovedbay, asway earday otay emay, ownay, inyay ymay adversityyay, ecamebay
atefulhay. Iyay ovidedpray yselfmay ithway ayay umsay ofyay oneymay, ogethertay ithway ayay ewfay ewelsjay
ichwhay adhay elongedbay otay ymay othermay, andyay epartedday.

Andyay ownay ymay anderingsway eganbay ichwhay areyay otay easecay utbay ithway ifelay. Iyay avehay
aversedtray ayay astvay ortionpay ofyay ethay earthyay andyay avehay enduredyay allyay ethay ardshipshay
ichwhay avellerstray inyay esertsday andyay arbarousbay ountriescay areyay ontway otay eetmay. Owhay Iyay
avehay ivedlay Iyay ardlyhay owknay; anymay imestay avehay Iyay etchedstray ymay ailingfay imbslay uponyay
ethay andysay ainplay andyay ayedpray orfay eathday. Utbay evengeray eptkay emay aliveyay; Iyay aredday
otnay ieday andyay eavelay ymay adversaryyay inyay eingbay.

Enwhay Iyay uittedqay Enevagay ymay irstfay abourlay asway otay aingay omesay ueclay ybay ichwhay Iyay
ightmay acetray ethay epsstay ofyay ymay iendishfay enemyyay. Utbay ymay anplay asway unsettledyay,
andyay Iyay anderedway anymay ourshay oundray ethay onfinescay ofyay ethay owntay, uncertainyay
atwhay athpay Iyay ouldshay ursuepay. Asyay ightnay approachedyay Iyay oundfay yselfmay atyay ethay
entranceyay ofyay ethay emeterycay erewhay Illiamway, Elizabethyay, andyay ymay atherfay
eposedray. Iyay enteredyay ityay andyay approachedyay ethay ombtay ichwhay arkedmay eirthay
avesgray. Everythingyay asway ilentsay exceptyay ethay eaveslay ofyay ethay eestray, ichwhay
ereway entlygay agitatedyay ybay ethay indway; ethay ightnay asway earlynay arkday, andyay ethay
enescay ouldway avehay eenbay olemnsay andyay affectingyay evenyay otay anyay uninterestedyay
observeryay. Ethay iritsspay ofyay ethay epartedday eemedsay otay itflay aroundyay andyay otay
astcay ayay adowshay, ichwhay asway eltfay utbay otnay eensay, aroundyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay
ournermay.

Ethay eepday iefgray ichwhay isthay enescay adhay atyay irstfay excitedyay uicklyqay avegay ayway otay
ageray andyay espairday. Eythay ereway eadday, andyay Iyay ivedlay; eirthay urderermay alsoyay ivedlay,
andyay otay estroyday imhay Iyay ustmay agdray outyay ymay earyway existenceyay. Iyay eltknay onyay ethay assgray
andyay issedkay ethay earthyay andyay ithway uiveringqay ipslay exclaimedyay, y“bay ethay
acredsay earthyay onyay ichwhay Iyay eelknay, ybay ethay adesshay atthay anderway earnay emay, ybay ethay
eepday andyay eternalyay iefgray atthay Iyay eelfay, Iyay earsway; andyay ybay eethay, Oyay Ightnay, andyay ethay
iritsspay atthay esidepray overyay eethay, otay ursuepay ethay ondæmay owhay ausedcay isthay iserymay,
untilyay ehay oryay Iyay allshay erishpay inyay ortalmay onflictcay. Orfay isthay urposepay Iyay illway
eservepray ymay ifelay; otay executeyay isthay earday evengeray illway Iyay againyay eholdbay ethay unsay
andyay eadtray ethay eengray erbagehay ofyay earthyay, ichwhay otherwiseyay ouldshay anishvay omfray ymay
eyesyay orfay everyay. Andyay Iyay allcay onyay youyay, iritsspay ofyay ethay eadday, andyay onyay youyay, anderingway
inistersmay ofyay engeancevay, otay aidyay andyay onductcay emay inyay ymay orkway. Etlay ethay ursedcay
andyay ellishhay onstermay inkdray eepday ofyay agonyyay; etlay imhay eelfay ethay espairday atthay ownay
ormentstay emay.”

Iyay adhay egunbay ymay adjurationyay ithway olemnitysay andyay anyay aweyay ichwhay almostyay assuredyay emay
atthay ethay adesshay ofyay ymay urderedmay iendsfray eardhay andyay approvedyay ymay evotionday, utbay
ethay uriesfay ossessedpay emay asyay Iyay oncludedcay, andyay ageray okedchay ymay utteranceyay.

Iyay asway answeredyay oughthray ethay illnessstay ofyay ightnay ybay ayay oudlay andyay iendishfay
aughlay. Ityay angray onyay ymay earsyay onglay andyay eavilyhay; ethay ountainsmay e-echoedray
ityay, andyay Iyay eltfay asyay ifyay allyay ellhay urroundedsay emay ithway ockerymay andyay aughterlay.
Urelysay inyay atthay omentmay Iyay ouldshay avehay eenbay ossessedpay ybay enzyfray andyay avehay
estroyedday ymay iserablemay existenceyay utbay atthay ymay owvay asway eardhay andyay atthay Iyay
asway eservedray orfay engeancevay. Ethay aughterlay iedday awayyay, enwhay ayay ell-knownway
andyay abhorredyay oicevay, apparentlyyay oseclay otay ymay earyay, addressedyay emay inyay anyay
audibleyay isperwhay, i“ay amyay atisfiedsay, iserablemay etchwray! Youyay avehay
eterminedday otay ivelay, andyay Iyay amyay atisfiedsay.”

Iyay artedday owardstay ethay otspay omfray ichwhay ethay oundsay oceededpray, utbay ethay evilday
eludedyay ymay aspgray. Uddenlysay ethay oadbray iskday ofyay ethay oonmay aroseyay andyay oneshay
ullfay uponyay ishay astlyghay andyay istortedday apeshay asyay ehay edflay ithway oremay anthay
ortalmay eedspay.

Iyay ursuedpay imhay, andyay orfay anymay onthsmay isthay ashay eenbay ymay asktay. Uidedgay ybay ayay
ightslay ueclay, Iyay ollowedfay ethay indingsway ofyay ethay Onerhay, utbay ainlyvay. Ethay
ueblay Editerraneanmay appearedyay, andyay ybay ayay angestray ancechay, Iyay awsay ethay iendfay
enteryay ybay ightnay andyay idehay imselfhay inyay ayay esselvay oundbay orfay ethay Ackblay Easay. Iyay
ooktay ymay assagepay inyay ethay amesay ipshay, utbay ehay escapedyay, Iyay owknay otnay owhay.

Amidstyay ethay ildsway ofyay Artarytay andyay Ussiaray, althoughyay ehay illstay evadedyay emay, Iyay
avehay everyay ollowedfay inyay ishay acktray. Ometimessay ethay easantspay, aredscay ybay
isthay orridhay apparitionyay, informedyay emay ofyay ishay athpay; ometimessay ehay imselfhay,
owhay earedfay atthay ifyay Iyay ostlay allyay acetray ofyay imhay Iyay ouldshay espairday andyay ieday,
eftlay omesay arkmay otay uidegay emay. Ethay owssnay escendedday onyay ymay eadhay, andyay Iyay awsay
ethay intpray ofyay ishay ugehay epstay onyay ethay itewhay ainplay. Otay youyay irstfay enteringyay
onyay ifelay, otay omwhay arecay isyay ewnay andyay agonyyay unknownyay, owhay ancay youyay understandyay
atwhay Iyay avehay eltfay andyay illstay eelfay? Oldcay, antway, andyay atiguefay ereway ethay
eastlay ainspay ichwhay Iyay asway estinedday otay endureyay; Iyay asway ursedcay ybay omesay evilday
andyay arriedcay aboutyay ithway emay ymay eternalyay ellhay; yetyay illstay ayay iritspay ofyay oodgay
ollowedfay andyay irectedday ymay epsstay andyay enwhay Iyay ostmay urmuredmay ouldway uddenlysay
extricateyay emay omfray eeminglysay insurmountableyay ifficultiesday. Ometimessay,
enwhay aturenay, overcomeyay ybay ungerhay, anksay underyay ethay exhaustionyay, ayay epastray
asway eparedpray orfay emay inyay ethay esertday atthay estoredray andyay inspiritedyay emay. Ethay
arefay asway, indeedyay, oarsecay, uchsay asyay ethay easantspay ofyay ethay ountrycay ateyay, utbay
Iyay illway otnay oubtday atthay ityay asway etsay erethay ybay ethay iritsspay atthay Iyay adhay
invokedyay otay aidyay emay. Oftenyay, enwhay allyay asway ydray, ethay eavenshay oudlessclay, andyay
Iyay asway archedpay ybay irstthay, ayay ightslay oudclay ouldway edimbay ethay yskay, edshay ethay
ewfay opsdray atthay evivedray emay, andyay anishvay.

Iyay ollowedfay, enwhay Iyay ouldcay, ethay oursescay ofyay ethay iversray; utbay ethay ondæmay
enerallygay avoidedyay esethay, asyay ityay asway erehay atthay ethay opulationpay ofyay ethay
ountrycay ieflychay ollectedcay. Inyay otheryay acesplay umanhay eingsbay ereway eldomsay
eensay, andyay Iyay enerallygay ubsistedsay onyay ethay ildway animalsyay atthay ossedcray ymay
athpay. Iyay adhay oneymay ithway emay andyay ainedgay ethay iendshipfray ofyay ethay illagersvay
ybay istributingday ityay; oryay Iyay oughtbray ithway emay omesay oodfay atthay Iyay adhay illedkay,
ichwhay, afteryay akingtay ayay allsmay artpay, Iyay alwaysyay esentedpray otay osethay owhay adhay
ovidedpray emay ithway irefay andyay utensilsyay orfay ookingcay.

Ymay ifelay, asyay ityay assedpay usthay, asway indeedyay atefulhay otay emay, andyay ityay asway uringday
eepslay aloneyay atthay Iyay ouldcay astetay oyjay. Oyay essedblay eepslay! Oftenyay, enwhay ostmay
iserablemay, Iyay anksay otay eposeray, andyay ymay eamsdray ulledlay emay evenyay otay aptureray. Ethay
iritsspay atthay uardedgay emay adhay ovidedpray esethay omentsmay, oryay atherray ourshay, ofyay
appinesshay atthay Iyay ightmay etainray engthstray otay ulfilfay ymay ilgrimagepay. Eprivedday ofyay
isthay espiteray, Iyay ouldshay avehay unksay underyay ymay ardshipshay. Uringday ethay ayday Iyay asway
ustainedsay andyay inspiritedyay ybay ethay opehay ofyay ightnay, orfay inyay eepslay Iyay awsay ymay
iendsfray, ymay ifeway, andyay ymay elovedbay ountrycay; againyay Iyay awsay ethay enevolentbay
ountenancecay ofyay ymay atherfay, eardhay ethay ilversay onestay ofyay ymay Elizabeth’syay
oicevay, andyay eheldbay Ervalclay enjoyingyay ealthhay andyay youthyay. Oftenyay, enwhay eariedway ybay
ayay oilsometay archmay, Iyay ersuadedpay yselfmay atthay Iyay asway eamingdray untilyay ightnay ouldshay
omecay andyay atthay Iyay ouldshay enthay enjoyyay ealityray inyay ethay armsyay ofyay ymay earestday
iendsfray. Atwhay agonisingyay ondnessfay idday Iyay eelfay orfay emthay! Owhay idday Iyay ingclay otay
eirthay earday ormsfay, asyay ometimessay eythay auntedhay evenyay ymay akingway ourshay, andyay
ersuadepay yselfmay atthay eythay illstay ivedlay! Atyay uchsay omentsmay engeancevay, atthay
urnedbay ithinway emay, iedday inyay ymay earthay, andyay Iyay ursuedpay ymay athpay owardstay ethay
estructionday ofyay ethay ondæmay oremay asyay ayay asktay enjoinedyay ybay eavenhay, asyay ethay
echanicalmay impulseyay ofyay omesay owerpay ofyay ichwhay Iyay asway unconsciousyay, anthay asyay ethay
ardentyay esireday ofyay ymay oulsay.

Atwhay ishay eelingsfay ereway omwhay Iyay ursuedpay Iyay annotcay owknay. Ometimessay, indeedyay, ehay
eftlay arksmay inyay itingwray onyay ethay arksbay ofyay ethay eestray oryay utcay inyay onestay atthay uidedgay
emay andyay instigatedyay ymay uryfay. y“may eignray isyay otnay yetyay
over”—theseyay ordsway ereway egiblelay inyay oneyay ofyay esethay
inscriptions—“youyay ivelay, andyay ymay owerpay isyay ompletecay. Ollowfay emay; Iyay
eeksay ethay everlastingyay icesyay ofyay ethay orthnay, erewhay youyay illway eelfay ethay iserymay ofyay
oldcay andyay ostfray, otay ichwhay Iyay amyay impassiveyay. Youyay illway indfay earnay isthay aceplay, ifyay
youyay ollowfay otnay ootay ardilytay, ayay eadday arehay; eatyay andyay ebay efreshedray. Omecay onyay, ymay
enemyyay; eway avehay yetyay otay estlewray orfay ouryay iveslay, utbay anymay ardhay andyay iserablemay
ourshay ustmay youyay endureyay untilyay atthay eriodpay allshay arriveyay.”

Offingscay evilday! Againyay oday Iyay owvay engeancevay; againyay oday Iyay evoteday eethay,
iserablemay iendfay, otay orturetay andyay eathday. Evernay illway Iyay ivegay upyay ymay earchsay
untilyay ehay oryay Iyay erishpay; andyay enthay ithway atwhay ecstasyyay allshay Iyay oinjay ymay
Elizabethyay andyay ymay epartedday iendsfray, owhay evenyay ownay eparepray orfay emay ethay
ewardray ofyay ymay edioustay oiltay andyay orriblehay ilgrimagepay!

Asyay Iyay illstay ursuedpay ymay ourneyjay otay ethay orthwardnay, ethay owssnay ickenedthay andyay ethay
oldcay increasedyay inyay ayay egreeday almostyay ootay everesay otay upportsay. Ethay easantspay ereway
utshay upyay inyay eirthay ovelshay, andyay onlyyay ayay ewfay ofyay ethay ostmay ardyhay enturedvay orthfay otay
eizesay ethay animalsyay omwhay arvationstay adhay orcedfay omfray eirthay iding-placeshay otay
eeksay orfay eypray. Ethay iversray ereway overedcay ithway iceyay, andyay onay ishfay ouldcay ebay
ocuredpray; andyay usthay Iyay asway utcay offyay omfray ymay iefchay articleyay ofyay aintenancemay.

Ethay iumphtray ofyay ymay enemyyay increasedyay ithway ethay ifficultyday ofyay ymay abourslay. Oneyay
inscriptionyay atthay ehay eftlay asway inyay esethay ordsway: epare“pray! Youryay oilstay
onlyyay eginbay; apwray yourselfyay inyay ursfay andyay ovidepray oodfay, orfay eway allshay oonsay enteryay
uponyay ayay ourneyjay erewhay youryay ufferingssay illway atisfysay ymay everlastingyay
atredhay.”

Ymay ouragecay andyay erseverancepay ereway invigoratedyay ybay esethay offingscay ordsway; Iyay
esolvedray otnay otay ailfay inyay ymay urposepay, andyay allingcay onyay Eavenhay otay upportsay
emay, Iyay ontinuedcay ithway unabatedyay ervourfay otay aversetray immenseyay esertsday,
untilyay ethay oceanyay appearedyay atyay ayay istanceday andyay ormedfay ethay utmostyay oundarybay
ofyay ethay orizonhay. Ohyay! Owhay unlikeyay ityay asway otay ethay ueblay easonssay ofyay ethay
outhsay! Overedcay ithway iceyay, ityay asway onlyyay otay ebay istinguishedday omfray andlay ybay
itsyay uperiorsay ildnessway andyay uggednessray. Ethay Eeksgray eptway orfay oyjay enwhay
eythay eheldbay ethay Editerraneanmay omfray ethay illshay ofyay Asiayay, andyay ailedhay ithway
aptureray ethay oundarybay ofyay eirthay oilstay. Iyay idday otnay eepway, utbay Iyay eltknay ownday
andyay ithway ayay ullfay earthay ankedthay ymay uidinggay iritspay orfay onductingcay emay inyay
afetysay otay ethay aceplay erewhay Iyay opedhay, otwithstandingnay ymay adversary’syay ibegay,
otay eetmay andyay applegray ithway imhay.

Omesay eeksway eforebay isthay eriodpay Iyay adhay ocuredpray ayay edgeslay andyay ogsday andyay usthay
aversedtray ethay owssnay ithway inconceivableyay eedspay. Iyay owknay otnay etherwhay ethay
iendfay ossessedpay ethay amesay advantagesyay, utbay Iyay oundfay atthay, asyay eforebay Iyay adhay
ailyday ostlay oundgray inyay ethay ursuitpay, Iyay ownay ainedgay onyay imhay, osay uchmay osay atthay
enwhay Iyay irstfay awsay ethay oceanyay ehay asway utbay oneyay ay’sday ourneyjay inyay advanceyay, andyay
Iyay opedhay otay interceptyay imhay eforebay ehay ouldshay eachray ethay eachbay. Ithway ewnay
ouragecay, ereforethay, Iyay essedpray onyay, andyay inyay otway aysday arrivedyay atyay ayay etchedwray
amlethay onyay ethay eashoresay. Iyay inquiredyay ofyay ethay inhabitantsyay oncerningcay ethay
iendfay andyay ainedgay accurateyay informationyay. Ayay iganticgay onstermay, eythay aidsay,
adhay arrivedyay ethay ightnay eforebay, armedyay ithway ayay ungay andyay anymay istolspay,
uttingpay otay ightflay ethay inhabitantsyay ofyay ayay olitarysay ottagecay oughthray earfay ofyay
ishay errifictay appearanceyay. Ehay adhay arriedcay offyay eirthay orestay ofyay interway
oodfay, andyay acingplay ityay inyay ayay edgeslay, otay awdray ichwhay ehay adhay eizedsay onyay ayay
umerousnay ovedray ofyay ainedtray ogsday, ehay adhay arnessedhay emthay, andyay ethay amesay
ightnay, otay ethay oyjay ofyay ethay orror-struckhay illagersvay, adhay ursuedpay ishay
ourneyjay acrossyay ethay easay inyay ayay irectionday atthay edlay otay onay andlay; andyay eythay
onjecturedcay atthay ehay ustmay eedilyspay ebay estroyedday ybay ethay eakingbray ofyay ethay
iceyay oryay ozenfray ybay ethay eternalyay ostsfray.

Onyay earinghay isthay informationyay Iyay ufferedsay ayay emporarytay accessyay ofyay espairday.
Ehay adhay escapedyay emay, andyay Iyay ustmay ommencecay ayay estructiveday andyay almostyay endlessyay
ourneyjay acrossyay ethay ountainousmay icesyay ofyay ethay oceanyay, amidstyay oldcay atthay ewfay
ofyay ethay inhabitantsyay ouldcay onglay endureyay andyay ichwhay Iyay, ethay ativenay ofyay ayay
enialgay andyay unnysay imateclay, ouldcay otnay opehay otay urvivesay. Yetyay atyay ethay ideayay
atthay ethay iendfay ouldshay ivelay andyay ebay iumphanttray, ymay ageray andyay engeancevay
eturnedray, andyay ikelay ayay ightymay idetay, overwhelmedyay everyyay otheryay eelingfay.
Afteryay ayay ightslay eposeray, uringday ichwhay ethay iritsspay ofyay ethay eadday overedhay
oundray andyay instigatedyay emay otay oiltay andyay evengeray, Iyay eparedpray orfay ymay ourneyjay.

Iyay exchangedyay ymay and-sledgelay orfay oneyay ashionedfay orfay ethay inequalitiesyay ofyay
ethay Ozenfray Oceanyay, andyay urchasingpay ayay entifulplay ockstay ofyay ovisionspray, Iyay
epartedday omfray andlay.

Iyay annotcay uessgay owhay anymay aysday avehay assedpay incesay enthay, utbay Iyay avehay enduredyay
iserymay ichwhay othingnay utbay ethay eternalyay entimentsay ofyay ayay ustjay etributionray
urningbay ithinway ymay earthay ouldcay avehay enabledyay emay otay upportsay. Immenseyay andyay
uggedray ountainsmay ofyay iceyay oftenyay arredbay upyay ymay assagepay, andyay Iyay oftenyay eardhay
ethay underthay ofyay ethay oundgray easay, ichwhay eatenedthray ymay estructionday. Utbay
againyay ethay ostfray amecay andyay ademay ethay athspay ofyay ethay easay ecuresay.

Ybay ethay uantityqay ofyay ovisionpray ichwhay Iyay adhay onsumedcay, Iyay ouldshay uessgay atthay
Iyay adhay assedpay eethray eeksway inyay isthay ourneyjay; andyay ethay ontinualcay otractionpray
ofyay opehay, eturningray ackbay uponyay ethay earthay, oftenyay ungwray itterbay opsdray ofyay
espondencyday andyay iefgray omfray ymay eyesyay. Espairday adhay indeedyay almostyay ecuredsay
erhay eypray, andyay Iyay ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay eneathbay isthay iserymay. Onceyay, afteryay
ethay oorpay animalsyay atthay onveyedcay emay adhay ithway incredibleyay oiltay ainedgay ethay
ummitsay ofyay ayay opingslay iceyay ountainmay, andyay oneyay, inkingsay underyay ishay atiguefay,
iedday, Iyay iewedvay ethay expanseyay eforebay emay ithway anguishyay, enwhay uddenlysay ymay eyeyay
aughtcay ayay arkday eckspay uponyay ethay uskyday ainplay. Iyay ainedstray ymay ightsay otay
iscoverday atwhay ityay ouldcay ebay andyay utteredyay ayay ildway ycray ofyay ecstasyyay enwhay Iyay
istinguishedday ayay edgeslay andyay ethay istortedday oportionspray ofyay ayay ell-knownway
ormfay ithinway. Ohyay! Ithway atwhay ayay urningbay ushgay idday opehay evisitray ymay earthay!
Armway earstay illedfay ymay eyesyay, ichwhay Iyay astilyhay ipedway awayyay, atthay eythay ightmay
otnay interceptyay ethay iewvay Iyay adhay ofyay ethay ondæmay; utbay illstay ymay ightsay asway
immedday ybay ethay urningbay opsdray, untilyay, ivinggay ayway otay ethay emotionsyay atthay
oppressedyay emay, Iyay eptway aloudyay.

Utbay isthay asway otnay ethay imetay orfay elayday; Iyay isencumberedday ethay ogsday ofyay eirthay
eadday ompanioncay, avegay emthay ayay entifulplay ortionpay ofyay oodfay, andyay afteryay anyay
our’shay estray, ichwhay asway absolutelyyay ecessarynay, andyay yetyay ichwhay asway itterlybay
irksomeyay otay emay, Iyay ontinuedcay ymay outeray. Ethay edgeslay asway illstay isiblevay, ornay
idday Iyay againyay oselay ightsay ofyay ityay exceptyay atyay ethay omentsmay enwhay orfay ayay ortshay
imetay omesay ice-rockyay oncealedcay ityay ithway itsyay interveningyay agscray. Iyay indeedyay
erceptiblypay ainedgay onyay ityay, andyay enwhay, afteryay earlynay otway aysday’ ourneyjay, Iyay
eheldbay ymay enemyyay atyay onay oremay anthay ayay ilemay istantday, ymay earthay oundedbay ithinway
emay.

Utbay ownay, enwhay Iyay appearedyay almostyay ithinway aspgray ofyay ymay oefay, ymay opeshay ereway
uddenlysay extinguishedyay, andyay Iyay ostlay allyay acetray ofyay imhay oremay utterlyyay anthay Iyay adhay
everyay oneday eforebay. Ayay oundgray easay asway eardhay; ethay underthay ofyay itsyay ogresspray, asyay
ethay atersway olledray andyay elledsway eneathbay emay, ecamebay everyyay omentmay oremay ominousyay
andyay errifictay. Iyay essedpray onyay, utbay inyay ainvay. Ethay indway aroseyay; ethay easay oaredray;
andyay, asyay ithway ethay ightymay ockshay ofyay anyay earthquakeyay, ityay itsplay andyay ackedcray ithway ayay
emendoustray andyay overwhelmingyay oundsay. Ethay orkway asway oonsay inishedfay; inyay ayay ewfay
inutesmay ayay umultuoustay easay olledray etweenbay emay andyay ymay enemyyay, andyay Iyay asway eftlay
iftingdray onyay ayay atteredscay iecepay ofyay iceyay atthay asway ontinuallycay esseninglay andyay
usthay eparingpray orfay emay ayay ideoushay eathday.

Inyay isthay annermay anymay appallingyay ourshay assedpay; everalsay ofyay ymay ogsday iedday, andyay Iyay
yselfmay asway aboutyay otay inksay underyay ethay accumulationyay ofyay istressday enwhay Iyay awsay youryay
esselvay idingray atyay anchoryay andyay oldinghay orthfay otay emay opeshay ofyay uccoursay andyay ifelay.
Iyay adhay onay onceptioncay atthay esselsvay everyay amecay osay arfay orthnay andyay asway astoundedyay
atyay ethay ightsay. Iyay uicklyqay estroyedday artpay ofyay ymay edgeslay otay onstructcay oarsyay, andyay
ybay esethay eansmay asway enabledyay, ithway infiniteyay atiguefay, otay ovemay ymay iceyay aftray inyay
ethay irectionday ofyay youryay ipshay. Iyay adhay eterminedday, ifyay youyay ereway oinggay outhwardssay,
illstay otay usttray yselfmay otay ethay ercymay ofyay ethay eassay atherray anthay abandonyay ymay
urposepay. Iyay opedhay otay induceyay youyay otay antgray emay ayay oatbay ithway ichwhay Iyay ouldcay ursuepay
ymay enemyyay. Utbay youryay irectionday asway orthwardsnay. Youyay ooktay emay onyay oardbay enwhay ymay
igourvay asway exhaustedyay, andyay Iyay ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay underyay ymay ultipliedmay
ardshipshay intoyay ayay eathday ichwhay Iyay illstay eaddray, orfay ymay asktay isyay unfulfilledyay.

Ohyay! Enwhay illway ymay uidinggay iritspay, inyay onductingcay emay otay ethay ondæmay, allowyay
emay ethay estray Iyay osay uchmay esireday; oryay ustmay Iyay ieday, andyay ehay yetyay ivelay? Ifyay Iyay oday,
earsway otay emay, Altonway, atthay ehay allshay otnay escapeyay, atthay youyay illway eeksay imhay
andyay atisfysay ymay engeancevay inyay ishay eathday. Andyay oday Iyay areday otay askyay ofyay youyay otay
undertakeyay ymay ilgrimagepay, otay endureyay ethay ardshipshay atthay Iyay avehay undergoneyay?
Onay; Iyay amyay otnay osay elfishsay. Yetyay, enwhay Iyay amyay eadday, ifyay ehay ouldshay appearyay, ifyay
ethay inistersmay ofyay engeancevay ouldshay onductcay imhay otay youyay, earsway atthay ehay
allshay otnay ive—swearlay atthay ehay allshay otnay iumphtray overyay ymay accumulatedyay
oesway andyay urvivesay otay addyay otay ethay istlay ofyay ishay arkday imescray. Ehay isyay eloquentyay
andyay ersuasivepay, andyay onceyay ishay ordsway adhay evenyay owerpay overyay ymay earthay; utbay
usttray imhay otnay. Ishay oulsay isyay asyay ellishhay asyay ishay ormfay, ullfay ofyay eacherytray
andyay iend-likefay alicemay. Earhay imhay otnay; allcay onyay ethay amesnay ofyay Illiamway,
Ustinejay, Ervalclay, Elizabethyay, ymay atherfay, andyay ofyay ethay etchedwray Ictorvay, andyay
ustthray youryay ordsway intoyay ishay earthay. Iyay illway overhay earnay andyay irectday ethay
eelstay arightyay.

Altonway, in_ay ontinuationcay._


Augustyay 26th, 17—.


Youyay avehay eadray isthay angestray andyay errifictay orystay, Argaretmay; andyay oday youyay otnay
eelfay youryay oodblay ongealcay ithway orrorhay, ikelay atthay ichwhay evenyay ownay urdlescay
inemay? Ometimessay, eizedsay ithway uddensay agonyyay, ehay ouldcay otnay ontinuecay ishay
aletay; atyay othersyay, ishay oicevay okenbray, yetyay iercingpay, utteredyay ithway
ifficultyday ethay ordsway osay epleteray ithway anguishyay. Ishay inefay andyay ovelylay eyesyay
ereway ownay ightedlay upyay ithway indignationyay, ownay ubduedsay otay owncastday orrowsay
andyay uenchedqay inyay infiniteyay etchednesswray. Ometimessay ehay ommandedcay ishay
ountenancecay andyay onestay andyay elatedray ethay ostmay orriblehay incidentsyay ithway ayay
anquiltray oicevay, uppressingsay everyyay arkmay ofyay agitationyay; enthay, ikelay ayay
olcanovay urstingbay orthfay, ishay acefay ouldway uddenlysay angechay otay anyay expressionyay
ofyay ethay ildestway ageray asyay ehay iekedshray outyay imprecationsyay onyay ishay ersecutorpay.

Ishay aletay isyay onnectedcay andyay oldtay ithway anyay appearanceyay ofyay ethay implestsay uthtray,
yetyay Iyay ownyay otay youyay atthay ethay etterslay ofyay Elixfay andyay Afiesay, ichwhay ehay owedshay emay,
andyay ethay apparitionyay ofyay ethay onstermay eensay omfray ouryay ipshay, oughtbray otay emay ayay
eatergray onvictioncay ofyay ethay uthtray ofyay ishay arrativenay anthay ishay asseverationsyay,
oweverhay earnestyay andyay onnectedcay. Uchsay ayay onstermay ashay, enthay, eallyray existenceyay!
Iyay annotcay oubtday ityay, yetyay Iyay amyay ostlay inyay urprisesay andyay admirationyay. Ometimessay Iyay
endeavouredyay otay aingay omfray Ankensteinfray ethay articularspay ofyay ishay
eature’scray ormationfay, utbay onyay isthay ointpay ehay asway impenetrableyay.

are“ay youyay admay, ymay iendfray?” aidsay ehay. or“ay itherwhay oesday youryay
enselesssay uriositycay eadlay youyay? Ouldway youyay alsoyay eatecray orfay yourselfyay andyay ethay
orldway ayay emoniacalday enemyyay? Eacepay, eacepay! Earnlay ymay iseriesmay andyay oday otnay eeksay
otay increaseyay youryay ownyay.”

Ankensteinfray iscoveredday atthay Iyay ademay otesnay oncerningcay ishay istoryhay; ehay askedyay
otay eesay emthay andyay enthay imselfhay orrectedcay andyay augmentedyay emthay inyay anymay acesplay,
utbay incipallypray inyay ivinggay ethay ifelay andyay iritspay otay ethay onversationscay ehay eldhay
ithway ishay enemyyay. ince“say youyay avehay eservedpray ymay arrationnay,” aidsay
ehay, i“ay ouldway otnay atthay ayay utilatedmay oneyay ouldshay ogay ownday otay
osteritypay.”

Usthay ashay ayay eekway assedpay awayyay, ilewhay Iyay avehay istenedlay otay ethay angeststray
aletay atthay everyay imaginationyay ormedfay. Ymay oughtsthay andyay everyyay eelingfay ofyay ymay
oulsay avehay eenbay unkdray upyay ybay ethay interestyay orfay ymay uestgay ichwhay isthay aletay
andyay ishay ownyay elevatedyay andyay entlegay annersmay avehay eatedcray. Iyay ishway otay oothesay
imhay, yetyay ancay Iyay ounselcay oneyay osay infinitelyyay iserablemay, osay estituteday ofyay
everyyay opehay ofyay onsolationcay, otay ivelay? Ohyay, onay! Ethay onlyyay oyjay atthay ehay ancay
ownay owknay illway ebay enwhay ehay omposescay ishay atteredshay iritspay otay eacepay andyay
eathday. Yetyay ehay enjoysyay oneyay omfortcay, ethay offspringyay ofyay olitudesay andyay
eliriumday; ehay elievesbay atthay enwhay inyay eamsdray ehay oldshay onversecay ithway ishay
iendsfray andyay erivesday omfray atthay ommunioncay onsolationcay orfay ishay iseriesmay oryay
excitementsyay otay ishay engeancevay, atthay eythay areyay otnay ethay eationscray ofyay ishay
ancyfay, utbay ethay eingsbay emselvesthay owhay isitvay imhay omfray ethay egionsray ofyay ayay
emoteray orldway. Isthay aithfay ivesgay ayay olemnitysay otay ishay everiesray atthay enderray
emthay otay emay almostyay asyay imposingyay andyay interestingyay asyay uthtray.

Ouryay onversationscay areyay otnay alwaysyay onfinedcay otay ishay ownyay istoryhay andyay
isfortunesmay. Onyay everyyay ointpay ofyay eneralgay iteraturelay ehay isplaysday
unboundedyay owledgeknay andyay ayay uickqay andyay iercingpay apprehensionyay. Ishay
eloquenceyay isyay orciblefay andyay ouchingtay; ornay ancay Iyay earhay imhay, enwhay ehay elatesray
ayay atheticpay incidentyay oryay endeavoursyay otay ovemay ethay assionspay ofyay itypay oryay ovelay,
ithoutway earstay. Atwhay ayay oriousglay eaturecray ustmay ehay avehay eenbay inyay ethay aysday
ofyay ishay osperitypray, enwhay ehay isyay usthay oblenay andyay odlikegay inyay uinray! Ehay eemssay
otay eelfay ishay ownyay orthway andyay ethay eatnessgray ofyay ishay allfay.

en“whay youngeryay,” aidsay ehay, i“ay elievedbay yselfmay estinedday orfay
omesay eatgray enterpriseyay. Ymay eelingsfay areyay ofoundpray, utbay Iyay ossessedpay ayay oolnesscay
ofyay udgmentjay atthay ittedfay emay orfay illustriousyay achievementsyay. Isthay entimentsay ofyay
ethay orthway ofyay ymay aturenay upportedsay emay enwhay othersyay ouldway avehay eenbay oppressedyay,
orfay Iyay eemedday ityay iminalcray otay owthray awayyay inyay uselessyay iefgray osethay alentstay atthay
ightmay ebay usefulyay otay ymay ellowfay eaturescray. Enwhay Iyay eflectedray onyay ethay orkway Iyay adhay
ompletedcay, onay esslay ayay oneyay anthay ethay eationcray ofyay ayay ensitivesay andyay ationalray
animalyay, Iyay ouldcay otnay ankray yselfmay ithway ethay erdhay ofyay ommoncay ojectorspray. Utbay
isthay oughtthay, ichwhay upportedsay emay inyay ethay ommencementcay ofyay ymay areercay, ownay
ervessay onlyyay otay ungeplay emay owerlay inyay ethay ustday. Allyay ymay eculationsspay andyay opeshay
areyay asyay othingnay, andyay ikelay ethay archangelyay owhay aspiredyay otay omnipotenceyay, Iyay amyay
ainedchay inyay anyay eternalyay ellhay. Ymay imaginationyay asway ividvay, yetyay ymay owerspay ofyay
analysisyay andyay applicationyay ereway intenseyay; ybay ethay unionyay ofyay esethay ualitiesqay Iyay
onceivedcay ethay ideayay andyay executedyay ethay eationcray ofyay ayay anmay. Evenyay ownay Iyay annotcay
ecollectray ithoutway assionpay ymay everiesray ilewhay ethay orkway asway incompleteyay. Iyay odtray
eavenhay inyay ymay oughtsthay, ownay exultingyay inyay ymay owerspay, ownay urningbay ithway ethay ideayay
ofyay eirthay effectsyay. Omfray ymay infancyyay Iyay asway imbuedyay ithway ighhay opeshay andyay ayay oftylay
ambitionyay; utbay owhay amyay Iyay unksay! Ohyay! Ymay iendfray, ifyay youyay adhay ownknay emay asyay Iyay onceyay
asway, youyay ouldway otnay ecogniseray emay inyay isthay atestay ofyay egradationday. Espondencyday
arelyray isitedvay ymay earthay; ayay ighhay estinyday eemedsay otay earbay emay onyay, untilyay Iyay ellfay,
evernay, evernay againyay otay iseray.”

Ustmay Iyay enthay oselay isthay admirableyay eingbay? Iyay avehay ongedlay orfay ayay iendfray; Iyay avehay
oughtsay oneyay owhay ouldway ympathisesay ithway andyay ovelay emay. Eholdbay, onyay esethay esertday
eassay Iyay avehay oundfay uchsay ayay oneyay, utbay Iyay earfay Iyay avehay ainedgay imhay onlyyay otay owknay ishay
aluevay andyay oselay imhay. Iyay ouldway econcileray imhay otay ifelay, utbay ehay epulsesray ethay ideayay.

i“ay ankthay youyay, Altonway,” ehay aidsay, or“fay youryay indkay intentionsyay owardstay osay
iserablemay ayay etchwray; utbay enwhay youyay eakspay ofyay ewnay iestay andyay eshfray
affectionsyay, inkthay youyay atthay anyyay ancay eplaceray osethay owhay areyay onegay? Ancay anyyay
anmay ebay otay emay asyay Ervalclay asway, oryay anyyay omanway anotheryay Elizabethyay? Evenyay
erewhay ethay affectionsyay areyay otnay onglystray ovedmay ybay anyyay uperiorsay excellenceyay,
ethay ompanionscay ofyay ouryay ildhoodchay alwaysyay ossesspay ayay ertaincay owerpay overyay ouryay
indsmay ichwhay ardlyhay anyyay aterlay iendfray ancay obtainyay. Eythay owknay ouryay
infantineyay ispositionsday, ichwhay, oweverhay eythay aymay ebay afterwardsyay odifiedmay,
areyay evernay eradicatedyay; andyay eythay ancay udgejay ofyay ouryay actionsyay ithway oremay
ertaincay onclusionscay asyay otay ethay integrityyay ofyay ouryay otivesmay. Ayay istersay oryay ayay
otherbray ancay evernay, unlessyay indeedyay uchsay ymptomssay avehay eenbay ownshay earlyyay,
uspectsay ethay otheryay ofyay audfray oryay alsefay ealingday, enwhay anotheryay iendfray,
oweverhay onglystray ehay aymay ebay attachedyay, aymay, inyay itespay ofyay imselfhay, ebay
ontemplatedcay ithway uspicionsay. Utbay Iyay enjoyedyay iendsfray, earday otnay onlyyay
oughthray abithay andyay associationyay, utbay omfray eirthay ownyay eritsmay; andyay ereverwhay
Iyay amyay, ethay oothingsay oicevay ofyay ymay Elizabethyay andyay ethay onversationcay ofyay
