Ervalclay illway ebay everyay isperedwhay inyay ymay earyay. Eythay areyay eadday, andyay utbay oneyay
eelingfay inyay uchsay ayay olitudesay ancay ersuadepay emay otay eservepray ymay ifelay. Ifyay Iyay
ereway engagedyay inyay anyyay ighhay undertakingyay oryay esignday, aughtfray ithway extensiveyay
utilityyay otay ymay ellowfay eaturescray, enthay ouldcay Iyay ivelay otay ulfilfay ityay. Utbay
uchsay isyay otnay ymay estinyday; Iyay ustmay ursuepay andyay estroyday ethay eingbay otay omwhay Iyay
avegay existenceyay; enthay ymay otlay onyay earthyay illway ebay ulfilledfay andyay Iyay aymay ieday.”

Ymay elovedbay Istersay,

Eptembersay 2d.


Iyay itewray otay youyay, encompassedyay ybay erilpay andyay ignorantyay etherwhay Iyay amyay everyay
oomedday otay eesay againyay earday Englandyay andyay ethay earerday iendsfray atthay inhabityay
ityay. Iyay amyay urroundedsay ybay ountainsmay ofyay iceyay ichwhay admityay ofyay onay escapeyay andyay
eatenthray everyyay omentmay otay ushcray ymay esselvay. Ethay avebray ellowsfay omwhay Iyay
avehay ersuadedpay otay ebay ymay ompanionscay ooklay owardstay emay orfay aidyay, utbay Iyay avehay
onenay otay estowbay. Erethay isyay omethingsay erriblytay appallingyay inyay ouryay
ituationsay, yetyay ymay ouragecay andyay opeshay oday otnay esertday emay. Yetyay ityay isyay
erribletay otay eflectray atthay ethay iveslay ofyay allyay esethay enmay areyay endangeredyay
oughthray emay. Ifyay eway areyay ostlay, ymay admay emesschay areyay ethay ausecay.

Andyay atwhay, Argaretmay, illway ebay ethay atestay ofyay youryay indmay? Youyay illway otnay earhay ofyay ymay
estructionday, andyay youyay illway anxiouslyyay awaityay ymay eturnray. Yearsyay illway asspay, andyay
youyay illway avehay isitingsvay ofyay espairday andyay yetyay ebay orturedtay ybay opehay. Ohyay! Ymay
elovedbay istersay, ethay ickeningsay ailingfay ofyay youryay eart-felthay expectationsyay isyay,
inyay ospectpray, oremay erribletay otay emay anthay ymay ownyay eathday. Utbay youyay avehay ayay usbandhay
andyay ovelylay ildrenchay; youyay aymay ebay appyhay. Eavenhay essblay youyay andyay akemay youyay osay!

Ymay unfortunateyay uestgay egardsray emay ithway ethay enderesttay ompassioncay. Ehay
endeavoursyay otay illfay emay ithway opehay andyay alkstay asyay ifyay ifelay ereway ayay ossessionpay
ichwhay ehay aluedvay. Ehay emindsray emay owhay oftenyay ethay amesay accidentsyay avehay
appenedhay otay otheryay avigatorsnay owhay avehay attemptedyay isthay easay, andyay inyay itespay
ofyay yselfmay, ehay illsfay emay ithway eerfulchay auguriesyay. Evenyay ethay ailorssay eelfay
ethay owerpay ofyay ishay eloquenceyay; enwhay ehay eaksspay, eythay onay ongerlay espairday; ehay
ousesray eirthay energiesyay, andyay ilewhay eythay earhay ishay oicevay eythay elievebay esethay
astvay ountainsmay ofyay iceyay areyay ole-hillsmay ichwhay illway anishvay eforebay ethay
esolutionsray ofyay anmay. Esethay eelingsfay areyay ansitorytray; eachyay ayday ofyay
expectationyay elayedday illsfay emthay ithway earfay, andyay Iyay almostyay eaddray ayay utinymay
ausedcay ybay isthay espairday.

Eptembersay 5th.


Ayay enescay ashay ustjay assedpay ofyay uchsay uncommonyay interestyay atthay, althoughyay ityay isyay
ighlyhay obablepray atthay esethay aperspay aymay evernay eachray youyay, yetyay Iyay annotcay
orbearfay ecordingray ityay.

Eway areyay illstay urroundedsay ybay ountainsmay ofyay iceyay, illstay inyay imminentyay angerday
ofyay eingbay ushedcray inyay eirthay onflictcay. Ethay oldcay isyay excessiveyay, andyay anymay ofyay
ymay unfortunateyay omradescay avehay alreadyyay oundfay ayay avegray amidstyay isthay enescay ofyay
esolationday. Ankensteinfray ashay ailyday eclinedday inyay ealthhay; ayay everishfay irefay
illstay immersglay inyay ishay eyesyay, utbay ehay isyay exhaustedyay, andyay enwhay uddenlysay
ousedray otay anyyay exertionyay, ehay eedilyspay inkssay againyay intoyay apparentyay
ifelessnesslay.

Iyay entionedmay inyay ymay astlay etterlay ethay earsfay Iyay entertainedyay ofyay ayay utinymay.
Isthay orningmay, asyay Iyay atsay atchingway ethay anway ountenancecay ofyay ymay iend—hisfray
eyesyay alfhay osedclay andyay ishay imbslay anginghay istlessly—ilay asway ousedray ybay alfhay
ayay ozenday ofyay ethay ailorssay, owhay emandedday admissionyay intoyay ethay abincay. Eythay
enteredyay, andyay eirthay eaderlay addressedyay emay. Ehay oldtay emay atthay ehay andyay ishay
ompanionscay adhay eenbay osenchay ybay ethay otheryay ailorssay otay omecay inyay eputationday
otay emay otay akemay emay ayay equisitionray ichwhay, inyay usticejay, Iyay ouldcay otnay efuseray.
Eway ereway immuredyay inyay iceyay andyay ouldshay obablypray evernay escapeyay, utbay eythay
earedfay atthay ifyay, asyay asway ossiblepay, ethay iceyay ouldshay issipateday andyay ayay eefray
assagepay ebay openedyay, Iyay ouldshay ebay ashray enoughyay otay ontinuecay ymay oyagevay andyay
eadlay emthay intoyay eshfray angersday, afteryay eythay ightmay appilyhay avehay urmountedsay
isthay. Eythay insistedyay, ereforethay, atthay Iyay ouldshay engageyay ithway ayay olemnsay
omisepray atthay ifyay ethay esselvay ouldshay ebay eedfray Iyay ouldway instantlyyay irectday ymay
oursecay outhwardssay.

Isthay eechspay oubledtray emay. Iyay adhay otnay espairedday, ornay adhay Iyay yetyay onceivedcay
ethay ideayay ofyay eturningray ifyay etsay eefray. Yetyay ouldcay Iyay, inyay usticejay, oryay evenyay inyay
ossibilitypay, efuseray isthay emandday? Iyay esitatedhay eforebay Iyay answeredyay, enwhay
Ankensteinfray, owhay adhay atyay irstfay eenbay ilentsay, andyay indeedyay appearedyay ardlyhay
otay avehay orcefay enoughyay otay attendyay, ownay ousedray imselfhay; ishay eyesyay arkledspay,
andyay ishay eekschay ushedflay ithway omentarymay igourvay. Urningtay owardstay ethay enmay,
ehay aidsay,

at“whay oday youyay eanmay? Atwhay oday youyay emandday ofyay youryay aptaincay? Areyay youyay, enthay,
osay easilyyay urnedtay omfray youryay esignday? Idday youyay otnay allcay isthay ayay oriousglay
expeditionyay? and“ay ereforewhay asway ityay oriousglay? Otnay ecausebay ethay ayway asway
oothsmay andyay acidplay asyay ayay outhernsay easay, utbay ecausebay ityay asway ullfay ofyay angersday andyay
errortay, ecausebay atyay everyyay ewnay incidentyay youryay ortitudefay asway otay ebay alledcay orthfay
andyay youryay ouragecay exhibitedyay, ecausebay angerday andyay eathday urroundedsay ityay, andyay
esethay youyay ereway otay avebray andyay overcomeyay. Orfay isthay asway ityay ayay oriousglay, orfay isthay
asway ityay anyay onourablehay undertakingyay. Youyay ereway ereafterhay otay ebay ailedhay asyay ethay
enefactorsbay ofyay youryay eciesspay, youryay amesnay adoredyay asyay elongingbay otay avebray enmay
owhay encounteredyay eathday orfay onourhay andyay ethay enefitbay ofyay ankindmay. Andyay ownay,
eholdbay, ithway ethay irstfay imaginationyay ofyay angerday, oryay, ifyay youyay illway, ethay irstfay
ightymay andyay errifictay ialtray ofyay youryay ouragecay, youyay inkshray awayyay andyay areyay ontentcay
otay ebay andedhay ownday asyay enmay owhay adhay otnay engthstray enoughyay otay endureyay oldcay andyay
erilpay; andyay osay, oorpay oulssay, eythay ereway illychay andyay eturnedray otay eirthay armway
iresidesfay. Ywhay, atthay equiresray otnay isthay eparationpray; yeyay eednay otnay avehay omecay
usthay arfay andyay aggeddray youryay aptaincay otay ethay ameshay ofyay ayay efeatday erelymay otay ovepray
yourselvesyay owardscay. Ohyay! Ebay enmay, oryay ebay oremay anthay enmay. Ebay eadystay otay youryay
urposespay andyay irmfay asyay ayay ockray. Isthay iceyay isyay otnay ademay ofyay uchsay uffstay asyay youryay
eartshay aymay ebay; ityay isyay utablemay andyay annotcay ithstandway youyay ifyay youyay aysay atthay ityay
allshay otnay. Oday otnay eturnray otay youryay amiliesfay ithway ethay igmastay ofyay isgraceday
arkedmay onyay youryay owsbray. Eturnray asyay eroeshay owhay avehay oughtfay andyay onqueredcay andyay
owhay owknay otnay atwhay ityay isyay otay urntay eirthay acksbay onyay ethay oefay.”

Ehay okespay isthay ithway ayay oicevay osay odulatedmay otay ethay ifferentday eelingsfay expressedyay
inyay ishay eechspay, ithway anyay eyeyay osay ullfay ofyay oftylay esignday andyay eroismhay, atthay ancay
youyay onderway atthay esethay enmay ereway ovedmay? Eythay ookedlay atyay oneyay anotheryay andyay ereway
unableyay otay eplyray. Iyay okespay; Iyay oldtay emthay otay etireray andyay onsidercay ofyay atwhay adhay
eenbay aidsay, atthay Iyay ouldway otnay eadlay emthay artherfay orthnay ifyay eythay enuouslystray
esiredday ethay ontrarycay, utbay atthay Iyay opedhay atthay, ithway eflectionray, eirthay ouragecay
ouldway eturnray.

Eythay etiredray andyay Iyay urnedtay owardstay ymay iendfray, utbay ehay asway unksay inyay anguorlay andyay
almostyay eprivedday ofyay ifelay.

Owhay allyay isthay illway erminatetay, Iyay owknay otnay, utbay Iyay adhay atherray ieday anthay
eturnray amefullyshay, ymay urposepay unfulfilledyay. Yetyay Iyay earfay uchsay illway ebay ymay
atefay; ethay enmay, unsupportedyay ybay ideasyay ofyay oryglay andyay onourhay, ancay evernay
illinglyway ontinuecay otay endureyay eirthay esentpray ardshipshay.

Eptembersay 7th.


Ethay ieday isyay astcay; Iyay avehay onsentedcay otay eturnray ifyay eway areyay otnay estroyedday.
Usthay areyay ymay opeshay astedblay ybay owardicecay andyay indecisionyay; Iyay omecay ackbay
ignorantyay andyay isappointedday. Ityay equiresray oremay ilosophyphay anthay Iyay ossesspay
otay earbay isthay injusticeyay ithway atiencepay.

Eptembersay 12th.


Ityay isyay astpay; Iyay amyay eturningray otay Englandyay. Iyay avehay ostlay ymay opeshay ofyay utilityyay
andyay oryglay; Iyay avehay ostlay ymay iendfray. Utbay Iyay illway endeavouryay otay etailday esethay
itterbay ircumstancescay otay youyay, ymay earday istersay; andyay ilewhay Iyay amyay aftedway
owardstay Englandyay andyay owardstay youyay, Iyay illway otnay espondday.

Eptembersay 9th, ethay iceyay eganbay otay ovemay, andyay oaringsray ikelay underthay ereway eardhay
atyay ayay istanceday asyay ethay islandsyay itsplay andyay ackedcray inyay everyyay irectionday. Eway ereway
inyay ethay ostmay imminentyay erilpay, utbay asyay eway ouldcay onlyyay emainray assivepay, ymay iefchay
attentionyay asway occupiedyay ybay ymay unfortunateyay uestgay osewhay illnessyay increasedyay inyay
uchsay ayay egreeday atthay ehay asway entirelyyay onfinedcay otay ishay edbay. Ethay iceyay ackedcray
ehindbay usyay andyay asway ivendray ithway orcefay owardstay ethay orthnay; ayay eezebray angspray omfray
ethay estway, andyay onyay ethay 11th ethay assagepay owardstay ethay outhsay ecamebay erfectlypay
eefray. Enwhay ethay ailorssay awsay isthay andyay atthay eirthay eturnray otay eirthay ativenay
ountrycay asway apparentlyyay assuredyay, ayay outshay ofyay umultuoustay oyjay okebray omfray emthay,
oudlay andyay ong-continuedlay. Ankensteinfray, owhay asway ozingday, awokeyay andyay askedyay ethay
ausecay ofyay ethay umulttay. ey“thay outshay,” Iyay aidsay, ecause“bay eythay
illway oonsay eturnray otay Englandyay.”

o“day youyay, enthay, eallyray eturnray?”

alas“ay! Yesyay; Iyay annotcay ithstandway eirthay emandsday. Iyay annotcay eadlay emthay
unwillinglyyay otay angerday, andyay Iyay ustmay eturnray.”

o“day osay, ifyay youyay illway; utbay Iyay illway otnay. Youyay aymay ivegay upyay youryay urposepay, utbay
inemay isyay assignedyay otay emay ybay Eavenhay, andyay Iyay areday otnay. Iyay amyay eakway, utbay
urelysay ethay iritsspay owhay assistyay ymay engeancevay illway endowyay emay ithway
ufficientsay engthstray.” Ayingsay isthay, ehay endeavouredyay otay ingspray omfray ethay
edbay, utbay ethay exertionyay asway ootay eatgray orfay imhay; ehay ellfay ackbay andyay aintedfay.

Ityay asway onglay eforebay ehay asway estoredray, andyay Iyay oftenyay oughtthay atthay ifelay asway
entirelyyay extinctyay. Atyay engthlay ehay openedyay ishay eyesyay; ehay eathedbray ithway
ifficultyday andyay asway unableyay otay eakspay. Ethay urgeonsay avegay imhay ayay omposingcay
aughtdray andyay orderedyay usyay otay eavelay imhay undisturbedyay. Inyay ethay eantimemay ehay
oldtay emay atthay ymay iendfray adhay ertainlycay otnay anymay ourshay otay ivelay.

Ishay entencesay asway onouncedpray, andyay Iyay ouldcay onlyyay ievegray andyay ebay atientpay. Iyay atsay
ybay ishay edbay, atchingway imhay; ishay eyesyay ereway osedclay, andyay Iyay oughtthay ehay eptslay; utbay
esentlypray ehay alledcay otay emay inyay ayay eeblefay oicevay, andyay iddingbay emay omecay earnay,
aidsay, alas“ay! Ethay engthstray Iyay eliedray onyay isyay onegay; Iyay eelfay atthay Iyay allshay
oonsay ieday, andyay ehay, ymay enemyyay andyay ersecutorpay, aymay illstay ebay inyay eingbay. Inkthay
otnay, Altonway, atthay inyay ethay astlay omentsmay ofyay ymay existenceyay Iyay eelfay atthay urningbay
atredhay andyay ardentyay esireday ofyay evengeray Iyay onceyay expressedyay; utbay Iyay eelfay yselfmay
ustifiedjay inyay esiringday ethay eathday ofyay ymay adversaryyay. Uringday esethay astlay aysday Iyay
avehay eenbay occupiedyay inyay examiningyay ymay astpay onductcay; ornay oday Iyay indfay ityay amableblay.
Inyay ayay itfay ofyay enthusiasticyay adnessmay Iyay eatedcray ayay ationalray eaturecray andyay asway
oundbay owardstay imhay otay assureyay, asyay arfay asyay asway inyay ymay owerpay, ishay appinesshay andyay
ell-beingway. Isthay asway ymay utyday, utbay erethay asway anotheryay illstay aramountpay otay
atthay. Ymay utiesday owardstay ethay eingsbay ofyay ymay ownyay eciesspay adhay eatergray aimsclay otay
ymay attentionyay ecausebay eythay includedyay ayay eatergray oportionpray ofyay appinesshay oryay
iserymay. Urgedyay ybay isthay iewvay, Iyay efusedray, andyay Iyay idday ightray inyay efusingray, otay
eatecray ayay ompanioncay orfay ethay irstfay eaturecray. Ehay owedshay unparalleledyay alignitymay
andyay elfishnesssay inyay evilyay; ehay estroyedday ymay iendsfray; ehay evotedday otay estructionday
eingsbay owhay ossessedpay exquisiteyay ensationssay, appinesshay, andyay isdomway; ornay oday Iyay
owknay erewhay isthay irstthay orfay engeancevay aymay endyay. Iserablemay imselfhay atthay ehay aymay
enderray onay otheryay etchedwray, ehay oughtyay otay ieday. Ethay asktay ofyay ishay estructionday asway
inemay, utbay Iyay avehay ailedfay. Enwhay actuatedyay ybay elfishsay andyay iciousvay otivesmay, Iyay
askedyay youyay otay undertakeyay ymay unfinishedyay orkway, andyay Iyay enewray isthay equestray ownay,
enwhay Iyay amyay onlyyay inducedyay ybay easonray andyay irtuevay.

yet“ay Iyay annotcay askyay youyay otay enounceray youryay ountrycay andyay iendsfray otay ulfilfay
isthay asktay; andyay ownay atthay youyay areyay eturningray otay Englandyay, youyay illway avehay
ittlelay ancechay ofyay eetingmay ithway imhay. Utbay ethay onsiderationcay ofyay esethay
ointspay, andyay ethay ellway alancingbay ofyay atwhay youyay aymay esteemyay youryay utiesday, Iyay
eavelay otay youyay; ymay udgmentjay andyay ideasyay areyay alreadyyay isturbedday ybay ethay earnay
approachyay ofyay eathday. Iyay areday otnay askyay youyay otay oday atwhay Iyay inkthay ightray, orfay Iyay
aymay illstay ebay isledmay ybay assionpay.

at“thay ehay ouldshay ivelay otay ebay anyay instrumentyay ofyay ischiefmay isturbsday emay; inyay
otheryay espectsray, isthay ourhay, enwhay Iyay omentarilymay expectyay ymay eleaseray, isyay ethay
onlyyay appyhay oneyay ichwhay Iyay avehay enjoyedyay orfay everalsay yearsyay. Ethay ormsfay ofyay
ethay elovedbay eadday itflay eforebay emay, andyay Iyay astenhay otay eirthay armsyay. Arewellfay,
Altonway! Eeksay appinesshay inyay anquillitytray andyay avoidyay ambitionyay, evenyay ifyay ityay
ebay onlyyay ethay apparentlyyay innocentyay oneyay ofyay istinguishingday yourselfyay inyay
iencescay andyay iscoveriesday. Yetyay ywhay oday Iyay aysay isthay? Iyay avehay yselfmay eenbay
astedblay inyay esethay opeshay, yetyay anotheryay aymay ucceedsay.”

Ishay oicevay ecamebay ainterfay asyay ehay okespay, andyay atyay engthlay, exhaustedyay ybay ishay
effortyay, ehay anksay intoyay ilencesay. Aboutyay alfhay anyay ourhay afterwardsyay ehay
attemptedyay againyay otay eakspay utbay asway unableyay; ehay essedpray ymay andhay eeblyfay, andyay
ishay eyesyay osedclay orfay everyay, ilewhay ethay irradiationyay ofyay ayay entlegay ilesmay assedpay
awayyay omfray ishay ipslay.

Argaretmay, atwhay ommentcay ancay Iyay akemay onyay ethay untimelyyay extinctionyay ofyay isthay
oriousglay iritspay? Atwhay ancay Iyay aysay atthay illway enableyay youyay otay understandyay ethay
epthday ofyay ymay orrowsay? Allyay atthay Iyay ouldshay expressyay ouldway ebay inadequateyay andyay
eeblefay. Ymay earstay owflay; ymay indmay isyay overshadowedyay ybay ayay oudclay ofyay
isappointmentday. Utbay Iyay ourneyjay owardstay Englandyay, andyay Iyay aymay erethay indfay
onsolationcay.

Iyay amyay interruptedyay. Atwhay oday esethay oundssay ortendpay? Ityay isyay idnightmay; ethay
eezebray owsblay airlyfay, andyay ethay atchway onyay eckday arcelyscay irstay. Againyay erethay
isyay ayay oundsay asyay ofyay ayay umanhay oicevay, utbay oarserhay; ityay omescay omfray ethay abincay
erewhay ethay emainsray ofyay Ankensteinfray illstay ielay. Iyay ustmay ariseyay andyay examineyay.
Oodgay ightnay, ymay istersay.

Eatgray Odgay! atwhay ayay enescay ashay ustjay akentay aceplay! Iyay amyay yetyay izzyday ithway ethay
emembranceray ofyay ityay. Iyay ardlyhay owknay etherwhay Iyay allshay avehay ethay owerpay otay etailday
ityay; yetyay ethay aletay ichwhay Iyay avehay ecordedray ouldway ebay incompleteyay ithoutway isthay
inalfay andyay onderfulway atastrophecay.

Iyay enteredyay ethay abincay erewhay aylay ethay emainsray ofyay ymay ill-fatedyay andyay admirableyay
iendfray. Overyay imhay unghay ayay ormfay ichwhay Iyay annotcay indfay ordsway otay
escribe—giganticday inyay aturestay, yetyay uncouthyay andyay istortedday inyay itsyay
oportionspray. Asyay ehay unghay overyay ethay offincay, ishay acefay asway oncealedcay ybay onglay
ockslay ofyay aggedray airhay; utbay oneyay astvay andhay asway extendedyay, inyay olourcay andyay
apparentyay exturetay ikelay atthay ofyay ayay ummymay. Enwhay ehay eardhay ethay oundsay ofyay ymay
approachyay, ehay easedcay otay utteryay exclamationsyay ofyay iefgray andyay orrorhay andyay ungspray
owardstay ethay indowway. Evernay idday Iyay eholdbay ayay isionvay osay orriblehay asyay ishay acefay, ofyay
uchsay oathsomelay yetyay appallingyay ideousnesshay. Iyay utshay ymay eyesyay involuntarilyyay andyay
endeavouredyay otay ecollectray atwhay ereway ymay utiesday ithway egardray otay isthay estroyerday.
Iyay alledcay onyay imhay otay aystay.

Ehay ausedpay, ookinglay onyay emay ithway onderway, andyay againyay urningtay owardstay ethay
ifelesslay ormfay ofyay ishay eatorcray, ehay eemedsay otay orgetfay ymay esencepray, andyay
everyyay eaturefay andyay esturegay eemedsay instigatedyay ybay ethay ildestway ageray ofyay omesay
uncontrollableyay assionpay.

at“thay isyay alsoyay ymay ictimvay!” ehay exclaimedyay. in“ay ishay urdermay ymay
imescray areyay onsummatedcay; ethay iserablemay eriessay ofyay ymay eingbay isyay oundway otay itsyay
oseclay! Ohyay, Ankensteinfray! Enerousgay andyay elf-devotedsay eingbay! Atwhay oesday ityay
availyay atthay Iyay ownay askyay eethay otay ardonpay emay? Iyay, owhay irretrievablyyay estroyedday eethay
ybay estroyingday allyay outhay ovedstlay. Alasyay! Ehay isyay oldcay, ehay annotcay answeryay
emay.”

Ishay oicevay eemedsay uffocatedsay, andyay ymay irstfay impulsesyay, ichwhay adhay uggestedsay otay
emay ethay utyday ofyay obeyingyay ethay yingday equestray ofyay ymay iendfray inyay estroyingday ishay
enemyyay, ereway ownay uspendedsay ybay ayay ixturemay ofyay uriositycay andyay ompassioncay. Iyay
approachedyay isthay emendoustray eingbay; Iyay aredday otnay againyay aiseray ymay eyesyay otay ishay
acefay, erethay asway omethingsay osay aringscay andyay unearthlyyay inyay ishay uglinessyay. Iyay
attemptedyay otay eakspay, utbay ethay ordsway iedday awayyay onyay ymay ipslay. Ethay onstermay
ontinuedcay otay utteryay ildway andyay incoherentyay elf-reproachessay. Atyay engthlay Iyay
atheredgay esolutionray otay addressyay imhay inyay ayay ausepay ofyay ethay empesttay ofyay ishay assionpay.

your“ay epentanceray,” Iyay aidsay, is“ay ownay uperfluoussay. Ifyay youyay
adhay istenedlay otay ethay oicevay ofyay onsciencecay andyay eededhay ethay ingsstay ofyay emorseray
eforebay youyay adhay urgedyay youryay iabolicalday engeancevay otay isthay extremityyay,
Ankensteinfray ouldway yetyay avehay ivedlay.”

and“ay oday youyay eamdray?” aidsay ethay ondæmay. o“day youyay inkthay atthay Iyay asway enthay
eadday otay agonyyay andyay emorseray? Ehay,” ehay ontinuedcay, ointingpay otay ethay orpsecay,
e“hay ufferedsay otnay inyay ethay onsummationcay ofyay ethay eedday. Ohyay! Otnay ethay
en-thousandthtay ortionpay ofyay ethay anguishyay atthay asway inemay uringday ethay
ingeringlay etailday ofyay itsyay executionyay. Ayay ightfulfray elfishnesssay urriedhay emay
onyay, ilewhay ymay earthay asway oisonedpay ithway emorseray. Inkthay youyay atthay ethay
oansgray ofyay Ervalclay ereway usicmay otay ymay earsyay? Ymay earthay asway ashionedfay otay ebay
usceptiblesay ofyay ovelay andyay ympathysay, andyay enwhay enchedwray ybay iserymay otay icevay
andyay atredhay, ityay idday otnay endureyay ethay iolencevay ofyay ethay angechay ithoutway
orturetay uchsay asyay youyay annotcay evenyay imagineyay.

after“ay ethay urdermay ofyay Ervalclay Iyay eturnedray otay Itzerlandsway, eart-brokenhay
andyay overcomeyay. Iyay itiedpay Ankensteinfray; ymay itypay amountedyay otay orrorhay; Iyay
abhorredyay yselfmay. Utbay enwhay Iyay iscoveredday atthay ehay, ethay authoryay atyay onceyay ofyay
ymay existenceyay andyay ofyay itsyay unspeakableyay ormentstay, aredday otay opehay orfay
appinesshay, atthay ilewhay ehay accumulatedyay etchednesswray andyay espairday uponyay emay
ehay oughtsay ishay ownyay enjoymentyay inyay eelingsfay andyay assionspay omfray ethay
indulgenceyay ofyay ichwhay Iyay asway orfay everyay arredbay, enthay impotentyay envyyay andyay itterbay
indignationyay illedfay emay ithway anyay insatiableyay irstthay orfay engeancevay. Iyay
ecollectedray ymay eatthray andyay esolvedray atthay ityay ouldshay ebay accomplishedyay. Iyay
ewknay atthay Iyay asway eparingpray orfay yselfmay ayay eadlyday orturetay, utbay Iyay asway ethay
aveslay, otnay ethay astermay, ofyay anyay impulseyay ichwhay Iyay etestedday yetyay ouldcay otnay
isobeyday. Yetyay enwhay eshay iedday! Aynay, enthay Iyay asway otnay iserablemay. Iyay adhay
astcay offyay allyay eelingfay, ubduedsay allyay anguishyay, otay iotray inyay ethay excessyay ofyay ymay
espairday. Evilyay enceforththay ecamebay ymay oodgay. Urgedyay usthay arfay, Iyay adhay onay
oicechay utbay otay adaptyay ymay aturenay otay anyay elementyay ichwhay Iyay adhay illinglyway
osenchay. Ethay ompletioncay ofyay ymay emoniacalday esignday ecamebay anyay insatiableyay
assionpay. Andyay ownay ityay isyay endedyay; erethay isyay ymay astlay ictimvay!”

Iyay asway atyay irstfay ouchedtay ybay ethay expressionsyay ofyay ishay iserymay; yetyay, enwhay Iyay alledcay
otay indmay atwhay Ankensteinfray adhay aidsay ofyay ishay owerspay ofyay eloquenceyay andyay
ersuasionpay, andyay enwhay Iyay againyay astcay ymay eyesyay onyay ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofyay ymay
iendfray, indignationyay asway ekindledray ithinway emay. etch“wray!” Iyay aidsay.
it“ay isyay ellway atthay youyay omecay erehay otay inewhay overyay ethay esolationday atthay youyay
avehay ademay. Youyay owthray ayay orchtay intoyay ayay ilepay ofyay uildingsbay, andyay enwhay eythay areyay
onsumedcay, youyay itsay amongyay ethay uinsray andyay amentlay ethay allfay. Ypocriticalhay iendfay!
Ifyay ehay omwhay youyay ournmay illstay ivedlay, illstay ouldway ehay ebay ethay objectyay, againyay ouldway
ehay ecomebay ethay eypray, ofyay youryay accursedyay engeancevay. Ityay isyay otnay itypay atthay youyay
eelfay; youyay amentlay onlyyay ecausebay ethay ictimvay ofyay youryay alignitymay isyay ithdrawnway
omfray youryay owerpay.”

oh“ay, ityay isyay otnay us—notthay usthay,” interruptedyay ethay eingbay.
yet“ay uchsay ustmay ebay ethay impressionyay onveyedcay otay youyay ybay atwhay appearsyay otay
ebay ethay urportpay ofyay ymay actionsyay. Yetyay Iyay eeksay otnay ayay ellowfay eelingfay inyay ymay iserymay.
Onay ympathysay aymay Iyay everyay indfay. Enwhay Iyay irstfay oughtsay ityay, ityay asway ethay ovelay ofyay
irtuevay, ethay eelingsfay ofyay appinesshay andyay affectionyay ithway ichwhay ymay olewhay eingbay
overflowedyay, atthay Iyay ishedway otay ebay articipatedpay. Utbay ownay atthay irtuevay ashay
ecomebay otay emay ayay adowshay, andyay atthay appinesshay andyay affectionyay areyay urnedtay intoyay
itterbay andyay oathinglay espairday, inyay atwhay ouldshay Iyay eeksay orfay ympathysay? Iyay amyay
ontentcay otay uffersay aloneyay ilewhay ymay ufferingssay allshay endureyay; enwhay Iyay ieday, Iyay amyay
ellway atisfiedsay atthay abhorrenceyay andyay opprobriumyay ouldshay oadlay ymay emorymay. Onceyay
ymay ancyfay asway oothedsay ithway eamsdray ofyay irtuevay, ofyay amefay, andyay ofyay enjoymentyay. Onceyay
Iyay alselyfay opedhay otay eetmay ithway eingsbay owhay, ardoningpay ymay outwardyay ormfay, ouldway
ovelay emay orfay ethay excellentyay ualitiesqay ichwhay Iyay asway apablecay ofyay unfoldingyay. Iyay asway
ourishednay ithway ighhay oughtsthay ofyay onourhay andyay evotionday. Utbay ownay imecray ashay
egradedday emay eneathbay ethay eanestmay animalyay. Onay uiltgay, onay ischiefmay, onay
alignitymay, onay iserymay, ancay ebay oundfay omparablecay otay inemay. Enwhay Iyay unray overyay ethay
ightfulfray ataloguecay ofyay ymay inssay, Iyay annotcay elievebay atthay Iyay amyay ethay amesay
eaturecray osewhay oughtsthay ereway onceyay illedfay ithway ublimesay andyay anscendenttray
isionsvay ofyay ethay eautybay andyay ethay ajestymay ofyay oodnessgay. Utbay ityay isyay evenyay osay; ethay
allenfay angelyay ecomesbay ayay alignantmay evilday. Yetyay evenyay atthay enemyyay ofyay Odgay andyay anmay
adhay iendsfray andyay associatesyay inyay ishay esolationday; Iyay amyay aloneyay.

you“ay, owhay allcay Ankensteinfray youryay iendfray, eemsay otay avehay ayay owledgeknay ofyay ymay
imescray andyay ishay isfortunesmay. Utbay inyay ethay etailday ichwhay ehay avegay youyay ofyay emthay
ehay ouldcay otnay umsay upyay ethay ourshay andyay onthsmay ofyay iserymay ichwhay Iyay enduredyay
astingway inyay impotentyay assionspay. Orfay ilewhay Iyay estroyedday ishay opeshay, Iyay idday
otnay atisfysay ymay ownyay esiresday. Eythay ereway orfay everyay ardentyay andyay avingcray; illstay
Iyay esiredday ovelay andyay ellowshipfay, andyay Iyay asway illstay urnedspay. Asway erethay onay
injusticeyay inyay isthay? Amyay Iyay otay ebay oughtthay ethay onlyyay iminalcray, enwhay allyay
umankindhay innedsay againstyay emay? Ywhay oday youyay otnay atehay Elixfay, owhay ovedray ishay
iendfray omfray ishay oorday ithway ontumelycay? Ywhay oday youyay otnay execrateyay ethay usticray
owhay oughtsay otay estroyday ethay avioursay ofyay ishay ildchay? Aynay, esethay areyay irtuousvay
andyay immaculateyay eingsbay! Iyay, ethay iserablemay andyay ethay abandonedyay, amyay anyay
abortionyay, otay ebay urnedspay atyay, andyay ickedkay, andyay ampledtray onyay. Evenyay ownay ymay
oodblay oilsbay atyay ethay ecollectionray ofyay isthay injusticeyay.

ut“bay ityay isyay uetray atthay Iyay amyay ayay etchwray. Iyay avehay urderedmay ethay ovelylay andyay
ethay elplesshay; Iyay avehay angledstray ethay innocentyay asyay eythay eptslay andyay aspedgray otay
eathday ishay oatthray owhay evernay injuredyay emay oryay anyyay otheryay ivinglay ingthay. Iyay avehay
evotedday ymay eatorcray, ethay electsay ecimenspay ofyay allyay atthay isyay orthyway ofyay ovelay andyay
admirationyay amongyay enmay, otay iserymay; Iyay avehay ursuedpay imhay evenyay otay atthay
irremediableyay uinray. Erethay ehay ieslay, itewhay andyay oldcay inyay eathday. Youyay atehay emay, utbay
youryay abhorrenceyay annotcay equalyay atthay ithway ichwhay Iyay egardray yselfmay. Iyay ooklay onyay ethay
andshay ichwhay executedyay ethay eedday; Iyay inkthay onyay ethay earthay inyay ichwhay ethay
imaginationyay ofyay ityay asway onceivedcay andyay onglay orfay ethay omentmay enwhay esethay andshay
illway eetmay ymay eyesyay, enwhay atthay imaginationyay illway aunthay ymay oughtsthay onay oremay.

ear“fay otnay atthay Iyay allshay ebay ethay instrumentyay ofyay uturefay ischiefmay. Ymay orkway
isyay earlynay ompletecay. Eithernay yoursyay ornay anyyay an’smay eathday isyay eedednay otay
onsummatecay ethay eriessay ofyay ymay eingbay andyay accomplishyay atthay ichwhay ustmay ebay oneday,
utbay ityay equiresray ymay ownyay. Oday otnay inkthay atthay Iyay allshay ebay owslay otay erformpay isthay
acrificesay. Iyay allshay uitqay youryay esselvay onyay ethay iceyay aftray ichwhay oughtbray emay
itherthay andyay allshay eeksay ethay ostmay orthernnay extremityyay ofyay ethay obeglay; Iyay allshay
ollectcay ymay uneralfay ilepay andyay onsumecay otay ashesyay isthay iserablemay amefray, atthay itsyay
emainsray aymay affordyay onay ightlay otay anyyay uriouscay andyay unhallowedyay etchwray owhay ouldway
eatecray uchsay anotheryay asyay Iyay avehay eenbay. Iyay allshay ieday. Iyay allshay onay ongerlay eelfay ethay
agoniesyay ichwhay ownay onsumecay emay oryay ebay ethay eypray ofyay eelingsfay unsatisfiedyay, yetyay
unquenchedyay. Ehay isyay eadday owhay alledcay emay intoyay eingbay; andyay enwhay Iyay allshay ebay onay
oremay, ethay eryvay emembranceray ofyay usyay othbay illway eedilyspay anishvay. Iyay allshay onay
ongerlay eesay ethay unsay oryay arsstay oryay eelfay ethay indsway ayplay onyay ymay eekschay. Ightlay,
eelingfay, andyay ensesay illway asspay awayyay; andyay inyay isthay onditioncay ustmay Iyay indfay ymay
appinesshay. Omesay yearsyay agoyay, enwhay ethay imagesyay ichwhay isthay orldway affordsyay irstfay
openedyay uponyay emay, enwhay Iyay eltfay ethay eeringchay armthway ofyay ummersay andyay eardhay ethay
ustlingray ofyay ethay eaveslay andyay ethay arblingway ofyay ethay irdsbay, andyay esethay ereway allyay otay
emay, Iyay ouldshay avehay eptway otay ieday; ownay ityay isyay ymay onlyyay onsolationcay. Ollutedpay ybay
imescray andyay orntay ybay ethay itterestbay emorseray, erewhay ancay Iyay indfay estray utbay inyay
eathday?

arewell“fay! Iyay eavelay youyay, andyay inyay youyay ethay astlay ofyay umankindhay omwhay esethay
eyesyay illway everyay eholdbay. Arewellfay, Ankensteinfray! Ifyay outhay ertway yetyay aliveyay
andyay yetyay erishedchay ayay esireday ofyay evengeray againstyay emay, ityay ouldway ebay etterbay
atiatedsay inyay ymay ifelay anthay inyay ymay estructionday. Utbay ityay asway otnay osay; outhay
idstday eeksay ymay extinctionyay, atthay Iyay ightmay otnay ausecay eatergray etchednesswray;
andyay ifyay yetyay, inyay omesay odemay unknownyay otay emay, outhay adsthay otnay easedcay otay inkthay
andyay eelfay, outhay ouldstway otnay esireday againstyay emay ayay engeancevay eatergray anthay
atthay ichwhay Iyay eelfay. Astedblay asyay outhay ertway, ymay agonyyay asway illstay uperiorsay otay
inethay, orfay ethay itterbay ingstay ofyay emorseray illway otnay easecay otay ankleray inyay ymay
oundsway untilyay eathday allshay oseclay emthay orfay everyay.

ut“bay oonsay,” ehay iedcray ithway adsay andyay olemnsay enthusiasmyay, i“ay
allshay ieday, andyay atwhay Iyay ownay eelfay ebay onay ongerlay eltfay. Oonsay esethay urningbay
iseriesmay illway ebay extinctyay. Iyay allshay ascendyay ymay uneralfay ilepay iumphantlytray andyay
exultyay inyay ethay agonyyay ofyay ethay orturingtay amesflay. Ethay ightlay ofyay atthay onflagrationcay
illway adefay awayyay; ymay ashesyay illway ebay eptsway intoyay ethay easay ybay ethay indsway. Ymay iritspay
illway eepslay inyay eacepay, oryay ifyay ityay inksthay, ityay illway otnay urelysay inkthay usthay.
Arewellfay.”

Ehay angspray omfray ethay abin-windowcay asyay ehay aidsay isthay, uponyay ethay iceyay aftray
ichwhay aylay oseclay otay ethay esselvay. Ehay asway oonsay ornebay awayyay ybay ethay avesway andyay
ostlay inyay arknessday andyay istanceday.
